Chapter 1450: A Six-Mark Oblivion Member's Life for My Duplicated Body's Life...

Chapter 1450: A Six-Mark Oblivion Member's Life for My Duplicated Body's Life
?
"Lord Ao Long, if we want to slay that Forbidden Zone cultivator, we would need to deploy at least one Six-Mark clansman. However, if a Six-Mark clansman takes action, they will inevitably be blocked by the opponent's powerhouses, and the target would likely flee immediately, making it impossible for our Six-Mark clansman to engage them.
Therefore, we should launch a surprise attack, committing a significant amount of force all at once to create an opportunity for a Six-Mark clansman to forcibly assassinate that cultivator in an instant."
A Five-Mark Oblivion clansman suggested.
"In that case, a Six-Mark Oblivion clansman will need to be sacrificed. Those with the potential to promote to Seven-Mark cannot be sacrificed. Find a Six-Mark clansman who has been heavily injured and has no chance of promotion. Let him do it, killing that cultivator at all costs. I will also take action on another front this time to draw the attention of a large number of their powerhouses and create an opportunity for you! Additionally, I will seek help from other clansmen at the Seven-Mark level and above to attack these damn Forbidden Zone creatures from multiple directions!"
Ao Long decided.
"Yes, Lord Ao Long!"
The many Oblivion clansmen responded.
....The area guarded by the War Ancestor.
Suddenly.
He sensed a large number of Oblivion clansmen attacking, including Seven-Mark Oblivion members.
"Stay alert, the Oblivion Clan is coming!"
The War Ancestor took action to intercept the Seven-Mark Oblivion member.
In other directions, the Oblivion Clan attacked simultaneously.
Under such circumstances, unless a defensive line was under little pressure, they could not provide reinforcements, and most defensive lines were unable to spare anyone.
In the area Ye Tian was guarding, they had just repelled a group of Oblivion clansmen not long ago, but he soon sensed another attack, and the scale was even larger than the last time.
"Request reinforcements!"
Ye Tian, the Peng Ancestor, and the others all called for help.
However, other directions were also under attack, so very few people could come to support, and it would take time to allocate manpower; they couldn't provide immediate assistance.
Boom!!!! The two sides clashed, and Ye Tian blocked three Four-Mark Oblivion clansmen and several Three-Mark Oblivion clansmen.
Abruptly.
Another Oblivion clansman appeared—a Six-Mark Oblivion member—and he went straight for Ye Tian.
"Not good, quickly support the Myriad Law War Ancestor!"
Many Supreme-level Domain Ancestors cried out in alarm.
At this moment, a Half-step Primordial Ancestor rushed over, but just as he was about to save Ye Tian, a Five-Mark Primordial Ancestor blocked him.
Everyone could see it—the Oblivion Clan was determined to kill Ye Tian!
"Escape!"
Ye Tian utilized his Void Escape Ancestral Technique to retreat rapidly.
He didn't want this duplicated body of his to perish like this, so he fled if he could.
"You cannot escape!"
The Six-Mark Oblivion member activated an Oblivion Clan talent, Space-Time, causing the effectiveness of Ye Tian's Void Escape Ancestral Technique to drop drastically.
Boom!!! One of the Six-Mark Oblivion member's hands clawed into space-time, reaching toward Ye Tian's position.
Crack, crack, crack!!!! The space-time around Ye Tian shattered.
The terrifying strike landed directly on Ye Tian's body. In an instant, Ye Tian's various defenses were shattered, and a claw pierced straight through his torso.
Had he not possessed the Oblivion Ancestral Talent, Ye Tian would not have been able to withstand such an attack; the erosion of Oblivion energy alone would have been enough to kill him.
But now that he had the Oblivion Ancestral Talent, although the attack annihilated ninety percent of his body, the Oblivion energy caused him no harm. Furthermore, he activated the Undying Ancestral Technique, managing to preserve his life just in time.
"Impossible, you're not dead?"
The Six-Mark Oblivion member was stunned.
His strength had reached the peak of a Half-step Primordial Ancestor among Forbidden Zone creatures. To fail to kill a Supreme-level Domain Ancestor who hadn't even reached the Half-step Primordial Ancestor level—especially in this space-time field that was completely advantageous to them—was unthinkable. One strike had actually failed to kill a Supreme-level Domain Ancestor.
"If you're not dead, then I'll do it again!"
The Six-Mark Oblivion member was determined to kill Ye Tian.
Such a monstrous existence, and so difficult to kill—if Ye Tian were allowed to grow, he would become a major threat to the Oblivion Clan.
Just as he was about to deliver the second strike, a Primordial Ancestor arrived.
At this point, if the Six-Mark Oblivion member retreated, he could still get away; even if the Primordial Ancestor pursued him, their Seven-Mark Oblivion members could intervene in time to save him.
But the key was that he wanted to kill Ye Tian at all costs. Therefore, he did not retreat but struck out again to crush Ye Tian.
"Was that really necessary?"
Ye Tian thought to himself.
Another claw fell, and Ye Tian's physical body was completely pulverized. This duplicated body was considered fallen.
Meanwhile, the Primordial Ancestor arrived and crushed the Six-Mark Oblivion member with one hand. Although the Oblivion Clan's Seven-Mark member had arrived, it was too late to save him.
With a bang! The Six-Mark Oblivion member was directly crushed to death by the Primordial Ancestor!
The gap between a Half-step Primordial Ancestor and a Primordial Ancestor was... just that large, almost impossible to bridge.
"Retreat!"
The Seven-Mark Oblivion member gave the order, and they began to withdraw.
In the blink of an eye, the Oblivion Clan had completely retreated.
The Primordial Ancestor also departed quickly, without lingering for a moment.
The Peng Ancestor did not know that this was Ye Tian's duplicated body and thought it was his original self. He sighed, "The Oblivion Clan is too cunning. They didn't deploy Seven-Mark members at first, so the Primordial Ancestors naturally wouldn't come to support immediately.
As a result, they actually sent a Six-Mark member to his death. Our request for reinforcements was a bit slow, which meant the Primordial Ancestor couldn't save the Myriad Law War Ancestor in time!"
"What a pity. If the Myriad Law War Ancestor had risen, he would have definitely had the hope of becoming a Primordial Ancestor in the future!"
Another Supreme-level Domain Ancestor spoke up.
"I don't think you need to feel pity. The Myriad Law War Ancestor shouldn't be dead!"
A mid-stage Supreme-level Domain Ancestor spoke.
He was a Supreme-level Domain Ancestor from the Firmament Holy Sect, so he knew a bit of information regarding the Myriad Law War Ancestor.
"The Myriad Law War Ancestor isn't dead? How is that possible? We saw it clearly; his body was forcibly slain by a Six-Mark Oblivion member, and both his flesh and soul were obliterated. How could he still be alive? Even Primordial Ancestors cannot resurrect a Supreme-level Domain Ancestor!"
The Peng Ancestor shook his head.
"That probably wasn't the Myriad Law War Ancestor's true body!"
The Supreme-level Domain Ancestor from the Firmament Holy Sect explained, "According to what I know, the Myriad Law War Ancestor seems to have a clone and a main body. That clone is very peculiar, almost identical to the main body—no one can tell them apart—and its combat power is also exactly the same.
I suspect the Myriad Law War Ancestor didn't come in person; what came was likely his clone.
Moreover, even if his clone perishes, it can be condensed once again!"
"There's a clone like that?"
The Peng Ancestor and the others were shocked.
In the Profound Void Holy Realm.
Ye Tian opened his eyes and murmured, "The duplicated body has fallen in battle..."
Because the distance was too great, it took a long time for the duplicated body to send back information, so he didn't know the full details of how it died.
"No matter. I'll just condense another duplicated body and head back to the Holy Domain Continent!"
Ye Tian said indifferently.

Chapter 1451: I'm Suited for Patrol!

Chapter 1451: I'm Suited for Patrol
!
Ye Tian accelerated time, and ten thousand years quickly passed, allowing him to condense another duplicate body.
Subsequently.
This duplicate body of Ye Tian headed to the War Ancestor Realm, asking the War Ancestor to send him to the Saint Realm Continent at the edge of the Dark Forbidden Zone.
....Saint Realm Continent.
When Ye Tian descended here once again, several Supreme-level Domain Ancestors who thought he had fallen were shocked to see him.
After explanations from other Supreme-level Domain Ancestors, they finally understood the reason and were all envious of Ye Tian's cloning technique.
Afterward, Ye Tian returned to the place he was stationed.
"Myriad Law War Ancestor, you really didn't perish!"
Peng Ancestor said happily upon seeing Ye Tian.
"No, the one who fell last time was merely one of my clones!"
Ye Tian explained.
"Hahaha, if the Desolation Race finds out, they'll probably be fuming. They sacrificed a Six-Mark Desolation member and still failed to kill you!"
Peng Ancestor and the others laughed heartily.
Peng Ancestor and the rest did not inquire about the secrets of Ye Tian's clones. After all, even if they asked, Ye Tian wouldn't tell them, and it would only serve to offend him.
Thus, they tactfully skipped over that question.
Afterward, life returned to normal.
In the blink of an eye, several thousand more years passed. The Desolation Race still didn't know Ye Tian wasn't dead because they hadn't attacked this particular line of defense again.
One day.
A small squad of the Desolation Race attacked Ye Tian's defensive line, and the two sides engaged in battle.
Ye Tian once again copied the talents of the Desolation Race. After all, this newly condensed duplicate body did not have the Desolation Ancestral Talent, so he had to copy it again.
During this skirmish, Ye Tian did not kill any members of the Desolation Race.
Consequently, the news that he wasn't dead was bound to be exposed.
....Desolation Race Territory.
A Four-Mark Desolation member reported the news of Ye Tian being alive to Ao Long.
"Lord Ao Long, that Forbidden Zone creature we sacrificed a Six-Mark member to kill last time has appeared again!"
The Four-Mark Desolation member reported.
"What? Are you sure?"
Ao Long said in disbelief.
"Certain. We exchanged blows with him; he is definitely still alive, and his strength is just as formidable!"
The Four-Mark Desolation member confirmed.
"How could he not be dead? His physical body was clearly annihilated, yet he's still alive? Could it be an avatar? No, if it were an avatar, we wouldn't fail to recognize it; it must be a true body! Besides, the clones of Supreme-level Domain Ancestors are usually very weak, and in this region of space-time, it's difficult for clones to exert their full strength. We would only need to slightly affect space-time to sever the connection, and their clones would be rendered useless."
Ao Long muttered to himself.
It was precisely because of this that those Supreme-level Domain Ancestors didn't bother spending effort to condense clones, as they were essentially useless.
In the following days, the Desolation Race attacked the defensive line where Ye Tian was located time and again, testing him repeatedly. They even isolated space-time to see if Ye Tian was a clone. In the end, no matter what they did, they couldn't affect Ye Tian's combat power.
Clearly, this body of Ye Tian's was not a clone, but a true body.
They couldn't understand how Ye Tian could still be alive, but they didn't dare to sacrifice the life of another Six-Mark Desolation member to test it, so they could only ignore him...
...and treat Ye Tian as an ordinary Supreme-level Domain Ancestor.
Meanwhile, Ye Tian copied many Ancestral Talents from the Desolation Race and exchanged the merit he earned from guarding this place for a stalk of ordinary Desolation Grass. This was a plant that contained concentrated desolation energy; to others, it was a poisonous weed, but to Ye Tian, it was a supreme treasure.
Afterward, Ye Tian requested leave to return, intending to bring this stalk of Desolation Grass back. More importantly, he wanted to send the Ancestral Talents he had copied onto his duplicate body back to his main body, as only then would they truly belong to him.
Otherwise, if the duplicate body died in battle, the Ancestral Talents would be lost again.
Profound Void Holy World.
Ye Tian's duplicate body returned.
"Desolation Ancestral Talent, bestow!"
"Time Ancestral Talent, bestow!"
Ye Tian's duplicate body bestowed each of the copied Ancestral Talents. He could fully integrate these talents, making his original Ancestral Talents even more powerful.
Of course, the Desolation Ancestral Talent and the Time Ancestral Talent were the most important, as these were talents Ye Tian did not possess before.
Once all the Ancestral Talents were bestowed, Ye Tian's duplicate body returned to the Saint Realm Continent.
For the Primordial Ancestors, sending someone into the Saint Realm Continent was just a matter of a single thought. Thus, they weren't afraid of the trouble, especially since it only happened once in a long while and didn't tax their minds at all.
Not long after.
Ye Tian fully integrated all the Ancestral Talents bestowed by the duplicate body.
"Desolation Grass, I wonder how effective it is?"
Ye Tian swallowed the Desolation Grass, which was rich in desolation energy, in one gulp.
Boom!!!!! Desolation energy erupted within Ye Tian's body. Then, under the influence of the Desolation Ancestral Talent, it began to temper Ye Tian's Ancestral Body and Supreme Domain Body.
After an unknown amount of time, the desolation energy within Ye Tian's body was completely refined by him.
"My Domain Body has strengthened quite a bit, and my Ancestral Body has also made some slight progress. It's a pity this was just the lowest grade of desolation treasure. If I had enough desolation treasures, my strength could probably improve rapidly, and my cultivation might even quickly rise to the middle stage of a Supreme-level Domain Ancestor!"
Ye Tian thought to himself.
Unfortunately, desolation treasures were very rare. Although he could exchange for them from the Primordial Ancestors, he needed merit.
Guarding the border of the Dark Forbidden Zone only earned a small amount of merit. He was only able to exchange for the Desolation Grass because he had killed several One-Mark Desolation members last time; otherwise, he would have needed to guard the place for countless ages to accumulate enough merit for it.
After all, for the Primordial Ancestors, desolation treasures could also improve their own cultivation, so they naturally wouldn't let others exchange for them easily.
Of course, even if Ye Tian had enough merit, if he kept exchanging for desolation treasures, the Primordial Ancestors would eventually discover his secret of being able to absorb desolation energy.
"The best choice is to go out and find desolation treasures myself! I should talk to the Primordial Ancestors about switching to a patrol mission.
With my strength and my immortal nature, patrolling is what suits me best. And only by patrolling is it easy to encounter desolation treasures!"
Ye Tian decided.
Thus, Ye Tian sought out the War Ancestor.
"War Ancestor, I want to take on a patrol mission. Staying stationed in that one area doesn't suit me!"
Ye Tian volunteered.
"Patrol!"
The War Ancestor thought about it carefully and realized it made sense. Although patrolling required at least the strength of a Half-Step Primordial Ancestor, while Ye Tian's strength wasn't quite there yet, the gap wasn't too large.
Moreover, it didn't matter if Ye Tian's clone died. A patroller could act as a rescue force; even if they encountered an attack from a Primordial Ancestor, Ye Tian could stall for a brief moment, buying time for other Supreme-level Domain Ancestors to escape.
Therefore, Ye Tian was indeed more suited for patrolling.
"Fine, I agree. I'll speak with the other Primordial Ancestors later and have you assigned as one of the patrollers!"
The War Ancestor agreed.

Chapter 1452: Nirvana Crystals, A Great Harvest!

Chapter 1452: Nirvana Crystals, A Great Harvest
!
Shortly after, the War Ancestor spoke with the other Ancestors. Many Ancestors agreed to let Ye Tian become one of the patrolmen, but many others disagreed.
Almost all the Ancestors who disagreed were from the Dark Destruction Domain. They already had conflicts with the Dark Holy Domain and were only reluctantly cooperating here due to the threat of the Nirvana Clan.
If the threat of the Nirvana Clan were removed in the future, the two sides would likely be at each other's throats again.
Therefore, it was normal for them to disagree with Ye Tian becoming a patrolman.
However, it was enough that some Ancestors agreed; it didn't matter if the others didn't.
Regardless... the War Ancestor allowed Ye Tian to become a patrolman, and there was nothing they could do about it.... "Myriad Law War Ancestor, you can now become a patrolman. This is a communication treasure specifically for patrols; it can be used here!"
The War Ancestor gave Ye Tian a black bracelet and said.
"Understood!"
Ye Tian nodded and accepted the bracelet.
From then on, he was one of the patrolmen of this region of space-time, patrolling various defense lines. Once the Nirvana Clan appeared anywhere, he had to go and provide support.
After becoming a patrolman, Ye Tian patrolled the defense lines one by one, which was quite easy.
In the blink of an eye, hundreds of thousands of years passed.
During this period, Ye Tian rescued various defense lines multiple times. He even fell three times—of course, this was because he attacked the Nirvana Clan frantically, even sacrificing his duplicated body to kill a one-mark Nirvana Clan member.
Although he fell three times, he killed a total of five one-mark Nirvana Clan members, earning a significant amount of contribution points. He exchanged these for two more stalks of Nirvana Grass. Additionally, during his patrols, he found two Nirvana treasures. Although they were very low-level treasures, they were still good gains.
He sent these Nirvana treasures back to the Profound Void Holy Realm for his main body to refine. His Ancestral Body and Supreme Territory Body made considerable progress, though they were still far from advancing.
One day.
While Ye Tian was on patrol, he sensed fluctuations of Nirvana energy.
Other Supreme-level Territory Ancestors, or even Ancestors, were likely inferior to him in sensing Nirvana energy fluctuations.
This was because he possessed the Nirvana Ancestral Talent, while other Supreme-level Territory Ancestors and Ancestors did not.
Swish! Ye Tian flew over. He felt that it was definitely a sign of a Nirvana treasure being born, and it wasn't very far from his current position, just slightly close to the Space-Time Corridor.
Soon, Ye Tian arrived at the place where the Nirvana energy fluctuations were abnormal.
In this area, Nirvana energy surged, and gray crystals were slowly condensing.
"This is..."
Ye Tian recognized these gray crystals.
These gray crystals were on the exchange list; they were called Nirvana Crystals and were a very common type of Nirvana treasure in this space-time.
Although common, they were very precious—far more precious than Nirvana Grass....
If Nirvana treasures were categorized, Nirvana Grass would at most be a low-level Nirvana treasure, while Nirvana Crystals were mid-level Nirvana treasures. One Nirvana Crystal was worth at least dozens of stalks of Nirvana Grass.
And there wasn't just one or two Nirvana Crystals about to be born here; there were at least a hundred.
"The Nirvana energy fluctuations are too large and are still expanding. Once the Nirvana Clan approaches this place, with their Nirvana Clan talents, they will definitely be able to sense it easily!"
Ye Tian thought to himself.
Immediately, he activated his Nirvana Ancestral Talent and began to absorb the Nirvana energy here, attempting to keep the fluctuations under control.
Soon, the Nirvana energy fluctuations were controlled by Ye Tian at a very stable level, so the Nirvana Clan could no longer sense them.
Of course, he had to maintain control at all times. Once he lost control, the Nirvana energy fluctuations would spread out.
As time passed, the Nirvana Crystals gradually began to condense.
In the blink of an eye, a thousand years passed.
Fortunately, there were no Nirvana Clan invasions during this time; otherwise, if he couldn't leave, the Ancestors would definitely blame him.
Rumble!!!! The Nirvana Crystals were completely condensed, turning into brilliant gray crystals. The fluctuations instantly affected a vast area, and even Ye Tian could no longer suppress them.
"Collect!"
Ye Tian quickly collected these Nirvana Crystals and then used the Void Evasion Ancestral Technique to return toward the Holy Domain continent at maximum speed.
Just a few seconds after Ye Tian left, a terrifying figure appeared there.
It was an eight-mark Nirvana Clan member! He looked around but found no Nirvana treasures. He snorted coldly, "I'm too late. I don't know who took them!"
The Ancestors were even slower to find out; by the time they arrived, there was nothing left to see.
These Ancestors thought the Nirvana treasures had been taken by the Nirvana Clan, unaware that Ye Tian had taken them.
After obtaining these Nirvana Crystals, Ye Tian immediately applied to return to the Dark Holy Domain.
Soon, he was sent back by the War Ancestor.
Afterward, he delivered the Nirvana Crystals to his main body and stayed for a few days before returning to the Holy Domain continent to resume his patrols.
Profound Void Holy Realm.
Ye Tian held a Nirvana Crystal in his hand and began to absorb its energy.
Boom!!!! Incredibly pure Nirvana energy flooded into Ye Tian's body, tempering his Supreme Territory Body and Ancestral Body.
"Such a powerful effect!"
Ye Tian said excitedly.
With so many Nirvana Crystals, he could likely temper his Supreme Territory Body to a level close to the middle stage, and even his Ancestral Body would be tempered significantly.
In the blink of an eye, ten million years passed.
By this time, Ye Tian had already refined these Nirvana Crystals, and his Supreme Territory Body was, as he had guessed, very close to the middle stage.
His strength also surged significantly, bringing him closer to having half-step Ancestor combat power.
....Unknowingly, Ye Tian's duplicated body had been guarding the border of the Dark Forbidden Zone for a full billion years. During this time, he had died countless times, but he had also harvested many Nirvana treasures and exchanged for some as well.
Unfortunately, he didn't have the same luck as he did with the Nirvana Crystals, so the Nirvana treasures he obtained were quite ordinary.
But even so, these Nirvana treasures allowed his strength to soar.
Now, he was using these Nirvana treasures to charge toward the middle stage of the Supreme Territory Body realm.
Once he succeeded, he would possess half-step Ancestor combat power.

Chapter 1453: Half-Step Ancestral Realm, Star Taboo Fruit!

Chapter 1453: Half-Step Ancestral Realm, Star Taboo Fruit
!
BOOM!!!!! One by one, Annihilation Crystals were consumed by Ye Tian, and the Supreme Domain Body within his body began to undergo a transformation.
At the same time, Ye Tian brought out countless energy treasures. After all, the advancement of the Supreme Domain Body required a massive amount of energy. Annihilation treasures only allowed Ye Tian's Supreme Domain Body to be rapidly tempered and break through its shackles, but energy replenishment could not rely entirely on Annihilation treasures.
Moreover, he wasn't so extravagant as to use Annihilation treasures solely for energy replenishment.
Soon.
Ye Tian's Supreme Domain Body officially broke through, and countless energy treasures were consumed by him.
At this moment, Ye Tian's body was transforming. Once the transformation was complete, he would reach the middle stage of the Supreme-level Domain Ancestor realm, completely crossing a bottleneck that other Supreme-level Domain Ancestors found difficult to overcome even over endless eons.
And since his foundation far surpassed other Supreme-level Domain Ancestors, the increase in strength from advancing a minor stage was far greater than the magnitude of improvement for others.
It was conceivable how exaggerated the boost from Annihilation treasures was for his strength.
Approximately several hundred thousand years passed before Ye Tian finally completed the breakthrough.
"I've finally reached the middle stage of the Supreme-level Domain Ancestor realm. My strength has skyrocketed. Now, I am capable of fighting a true Half-step Progenitor without falling into a disadvantage!"
Ye Tian possessed such confidence.
However, after his cultivation reached the middle stage of the Supreme-level Domain Ancestor realm, advancing to the late stage would be even more difficult, requiring even more Annihilation treasures.
His duplicated bodies could slowly collect Annihilation treasures; there was no need for his main body to worry about it.
Furthermore, he couldn't place all his hopes solely on Annihilation treasures.
Within the Dark Forbidden Zone, many precious treasures were no less effective than Annihilation treasures, and some were even more precious than average Annihilation treasures. Otherwise, the Dark Forbidden Zone wouldn't have given birth to so many Progenitors.
For instance, if a new Ancestral Realm were born, it would be enough to tempt even a Progenitor.
After all, when an Ancestral Realm is first born, many Innate items are created. The Innate items of an Ancestral Realm far surpass those of ordinary worlds, enough to drive even Supreme-level Domain Ancestors mad. Obtaining just one would be enough to significantly increase one's strength.
The Xuanxu Holy Realm was naturally still a long way from becoming an Ancestral Realm, but it now far surpassed any Holy Realm.
If one were to describe its level, it would be a Half-step Ancestral Realm.
Time flowed by.
On this day.
A special world was born within the Xuanxu Holy Realm. As soon as this world appeared, Ye Tian immediately sealed it, forbidding anyone from entering. Even the Invincible Domain Ancestors of the human race were not allowed to enter, nor were they even allowed to know the situation of this world.
Regarding this, the Invincible Domain Ancestors of the human race did not dare to have any objections.
After all, everything the human race possessed now was given by Ye Tian. Even if they knew, they wouldn't dare to have any designs on it. Ye Tian's strength had reached a height they could never hope to attain; no one dared to oppose him.
At this moment, Ye Tian appeared within this special world.
"This world is actually giving birth to Ancestral Qi!"
Ye Tian murmured.
He sensed wisps of Ancestral Qi permeating the void. Although very faint, it definitely existed.
Ancestral Qi only appeared in Ancestral Realms. For Domain Ancestors, Ancestral Qi was a higher level of energy. Therefore, cultivating in an Ancestral Realm far surpassed cultivating in a Holy Realm.
But a Holy Realm could not produce Ancestral Qi.
Now, if the news that the Xuanxu Holy Realm was producing Ancestral Qi leaked out, trouble would follow. Even Progenitors might come to investigate.
The situation of the Xuanxu Holy Realm could not withstand a Progenitor's investigation. Back then, a mere thought from the Progenitor of War had arrived at the Xuanxu Holy Realm and almost frightened him, fearing the secrets of the Xuanxu Holy Realm would be exposed. However, a single thought from a Progenitor didn't have that much power, and the Progenitor of War hadn't intentionally investigated the Xuanxu Holy Realm.
Thus, the secrets of the Xuanxu Holy Realm remained hidden.
But if a Progenitor were to investigate intentionally, even if they couldn't find the Creation Primordial Well, they would easily discover the extraordinary and unique nature of the Xuanxu Holy Realm.
"Ancestral Qi has been born. The Xuanxu Holy Realm is evolving toward an Ancestral Realm, and this world is... the starting point of that evolution!"
Ye Tian murmured.
He could feel the Ancestral Qi in this world slowly increasing. In the future, it would surely become the core of the Xuanxu Holy Realm, and the core of the future Xuanxu Ancestral Realm.
Because of this, he sealed this world. He would stall for as much time as possible. Once his strength grew, he would fear nothing.
Even if the Progenitors knew the Xuanxu Holy Realm would become an Ancestral Realm, so what? If he possessed combat power comparable to a Progenitor, then owning an Ancestral Realm would be perfectly normal.
"This world will become the core of the Xuanxu Holy Realm and even the Xuanxu Ancestral Realm in the future. Let's call it the Heavenly Human Realm!"
Ye Tian gave the world a name.
In the blink of an eye, another hundred million years passed.
On this day.
A change occurred in the Heavenly Human Realm; a small tree was born.
The birth of this small tree caught Ye Tian's attention.
"An Innate item!"
He revealed a look of pleasant surprise.
Moreover, this was not a Holy Realm Innate item, but one equivalent to an Ancestral Realm Innate item, which could also be called an Innate Ancestral Item, distinct from ordinary Innate items.
At this moment, this small tree was frantically absorbing the Ancestral Qi of the Heavenly Human Realm.
BOOM!!!! Ye Tian's consciousness touched the small tree, and after some deduction, he learned part of its information.
Innate Ancestral Item—Star Taboo Tree!
According to his deductions, the Star Taboo Fruit produced by this Star Taboo Tree could temper the body and even had a certain effect on tempering the Supreme-level Domain Body. For Supreme-level Domain Ancestors, its value was incredibly precious.
If an Invincible Domain Body were to refine a Star Taboo Fruit, just one would be enough to allow an Invincible Domain Ancestor to advance directly from the early stage to the perfection stage of the Invincible Domain Ancestor realm.
Of course.
Such a Star Taboo Tree required a sufficiently long time to grow from birth to maturity.
Thus.
In the following days, Ye Tian set up a time acceleration array around the Star Taboo Tree and mobilized countless resources to supply its growth.
Under Ye Tian's strenuous cultivation, after three hundred million years had passed, the Star Taboo Tree reached maturity, transforming into a divine tree billions of miles tall, and it even grew 108 Star Taboo Fruits.
Each Star Taboo Fruit was as large as a star, emitting an enticing, refreshing fragrance.

Chapter 1454: The Ji Mie Clan are Leeks, This is the Truth!

Chapter 1454: The Ji Mie Clan are Leeks, This is the Truth
!
Ye Tian picked all 108 Star Forbidden Fruits, intending to use some for himself and bestow the rest upon his relatives.
However, it would take an even longer period for this Star Forbidden Tree to produce a second batch of Star Forbidden Fruits. Thus, he did not continue cultivating the tree there and instead departed.
Subsequently.
Ye Tian summoned Ye Xingchen, Ye Xingyue, his wife Xiao Yue, and other relatives to his side.
"Father!"
"Husband!"
"Brother!"
After they arrived, they called out to him.
"You've come!"
Ye Tian said with a smile, then took out the Star Forbidden Fruits one by one.
"These are Star Forbidden Fruits. Just one is enough to raise your cultivation to the limit of an Invincible Territory Ancestor. Take them and refine them; it will save you countless years of bitter cultivation.
Otherwise, with your current cultivation speed, reaching the limit of the Invincible Territory Ancestor realm would likely take an incredibly long time!"
Ye Tian explained.
"Star Forbidden Fruits? To think there's such a good thing!"
Ye Xingchen and the others said with great excitement.
Soon, each of them took one Star Forbidden Fruit. They didn't take more, as one was indeed enough for each person.
Afterward, they returned to begin refining the Star Forbidden Fruits.
With the help of the Star Forbidden Fruits, the four of them—Ye Xingchen, Ye Xingyue, Xiao Yue, and Ye Yu—successively raised their cultivation to the limit of the Invincible Territory Ancestor realm within a million years.
Their strength also increased significantly, approaching the combat power of a First-Step Invincible Territory Ancestor.
Once they achieved some results in mastering the limits of the physical body, they would definitely possess the combat power of a First-Step Invincible Territory Ancestor.
Meanwhile, Ye Tian was also refining the Star Forbidden Fruits. Although the fruits weren't of immense help to him, he couldn't ignore the sheer quantity! One Star Forbidden Fruit was enough to push his progress from the middle stage of the Supreme-level Territory Ancestor realm toward the late stage by about three percent.
Ye Tian's speed in refining the Star Forbidden Fruits was much faster than Ye Xingchen and the others; he could refine one fruit in nearly ten thousand years.
Thus, now that a million years had passed, Ye Tian had refined all 100 Star Forbidden Fruits, leaving only the final four to be reserved for the geniuses of the human race in the future.
What Ye Tian didn't know was that in the border spacetime of the Dark Forbidden Domain, six Ancestors were opening a very important meeting.
Within a void palace, six Ancestors sat.
Among these six Ancestors, two came from the Dark Holy Domain, three from the Dark Destruction Domain, and one was the leader of a certain Supreme Sect within the Dark Forbidden Domain.
These six Ancestors were no ordinary Ancestors; they were top-tier Ancestors who stood above the average, with strength comparable to an Eight-Mark Ji Mie Clan member.
"Everyone, another cycle has turned. The third Dark Holy Land is about to arrive. We have delayed at this border for far too long!"
The speaker was the Spacetime Ancestor of the Dark Destruction Domain, the same one who had constructed the Spacetime Gate. His strength was incredibly formidable, far surpassing that of an ordinary Ancestor.
"Indeed, the value of the third Dark Holy Land is much higher than this place!"
The speaker was the World Ancestor, an Ancestor from the Battle Sect.
Others believed the Battle Sect had only one Ancestor, but in reality, there were two: the Battle Ancestor and the World Ancestor. The Battle World Tower was actually the World Ancestor's sacred object.
The Battle Ancestor's strength was only comparable to a top-tier Seven-Mark Ji Mie Clan member, while the World Ancestor was the second Ancestor of the Battle Sect, yet his strength surpassed the Battle Ancestor, reaching the combat power of an Eight-Mark Ji Mie Clan member, second only to the first Ancestor of the Dark Holy Domain—the Holy Ancestor.
The Holy Ancestor's strength was actually comparable to a Nine-Mark Ji Mie Clan member, much stronger than even the Spacetime Ancestor.
In a one-on-one fight, if the Spacetime Ancestor didn't run, he might even be killed by the Holy Ancestor.
Of course, the Dark Destruction Domain also had an Ancestor comparable to a Nine-Mark Ji Mie Clan member: the Destruction Ancestor, known as the source of endless destruction.
With the Destruction Ancestor and three top-tier Ancestors in one sect, plus many ordinary Ancestors, the Dark Holy Domain's strength was actually slightly inferior.
Of course.
The potential of the Dark Holy Domain was very high. Had it not been born so late, it wouldn't be inferior to the Dark Destruction Domain.
There are currently two Dark Holy Lands in the Dark Forbidden Domain. The first is the Dark Destruction Domain, and the second is the Dark Holy Domain. This is something many cultivators are unaware of, as they assume the Dark Destruction Domain was born later.
However, when a Dark Holy Land is born, there is a protection period during which Ancestors cannot enter. Otherwise, the Dark Holy Domain would have long been destroyed or occupied by the Dark Destruction Domain.
If Ye Tian knew the true strength of these Ancestors, he would be very confused. Their side possessed two Ancestors comparable to Nine-Mark Ji Mie Clan members, while the Ji Mie Clan only had one. Why had they never defeated the Ji Mie Clan and could only barely hold them back?
There was only one reason: Ji Mie Treasures! Once the Ji Mie Clan was wiped out, this special spacetime would cease to exist, making it difficult for Ji Mie Treasures to continue being born.
The Ji Mie Treasures were valuable to them, and presiding over this place was very safe, allowing them to harvest "leeks" time and time again.
This was the real reason why the Ji Mie Clan continued to exist without being exterminated.
As for the occasional fall of a Supreme-level Territory Ancestor, it meant nothing to them. What did the death of a few Supreme-level Territory Ancestors matter? When these factions fought each other, many Supreme-level Territory Ancestors fell, so this loss was negligible.
Of course.
Such secrets could not be told to the Supreme-level Territory Ancestors, otherwise, the impact would be too great.
Furthermore, the Supreme-level Territory Ancestors might not fight the Ji Mie Clan seriously. If they relied solely on these Ancestors, they wouldn't be able to intercept all the Ji Mie Clan members. If some escaped, it would truly be a major problem.
After all, the Ji Mie Clan grew very quickly. If given enough resources and territory, they could truly produce several Nine-Mark Ji Mie Clan members.
Thus, this was not a scene they wished to see.
But things were different now. The third Dark Holy Land was about to be born; this was a rule of the Dark Forbidden Domain and something the Ancestors had calculated.
As for where the third Dark Holy Land would appear, they could not calculate it and could only wait silently.
But one thing was very clear: once the third Dark Holy Land was born, the Supreme-level Territory Ancestors could not remain here; they had to contribute to the struggle for the third Dark Holy Land.
At that time, these factions would no longer be able to cooperate.
Therefore, they had to crush the Ji Mie Clan and destroy this place. They could no longer leave it be, or their forces would be tied down, and many things would be impossible to accomplish.

As for Ancestors of the War Ancestor's level, they clashed with the Seven-Mark Oblivions.

Chapter 1456: The Nirvana Race Has Been Wiped Out Just Like That!

Chapter 1456: The Nirvana Race Has Been Wiped Out Just Like That!
!
Ye Tian did not engage any members of the Nirvana Race above five marks. Although his strength was comparable to a five-mark Nirvana member, he was unable to actually kill one.
Therefore, he directly targeted those below five marks. This way, he could not only slaughter a large number of them but also harvest some Nirvana treasures.
This time, his primary goal was to obtain a batch of Nirvana treasures.
At the same time, his Copy Talent continuously enveloped the surrounding area, copying the talents of one Nirvana member after another.
Only in this way could he maximize his gains.
Boom! A two-mark Nirvana member was strangled by a casual Golden Silk Ancestral Technique from Ye Tian, and its corpse was collected by him.
The Nirvana members here were different from those who attacked the defense line. Once the Nirvana Race attacked the defense line, they were not allowed to carry any resources except for their own weapons.
This was to prevent resources from being seized by the creatures of the Dark Forbidden Zone after the Nirvana members died in battle.
But now, this was the Nirvana Race's territory, and they carried their resources with them. Thus, killing a single Nirvana member allowed him to obtain a certain amount of Nirvana treasures and resources, which was why Ye Tian was so keen on killing them.
The other Supreme Domain Ancestors didn't seem to know the value of Nirvana treasures, so they didn't have the same idea.
Puff, puff, puff! One after another, one-mark and two-mark Nirvana members died under Ye Tian's Golden Silk Ancestral Technique.
Ye Tian also continuously utilized his Void Escape Ancestral Technique. His speed was incredibly fast as he crossed one Nirvana territory after another, constantly copying a vast number of Nirvana talents while searching for weaker members to kill, occasionally saving a few Supreme Domain Ancestors along the way.
However, even so, some Supreme Domain Ancestors still fell, and the number was not small.
Yet, compared to the Nirvana Race, the number of fallen Supreme Domain Ancestors was almost negligible.
Boom! A seven-mark Nirvana member was blasted to death, triggering a chain reaction.
Following that, one seven-mark Nirvana member after another was slain.
It had to be said that the life-saving capabilities of the seven-mark Nirvana members were too poor, whereas Ancestors were not easily killed.
Strictly speaking, the Ancestors were perfect lifeforms, while the Nirvana Race possessed significant flaws.
Otherwise, not a single Ancestor would have fallen to this day, while several seven-mark Nirvana members had already perished.
The same applied to the Supreme Domain Ancestors. Although many were eroded by Nirvana power and suffered heavy injuries, they simply wouldn't die.
In contrast, once a Nirvana member suffered the same level of injury, they were doomed.
As time passed, Ye Tian copied an immense number of Nirvana talents.
After all, he could easily traverse various territories. Essentially, by staying in a territory for a single second, he could copy the talents of every Nirvana member in that area.
The other Supreme Domain Ancestors didn't know Ye Tian was copying talents; they thought he was rushing around to provide support, so they didn't pay much attention.
Before long, Ye Tian had visited every territory and had copied the talents of almost every Nirvana member.
Only then did he begin to attack with full force, even breaking into the buildings within the Nirvana territories to plunder resources.
Although many Supreme Domain Ancestors didn't know the exact value of the Nirvana treasures and resources, they began to collect them upon seeing them. After all, the Ancestors offered options to exchange for Nirvana treasures, so they were definitely valuable. There was no reason to leave them behind.
Ten days! One month! One year! Ten years! This battle lasted for a full hundred years. A massive number of Nirvana members fell, and finally, the Ancestors were able to free themselves up.
This was because the Ancestors had killed almost all of the seven-mark and eight-mark Nirvana members.
Once these Ancestors joined the battlefield against the six-mark and lower Nirvana members, it became a total massacre.
In a short while, the Nirvana Race was completely wiped out.
Subsequently, the Ancestors began to collect the corpses of these Nirvana members and started plundering the resources within their territories.
Ye Tian naturally couldn't compete with the Ancestors, but he entered some smaller territories to begin gathering Nirvana resources.
Some Supreme Domain Ancestors seemed to realize something and joined the ranks of those plundering resources.
Suddenly.
From the depths of endless time and space came the voice of the nine-mark Nirvana member, Ji: "Saint Ancestor, Destruction Ancestor, the two of you hid your strength so deeply! I am unwilling!"
Accompanied by a loud bang.
The depths of endless time and space seemed to be shattered, and the nine-mark Nirvana member, Ji, was blasted to death.
Crack! The Saint Ancestor and the Destruction Ancestor stepped out from the depths of time and space. They looked slightly disheveled, but their condition was excellent.
"Even a nine-mark Nirvana member was killed by the combined efforts of the Saint Ancestor and the Destruction Ancestor. They really were hiding their strength," Ye Tian thought to himself.
Why would the Destruction Ancestor and the Saint Ancestor hide their strength? Based on their power, they probably could have solved the Nirvana Race problem long ago. Why wait until today? "Were they harvesting leeks?"
Ye Tian thought of this possibility.
Perhaps the Ancestors also needed Nirvana treasures, which was why they kept the Nirvana Race around. Regardless, the Nirvana Race wasn't a threat to them. Even if they needed to guard this place, couldn't they cultivate anywhere? Therefore, they had never wiped out the Nirvana Race.
As for why they chose to destroy them now, something must have happened that he wasn't aware of.
"The Ancestors probably all know the reason, but the Supreme Domain Ancestors likely don't. Otherwise, those Supreme Domain Ancestors wouldn't be so terrified of the Nirvana Race! Even the Fire-Mark War Ancestor was afraid. Clearly, even veteran Supreme Domain Ancestors like him were kept in the dark," Ye Tian mused.
He could go ask the War Ancestor, but the War Ancestor likely wouldn't tell him; otherwise, such news would have leaked out long ago.
At this moment.
Many Supreme Domain Ancestors also felt that something was off, but since the Nirvana Race had already been wiped out, what could they say? To question the Ancestors would be seeking death. In short, they had survived, and that was enough.
As for the fallen Supreme Domain Ancestors, they were mostly those with insufficient strength. Not a single truly powerful Supreme Domain Ancestor had perished, though some were heavily injured.
"Everyone, leave!"
The Ancestors spoke.
Immediately.
One by one, the Supreme Domain Ancestors found themselves being teleported out of this space-time by the Ancestors.
When Ye Tian regained his senses, he found himself back in the War Ancestor Realm. The other Supreme Domain Ancestors of the War Ancestor Realm had also returned.
This time, not a single Supreme Domain Ancestor from the War Ancestor Realm had fallen. The Supreme Domain Ancestors from the Dark Holy Region who died mostly belonged to those Holy Lands.
One could imagine that the Seventy-Two Holy Lands would likely undergo a major reshuffle.
But Ye Tian no longer cared about such trivial matters.
At this moment, he immediately returned to the Profound Void Holy Realm. He wanted to deliver the Nirvana treasures he had obtained to his main body so that his main body could refine them and increase his strength.
Once those Nirvana treasures were refined, his strength would likely receive a terrifying boost.

Chapter 1457: Ultimate Ancestral Talent!

Chapter 1457: Ultimate Ancestral Talent
!
"So many Nirvana treasures!"
Ye Tian was extremely excited to see these dense clusters of Nirvana treasures.
Moreover, among them were many high-level and top-tier Nirvana treasures, whose effects were far more powerful than Nirvana crystals.
"I'll fuse the Ancestral Talents of the Nirvana Race first. Once the fusion is successful, there might be unexpected results!"
Ye Tian murmured.
Subsequently, in the following days, Ye Tian began to fuse these Ancestral Talents, constantly merging those of the same category together.
One Ancestral Talent, fused! Ten Ancestral Talents, fused! A hundred Ancestral Talents, fused! .... Ye Tian had copied almost all the Ancestral Talents of the Nirvana Race, and now he was merging them all. Although it would take a vast amount of time, Ye Tian could clearly sense that the several types of Ancestral Talents he had copied and fused were constantly evolving and strengthening.
Strength Ancestral Talent! Speed Ancestral Talent! Defense Ancestral Talent! Nirvana Ancestral Talent! Time Ancestral Talent! These five major Ancestral Talents were all becoming stronger at an incredible speed.
In the blink of an eye, a hundred million years passed, and within the time acceleration array, Ye Tian had spent an even more localized and lengthy period of time.
Finally, when nearly all of these Ancestral Talents were fused, Ye Tian's Strength Ancestral Talent underwent a qualitative change.
Boom!!!!! Deep within his soul, the mark of Ye Tian's Strength Ancestral Talent seemed to be evolving into a world—a world belonging to the talent of strength.
After a long time, this miniature world was born.
"Ultimate Ancestral Talent!"
Ye Tian murmured.
With the birth of this miniature Strength Ancestral Talent world, his Strength Ancestral Talent transformed into an Ultimate Ancestral Talent. Although it was still an Ancestral Talent, it had reached the ultimate peak of the grade, essentially becoming a different level of Ancestral Talent.
Furthermore, this Ultimate Ancestral Talent was different from ordinary ones. Even if an ordinary Ancestral Talent was activated, it could at most unleash power comparable to a Saint Technique; if it couldn't be properly utilized, it was almost useless.
Much like the Nirvana Race—although every one of them possessed an Ancestral Talent, their comprehension was poor. Consequently, they couldn't create Ancestral Techniques and could only purely activate their Ancestral Talents for attacks. Thus, they could only unleash the power of a Saint Technique at most; otherwise, they wouldn't have been wiped out by the Progenitors.
An Ultimate Ancestral Talent, however, could unleash power surpassing an Ancestral Technique, though it was only the power of a single strike.
For example, once the Ultimate Strength Ancestral Talent erupted, it was equivalent to mobilizing the power of the entire Ultimate Strength Ancestral Talent world for a single, terrifying explosive strike.
But for Ye Tian, with the Ultimate Strength Ancestral Talent, he could easily cultivate various Strength Ancestral Techniques to the Perfection stage.
In the future, he even had the hope of deducing Strength Ancestral Techniques to the level of Ultimate Ancestral Techniques. At that point, he might be able to kill Progenitors while at a lower level.
"Let's bring out the other Ultimate Ancestral Talents one by one!"
Ye Tian murmured.
With continuous fusion, the Ultimate Defense, Ultimate Speed, Ultimate Nirvana, and Ultimate Time Ancestral Talents were born one after another.
Additionally.
Ye Tian discovered that after his Nirvana Ancestral Talent reached the Ultimate level, his speed in refining Nirvana treasures became faster, and his utilization rate was higher, reaching a level of nearly 100% utilization.
With his Ultimate Nirvana Ancestral Talent and the Nirvana treasures he had obtained, he had enough to push his cultivation to the peak of the Supreme Realm Ancestor level, which was also the limit he could reach.
For him, it was impossible to take the Half-Step Progenitor route, so the next step was... Progenitor. As for how long it would take him to become a Progenitor, he didn't know; it would likely be a very long time.
After all, he currently had no clue at all.
"Let's raise my cultivation first; I'll worry about future matters later!"
Ye Tian continued his secluded cultivation and began refining that massive amount of Nirvana treasures.
Piece after piece of Nirvana treasures were refined by Ye Tian, causing his cultivation to advance continuously.
One hundred million years! One billion years! In the blink of an eye, three billion years passed.
To... Supreme Realm Ancestors, this amount of time really wasn't much, and to... Progenitors, it was merely the time it took to take a nap.
At this time, under the accumulation and refining of Nirvana treasures, Ye Tian finally raised his cultivation to the peak of the Supreme Realm Ancestor level, reaching a point where his cultivation could progress no further.
More importantly, Ye Tian now began to use Nirvana treasures to temper his Ancestral Body.
Nirvana treasures also had an effect on tempering the Ancestral Body, but he had been focusing on: raising his cultivation and had set aside the tempering of his Ancestral Body. Thus, he could now continue using Nirvana treasures for that purpose.
All along, Ye Tian's Ancestral Body had been at the Small Success stage.
Of course.
The Ancestral Body could raise its realm through evolution to complete rapid cultivation, but if there were resources like Nirvana treasures, the speed of progress would naturally be even faster.
Thus.
Ye Tian worked in synchronization with his duplicated body. The duplicated body evolved the Ancestral Body, while the original body used Nirvana treasures to temper it. This allowed him to push the Ancestral Body toward the Great Success stage more quickly.
In the blink of an eye, another billion years passed.
However, Ye Tian's Nirvana treasures were exhausted, and his Ancestral Body had only been deduced to the peak of the Small Success stage. He was still one step away from the Great Success stage, but this step was extremely difficult to cross.
"It's enough. To have increased my strength to this point is already very fast!"
Ye Tian murmured.
In the following days, Ye Tian exchanged for some more Strength, Defense, Speed, and Time-type Saint Techniques from the Battle Gate.
Afterward, he began practicing these Saint Techniques, easily elevating them to Ancestral Techniques and then effortlessly cultivating those Ancestral Techniques to the Perfection stage.
In reality, practicing more Ancestral Techniques didn't provide a significant boost for... Ye Tian.
But the more Ancestral Techniques he practiced, the deeper his insight into that specific path became, which would help Ye Tian deduce Ancestral Techniques into Ultimate Ancestral Techniques in the future.
It was precisely because of this that Ye Tian practiced Saint Techniques and Ancestral Techniques so frantically instead of wasting time.
On this day, a message came from the Battle Gate, cutting off Ye Tian's thoughts of continuing his secluded cultivation.
"So that's how it is..."
Ye Tian was shocked.
Only now did he finally learn why the Progenitors had so suddenly invaded and wiped out the Nirvana Race.
It was because the third Dark Holy Land of the Dark Forbidden Zone was about to be born.
"As expected, the Nirvana Race were just leeks. The birth of the third Dark Holy Land is many times more important than the Nirvana Race. That's why the Progenitors didn't want to continue guarding the Nirvana Race's borders and acted to wipe them out! The Supreme Realm Ancestors were just small soldiers on the front lines, and uninformed ones at that!"
Ye Tian murmured.
Suddenly.
Ye Tian thought of something. Where was the third Dark Holy Land? "Could it be that the Dao Mountain Territory where I am located is... the third Dark Holy Land?"
Ye Tian thought to himself.
"No!"
Ye Tian shook his head. "Dark Holy Lands are places like the Dark Destruction Realm and the Dark Holy Realm. They are born naturally, precious lands evolved from the rules of the Dark Forbidden Zone. The Dao Mountain Territory was created by me using the Creation Primordial Well; it cannot be the third Dark Holy Land.
However, the Dao Mountain Territory might develop into the fourth Dark Holy Land in the future, but that would require a very long time."
Thinking this, he breathed a sigh of relief.
Otherwise, if the Dao Mountain Territory really were the third Dark Holy Land, he would have no choice but to move; he wouldn't be able to withstand that immense pressure.

Chapter 1458: The Third Dark Holy Land, It's Simply Made For...

Chapter 1458: The Third Dark Holy Land, It's Simply Made For Me
!
As the news of the imminent birth of the third Dark Holy Land spread, the entire Dark Holy Domain was in a frenzy.
The third Dark Holy Land—this was a brand-new holy land comparable to the Dark Holy Domain itself. The key was the countless resources within; it was absolutely the stuff of dreams for innumerable cultivators.
Moreover, while such a holy land was of great importance to the Ancestors, it was also an incredibly precious opportunity for ordinary Domain Ancestors. If they could enter the third holy land and seize some resources, they might be able to rise to prominence.
For instance, those Invincible Domain Ancestors who had been stuck at that level for countless ages might find a supreme treasure within the third holy land that could forcibly help them break through their shackles and promote them to Supreme-level Domain Ancestors.
As for physical body control, they could completely bypass it for now. Once they became Supreme-level Domain Ancestors, they could slowly master their bodies later; that was also an option.
Furthermore, many Invincible Domain Ancestors didn't care about foundations or the like; they would be satisfied just to become Supreme-level Domain Ancestors.
In short, once the third Dark Holy Land was born, the endless Domain Ancestors of the entire Dark Holy Domain would all want to fight for a chance at fortune.
On this day.
The War Gate opened a meeting. It was initiated by the two Ancestors of the War Gate, and all Supreme-level Domain Ancestors were required to participate.
Thus, Ye Tian arrived at the War Ancestor World immediately.
Inside the War Ancestor Hall of the War Ancestor World.
One by one, Supreme-level Domain Ancestors appeared, and Ye Tian entered as well.
Here, he saw several familiar figures, all of whom were Supreme-level Domain Ancestors of the War Gate, as well as some Half-step Ancestors.
"Fifty-eight Supreme-level Domain Ancestors and thirteen Half-step Ancestors... is this the true strength of the War Gate?"
Ye Tian was quite surprised.
This was more Supreme-level Domain Ancestors than had participated in the previous invasion of the Silent Clan, which showed that some had not taken part last time.
After all, any Saint Gate needed to maintain its strength and could not afford to send everyone out at once.
Moreover, Ye Tian was certain that the Supreme-level Domain Ancestors here were likely not all of them. There might be others roaming the Dark Forbidden Zone, or perhaps some were being kept hidden.
Therefore, the total number of Supreme-level Domain Ancestors and Half-step Ancestors in the War Gate was definitely over a hundred.
If one Saint Gate possessed over a hundred Supreme-level Domain Ancestors, then among the ten Great Saint Gates of the Dark Holy Domain, the number of experts at or above the Supreme-level Domain Ancestor rank would be over a thousand. Adding in the other holy lands, loose organizations, and rogue Supreme-level Domain Ancestors...
It could be said that there were at least two thousand experts at or above the Supreme-level Domain Ancestor rank in the Dark Holy Domain, perhaps even more.
Meanwhile, the Dark Destruction Domain had many more Supreme-level Domain Ancestors than the Dark Holy Domain. After all, it was the first Dark Holy Land and had been born in a much more ancient era, so it likely had three to four thousand Supreme-level Domain Ancestors.
Adding in the scattered Supreme-level experts across the Dark Forbidden Zone...
The total number of Supreme-level Domain Ancestors in the entire Dark Forbidden Zone was at least ten thousand.
Yet last time, when all the major forces moved out, they had only mobilized a little over three thousand Supreme-level Domain Ancestors.
"During the last invasion of the Silent Clan, all the major forces were hiding their strength. They really are playing it safe!"
Ye Tian thought to himself.
If the third Dark Holy Land was born this time, the number of Supreme-level Domain Ancestors in the entire Dark Forbidden Zone would likely increase significantly again.
Soon, the meeting began.
The one speaking was the World Ancestor, as he was the strongest.
"I have summoned you all here today to discuss the birth of the third Dark Holy Land."
The World Ancestor said solemnly, "When the third Dark Holy Land is born, many worlds will be created. Of course, it's estimated that Ancestor Worlds won't be born at the start, and the range won't be too large.
Furthermore, due to the restrictions of the laws, Ancestors are not allowed to enter the Holy Land at the beginning. Even Supreme-level Domain Ancestors will have no way to enter.
According to convention, during the first hundred million years, only Half-step Domain Ancestors are allowed to enter.
After a hundred million years, and within a trillion years, only those below Peerless Domain Ancestors are allowed to enter.
Within one Domain Year, Supreme-level Domain Ancestors will be allowed to enter. As for the Ancestors, it will likely take a hundred Domain Years before they can enter the third Dark Holy Land.
If no Ancestor is born within the third Dark Holy Land within those hundred Domain Years, it will be successfully invaded by us, and we will occupy it.
But if an Ancestor is born there, we will be unable to invade and can only snatch some resources.
Just like the Dark Holy Domain back then—if the Saint Ancestor hadn't become an Ancestor within a hundred Domain Years, our Dark Holy Domain would have also fallen and become a part of the Dark Destruction Domain."
"World Ancestor, why does the birth of a single Ancestor protect the Holy Land? The Dark Destruction Domain and the Dark Holy Domain have many Ancestors, and with the strength of the Saint Ancestor or the Destruction Ancestor, they should be able to instantly kill an ordinary Ancestor!"
A Supreme-level Domain Ancestor asked curiously.
The other Supreme-level Domain Ancestors also looked toward the World Ancestor. They were not privy to this secret and were equally curious.
"Because the first Ancestor born in a Dark Holy Land becomes the Lord of the Holy Land. They can mobilize the power of the Dark Holy Land to exert the combat power of a Strongest Ancestor.
Of course, once they leave the Dark Holy Land, their strength immediately reverts to its original form.
Whether it is the Saint Ancestor or the Destruction Ancestor, although their strength is very close to a Strongest Ancestor, they are still not quite there. Therefore, they cannot kill a Lord of the Holy Land within their own domain!"
The World Ancestor explained.
"So that's how it is!"
Many Supreme-level Domain Ancestors came to an understanding.
At this moment.
Ye Tian was internally very excited.
When the third Dark Holy Land is born, other Supreme-level Domain Ancestors cannot enter, and neither can the Ancestors.
However, he could enter!
Once he copied the body of a Half-step Domain Ancestor, he could enter the third Dark Holy Land. At that time, who could compete with him? Wouldn't the greatest benefits there belong to him? Moreover, he could rapidly increase his cultivation in that third Dark Holy Land and might even have the hope of becoming an Ancestor there.
If he didn't care about his foundation, he really could quickly cultivate to the Supreme-level Domain Ancestor rank and then rely on that Space Ancestor Law to become an Ancestor.
The Space Ancestor Law was an Ancestor Law he had obtained, and it was very complete. Furthermore, the Ancestor who created this Space Ancestor Law had fallen, so he could completely use that law to become an Ancestor.
However, his main body looked down on the Space Ancestor Law, as it was someone else's law. Relying on such a law to become an Ancestor would make it very difficult to become a powerhouse like the Saint Ancestor in the future.
But this was just a copied body; it wouldn't affect his main body.
Furthermore, if a copied body became an Ancestor, it would even benefit his main body. At the very least, he would understand the mysteries of an Ancestor, providing insights for when he eventually created his own Ancestor Law to become an Ancestor in the future.
It could be said that the birth of the third Dark Holy Land was a massive opportunity practically tailored for him, and perhaps even a great opportunity for the rise of the Human Race.

Chapter 1459: Selection of the Human Race's 100,000 Geniuses!

Chapter 1459: Selection of the Human Race's 100,000 Geniuses
!
While the Supreme Domain Ancestors were contemplating the third Dark Holy Land, the World Ancestor continued, "The birth of the third Dark Holy Land will initially involve a struggle between Half-step Domain Ancestors. Although the grade of the treasures born at the beginning... won't be very high, it is still a great opportunity.
Therefore, every major power has a quota for how many Half-step Domain Ancestors they can send in.
Each of you Supreme Domain Ancestors has 100,000 slots. You can send 100,000 Half-step Domain Ancestors, or you can train them yourselves.
If you can keep the benefits and opportunities these Half-step Domain Ancestors obtain under your control, those opportunities will belong to you as well.
After all, since you cannot enter the Dark Holy Land yourselves, you can only rely on those Half-step Domain Ancestors to seize the opportunities!"
"Yes!"
The Supreme Domain Ancestors responded one after another.
As for after a hundred million years, they could also send a certain number of top-tier Domain Ancestors into it.
It would only be after a trillion years, within one Realm Year, that Supreme Domain Ancestors like them would have the chance to take the stage.
"Go back and prepare. According to the calculations of us Progenitors, the third Dark Holy Land will be born in approximately 3 million years!"
The World Ancestor reminded them.
Subsequently, the Supreme Domain Ancestors went back to prepare.
The two Progenitors of the Battle Gate also needed to make some preparations for their future struggle for the opportunities within the third Dark Holy Land.
....In the Profound Void Holy Realm, the Human Race.
Ye Tian immediately began a selection process covering the billions of Half-step Domain Ancestors within the human race. Countless Half-step Domain Ancestors across the human territories would undergo rounds of assessments and battles to select those with the highest talent, strongest combat power, and greatest potential.
For this battle, Ye Tian specifically obtained a projection of the Battle Realm Tower from the Battle Gate to be used for the human race's selection.
And so.
The human race's internal selection began.
Although many human Half-step Domain Ancestors did not understand the significance of this selection, this was an order issued by the strongest of the human race and the creator of the human rise, the Myriad Law War Ancestor. It was bound to be a truly great opportunity.
Consequently, countless human Half-step Domain Ancestors went wild, cultivating hard for this selection. After all, this selection was set to last for 300 years, meaning even those with slightly lower cultivation or those who had just broken through to the Half-step Domain Ancestor realm could participate.
As long as they performed well, they could receive rewards from the human race to rapidly increase their cultivation.
In short, the selection rules set by Ye Tian would not miss a single genius.
Soon, the million-year period was nearing its end.
At this time, the 100,000 human geniuses who had emerged from a million years of slaughter were born.
What no one knew was that Ye Tian had killed a human Half-step Domain Ancestor who had committed a capital crime, replicated that person's body, and then bestowed some ancestral talents upon this body.
In this way, this body's talent remained a monstrous talent second only to his original body, and its cultivation was at the Half-step Domain Ancestor realm, possessing high growth potential.
Furthermore, Ye Tian spent a huge price to reshape and even modify this body.
Most importantly, the origin of this body could be fully traced; even the Progenitors would not be able to see any problems.
Thus, Ye Tian's replicated body, along with the other 99,999 geniuses, would enter the third Dark Holy Land shortly.
On this day.
In the Profound Void Holy Realm, before the Human Holy Palace.
The 100,000 geniuses gathered here, and Ye Tian appeared as well.
"Greetings, Lord Myriad Law War Ancestor!"
The human geniuses said respectfully.
Ye Tian looked at these 100,000 human geniuses and said, "You may be very curious as to why I held such a selection process, and you might even be guessing what kind of rewards there will be.
However, I tell you, there are no rewards, only one great opportunity!"
Opportunity? The 100,000 geniuses all became curious. What kind of opportunity would make the human race go to such great lengths to hold a selection for a million years?
"You should all know about the Dark Holy Realm and the Dark Destruction Domain from the human library. Now, the third Dark Holy Land of the Dark Forbidden Zone is being born. It is filled with endless resources. Obtaining any treasure at random can easily allow you to promote to a Domain Ancestor. If you obtain enough opportunities, there is even hope of promoting to a Supreme Domain Ancestor in the future."
Ye Tian spoke truthfully.
Boom!!!! The 100,000 geniuses were excited.
What a massive opportunity this was! They never expected that they would be able to obtain it.
An opportunity to become a Supreme Domain Ancestor could not be found in the Profound Void Holy Realm at all.
In the entire human race, after countless years, there was currently only one Supreme Domain Ancestor, Ye Tian. Even the ten Great Holy Gates of the Dark Holy Realm did not have many Supreme Domain Ancestors! Once one became a Supreme Domain Ancestor, they could create a Holy Land-level power.
Ye Tian gave some instructions and also warned that this opportunity was extremely dangerous; one could fall if they were not careful. If they were afraid, they could withdraw.
However, no one withdrew.
If they withdrew, they might never have such an opportunity again for the rest of their lives.
For them, having raised their cultivation to Half-step Domain Ancestor and having cultivated for long years, they had lived long enough. Their goals were the Domain Ancestor realm and the Supreme Domain Ancestor realm. Now that such a great opportunity was before them, how could they refuse out of fear of death?
Time passed slowly, and another several tens of thousands of years went by.
On this day.
The World Ancestor sent a message: the third Dark Holy Land was about to be born, and all major powers were to be prepared.
....Deep within the Dark Forbidden Zone.
In an area far away from the Dark Holy Realm and the Dark Destruction Domain, a massive vortex was generated. The area of this vortex far exceeded that of a large Great Realm. It wasn't very large at first, but it gradually expanded to a size comparable to the Dark Holy Realm.
At this time.
In the center of this vortex, worlds were being born, and continents were evolving.
Countless domains were born one by one, and later, the first Holy Realm was born.
At the same time, these worlds also gave birth to a large number of innate beings and ancient primordial chaos gods and demons.
As for Taboo Creatures, they had not yet been born. After all, Taboo Creatures were comparable to Domain Ancestors, so they naturally wouldn't be born so quickly; otherwise, how would the ordinary beings of this third world survive?
Suddenly.
A figure emerged here, and a massive Gate of Space-Time appeared behind him.
He was the Spacetime Progenitor of the Dark Destruction Domain.
Next, a giant golden tower appeared, and a person walked out from within the tower—it was the World Ancestor of the Battle Gate.
Not long after the World Ancestor arrived, the Holy Progenitor also arrived, and the Destruction Progenitor came as well.
In terms of speed, the Spacetime Progenitor and the World Ancestor were the fastest, but in terms of strength, the Holy Progenitor and the Destruction Progenitor were the most powerful.
One Progenitor after another arrived, their gazes fixed upon this third Dark Holy Land.
"What a familiar scene!"
The Destruction Progenitor grinned, revealing a cruel smile.
If he could, he would even want to wipe out all the living beings here and transform it into a second Destruction Domain.
Unfortunately, he couldn't do it at the moment. Even if he could, the practitioners of the Dark Holy Realm would surely stop him.
