Chapter 1460: Dark Soul Domain, Soul Dao!

Chapter 1460: Dark Soul Domain, Soul Dao
!
"This Dark Holy Land seems a bit special!"
The Holy Ancestor murmured.
"It is indeed a bit special!"
The Destruction Ancestor also noticed it.
Every Dark Holy Land has a unique cultivation system. For example, the Dark Destruction Domain absorbs destruction energy from countless regions of the Dark Forbidden Zone, using destruction as its cultivation system. Thus, the Path of Destruction prevails in the Dark Destruction Domain. Coupled with their natural bloodline advantages, they can grow simply by destroying everything.
The Dark Holy Domain, on the other hand, is a holy land for cultivators, focusing on cultivation and the comprehension of Taboo Great Daos.
But this third Dark Holy Land was completely different; the rules here were very peculiar.
"The rules here lean toward the soul!"
The Holy Ancestor said in surprise.
The soul! The other Ancestors investigated and deduced one by one.
Indeed, the rules of this Dark Holy Land leaned toward the Path of the Soul.
It was normal for some worlds to lean toward soul rules, but for an entire Dark Holy Land to lean toward the Path of the Soul meant that the mainstream cultivation path of this Dark Holy Land was... the Soul Dao.
The mainstream of the Dark Destruction Domain was the Bloodline Dao, while the mainstream of the Dark Holy Domain was the Physical Body Dao—for instance, Domain Ancestors increased their cultivation by tempering their Domain Bodies.
If the mainstream was the Soul Dao, then one must increase their soul realm to increase their cultivation level.
"Interesting. In a Dark Holy Land where the Soul Dao is mainstream, many of the treasures born within might be items that increase the soul realm, or perhaps treasures that can temper the souls of us Ancestors.
It is difficult for our physical bodies to improve further, but if we temper our souls, our strength will see a certain degree of growth!"
The Time-Space Ancestor said excitedly.
The other Ancestors were also very excited. Unfortunately, they could not enter; otherwise, they would have charged into this third Dark Holy Land immediately.
"What should we name this Dark Holy Land?"
The various Ancestors prepared to name this holy land.
"Let's call it the Dark Soul Domain!"
The Holy Ancestor named it casually.
"Since the Holy Ancestor has named this Dark Holy Land, then let it be called the Dark Soul Domain!"
The other Ancestors all agreed.
Once the location of the Dark Soul Domain was confirmed, they each established teleportation points there.
On the side of the Dark Destruction Domain, the Time-Space Ancestor established a permanent Time-Space Gate.
On the side of the Dark Holy Domain, the World Ancestor condensed a sub-tower of the War World Tower and opened permissions, allowing passage through the War World Tower.
Previously, using the War World Tower to travel consumed too much energy, which was why the World Ancestor had disabled that function, making the War World Tower unusable for travel. Only the Wu Ancestor of the War Gate had a small amount of permission to temporarily travel between two places, but even then, he could not stray too far from the range of the War World Tower.
Back then, the Ancient Sea Domain Ancestor had used this to reach the Profound Void Holy Realm to help Ye Tian.
But now, permissions were opened so that anyone could travel between the two places via the War World Tower, though this was only a temporary opening to send the half-step Domain Ancestors of the Dark Holy Domain over.
On the side of the Eternal Cult, a massive teleportation array was also constructed to bring their half-step Domain Ancestors over.
In reality, the Ancestors could have sent the half-step Domain Ancestors over one by one, but the speed would be too slow.
The Ancestors could not send too many people at once because their divine thoughts could not envelop everyone. After all, crossing such a vast distance imposed great restrictions; if they forced people through, those half-step Domain Ancestors would decompose into nothingness midway.
Just as when they sent Supreme Domain Ancestors to the Holy Domain Continent at the edge of the Dark Forbidden Zone, the Ancestors had to send them one by one rather than all at once.
Otherwise, if an Ancestor could carry countless half-step Domain Ancestors and easily cross endless territories, it would be unrealistic.
The Ancestors themselves could cross endless time and space with a single thought and descend anywhere in the Dark Forbidden Zone because their own thoughts were eternal and indestructible and their bodies were too powerful, but others could not do the same.
Soon.
One by one, the half-step Domain Ancestors of the Dark Holy Domain passed through the War World Tower and arrived at the Dark Soul Domain.
Ye Tian also went directly to the Dark Soul Domain through the War Ancestor Realm of the Profound Void Realm. This was because the World Ancestor had opened permissions, making it very convenient.
BOOM!!!!! Led by Ye Tian's main body, one hundred thousand human Domain Ancestors descended upon the edge of the Dark Soul Domain.
But when Ye Tian appeared, many Ancestors were surprised.
The peak stage of the Supreme Domain Ancestor realm! They saw through Ye Tian's cultivation level, but previously, Ye Tian was only at the middle stage of the Supreme Domain Ancestor realm! How much time had passed, and Ye Tian's cultivation had already reached the peak stage? This speed of improvement was far too fast! The Ancestors of the Dark Destruction Domain all wanted to eliminate Ye Tian, but since the many Ancestors of the Dark Holy Domain were present, they naturally could not do such a thing.
"Let the half-step Domain Ancestors enter!"
The Ancestors spoke.
Swish swish swish!!!! Countless half-step Domain Ancestors were thrown into the Dark Soul Domain by the Supreme Domain Ancestors.
Ye Tian also waved his hand, enveloping the one hundred thousand human geniuses and sending them into the Dark Soul Domain. Furthermore, he sent them to a remote region rather than the core area.
The Human Race's foundation was still relatively low, and their innate racial advantages were not great. There was no need to compete with other forces at the half-step Domain Ancestor stage, so developing in a remote region was fine.
Besides, with his duplicated bodies present to help the Human Race rise within the Dark Soul Domain, it would be quite easy and didn't require a prime territory.
Before long, countless half-step Domain Ancestors flooded into the Dark Soul Domain.
Meanwhile, the various Ancestors remained there to cultivate, not leaving the area.
They even meditated on the rules of the Dark Soul Domain, which was a form of cultivation for them as well.
Dark Soul Domain, a remote territory.
The one hundred thousand half-step Domain Ancestor geniuses of the Human Race descended here. They began to familiarize themselves with the environment and immediately occupied a Domain Realm.
Ye Tian had long since instructed them that after entering the Dark Soul Domain, the Human Race must unite, stay low-profile at the beginning, cultivate diligently, and not wander aimlessly.
The Dark Soul Domain had existed for a long time, so many races had already appeared here, and the cultivation system had begun to take shape.
"Soul Dao!"
The Human Race gathered a lot of information, including the cultivation system of this world.
The practitioners of this world did not value the physical body; they only valued the soul, believing the soul to be the foundation. If the physical body was destroyed, it could be completely reconsolidated, but if the soul was annihilated, then one truly perished.
When Ye Tian saw the Soul Dao, he immediately felt that this path had immense potential.
Moreover, to become an Ancestor in the Dark Soul Domain, one must also cultivate the Soul Dao.
For the non-underlined version of the novel, please download Stone Novels.

Chapter 1461: Soul Ancestor, Rise of the Human Race!

Chapter 1461: Soul Ancestor, Rise of the Human Race
!
"The Soul Dao specifically cultivates the soul but neglects the physical body; this path is also incomplete.
However, in the future, I can combine the Soul Dao with the Physical Body Dao to create a more perfect path,"
Ye Tian thought to himself.
Therefore, he prepared to use this cloned body to walk the path of the Soul Dao.
Through his understanding, the Soul Dao in this Dark Soul Domain had currently developed to the Soul Ancestor level, which was equivalent to the Domain Ancestor realm.
The cultivation of a Soul Ancestor also involved soul transformations time and again. Furthermore, the soul strength of a newly promoted Soul Ancestor was already comparable to that of a peak Domain Ancestor.
Otherwise, there would be no way to match the combat power of a Domain Ancestor using soul power alone.
In the following days, a portion of the human race began to follow the Soul Dao, while another portion continued with their previous cultivation paths.
However, they discovered that it was very difficult to increase their cultivation here using their old paths; even attempting to break through to the Domain Ancestor realm felt like an insurmountable chasm.
Consequently, the human Half-step Domain Ancestors abandoned the path of the Domain Ancestor and began to follow the path of the Soul Ancestor.
But soon, Ye Tian discovered a problem: their souls were too weak to become Soul Ancestors.
Now, not only were the human Half-step Domain Ancestors stunned, but even the Supreme Half-step Domain Ancestors from other factions were bewildered.
If they couldn't become Soul Ancestors, how would they obtain more opportunities in the future, or fight against the native soul practitioners of the Dark Soul Domain? Currently, the Dark Soul Domain also had many Half-step Soul Ancestors; though their individual strength wasn't great, their numbers were vast.
Once these Half-step Soul Ancestors promoted to the Soul Ancestor realm, if the outsiders couldn't become Soul Ancestors themselves, they wouldn't be able to defeat them, let alone occupy this place in the future.
"I must create a cultivation technique to re-cultivate the Soul Dao and transform the bodies of human Half-step Domain Ancestors into Half-step Soul Ancestors!"
Ye Tian decided.
This step was extremely difficult, one could even say it was like an insurmountable chasm.
But at this time, Ye Tian noticed that Half-step Domain Ancestors from many factions were emerging from the Dark Soul Domain, bringing out a large number of Soul Dao techniques.
Thus, Ye Tian also had his cloned body exit the Dark Soul Domain.
Afterward, Ye Tian dispelled the clone, began to duplicate his original body, and used his Evolution characteristic to deduce techniques over and over again.
By consuming Sacred Souls to deduce techniques, his efficiency was many times faster than even an Ancestor.
Time and again, his cloned bodies collapsed, only for him to clone again and continue the evolution.
In this way, time passed, and a million years went by in the blink of an eye.
During these million years, the Ancestors were all deducing techniques to achieve the transformation from Half-step Domain Ancestor to Half-step Soul Ancestor.
While the other Ancestors had yet to complete their technique transformations, Ye Tian, relying on countless evolutions, finally created a technique—the Body-Merging Soul Technique!
The so-called Body-Merging Soul Technique was... to convert the power of a Half-step Domain Ancestor into soul power, thereby achieving a qualitative change in the soul, stepping into the Half-step Soul Ancestor realm, and embarking on the Soul Dao in one fell swoop.
Ye Tian had only created the Body-Merging technique at the Half-step Domain Ancestor level and had not created one for the Domain Ancestor level; therefore, it was only suitable for Half-step Domain Ancestors.
After creating the Body-Merging Soul Technique, Ye Tian once again cloned that... Half-step Domain Ancestor body and sent it back into the Dark Soul Domain.
Upon returning to the Dark Soul Domain, Ye Tian, in his capacity as the leader of the ten geniuses, gathered the 100,000 geniuses.
During these million years, the 100,000 human geniuses had made little progress in their cultivation, and some had even fallen. They had obtained a large amount of resources and treasures, but unfortunately, since their cultivation couldn't improve, they couldn't utilize them.
"The Myriad Law Combat Ancestor has created a technique that can allow us to become Half-step Soul Ancestors. However, everyone must swear an oath not to leak this technique. Since other factions do not have such a technique yet, once it is leaked, our human race's advantage will be gone,"
Ye Tian commanded.
"Yes!"
One by one, the geniuses swore their oaths—the most serious and harsh Life Oaths—before receiving the inheritance of the Body-Merging Soul Technique.
With the Body-Merging Soul Technique, the human geniuses transformed into Half-step Soul Ancestors one by one. Then, utilizing the resources and soul treasures they had acquired, they broke through to the Soul Ancestor realm.
After 100,000 years, all the human geniuses had stepped into the Soul Ancestor realm. At this point, they could no longer leave; otherwise, once they exited the Dark Soul Domain, they wouldn't be able to return.
After becoming Soul Ancestors, the human geniuses began to expand their territory, even establishing a faction called the Sacred Hall, recruiting native residents of the Dark Soul Domain on a large scale to continuously expand their influence.
With territory and more resources, the human Soul Ancestors' strength increased very rapidly.
In just a few million years, the human Soul Ancestors had all reached the level of top-tier Soul Ancestor combat power, while Ye Tian's cultivation improved the fastest, already reaching the Peak Soul Ancestor realm.
The path of the Soul Ancestor and the path of the Domain Ancestor seemed different, but they still shared similarities. Furthermore, since Ye Tian was at the peak of the Supreme Domain Ancestor level, reverse-engineering the Soul Ancestor path was naturally not difficult—at least not before reaching the Supreme Soul Ancestor realm.
Additionally, Ye Tian created several Sacred Skills suitable for Soul Ancestors, as well as a pile of soul techniques at the Domain Ancestor level, sufficient for the human Soul Ancestors to practice.
Dark Soul Domain, Sacred Hall Headquarters.
As the Master of the Sacred Hall, Ye Tian gathered the human Soul Ancestors.
"Everyone, it is time for us to occupy a more vast territory. This place is a remote area of the Dark Soul Domain, but now, with our human race's strength, occupying the core region would pose no problem.
I plan to seize a Holy Realm within the Dark Soul Domain!"
Ye Tian planned.
"A Holy Realm!"
Everyone was excited upon hearing this plan.
Even the Daoshan Domain only had one Holy Realm, the Xuanxu Holy Realm. Now, they were about to conquer a Holy Realm in the Dark Soul Domain. If they succeeded, the human race would effectively possess two Holy Realms.
Subsequently, they began planning which Holy Realm to attack.
Currently, the Dark Soul Domain possessed dozens of Holy Realms, each occupied by numerous factions; no single faction yet held ownership over an entire Holy Realm.
This was because completely occupying a Holy Realm was extremely difficult.
"Let's conquer the Shifang Holy Realm!"
Ye Tian said, pointing to a Holy Realm on the map.
The Shifang Holy Realm contained many factions. According to the human race's investigation, most of these factions belonged to certain races from the Dark Destruction Domain.
The Sacred Hall left behind only a small portion of the human race, but there were still many native Soul Ancestors stationed there. These Soul Ancestors had joined the Sacred Hall when they were very weak and had no idea that the Sacred Hall consisted of outsiders; even if they knew, they wouldn't have any particular thoughts about it.
After all, they were all nurtured by the Sacred Hall, so they naturally wouldn't betray it.
Moreover, the human race had not done anything excessive. Only factions like those from the Dark Destruction Domain aimed to destroy everything, which was why they were hated and had faced the full resistance of the Dark Holy Domain in the past.
Ye Tian leading tens of thousands of top-tier Soul Ancestors, crossed a vast distance. It took a full several months before they reached the core region of the Dark Soul Domain and arrived before the Shifang Holy Realm.

Chapter 1462: Occupying the Ten Directions Sacred Realm!

Chapter 1462: Occupying the Ten Directions Sacred Realm
!
Before the Ten Directions Sacred Realm.
Ye Tian led the human army as they descended, directly entering the Ten Directions Sacred Realm.
"From this day forth, the Ten Directions Sacred Realm belongs to our Human Race!"
Ye Tian's voice permeated the entire Ten Directions Sacred Realm.
Such an arrogant declaration immediately incensed many factions within the Ten Directions Sacred Realm.
....Ten Directions Sacred Realm, Destruction Dragon Mountain.
This was the territory conquered by the geniuses of the Dragon Evil Clan, one of the three thousand evil clans of the Dark Sacred Domain.
The Dragon Evil Clan held a very respectable position among the three thousand evil clans, possessing three Supreme-level Realm Ancestors and several Invincible Realm Ancestors.
At this moment, the gaze of the Dragon Evil Clan's genius leader, Gu Luolu, pierced through layers of void, looking toward the direction of the Human Race.
By now, the various major powers of the entire Dark Sacred Domain had long since obtained techniques to transform into Half-Step Soul Ancestors. After the Dragon Evil Clan members transformed into Half-Step Soul Ancestors, they had one by one ascended to become Soul Ancestors.
Moreover, the Ten Directions Sacred Realm was rich in resources. Coupled with the Dragon Evil Clan's heavy support and full efforts to nurture Gu Luolu, his cultivation had been raised to the level of a Paramount Soul Ancestor. It could be said that the strength of an entire clan was concentrated on nurturing one person.
Within the Ten Directions Sacred Realm, Gu Luolu's strength was sufficient to rank in the top ten.
"The Human Race? Is that the race the Myriad Law War Ancestor belongs to?"
Gu Luolu said coldly, "The Myriad Law War Ancestor's strength is indeed powerful, comparable to a Half-Step Primordial Ancestor. However, the Human Race has only produced one Myriad Law War Ancestor; everyone else is an ant. For a group of humans to dare claim they will occupy the Ten Directions Sacred Realm is truly arrogant!"
Currently.
His Dragon Evil Clan also occupied a region in the Ten Directions Sacred Realm and had nurtured a large number of subordinates, possessing immense strength.
"Hear my command: exterminate the Human Race!"
Gu Luolu ordered.
Boom!!!!!! One Soul Ancestor after another set out, and a large number of Half-Step Soul Ancestors were also mobilized, charging toward the Human Race.
This time, the Human Race had angered the factions of the entire Ten Directions Sacred Realm. Numerous powers attacked one after another, swearing to slaughter the humans.
"They're here!"
Ye Tian sensed the arrival of a large number of Soul Ancestors, as terrifying tides of soul energy surged forward.
Compared to so many Soul Ancestors, the Human Race was indeed lacking in numbers.
However, the Human Race's Soul Ancestors were all top-tier Soul Ancestors. Combined with Ye Tian, a nearly invincible Paramount Soul Ancestor, ordinary Paramount Soul Ancestors were like ants in his eyes.
The first to arrive was the Dragon Evil Clan.
"Kill them!"
Gu Luolu commanded.
As one of the evil clans, they knew nothing of hesitation; they killed upon encounter without any nonsense.
"Kill!"
With Ye Tian's command, the top-tier Soul Ancestors of the Human Race struck out together.
As soon as they clashed, Gu Luolu was stunned. "They are all top-tier Soul Ancestors? How can this be? Why has the Human Race progressed so quickly?"
Gu Luolu said in disbelief.
He watched as the two sides collided, and the Soul Ancestors of the Dragon Evil Clan were blasted apart one after another.
Gu Luolu did not dare to engage so many top-tier human Soul Ancestors. A Paramount Soul Ancestor like him was not truly powerful; after all, his cultivation time was short. He had only reached the level of a Paramount Soul Ancestor in cultivation but had not even mastered a few soul techniques at the Soul Ancestor level. His combat power was only comparable to an ordinary Paramount Realm Ancestor, and he had no way to resist tens of thousands of top-tier Soul Ancestors by himself.
Suddenly.
Ye Tian made his move. A Soul Spear instantly pierced through the air.
With a soft "puchi" sound, Gu Luolu was killed in a single strike, without even the slightest power to resist.
Soon, the Dragon Evil Clan was wiped out.
Subsequently, one faction after another encountered the Human Race.
Ye Tian led the Human Race to annihilate faction after faction, virtually sweeping through the Ten Directions Sacred Realm.
Finally, dozens of Paramount Realm Ancestors in the Ten Directions Sacred Realm united, preparing to assassinate Ye Tian together.
The result, however, was that Ye Tian instantly killed these dozens of Paramount Soul Ancestors.
Several decades later, the Human Race unified the Ten Directions Sacred Realm, occupying it completely.
Outside the Dark Soul Domain.
The Supreme-level Realm Ancestors of the Dragon Evil Clan already knew that their clan's geniuses had been wiped out by the Human Race, and they were instantly furious.
But they did not dare to vent their anger. After all, their strength was very weak, far inferior to Ye Tian's; they had no right to be angry with him.
However, the fact that the Human Race had occupied the Ten Directions Sacred Realm caught the attention of the Primordial Ancestors.
After all, the Dark Soul Domain currently only had a few dozen Sacred Realms. If the War Sect had occupied a Sacred Realm, it would have been relatively normal.
But now, a single Human Race had occupied a Sacred Realm all by itself; this was far too shocking.
Especially when they learned that a Paramount Soul Ancestor had swept through everything and was unstoppable, they suspected the Human Race had cheated.
But no matter how they investigated, they could not find any problems.
"From now on, pay close attention to the Human Race!"
The Primordial Ancestors of the Dark Sacred Domain and the Eternal Cult issued this directive one after another.
Other Sacred Sects of the Dark Sacred Domain also began to take the Human Race seriously. After all, since the Human Race occupied a Sacred Realm, their future development speed would inevitably be extremely fast, making them a major threat.
After the Human Race occupied the Ten Directions Sacred Realm, Ye Tian concentrated a large amount of resources to continuously advance his Soul Ancestor cultivation. At the same time, his main body placed no restrictions on itself, continuing to create various soul techniques and even Sacred Techniques suitable for Soul Ancestors.
In the blink of an eye, one hundred million years had passed since the Human Race entered the Dark Soul Domain.
At this time, the Dark Soul Domain underwent its second transformation, and Realm Ancestors below the Paramount level were now permitted to enter.
Consequently.
A large number of top-tier Realm Ancestors entered, including many at the Holy Son level who could kill ordinary Paramount Realm Ancestors across levels. There were even Holy Talent Possessors among them.
These top-tier Realm Ancestors entering the Soul Domain naturally would not follow the path of a Soul Ancestor. Moreover, the Primordial Ancestors had no way to deduce techniques that would turn a Realm Ancestor into a Soul Ancestor.
These top-tier Realm Ancestors were fully confident in entering the Paramount Realm Ancestor stage. Even though following the path of a Realm Ancestor in the Dark Soul Domain was extremely difficult, they still had hope of forcibly breaking through the shackles and ascending to become Paramount Realm Ancestors.
Once they ascended to Paramount Realm Ancestors, their strength would be immense, even crushing the Paramount Soul Ancestors of the Dark Soul Domain.
In this way, the landscape of the Dark Soul Domain would change, and the territories of various powers would also shift.
For instance, the Dragon Evil Clan and other factions dispatched a large number of top-tier Realm Ancestors. The Dragon Evil Clan even sent a Holy Talent Possessor, the offspring of one of the three Supreme Realm Ancestors of the Dragon Evil Clan, the Hundred Ghost Evil Ancestor. Named the Scorpio Holy Son, his strength was immense. Once he entered the Dark Soul Domain, he could immediately charge toward the Paramount Realm Ancestor stage.
Once the Scorpio Holy Son stepped into the Paramount Realm Ancestor stage, there was no telling how many times stronger he would be than an ordinary Paramount Realm Ancestor.
Combined with the resources of the Dragon Evil Clan, his strength would rise once more.
At that time, they would launch an attack against the Human Race in the Ten Directions Sacred Realm.

Chapter 1463: The Armies of the Three Great Evil Races are Completely Wiped Out!

Chapter 1463: The Armies of the Three Great Evil Races are Completely Wiped Out!
!
Like other forces, Ye Tian also dispatched many top-tier human Domain Ancestors to the Dark Soul Realm. However, limited by the number of slots, he could only send thirty thousand top-tier Domain Ancestors.
Once these thirty thousand top-tier Domain Ancestors entered the Dark Soul Realm, approximately a small portion of them would be able to break through to the level of Supreme Domain Ancestor.
In this way, it could increase the strength of the humans in the Shifang Saint Realm and also alleviate some of Ye Tian's pressure.
After these top-tier Domain Ancestors flooded into the Dark Soul Realm, there was no internal fighting among them, but they encountered opposition from the local native forces.
After all, the native forces had also risen by now, and they possessed the home-field advantage, being favored by the providence of the Dark Soul Realm, making cultivation much easier. Moreover, many monstrous geniuses had been born among them, who were not at all weaker than the Domain Ancestors from the Dark Saint Domain, the Dark Destruction Domain, or the Eternal Cult.
After a period of fighting, neither side could do anything to the other, so they called it a day.
However, once these top-tier Domain Ancestors broke through to become Supreme Domain Ancestors, the Dark Soul Realm would usher in a new round of contention.
In the blink of an eye, another tens of millions of years passed.
At this time, the first batch of Supreme Domain Ancestors was born.
Outside the Shifang Saint Realm, groups of Domain Ancestors and Soul Ancestors arrived.
Leading them were three Saint-Talented ones from the evil races. One of them was... the Scorpion Holy Son, while the other two were from the Demon Prison Race and the Dream Race respectively.
To be able to lead the top-tier Domain Ancestors of the three races into the Dark Soul Realm, one could imagine how powerful their strength was. They were bound to far surpass ordinary people, belonging to the top ranks even among Saint-Talented ones.
Now, these three Saint-Talented ones had all stepped into the ranks of Supreme Domain Ancestors. Furthermore, with the treasures bestowed by their Ancestors, they had forcibly raised their cultivation to the peak of the Supreme Domain Ancestor realm within the Dark Soul Realm.
Of course, if they wanted to condense Soul Saint Light and then condense a Saint Soul, that would require a long period of time.
If they didn't care about their foundation, the Ancestors also had ways to forcibly push them into the Invincible Domain Ancestor realm.
However, fighting for a temporary advantage... was useless. Even if a few Invincible Domain Ancestors were born, it wouldn't change anything.
Moreover, no Saint-Talented one was willing to waste their talent and destroy their own foundation to forcibly break through to the Invincible Domain Ancestor level.
This time.
The Scorpion Holy Son, also known as the Scorpion Domain Ancestor, and the other two Saint-Talented ones led tens of thousands of Supreme Domain Ancestors to the Shifang Saint Realm. Their goal was to clear out the humans and occupy the Shifang Saint Realm; this was also one of the orders given to them by the Ancestors.
"Xiefeng Domain Ancestor, Mingying Domain Ancestor, in a moment, the three of us Saint-Talented ones will strike together to assassinate the leader of the humans in the Shifang Saint Realm, Soul Ancestor Qingye. We must strive to kill him instantly."
The Scorpion Domain Ancestor proposed.
"No problem, this is but a simple matter. That Soul Ancestor Qingye was only a Half-step Domain Ancestor back then. Although his cultivation improved quickly after coming to the Dark Soul Realm and he is now a Supreme Soul Ancestor, his cultivation time is short. He has the cultivation level but likely hasn't mastered many powerful soul techniques. Even if he is a Saint-Talented one, he probably hasn't even mastered a single Saint Technique to the Perfected stage.
Furthermore, the power of Saint Techniques from the Dark Saint Domain drops significantly when used by a Soul Ancestor, and there are probably very few Saint Techniques suitable for Soul Ancestors. It's too late for him to learn them now.
Meanwhile, all three of us Saint-Talented ones have mastered two Perfected Saint Techniques. Killing a Supreme Soul Ancestor is naturally very simple!"
The Mingying Domain Ancestor said with full confidence.
"Still, be careful. This is an order issued by the Ancestors."
The Scorpion Domain Ancestor reminded.
The Mingying Domain Ancestor and the Xiefeng Domain Ancestor nodded. They then led the numerous Supreme Domain Ancestors and a large number of top-tier Domain Ancestors to attack the Shifang Saint Realm.
With their strength, they could simply crush their way through.
.... "Lord Soul Ancestor Qingye, a large number of ancestors are attacking our Shifang Saint Realm!"
A human Supreme Domain Ancestor reported to Ye Tian.
Soul Ancestor Qingye was... this cloned body. No one knew this was Ye Tian's clone, not even the humans.
Furthermore, Ye Tian was currently using entirely new methods, so no one could guess his identity.
"Let them enter the Shifang Saint Realm. When the time comes, you all activate the grand array of the Shifang Saint Realm. Do not allow a single person to escape!"
Ye Tian ordered.
"Lord Soul Ancestor Qingye, the opponent's numbers are too great, I worry..."
This human Supreme Domain Ancestor clearly didn't know Ye Tian's true strength, hence his concern.
"Rest assured, I can kill them all. You just need to assist!"
Ye Tian said indifferently.
"Yes!"
The Supreme Domain Ancestor nodded.
The Supreme Domain Ancestors and top-tier Domain Ancestors of the three evil races easily broke into the Shifang Saint Realm and then charged toward the human headquarters.
BOOM!!!!! The Shifang Saint Realm was sealed off, and human Supreme Domain Ancestors appeared one after another.
Ye Tian stood at the very front, his gaze directly meeting the Supreme Domain Ancestors of the three evil races.
Neither side spoke; they clashed immediately.
"Kill!"
The three Saint-Talented ones—the Scorpion Domain Ancestor, Mingying Domain Ancestor, and Xiefeng Domain Ancestor—targeted Ye Tian immediately.
RUMBLE!!!! Three Perfected Saint Techniques were unleashed, sealing off the void around Ye Tian from all directions.
"Soul Ancestor Qingye, be careful! Those are three Saint-Talented ones!!!!"
The other human Supreme Domain Ancestors cried out in worry.
However, Ye Tian gave a cold smile: "Three Saint-Talented ones? Merely ants!"
With a wave of Ye Tian's hand, countless golden threads of soul appeared.
"Saint Technique—Soul Golden Silk!"
This was not the Soul Golden Silk of the Perfected stage, but the Soul Golden Silk of the Limit stage.
Moreover, the Soul Golden Silk Saint Technique Ye Tian had created was a top-tier Saint Technique, very close to an Ancestor Technique.
However, Ye Tian had not yet created a Soul Golden Silk at the Ancestor Technique level. After all, it wasn't good to be too high-profile right now. Otherwise, with Ye Tian's attainment in practicing a large number of Perfected stage Ancestor Techniques, it wouldn't be difficult to push the Soul Golden Silk to the Ancestor Technique level.
Puff puff puff!!!! The three Saint-Talented ones were sliced apart, while their three Saint Technique attacks landed on Ye Tian's body, only to be blocked by Ye Tian's Spirit Light Saint Armor, failing to harm him in the slightest.
And the Saint Technique Spirit Light Saint Armor had also been cultivated to the Limit stage by Ye Tian.
"Not good, a Saint Technique at the Limit stage! How is this possible? How can the humans still have such a monstrous Saint-Talented one? Could he be a descendant of the Myriad Law War Ancestor?"
But they felt something was wrong.
The Myriad Law War Ancestor did indeed have descendants, but they were born before he became a Supreme Domain Ancestor, and none of them were Soul Ancestor Qingye! Although there were treasures in the Dark Forbidden Zone that could grant someone a Saint Talent, they were too rare, and the Saint-Talented ones created that way were definitely not as monstrous as true Saint-Talented ones.
Soul Ancestor Qingye had only become a Soul Ancestor for a hundred million years. What could such a short time achieve? Could it be that Soul Ancestor Qingye had already mastered Limit stage Saint Techniques when he was a Half-step Domain Ancestor? That was absolutely impossible; the Dark Forbidden Zone had never produced such a monstrous existence.
Then there was only one possibility: Soul Ancestor Qingye had found a treasure in the Dark Soul Realm that could rapidly assist in comprehending Saint Techniques, which allowed him to raise his Saint Techniques to the Limit stage in a short time.
At this moment.
The Scorpion Domain Ancestor and the others felt immense regret, but it was already too late.
Puff puff puff!!!! Under the Soul Golden Silk, the three Saint-Talented ones couldn't resist at all.
In a short while, they were all slain by Ye Tian.
Subsequently.
Ye Tian single-handedly swept through the armies of the three evil races. A large number of Supreme Domain Ancestors and top-tier Domain Ancestors were slaughtered by him alone.
Some Supreme Domain Ancestors and top-tier Domain Ancestors tried to escape, but they were trapped by the human Supreme Domain Ancestors and the grand array. Not a single one escaped.
With this, the armies of the three evil races were completely annihilated.

Chapter 1464: Supreme-level Soul Ancestor, A Bold Idea...

Chapter 1464: Supreme-level Soul Ancestor, A Bold Idea
!
The fall of the three Saint Talent Users—the Scorpio Domain Ancestor, the Dark Eagle Domain Ancestor, and the Evil Wind Domain Ancestor—was immediately known to their parents.
At this, the three evil races of the Dark Destruction Domain were enraged.
Through divination, they learned that all the Domain Ancestors they had sent into the Dark Soul Domain had perished. They had fallen without serving much of a purpose at all.
This was a massive loss! Furthermore, losing three Saint Talent Users was a blow so heavy they could barely withstand it.
More importantly, the fact that all their clansmen had fallen meant total failure; the benefits of the Dark Soul Domain now had nothing to do with them.
It would be another trillion years before it was the turn of Supreme-level Domain Ancestors like them to enter the Dark Soul Domain.
During this time, they would have no way to obtain any benefits from the Dark Soul Domain, which was the true loss.
....After Ye Tian wiped out the three evil race Domain Ancestors from the Dark Saint Domain, he continued to consolidate the Human Race's territory.
Whenever a precious treasure was born in a certain location, he would head there to seize it.
In this way, the long years slowly passed. Under Ye Tian's leadership, the Human Race grew stronger and stronger within the Dark Soul Domain, seizing many treasures, some of which were useful even to Supreme-level Domain Ancestors.
A portion of these treasures obtained by the Human Race was used for themselves, while another portion was taken out of the Dark Soul Domain and sent to the Human Race headquarters in the Profound Void Saint Realm.
It could be said that with the resources from the Dark Soul Domain, the strength of the Human Race developed extremely rapidly.
In the blink of an eye, ten billion years passed.
By this time, Ye Tian's duplicated body in the Dark Soul Domain had already grown to the Invincible Soul Ancestor realm and had reached the peak of that realm.
The path for an Invincible Soul Ancestor to promote to a Supreme Soul Ancestor had also been deduced by now.
For an Invincible Domain Ancestor to promote to a Supreme Domain Ancestor, one must master the physical body and complete nine transformations. The path for an Invincible Soul Ancestor was similar.
An Invincible Soul Ancestor must... control the soul. After mastering 365 times the soul power, they would undergo nine soul transformations, at which point they could step into the Supreme-level Soul Ancestor realm.
Currently, there were many experts in the Dark Soul Domain who had reached the Invincible Soul Ancestor level. Most were native Soul Ancestors, as the natives were favored by providence and their cultivation was very smooth, while outsiders faced a certain degree of suppression.
Ye Tian's duplicated body had also cultivated to the peak of the Invincible Soul Ancestor realm and was beginning to master the soul.
Although mastering the soul was different from mastering the physical body, Ye Tian's realm was simply too high. Furthermore, by occasionally using his Derivation Trait and consuming a tiny bit of Saint Soul power to deduce how to master the soul, the impact on his main body was negligible.
Consequently, Ye Tian's speed in mastering the soul was many times faster than other Invincible Soul Ancestors.
Although Supreme-level Domain Ancestors could not enter for a trillion years, and the Primordial Ancestors certainly couldn't enter either...
Ye Tian wanted to raise his cultivation to the peak of the Supreme Soul Ancestor realm within that trillion-year period.
That way, even when the other Supreme-level Domain Ancestors entered the Dark Soul Domain, they would still be unable to contend with him.
Moreover, Ye Tian knew that at the one-trillion-year mark, a world-shaking opportunity would be born in the Dark Soul Domain, which would also be the time of the fiercest competition.
Right now, the Dark Soul Domain was only in its initial stages.
The grade of the treasures being born was limited.
The years flowed by, 100 million years at a time.
In the 70th billion year, Ye Tian finally completed his nine soul transformations and stepped into the Supreme-level Soul Ancestor realm.
BOOM!!!!! Endless soul energy surged from all corners of the Dark Soul Domain into the Ten Directions Saint Realm, where it was absorbed and refined by Ye Tian.
The commotion of his breakthrough was too massive, attracting the attention of many experts. Even the Primordial Ancestors noticed the disturbance caused by Ye Tian's breakthrough.
"A Supreme Domain Ancestor has been born in the Dark Soul Domain. Such speed! Who is it?"
The Primordial Ancestors were all incredibly curious.
Soon, they found out.
"The Human Race, Qingye Soul Ancestor. It's him!"
The Primordial Ancestors were dumbfounded.
In order to nurture Invincible Soul Ancestors, they had even brought out some of their own treasures. However, the path of the Soul Ancestor was, after all, an unfamiliar one, and it was difficult for them to quickly help Soul Ancestors promote to the Supreme level.
Yet even so, with their resources and guidance, they were beaten to it by a Soul Ancestor of the Human Race.
What was the Human Race? They only had a single Supreme-level Domain Ancestor. To them, this faction was practically an ant.
But it was such a small faction that had nurtured a terrifying genius whom their own descendants and disciples could not surpass.
Once Ye Tian's duplicated body entered the Supreme-level Soul Ancestor realm, he no longer had any reservations.
In his identity as the Qingye Soul Ancestor, Ye Tian began to sweep through everything. He stepped into the headquarters of various factions, seizing all their resources. Even the outposts of the Destruction Saint Race and the various Saint Sects of the Dark Saint Domain were visited by him.
Of course, he did not kill indiscriminately. After all, the Human Race headquarters and his main body were in the outside world; he naturally couldn't afford to excessively offend these Primordial Ancestors.
Therefore, Ye Tian only seized resources and did not kill.
In this way, many resources of the Dark Soul Domain were gathered into the hands of the Human Race, and many precious lands were occupied by them.
Many factions united, wanting to resist Ye Tian, but they were still no match for him.
"Forget it. The real battlefield begins after the Dark Soul Domain has existed for a trillion years. The treasures born then will be truly precious. What does it matter if we yield these current resources to the Human Race? Is it possible that this Qingye Soul Ancestor can grow to a level where he can contend with those peak Supreme-level Domain Ancestors in a mere trillion years?"
The Primordial Ancestors thought to themselves.
The Primordial Ancestors gave up on competing during this period; thus, in this era, the Dark Soul Domain was dominated and controlled by the Human Race.
Gathering the resources of the Dark Soul Domain, Ye Tian nurtured several Soul Ancestors of the Human Race to the Invincible Soul Ancestor realm.
However, it remained extremely difficult for them to promote to the Supreme-level Soul Ancestor realm.
Still, with his guidance and lectures, by the time the trillion-year mark arrived, there was hope for the Human Race to give birth to several Supreme-level Soul Ancestors.
Ye Tian's duplicated body was also cultivating diligently, refining countless resources just so he could raise his strength to the peak of the Supreme Soul Ancestor realm.
But this step was not easy.
"Time is insufficient. A mere trillion years is indeed not long. Moreover, during this period, the Dark Soul Domain cannot produce resources that allow a Supreme Soul Ancestor's cultivation to progress rapidly. My main body has also finished refining the Nirvana treasures there. Without more Nirvana treasures, there's no way to quickly increase my cultivation!"
Ye Tian thought to himself.
After thinking it over, Ye Tian could only think of one solution.
"The Nirvana Clan was wiped out, but strictly speaking, I can be considered a member of the Nirvana Clan. After all, I possess all the Ancestral Talents of the Nirvana Clan. If I am willing, I could also create a region of Nirvana Space-Time!"
Ye Tian suddenly realized.

Chapter 1465: Creating Nirvana Spacetime, Cultivation Breakthrough...

Chapter 1465: Creating Nirvana Spacetime, Cultivation Breakthrough to the Peak of Supreme Soul Ancestor!
!
Creating a Nirvana Spacetime was indeed a very bold idea.
If he were in the outside world, the Ancestors would easily find out, and then he would be in trouble.
However, this was the Dark Soul Domain, and currently, the Ancestors could not enter.
Therefore, if he created a Nirvana Spacetime within the Dark Soul Domain, the Ancestors would definitely not be able to discover it.
Moreover, he didn't need to create a large-scale Nirvana Spacetime; he only needed to create a small patch of it.
As long as a single member of the Nirvana Clan existed, a Nirvana Spacetime could persist indefinitely, as the Nirvana Ancestral Talent of the Nirvana Clan could continuously influence it.
Of course, Nirvana Spacetime also required energy to sustain it. If it absorbed a large amount of external energy, it could continuously convert it into Nirvana energy. Nirvana energy had a massive effect on both Supreme Domain Ancestors and Supreme Soul Ancestors.
However, the prerequisite was being able to withstand the erosion of Nirvana energy. Other Supreme Domain Ancestors could not withstand its erosion; only the Ancestors themselves could refine Nirvana energy.
But Ye Tian could refine Nirvana energy.
"The Dark Soul Domain does not lack resources. I can completely create a small patch of Nirvana Spacetime and then integrate a large amount of resources into it.
Back then, the reason the Nirvana Clan frantically invaded the Dark Forbidden Domain was... because they wanted to occupy a large amount of territory and devour the energy resources of the Dark Forbidden Domain to convert them into Nirvana energy, thereby strengthening the Nirvana Clan."
Ye Tian murmured to himself.
Thus, for him now, all of this was very easy to achieve, and he didn't have to worry about being discovered by the Ancestors.
In any case... those low-level resources were useless to him now. It was better to put them to use by converting them into Nirvana energy, which was a way to rapidly increase his cultivation.
"Let's do it!"
Ye Tian decided.
No sooner said than done.
Ye Tian chose the Ten Directions Sacred Realm and then sealed off an area, not allowing anyone to enter—not even the Invincible Domain Ancestors of the human race.
Subsequently, he began to manifest the Nirvana Ancestral Talent.
This duplicated body had also been bestowed with the Nirvana Ancestral Talent by his main body, so it could influence the spacetime here.
Boom!!!!! An area of spacetime was invaded by the Nirvana Ancestral Talent, gradually forming a special spacetime region.
Initially, this spacetime region was very small, but it gradually expanded to the size of a universe.
"That's about enough. A range this large is sufficient!"
Once the Nirvana Spacetime was created, it still needed to be stabilized; otherwise, it would gradually dissipate.
In the days that followed, Ye Tian integrated a sea of resources into this Nirvana Spacetime, using the Nirvana Ancestral Talent to smelt this energy and increase the power of this spacetime region.
From the beginning, the Nirvana energy in this Nirvana Spacetime was extremely thin, but it gradually became concentrated.
Even without Nirvana treasures, cultivating by absorbing Nirvana energy here was many times faster than in the outside world.
Under the accumulation of massive resources, a Nirvana treasure finally began to be born within this Nirvana Spacetime.
Buzz!!!! Somewhere within the Nirvana Spacetime, a treasure was born.
"Nirvana Blood Flower, a mid-grade Nirvana treasure. A good harvest!"
Ye Tian waited for some time, and when the flower bloomed and matured, he plucked it.
In the following days, one Nirvana treasure after another was born, all falling into Ye Tian's hands, with no one to compete with him.
Meanwhile, the Dark Soul Domain continuously produced a large number of treasures, almost all of which fell into the hands of the human race, and the majority of the human race's resources were concentrated on Ye Tian.
Consequently, Ye Tian did not lack resources at all, pouring them all into the Nirvana Spacetime.
With enough Nirvana treasures, Ye Tian began to refine them to temper his soul and increase his cultivation.
After only tens of millions of years, Ye Tian's cultivation rose to the mid-stage Supreme Soul Ancestor realm.
In the blink of an eye, several billion years passed in the Dark Soul Domain.
By this time, a second Supreme Soul Ancestor had still not been born in the Dark Soul Domain, while Ye Tian's cultivation, with the help of Nirvana treasures, had already risen to the peak of the Supreme Soul Ancestor level, consistent with his main body.
"Hahaha, if I didn't care about my foundation and just wanted to become an ordinary Ancestor, I would truly have hope of becoming one within a single Realm Year!"
Ye Tian thought to himself.
As for the Ancestors wanting to enter the Dark Soul Domain, it would likely take them a hundred Realm Years.
A hundred Realm Years was not a very long time for the Ancestors—which Ancestor hadn't lived through millions of Realm Years since they began cultivating? But for Ye Tian, within a hundred Realm Years, even if he were mediocre, he would have already become an Ancestor.
Of course, his main body pursued becoming the strongest Ancestor, so he would not rush to break through. He wanted to create the strongest Ancestor Law before attempting to break through to the Ancestor realm.
"The coming days will be spent... deducing a batch of Ancestral Techniques, cultivating them to the Perfection stage, and then beginning to practice the Spatial Ancestor Law!"
Ye Tian decided.
Once he broke through to the Ancestor realm with the help of the Spatial Ancestor Law, he would be a Spatial Ancestor. Moreover, since he would become a Spatial Ancestor within the Dark Soul Domain, even as a Future One, he could control a small portion of the Dark Soul Domain's power and exert formidable strength.
Furthermore, after cultivating for a hundred Realm Years, his strength would be even greater, and he would definitely have hope of contending with the likes of the Destruction Ancestor and the Holy Ancestor.
Once the Dark Soul Domain was secured as a foundation, the strength of the human race would likely reach a terrifying level.
Moreover, the Profound Void Sacred Realm could definitely become comparable to a Dark Sacred Ground in the future.
Time flowed by.
In the blink of an eye, 1 billion years passed.
By this time, the Dark Soul Domain had already given birth to hundreds of Supreme Soul Ancestors. Most of them were native inhabitants; after all, at the beginning of the Dark Soul Domain's birth, it was too easy for natives to cultivate. However, it would be difficult to produce so many Supreme Soul Ancestors in the future; this was a benefit of the birth of a Dark Sacred Ground.
These Supreme Soul Ancestors were all at the early stage. To reach the mid-stage, they would likely have to wait for the great opportunity that would come after a trillion years.
Furthermore, over a trillion years, many treasures would be born that could allow Supreme Domain Ancestors to rapidly increase their strength.
However, what no one knew was that by this time, Ye Tian had already cultivated a large number of Ancestral Techniques to the Perfection stage, and his cultivation had reached the limit of a Supreme Soul Ancestor. He had even begun to temper his physical body, hoping to achieve something in the path of the physical body.
However, this step was too difficult. Once one became a Supreme Soul Ancestor, the physical body was almost entirely soul-energized, making it impossible to possess a physical body as terrifying as that of a Supreme Domain Ancestor.
But this was also quite normal.
Because a Supreme Domain Ancestor also had no way of possessing a soul as heaven-defying as that of a Supreme Soul Ancestor. It was too difficult to completely combine the two.
During these 10 billion years, Ye Tian also began to comprehend the Spatial Ancestor Law, and had currently comprehended one-fifth of it.
By the time a trillion years passed, he would definitely be able to fully comprehend the Spatial Ancestor Law and step into the Ancestor realm with a single thought.
"Then I will wait until the trillion-year mark to break through to the Ancestor realm and shock those Ancestors!"
Ye Tian said with a smile.

Chapter 1466: The Birth of the Primordial Ancestral Realm, About to Impact...

Chapter 1466: The Birth of the Primordial Ancestral Realm, About to Impact the Ancestor Realm!
One hundred billion years, one hundred billion years, passed just like that.
Over the long years, the overall strength of the Dark Soul Domain grew rapidly, but the growth rate of Supreme-level Soul Ancestors became slower and slower. Later on, it was difficult for even one Supreme-level Soul Ancestor to be born in ten billion years. Additionally, Supreme-level Soul Ancestors fought among themselves, and occasionally one or two would fall, causing the number of Supreme-level Soul Ancestors in the Dark Soul Domain to stabilize at a certain figure, occasionally dropping by one or two.
With the help of a nearly invincible Supreme-level Soul Ancestor like Ye Tian, the strength of the human race developed very quickly. With sufficient resources, the human race produced a large number of Invincible Domain Ancestors and even ten Supreme-level Soul Ancestors. This was an opportunity for the human race.
But after the birth of ten Supreme-level Soul Ancestors, it became difficult for the human race to produce more. This was not only related to the end of the Dark Soul Domain's benefits but also to providence.
For the same force, once a dozen or so Supreme-level Soul Ancestors have been born, it becomes very difficult to continue producing more.
Of course, if there are enough resources and opportunities, more Supreme-level Soul Ancestors can still be born, but it will definitely take a long time.
At this time.
Ye Tian had already fully comprehended the Space Ancestor Law and could step into the Ancestor Realm at any time with its help.
Besides him, the strongest Supreme-level Soul Ancestor in the Dark Soul Domain was a mid-stage Supreme-level Soul Ancestor, a native resident, who was far from being Ye Tian's match and was like an ant in Ye Tian's eyes.
"It's coming soon. The one trillion-year mark is approaching. At that time, the Dark Soul Domain will no longer be able to restrict Supreme-level Domain Ancestors from entering. Moreover, the first Ancestral Realm will be born, and a large number of innate items will appear—specifically, innate items of the Ancestral Realm.
Furthermore, the first Ancestral Realm born in the Dark Holy Land is... the Primordial Ancestral Realm.
When the Primordial Ancestral Realm is born, the Primordial Ancestral Spring will inevitably appear. Soaking in the Primordial Ancestral Spring will rapidly increase one's cultivation and even allow a Supreme-level Domain Ancestor's body to be tempered a second time. This is a truly great opportunity!"
Ye Tian murmured.
At that time, his main body could also enjoy the opportunities of the Primordial Ancestral Realm, allowing his Supreme Domain Body to undergo a second transformation. This was the only chance in the Dark Holy Land; Ancestral Realms born afterward would no longer produce the Primordial Ancestral Spring.
In the distant past, when the Dark Holy Domain was first born, the Primordial Ancestral Realm was shattered. But even now, the Ancestors still craved the opportunities of the Primordial Ancestral Realm.
It was clear how precious the birth of the Primordial Ancestral Realm was; countless Supreme-level Domain Ancestors would fight for it.
Ye Tian could not deny that his strength was indeed very powerful, but that didn't mean the Supreme-level Domain Ancestors of other forces were weak.
Various major forces had hidden their strength. In the Silent Spacetime, those Supreme-level Domain Ancestors didn't seem to have any monstrously talented individuals, but who knew if there were any truly exceptional ones? Moreover, if there were peak Supreme-level Domain Ancestors who had long reached the level where they could become Ancestors but had been refraining from breaking through, once they entered the Dark Soul Domain, they might immediately break through to become Ancestors. In this way, they would be confident in controlling the Dark Soul Domain and even preventing other Supreme-level Soul Ancestors from impacting the Ancestor Realm in the future.
Back then, the Dark Soul Domain gave birth to the Saint.
Additionally, it was the first time the Dark Soul Domain learned that another Dark Holy Land would be born outside the Dark Destruction Domain. They were completely unprepared, and the Dark Holy Domain rose.
But this time is different. The Dark Destruction Domain and the Dark Holy Domain are fully prepared, vowing to take over the Dark Soul Domain. Therefore, it is almost unrealistic for the native residents of the Dark Soul Domain to want to be the first to give birth to an Ancestor and completely control the Dark Soul Domain.
...."The major forces really do have peak Supreme-level Domain Ancestors who can become Ancestors very quickly, but it will be difficult for them to achieve that in the Dark Soul Domain; it will take quite some time. After all, they are Domain Ancestors, not Soul Ancestors.
But my duplicate body is different; it is a Supreme-level Soul Ancestor. Therefore, becoming an Ancestor in the Dark Soul Domain will be many times easier!"
Ye Tian murmured.
Soon, the one trillion-year deadline was approaching.
Outside the Dark Soul Domain.
A large number of Supreme-level Domain Ancestors arrived, and even some unfamiliar Supreme-level Domain Ancestors appeared, clearly the hidden trump cards of various major forces.
Some of these Supreme-level Domain Ancestors were too ancient, some even older than the Ancestors themselves. Each of their auras was incredibly terrifying. Clearly, they had all formed Ancestral Bodies and cultivated them to a high level, and they were terrifying existences who mastered powerful Ancestral Techniques.
As a peak Supreme-level Domain Ancestor, Ye Tian naturally had to enter the Dark Soul Domain as well.
It could be said that almost all Supreme-level Domain Ancestors were going to enter the Dark Soul Domain to compete for this opportunity.
One could imagine that the Primordial Ancestral Realm would likely fall into a terrifying war this time, which might even cause the Primordial Ancestral Realm of the Dark Soul Domain to crack.
This day.
"It's here!"
Ye Tian said in a low voice.
Boom!!!! The Dark Soul Domain underwent a transformation, and the rules changed dramatically.
At the same time, in the central region of the Dark Soul Domain, an incredibly massive world was born in one location.
This world was the Primordial Ancestral Realm! As soon as the Primordial Ancestral Realm was born, many Supreme Soul Ancestors of the Dark Soul Domain descended here. Ye Tian's duplicate body, Soul Ancestor Qing Ye, also arrived here.
Whoosh! Whoosh! Whoosh! One by one, Supreme-level Domain Ancestors from the outside world stepped into the Dark Soul Domain.
Many Supreme-level Domain Ancestors exuded the aura of the peak Supreme-level Domain Ancestor stage, far surpassing ordinary Supreme-level Soul Ancestors.
Moreover, these Supreme-level Soul Ancestors had cultivated for a short time and had not mastered Ancestral Techniques or Ancestral Bodies, so they were naturally far from being able to contend with these ancient peak Supreme-level Domain Ancestors.
For a moment, many Supreme-level Soul Ancestors in the Dark Soul Domain were terrified, fearing they would be wiped out.
From the birth of the Primordial Ancestral Realm to the birth of the Primordial Ancestral Spring, some time was needed in between.
Therefore, this period was an opportunity for the Supreme-level Soul Ancestors to increase their strength.
Consequently, many Supreme-level Soul Ancestors instantly fled into the Primordial Ancestral Realm and hid, searching for innate items that could help them quickly increase their strength.
Ye Tian's main body also arrived at the Primordial Ancestral Realm and began searching for various innate items.
Meanwhile, his duplicate body began to impact the Ancestor Realm.
At this time, the benefits of being the first to reach the Ancestor Realm were too great; there was no need to wait for the birth of the Primordial Ancestral Spring.
He believed that there were likely other peak Supreme-level Domain Ancestors also preparing to impact the Ancestor Realm.

Chapter 1467: The Copy Body Has Become an Ancestor!

Chapter 1467: The Copy Body Has Become an Ancestor!
!
Whether one is a Supreme-level Soul Ancestor or a Supreme-level Domain Ancestor, the method for breaking through to become an Ancestor is largely the same: one must use an Ancestor Law to achieve the breakthrough.
An Ancestor Law is... the ultimate of the Dao, the origin of the Dao, and the incarnation of the Dao.
To break through using an Ancestor Law is to... transform oneself into the Dao.
The Space Ancestor Law involves transforming the body into a Space Origin Ancestor Body, shattering the limits of a Supreme-level Soul Body or a Supreme-level Domain Body to achieve an Ancestor physique.
The Ancestor physique achieved by a Supreme-level Domain Ancestor is a physical body, while the Ancestor physique achieved by a Supreme-level Soul Ancestor is a soul body.
In reality, however, they are much the same. Once an Ancestor Body is achieved, the soul is the body and the body is the soul; both are incomparably powerful in every aspect.
That said, the accumulation of a peak Supreme-level Domain Ancestor or Soul Ancestor at the Supreme level varies. Once they break through, their strength will naturally differ as well.
Ye Tian’s copy body had accumulated enough; although it was not as powerful as his main body, it far surpassed other Supreme-level Domain Ancestors.
Therefore, once Ye Tian became an Ancestor, his strength would inevitably surpass that of ordinary Ancestors.
....Boom!!!! Ye Tian’s body began to reshape itself according to the profound mysteries of the Space Ancestor Law, evolving toward a Space Ancestor physique.
Having long since mastered the Space Ancestor Law, Ye Tian could naturally condense a Space Ancestor physique with ease.
In the midst of this, the origin power of the Dark Forbidden Domain poured into Ye Tian’s body.
The Space Ancestor physique Ye Tian condensed was different from that of other Ancestors; thus, the Dao he practiced did not conflict with others.
A single Dao only allows one person to become an Ancestor. Of course, the Space Ancestor Dao is divided into many types, but if one becomes an Ancestor using the exact same Ancestor Law, it counts as the same Ancestor Dao. During a breakthrough, repulsion occurs, and one's own Ancestor Dao would be shattered by the opponent's Ancestor Dao.
Therefore, once he broke through to the Ancestor realm, others who practiced this specific Space Ancestor Law in the future would be unable to become Ancestors, though they could still merge with a fragmented Ancestor Dao to become Half-step Ancestors.
Endless energy surged into Ye Tian’s copy body, helping him achieve his Ancestor physique.
Outside the Dark Soul Domain.
One Ancestor after another looked toward the Dark Soul Domain, their faces filled with shock.
"Someone is charging for the Ancestor realm? How can it be so fast?"
The Ancestors exclaimed in shock.
They had speculated that some peak Supreme-level Domain Ancestors would attempt to break through to the Ancestor realm. Once prepared, there was hope of becoming an Ancestor within the Dark Soul Domain. Perhaps due to the nature of the Domain Ancestor Dao, they might not be able to take control of the Dark Soul Domain, but once an Ancestor was born, they could influence the domain's direction.
If a Supreme-level Domain Ancestor from the Dark Destruction Domain became an Ancestor, they could use their Ancestor lineage to continuously influence the Dark Soul Domain, creating countless destructive races to destroy regions of the Dark Soul Domain and establish a second Destruction Domain.
If an Ancestor was born from the Dark Holy Domain, they would tear into the Domain Ancestor Dao within the Dark Soul Domain, allowing the Domain Ancestors to cultivate faster.
But logically, peak Supreme-level Domain Ancestors shouldn't be able to promote to the Ancestor realm so quickly; the suppression of a Dark Holy Land was no joke.
"Wait, it’s not a Supreme Domain Ancestor charging for the Ancestor realm—it’s a Supreme-level Soul Ancestor!!!!"
The Ancestors realized.
Soon, Supreme-level Domain Ancestors went to investigate, and before long, they locked onto the target.
Before the Destruction Ancestor, a Supreme-level Domain Ancestor emerged from the domain and reported: "Lord Destruction Ancestor, the person charging for the Ancestor realm is the Human Race's Green Leaf Soul Ancestor!"
"The Human Race, Green Leaf Soul Ancestor? That human genius who entered the Soul Domain? In such a short time, he transformed from a Half-step Domain Ancestor to a Half-step Soul Ancestor, and now he’s charging for the Ancestor realm? How is this possible?"
Even the Destruction Ancestor was shocked, his expression changing.
In a period as short as a trillion years, someone had risen from the beginning of cultivation to the Ancestor realm? Even he couldn't have done it back then, and the Holy Ancestor of the Dark Holy Domain couldn't have done it either.
The Holy Ancestor of the Dark Holy Domain broke through to the Ancestor realm in the 28th Realm Year, and that was with no one obstructing him and the providence of the Dark Holy Domain concentrated upon him.
A mere trillion years was nothing more than a fraction of a single Realm Year.
To do it in such a short time, and as a genius of the Human Race rather than a disciple under the Holy Ancestor, was simply unbelievable to him.
On the side of the Dark Holy Domain, the Holy Ancestor and a group of other Ancestors were also stunned.
The War Ancestor and Realm Ancestor of the War Gate were also completely bewildered. How did the Human Race suddenly produce such a monstrous existence? Setting aside combat power and looking only at the achievement of becoming an Ancestor, he was even more monstrous than Ye Tian! At the very least, Ye Tian had cultivated for so many long years and had yet to become an Ancestor.
...."Myriad Law War Ancestor, what exactly is going on with that Green Leaf Soul Ancestor of your Human Race? How did he suddenly charge into the Ancestor realm?"
The War Ancestor asked one of Ye Tian’s avatars.
When Supreme-level Domain Ancestors entered the Dark Soul Domain, they would leave an avatar behind to report on the situation inside at any time.
"He probably encountered a fortuitous opportunity!"
Ye Tian replied.
He couldn't say that it was his own copy body; otherwise, if other Ancestors specifically targeted his main body, it would be disastrous! Once the main body perished, it was a true death!
At this moment, the War Ancestor was thoroughly envious. The Human Race had already produced a genius as monstrous as Ye Tian, who was almost certain to become an Ancestor in the future. He hadn't expected them to produce an even more monstrous Green Leaf Soul Ancestor—who would be called the Green Leaf Ancestor in the future.
Crucially, once the Green Leaf Ancestor successfully broke through, he could take control of a portion of the Dark Soul Domain! In that case, the Green Leaf Ancestor would be truly invincible within the Dark Soul Domain!
As time passed.
Ye Tian’s transformation grew faster and faster. Some tried to interrupt Ye Tian’s breakthrough, but Ye Tian’s main body was nearby. Whenever a Supreme-level Domain Ancestor made a move, they were all suppressed and killed by Ye Tian.
Even those ancient peak Supreme-level Domain Ancestors were no match for Ye Tian’s main body.
Although Ye Tian’s main body was not yet a match for an Ancestor, even a Half-step Ancestor comparable to the Six-Mark Silence Clan was no match for him.
A million years finally passed.
On this day, Ye Tian’s copy body finally fully condensed its Ancestor physique, stepping into the Ancestor level and becoming a Space Ancestor.
Outside the Dark Soul Domain, at the War Gate station.
Ye Tian’s avatar was discussing a matter with the War Ancestor and the Realm Ancestor.
"War Ancestor, Realm Ancestor, there are currently two peak Supreme-level Domain Ancestors in the Dark Soul Domain attempting to break through to the Ancestor realm. One is an Ancestor from the Dark Destruction Domain, and the other is a Domain Ancestor from the Myriad Things Holy Sect of the Dark Holy Domain. Should I move to kill them?"
"Kill them!"
The Realm Ancestor nodded.
Although they were in an alliance before, now that the Silence Clan had been wiped out, everyone was an enemy.
Therefore, the War Gate naturally did not want other forces to produce an Ancestor.
"Myriad Law War Ancestor, your Human Race's Green Leaf Ancestor can only act once. This is because Ancestors are not permitted to act against Supreme-level Domain Ancestors; this is a tacit rule.
The Green Leaf Ancestor has just broken through and does not know this rule, so he can act, and the other Ancestors won't be able to say anything.
But once he is informed, he can no longer act.
Therefore, the Green Leaf Ancestor must act immediately."
The War Ancestor reminded him.
"Understood!"
Ye Tian nodded.
Inside the Dark Soul Domain, Ye Tian’s copy body, through his control over the domain, sensed the locations of the two peak Supreme-level Domain Ancestors who were attempting to break through.
In the next instant.
With a single thought, Ye Tian arrived beside the two peak Supreme-level Domain Ancestors and reached out with a hand.
No matter how they resisted, it was in vain.
Bang!!! The two peak Supreme-level Domain Ancestors were easily wiped out by Ye Tian, annihilated without any power to resist.

Chapter 1468: The Ancestor-level Copied Body Becomes a Permanent Clone!

Chapter 1468: The Ancestor-level Copied Body Becomes a Permanent Clone!
!
The two peak Supreme-level Domain Ancestors who were in the process of breaking through to the Ancestor level had fallen, and their incarnations outside the Dark Soul Domain naturally dissipated immediately.
Consequently, the Ancestors backing these two peak Supreme-level Domain Ancestors also found out instantly.
In an instant, the Ancestors of the two factions were enraged.
These two peak Supreme-level Domain Ancestors had an eighty to ninety percent chance of becoming Ancestors. For the sake of this opportunity in the Dark Soul Domain, they had been holding back and refraining from breaking through.
It could be said that these two factions had invested far too many resources and opportunities into these two peak Supreme-level Domain Ancestors.
Now, everything had come to naught! Boom!!! The Destruction Ancestor and the other Ancestors of the Destruction Holy Race turned their gazes toward the War Sect, and the All-Things Ancestor of the All-Things Holy Sect could no longer suppress his killing intent.
The All-Things Holy Sect only had him as an Ancestor. If that peak Supreme-level Domain Ancestor had been willing, the All-Things Holy Sect would have long since birthed a second Ancestor.
But now, the hope for the All-Things Holy Sect's rise was shattered, and he wished he could wipe out the Human Race.
"Wanfa Zhanzu, your Human Race's Qingye Ancestor killed our All-Things Holy Sect's Guanghong Holy Ancestor!!!"
The All-Things Ancestor roared in fury.
He didn't even need to investigate to know it was Qingye Ancestor's doing.
After all, Guanghong Holy Ancestor was a peak Supreme-level Domain Ancestor with immense combat power, no weaker than a weaker half-step Ancestor. Furthermore, he possessed an Ancestor-level defensive weapon bestowed upon him; even a powerful half-step Ancestor would find it difficult to kill him in a short time.
Yet just now, Guanghong Holy Ancestor's incarnation didn't even have the chance to call for help before his main body was slain and his incarnation dissipated.
This indicated that Guanghong Holy Ancestor had been insta-killed, and the only person capable of doing that was the Qingye Ancestor, who had just successfully broken through to the Ancestor level.
"I don't know anything about that. Besides, it's just the death of a Supreme-level Domain Ancestor! In the battles of the Dark Soul Domain, isn't it normal for one or two Supreme-level Domain Ancestors to die? What, does your All-Things Holy Sect intend to go to war with our War Sect?"
Ye Tian said coldly.
"Ancestors are not permitted to take action against peak Supreme-level Domain Ancestors; this is a regulation among Ancestors!"
The Destruction Ancestor also spoke with great fury.
After all, the Destruction Holy Race had also lost a quasi-ancestor. If he hadn't died, an Ancestor from the Destruction Holy Race would have appeared within the Dark Soul Domain. This would have been great news for the Destruction Holy Race, enough to seize control of vast territories within the Dark Soul Domain and even obtain massive amounts of resources.
But now, that peak Supreme-level Domain Ancestor had fallen.
How could he not be angry? If Ye Tian's true body were here, he likely would have crushed him with a single thought.
Unfortunately, the Ye Tian here was merely an incarnation.
Boom!!!!! Jiezu blocked the enraged All-Things Ancestor and the Ancestors of the Dark Destruction Domain, explaining: "Qingye Ancestor was initially only a half-step Domain Ancestor and rapidly ascended to the Ancestor realm within the Dark Soul Domain. He is unaware of the Ancestor agreements. I have already had Wanfa Zhanzu notify Qingye Ancestor; Qingye will no longer kill Supreme-level Domain Ancestors or Supreme-level Soul Ancestors!"
"Is our All-Things Holy Sect's quasi-ancestor just supposed to have died for nothing?"
The All-Things Ancestor said angrily.
"Quasi-ancestor? That is merely your claim. Who knows if he was just an ordinary peak Supreme-level Domain Ancestor? Besides, life and death are determined by fate. Since he entered the Dark Soul Domain, if he's dead, he's dead."
Jiezu said coldly.
The All-Things Ancestor snorted coldly and said no more.
In terms of strength, he was far from being Jiezu's match, and there was no benefit in making an enemy of Jiezu.
Thus, he could only let the matter drop.
Although the Destruction Ancestor was furious, it was impossible for him to kill Zhanzu or Jiezu over this. Moreover, while Jiezu was not his match, he had many means of escape, and there was no way to kill him.
Furthermore, the Holy Ancestor of the Dark Holy Domain would definitely not allow the Dark Holy Domain to lose a powerful combatant like Jiezu and would certainly intervene to stop him.
"Once the Dark Soul Domain allows Ancestors to enter, I will surely kill that Qingye Ancestor!"
The Destruction Ancestor thought to himself.
Although Qingye Ancestor held authority over a portion of the Dark Soul Domain, he was not a true native resident after all and could not completely control the Dark Soul Domain.
If Ancestors were divided into three tiers: Ordinary Ancestors, Elite Ancestors, and Top-tier Ancestors.
Then, when the Dark Holy Domain was first born, the Holy Ancestor, relying on the power of the Dark Holy Domain, could exert the combat power of a peak Elite Ancestor. At that time, he was also only an Elite Ancestor, so he could do nothing to the Holy Ancestor.
But now, he was a Top-tier Ancestor, and the Holy Ancestor was also a Top-tier Ancestor.
Qingye Ancestor, with the help of the Dark Soul Domain, could at most exert the combat power of a weaker Elite Ancestor. He was confident he could kill such a Qingye Ancestor.
He believed the Holy Ancestor would not stop him. After all, if Qingye Ancestor were allowed to live, once he used the Dark Soul Domain to grow into an Elite Ancestor, he could then exert Top-tier Ancestor combat power with its help.
In that case, the Dark Soul Domain would fall into the hands of the Human Race, which was equivalent to falling into the hands of the War Sect.
The Holy Ancestor would protect the powerful Ancestors of the Dark Holy Domain, but he also suppressed them to a certain extent.
Therefore, if he killed Qingye Ancestor, it was impossible for the Holy Ancestor to intervene.
If the Holy Ancestor didn't intervene, the other Ancestors would be even less able to stop him.
....Ye Tian did not know that the Destruction Ancestor wanted to kill Qingye Ancestor, and even if he did, he wouldn't be worried. After all, Qingye Ancestor was merely his copied body.
Moreover, there was still a very long time before the hundred-domain limit. Qingye Ancestor could continue to increase his strength, and by then, there was much hope of growing to a level where he could contend with the Destruction Ancestor.
But at this moment, Ye Tian was completely immersed in the new changes of his Copying Talent.
No, it should be said he was immersed in the changes of his copying ability.
Ye Tian's copying ability could copy creatures with cultivation equal to or lower than his own, but he could only copy one.
But now it was different. When the copied body broke through to the Ancestor realm, this copied body was no longer just a copied body; it had become solidified, turning into a special clone that no longer occupied the slot for a copied body.
In other words, the body of Qingye Ancestor existed independently as a special clone that could exist permanently and cultivate on its own, while Ye Tian could continue to use his copied body ability.
However, he could still only copy peak Supreme-level Domain Ancestors and could not copy Ancestors. After all, the ability of the copied body was determined by his main body, not by his clones.
"Not bad, it's equivalent to having an extra Ancestor clone! Hahaha, this way, I can continue to use the copied body ability to copy bodies, and then continuously use the Evolution ability to deduce and create Ancestor Laws suitable for myself! I can even help the Ancestor clone deduce more powerful Ancestral Techniques."
Ye Tian thought to himself.
