Chapter 1469: The Human Race Controls the Dark Soul Domain!

Chapter 1469: The Human Race Controls the Dark Soul Domain
!
After Ye Tian’s clone became a Primordial Ancestor, many Supreme Domain Ancestors from the Dark Destruction Domain withdrew one after another. Even many Saint Gates of the Dark Saint Domain withdrew their Supreme Domain Ancestors.
There was no other way; the Human Race had birthed a Primordial Ancestor who now controlled a portion of the Dark Soul Domain.
Although a Primordial Ancestor could not easily kill a Supreme Domain Ancestor, it did not mean they couldn't trap or injure them.
It could be said that as long as Primordial Ancestor Qing Ye caused even a slight bit of trouble for those Supreme Domain Ancestors or locked onto their positions, Ye Tian alone could sweep through them and easily slay them.
In the Dark Soul Domain, no Supreme Domain Ancestor could evade the detection of Primordial Ancestor Qing Ye.
To prevent further losses of their Supreme Domain Ancestors, these factions naturally did not dare let them remain in the Dark Soul Domain; otherwise, they could easily fall.
The only Supreme Domain Ancestors who truly dared to stay in the Dark Soul Domain were almost all from the War Gate or those with good relations with the War Gate. After these factions greeted the Primordial Ancestors of the War Gate and Ye Tian, Ye Tian naturally would not make a move against them.
Subsequently.
Ye Tian took control of the Primordial Ancestral World within the Dark Soul Domain. With the strength of his Primordial Ancestor clone, it was not difficult to seal off the Primordial Ancestral World; he could even drive out all the Supreme Domain Ancestors and Supreme Soul Ancestors.
He would not show excessive mercy. He only allowed the Domain Ancestors and Soul Ancestors of the Human Race, as well as those from the War Gate, to enter the Primordial Ancestral World. It was impossible for other factions to enter.
In the Dark Soul Domain, no one could resist Primordial Ancestor Qing Ye.
This was much like when the Dark Saint Domain was first born; the Dark Saint Gate was the oldest and most powerful Saint Gate, and all the best resources fell into its hands.
This was solely because the Dark Saint Gate possessed the Saint Ancestor, the most powerful Primordial Ancestor.
Of course, the current Dark Saint Gate had two other Primordial Ancestors besides the Saint Ancestor, but unfortunately, those two were of average strength. Thus, aside from the Saint Ancestor, the Dark Saint Gate's strength did not hold a dominant advantage among the Ten Great Saint Gates, though they did have more Supreme Domain Ancestors.
Furthermore, the current Dark Saint Domain could no longer provide a strength boost to the Saint Ancestor.
Coupled with the other Primordial Ancestors working together to restrain him, even the Saint Ancestor could no longer dominate the Dark Saint Domain.
The same would eventually happen to the Dark Soul Domain. Sooner or later, Ye Tian would also lose the strength boost from the Dark Soul Domain, as the boost had a time limit—specifically, one hundred thousand domain years.
If Primordial Ancestor Qing Ye’s own strength was not great enough after one hundred thousand domain years, it was inevitable that other Primordial Ancestors would carve away parts of his territory.
....On this day.
Ye Tian brought his family into the domain. After all, the Dark Soul Domain was currently safer than the Profound Void Saint Realm.
Moreover, Ye Tian hoped to let his family enjoy the benefits of the Primordial Ancestral Spring. After all, Ye Tian’s wife, daughter, son, and sister had all ascended to the Supreme Domain Ancestor realm under his full cultivation, though they were only at the early stage.
Once they entered the Primordial Ancestral Spring, they could easily advance to the peak of the Supreme Domain Ancestor realm.
Combined with several other Human Race Supreme Domain Ancestors also breaking through to the peak stage, the Human Race’s strength would become terrifying, potentially even stronger than a single Saint Gate.
More time passed.
On this day, the Primordial Ancestral Spring within the Primordial Ancestral World was born. Ye Tian’s main body, along with the Supreme Domain Ancestors of the Human Race and the War Gate, arrived here. They could all enter the Primordial Ancestral Spring to obtain its benefits.
Peak Supreme Domain Ancestors could obtain a second transformation of their Supreme Domain Body, which offered the greatest benefit.
Other Supreme Domain Ancestors could also rapidly temper their Supreme Domain Bodies, and their cultivation would increase swiftly, which was also a significant advantage.
"Wanfa War Ancestor, it is all thanks to your Human Race’s Primordial Ancestor Qing Ye this time. Otherwise, if our War Gate’s Supreme Domain Ancestors wanted to enter the Primordial Ancestral Spring, we would likely have had to go through a tragic and bloody battle. A Supreme Domain Ancestor like me wouldn't even have been qualified to enter!"
Fire Pattern War Ancestor said with a smile.
Indeed, he was only at the middle stage of the Supreme Domain Ancestor realm; his strength was too weak, and there were far too many Supreme Domain Ancestors stronger than him.
But this time, he was lucky. He could enter the Primordial Ancestral Spring. Once tempered by its waters, while he might not have hope of completing a second transformation to break the limits of the Supreme Domain Body, he could still raise his cultivation to the peak of the Supreme Domain Ancestor realm.
By then, he would be among the most powerful group of Supreme Domain Ancestors in the Dark Saint Domain.
"Everyone, go in and cultivate. Who gains the most will depend on your own abilities!"
Ye Tian spoke.
After all, an opportunity as terrifying as the Primordial Ancestral Spring only appeared when a Primordial Ancestral World was born. It would not exist forever; it was a one-time consumable resource. Once the spring water was exhausted, it would not be replenished.
In the past, when the Dark Saint Domain was born, the Saint Ancestor and several other Primordial Ancestors used the spring water to complete their accumulation from the early to the peak stage of the Supreme Domain Ancestor realm, allowing them to break through to the Primordial Ancestor realm in a short amount of time.
Otherwise, the Saint Ancestor would not have been able to break through before the Primordial Ancestors of the Dark Destruction Domain descended.
The Supreme Domain Ancestors of the Human Race and the War Gate entered the Primordial Ancestral Spring one after another.
Boom!!!! The energy of the Primordial Ancestral Spring surged into their bodies, helping them temper their Supreme Domain Bodies.
While these Supreme Domain Ancestors were cultivating, many Primordial Ancestors outside the Dark Soul Domain departed, and many Supreme Domain Ancestors left as well.
After all, with Primordial Ancestor Qing Ye present in the Dark Soul Domain, the various factions could not gain any benefits. Even if they started a war outside, it wouldn't affect the situation inside the Dark Soul Domain.
Thus, they simply left.
They would wait until the 100 domain years passed and the Primordial Ancestors could descend; they would settle the scores then.
From now until that 10-domain-year mark, the Dark Soul Domain was almost entirely under the control of the Human Race.
Time flowed slowly, and the energy of the Primordial Ancestral Spring continuously decreased.
In particular, the amount of energy Ye Tian absorbed was immense. At this rate of absorption, many Supreme Domain Ancestors might not be able to raise their cultivation to the peak stage.
Everyone was working hard to absorb it, but some Supreme Domain Ancestors had low strength, and their absorption speed was too slow.
"It's almost time. My Supreme Domain Body can undergo one more transformation and break the ultimate limit of the Supreme Domain Body!"
Ye Tian murmured.

Chapter 1470: The Power of Ultimate Ancestral Techniques!

Chapter 1470: The Power of Ultimate Ancestral Techniques
!
Boom!!!! Ye Tian's Supreme Domain Body underwent a qualitative change under the tempering of a large amount of Primordial Ancestral Spring water.
The peak of the Supreme Domain Body was originally the limit of domain bodies; an Ancestor's body was no longer considered a domain body.
Originally, no treasure could temper a peak Supreme-level domain body, but with the help of the Primordial Ancestral Spring, Ye Tian was finally able to break through the peak of the Supreme-level domain body.
Crack!!!! Ye Tian's Supreme-level domain body shattered into countless fragments, but it quickly restored itself.
At this moment, he had already broken through the shackles and began to frantically absorb the energy here to push his Supreme-level domain body toward a breakthrough.
Time passed slowly, and the second transformation of Ye Tian's Supreme-level domain body was completely finished.
"Ten times!"
Ye Tian felt his brand-new Supreme-level domain body; it was ten times stronger than before.
While a ten-fold increase in the Supreme-level domain body didn't mean his overall combat power reached ten times its previous level, it had still increased by several times! At the peak stage of a Supreme-level Domain Ancestor, every bit of progress usually required endless years, and sometimes there was no progress at all.
But now, having increased his strength several times over in such a short period, it was already terrifying.
After his breakthrough, Ye Tian looked at his family again.
His son and daughter's cultivation levels were also rising very quickly, already reaching the late stage of the Supreme-level Domain Ancestor realm. Moreover, their speed of absorbing the spring's energy was faster than that of ordinary Supreme-level Domain Ancestors, as Ye Tian had bestowed upon them many Saint Talents and even Ancestral Talents.
Therefore, other Supreme-level Domain Ancestors simply couldn't compare to them.
It could be said that before the Primordial Ancestral Spring was completely depleted, they would definitely be able to break through to the peak stage of the Supreme-level Domain Ancestor realm.
In the blink of an eye, another several hundred thousand years passed.
On this day.
The Primordial Ancestral Spring was completely depleted; the spring water inside had been exhausted.
Boom boom boom!!! One after another, powerful peak Supreme-level Domain Ancestors and Supreme Soul Ancestors revealed their auras. For instance, several peak Supreme-level Domain Ancestors of the Battle Gate had also completed their second transformations at this time, their strengths greatly increased, though they were still like ants compared to Ye Tian.
As for the other Supreme-level Domain Ancestors, almost all of them had improved to the late or peak stages of the Supreme-level Domain Ancestor realm.
The same was true for the Human Race; the Supreme Soul Ancestors had all reached the late stage of the Supreme Soul Ancestor realm.
It was a pity that the energy of the Primordial Ancestral Spring was limited, and with a massive energy consumer like Ye Tian present, it wasn't possible for all the Supreme Soul Ancestors and Supreme Domain Ancestors to break through to the peak stages of their respective realms.
However, they were still very satisfied.
Because after the tempering of the Primordial Ancestral Spring, their future cultivation would be much easier, and they had full confidence in reaching the peak stages of the Supreme-level Domain Ancestor and Supreme-level Soul Ancestor realms in the future.
In the following days.
Ye Tian moved practitioners from the Profound Void Sacred Realm to the Dark Soul Domain. The Battle Gate naturally wouldn't stop him, and the other forces no longer had the heart to interfere.
Consequently, the number of humans in the Dark Soul Domain grew larger and larger.
With a massive supply of resources, the number of Invincible Domain Ancestors in the Human Race increased, but it remained very difficult to give birth to a Supreme Soul Ancestor.
This was because the initial benefits of the Dark Soul Domain were gone, and all practitioners now cultivated just as they did in the outside world.
For example, in the Dark Sacred Realm, even the descendants of Ancestors found it very difficult to become Supreme-level Domain Ancestors.
The current Dark Soul Domain was the same; it was too hard to give birth to a new Supreme Soul Ancestor.
Ye Tian didn't mind this; as long as the Human Race could produce a large number of Invincible Soul Ancestors, that was enough.
With a large number of Invincible Soul Ancestors, some would eventually break through to the Supreme Soul Ancestor realm in the future.
Meanwhile, Ye Tian himself continued his secluded cultivation, constantly using his duplicated bodies to evolve Ancestral Laws.
He prepared to start creating his own Ancestral Law, using it to charge toward the Ancestor realm.
His Ancestor clone wasn't idle either; the clone also needed to cultivate to improve its strength. Otherwise, after one hundred domain years when the Ancestors descended, they definitely wouldn't let him off.
Especially the Destruction Ancestor, who certainly wouldn't mind killing this Ancestor clone of his.
It wouldn't matter much if the Ancestor clone fell, but without its protection, the Human Race would be in trouble. Even his main body might be forced to hide within the Battle Gate.
After all, the Human Race had offended almost every force except for the Battle Gate this time by occupying the resources of the Dark Soul Domain—resources so vast that even Ancestors would be moved.
Of course.
To win over the Ancestors of the Battle Gate, Ye Tian also yielded a portion of the Dark Soul Domain's resources to them, which would allow the Battle Gate to produce a large number of Invincible Domain Ancestors and some Supreme-level Domain Ancestors.
At the very least, after one hundred domain years, the two Ancestors of the Battle Gate would definitely help him.
...."It is very difficult for an Ancestor to improve their strength. Although the Dark Soul Domain has produced resources useful even to Ancestors, the resources that will truly cause Ancestors to fight to the death will only appear after one hundred domain years..."
Ye Tian thought to himself.
Therefore, he had to find a way to improve the strength of his Ancestor clone.
He had communicated with the two Ancestors of the Battle Gate. For an Ancestor to improve their strength, they mainly needed to increase their Ancestral Power, strengthen their Ancestor Body, and bolster their Ancestor Soul.
This was similar to Domain Ancestors—it was simply... an increase in cultivation.
Ancestors didn't have specific realm divisions, only combat power classifications.
Ordinary Ancestors, Elite Ancestors, and Top-tier Ancestors.
Most Ancestors were Ordinary Ancestors; even the Battle Ancestor was an Ordinary Ancestor, while the Realm Ancestor was a powerful Elite Ancestor, second only to the Top-tier Ancestors.
Improving cultivation required time... but there was another way to significantly increase strength, and that was to master an Ultimate Ancestral Technique!
However, no more than five Ancestors had mastered an Ultimate Ancestral Technique. Of course, this was public information; if any Ancestor had hidden their strength, others would have no way of knowing.
The Realm Ancestor mastered one Ultimate Ancestral Technique. The Saint Ancestor, the Destruction Ancestor, the Eternal Sect Leader, and the Space-Time Ancestor—these five Ancestors each mastered an Ultimate Ancestral Technique.
It was precisely because of these Ultimate Ancestral Techniques that they were so powerful.
If Ye Tian could master an Ultimate Ancestral Technique, even if his Ancestor cultivation was lower, he would immediately possess the combat power of a weaker Elite Ancestor.
By then, with a slight increase in his Ancestor cultivation and by wielding a portion of the Dark Soul Domain's power, he would definitely be confident in fighting the Destruction Ancestor.

Chapter 1471: The First Ultimate Ancestral Technique—Ultimate..

Chapter 1471: The First Ultimate Ancestral Technique
—Ultimate Ancestral Armor!
"Ultimate Ancestral Techniques are... very difficult for other Ancestors to master, but for me, although it is also difficult, the hope is very high!"
Ye Tian thought to himself.
This was because he possessed several Ultimate Ancestral Talents, all of which were formed by copying the ancestral talents of the Nirvana Clan and continuously merging them.
Currently, he possessed five major Ultimate Ancestral Talents: the Ultimate Strength Ancestral Talent, the Ultimate Defense Ancestral Talent, the Ultimate Speed Ancestral Talent, the Ultimate Nirvana Ancestral Talent, and the Ultimate Time Ancestral Talent.
Therefore, he had hope of mastering these five types of Ultimate Ancestral Techniques, and the difficulty was at least a thousand or ten thousand times lower than for other Ancestors.
Of course, Ye Tian could not place all his hopes on Ultimate Ancestral Techniques. What if one hundred domain years was not enough? Therefore, he also had to increase his cultivation.
"Increasing an Ancestor's cultivation is not easy; one must rely on Nirvana treasures!"
Ye Tian thought.
Now that the human race controlled the Dark Soul Domain, if he created a large area of Nirvana Spacetime and used many high-level resources to evolve it, he could produce more Nirvana resources. He could then give them all to his clone, Ancestor Qing Ye, to increase the clone's cultivation.
One hundred domain years would be enough for Ancestor Qing Ye's cultivation to surge, and his strength would very likely reach the Elite Domain Ancestor realm. If he mastered an Ultimate Ancestral Technique, his combat power would soar to rival that of a World Ancestor.
Only then could he use the power of the Dark Soul Domain to contend with top Ancestors like the Holy Ancestor and the Destruction Ancestor.
On this day.
Ye Tian used his Ultimate-level Nirvana Ancestral Talent to begin creating a Nirvana Spacetime. Such a Nirvana Spacetime was larger than previous ones and more likely to give birth to high-quality Nirvana treasures.
After all, even the Nirvana Clan did not possess a Nirvana Ancestral Talent at the Ultimate level! Both the clone Ancestor Qing Ye and Ye Tian's main body worked hard to manage this Nirvana Spacetime. The main body's task was to... deduce Ancestral Laws and Ultimate Ancestral Techniques, while the clone Ancestor Qing Ye's task was to... refine Nirvana treasures and increase cultivation.
As the long years passed, the human population in the Dark Soul Domain saw a terrifying increase. The humans born later were considered native residents of the Dark Soul Domain and received its recognition.
With ample resources and almost exclusive control over a Dark Holy Land, the human race's strength had long since surpassed that of ordinary Holy Sects.
Under these circumstances, various Holy Land-level forces emerged within the human race.
Of course, the most powerful force was the Human Race Temple; any human force had to be under the Temple's jurisdiction.
Even those Supreme Domain Ancestors, if they established their own forces, had to register their names with the Temple.
These Supreme Domain Ancestors were almost all nurtured by Ye Tian, so naturally, they did not dare to have any ulterior motives.
One domain year quickly passed.
For... many humans, this was a long period of time, yet in such a long time, the human race only gained three more Supreme Domain Ancestors.
To Ye Tian, this was not a fast speed, but for those Holy Sects, gaining three Supreme Domain Ancestors in one domain year was incredibly fast. If that speed could be maintained, how terrifying would that be! But later on, it might not even be possible to birth a single Supreme Domain Ancestor in a domain year.
This was not just a limitation of a race's providence, but also a limitation of a Dark Holy Land.
In one domain year, Ye Tian refined a massive amount of Nirvana treasures. If given to Supreme Domain Ancestors capable of refining them, they could have created hundreds of peak Supreme Domain Ancestors.
Yet so many Nirvana treasures only increased Ancestor Qing Ye's strength several times over, and the further he progressed, the slower the improvement became.
"Fortunately, the quality of the treasures and resources recently born in the Dark Soul Domain has become higher, so the Nirvana treasures nurtured in the future will also be of higher quality.
Moreover, the longer the Nirvana Spacetime is managed, the higher the quality of the Nirvana treasures born will be.
And the Nirvana Spacetime here is different from the one at the edge of the Dark Forbidden Zone back then. The Nirvana Spacetime there had a large number of Nirvana Clan members, and with the Ancestors 'harvesting' them, the Nirvana energy there could not grow.
But I am constantly pouring in resources, so the Nirvana energy is constantly skyrocketing.
At this rate, I can definitely nurture top-tier Nirvana treasures, and in large quantities.
In one hundred domain years, I can definitely stack my cultivation and strength to the Elite Domain Ancestor level!"
Ye Tian said with full confidence.
However, after such a long time, Ye Tian still had not pushed a single Ancestral Technique to the Ultimate level, though he had found some leads.
Furthermore, Ye Tian had also made some progress in creating his own Ancestral Laws, but it was only a lead and required a longer time to create and deduce.
Two domain years passed! Three domain years passed! Ten domain years passed! Unknowingly, eighteen domain years had passed in the Dark Soul Domain.
On this day, Ye Tian let out a great laugh, his voice spreading throughout the entire Primordial Ancestral World.
The reason he was so excited was that he had finally created an Ultimate Ancestral Technique.
This technique was deduced based on the Ancestral Armor. After eighteen domain years of deduction and countless instances of his duplicate bodies shattering, he finally evolved the Ultimate Ancestral Technique—Ultimate Ancestral Armor!
"I possess the Ultimate Strength Ancestral Talent at the Ultimate level, and I repeatedly used the Holy Soul of my duplicate bodies to deduce and evolve, exhausting the power of the Holy Soul countless times. It took eighteen domain years to deduce an Ultimate Ancestral Technique. If the Destruction Ancestor, the Holy Ancestor, and the World Ancestor do not have great opportunities, they probably wouldn't be able to create an Ultimate Ancestral Technique even in a hundred thousand or a million domain years.
And the Dark Holy Territory seems to have only existed for several hundred thousand domain years, yet they actually mastered Ultimate Ancestral Techniques. They must have encountered a great opportunity beyond my imagination!"
Ye Tian speculated.
However, he did not bother guessing the great opportunities of the Holy Ancestor and the Destruction Ancestor; in short, no matter how great the opportunity, it could not be greater than the talent of copying.
Now that he had created the Ultimate Ancestral Armor, his defense alone had reached a terrifying level. Except for the Holy Ancestor and the Destruction Ancestor, other Ancestors could not harm him in the slightest. If he borrowed the power of the Dark Soul Domain, even the Holy Ancestor and the Destruction Ancestor would be unable to kill him.
"In the Dark Soul Domain, the Holy Ancestor and the Destruction Ancestor cannot kill me, but they can kill the human race. I must also master an offensive Ultimate Ancestral Technique!"
Ye Tian thought to himself.
Thus, he began to research a Strength-type Ultimate Ancestral Technique.
Once he created an offensive Strength-type Ultimate Ancestral Technique, with the amplification of the Dark Soul Domain, his combat power would soar to a level comparable to the Destruction Ancestor and the Holy Ancestor. Even if he were slightly weaker, he wouldn't be much weaker.

Chapter 1472: Creating One Ancestral Method After Another!

Chapter 1472: Creating One Ancestral Method After Another
!
Ye Tian chose the Tyrant Strength Ancestral Technique from among his ancestral techniques as the subject of his research and deduction, striving to deduce the Tyrant Strength Ultimate Ancestral Technique.
After all, he had already successfully created one Ultimate Ancestral Technique and gained experience; thus, while researching a second one remained difficult, it would at least save some time.
Thus, over the following domain years, Ye Tian spent most of his time on creating the Tyrant Strength Ultimate Ancestral Technique.
As for the affairs of the human race, he almost completely ignored them, leaving them to be managed by the various Supreme-level Soul Ancestors and Supreme-level Domain Ancestors of the Temple.
In this way, seventeen domain years passed.
On this day.
Ye Tian finally created the Tyrant Strength Ultimate Ancestral Technique, and his strength soared.
Next, Ye Tian spent another dozen or so domain years creating a speed-type Ultimate Ancestral Technique—the Streamer Ultimate Ancestral Technique! Defense, speed, and strength—with all three of these Ultimate Ancestral Techniques created, it could be said that Ye Tian's strength had exploded, and he had no weaknesses.
Coupled with the continuous refining of massive amounts of Nirvana treasures over dozens of domain years, his cultivation had increased significantly.
Consequently, Ye Tian's current strength had already reached the level of an extremely powerful Elite Domain Ancestor; this was a perception and realization he had as an Ancestor, requiring no combat test.
If he utilized the power of the Dark Soul Domain, Ye Tian would absolutely not fear the Holy Ancestor or the Destruction Ancestor.
"Finally, I no longer need to worry about the Destruction Ancestor and the Holy Ancestor! With dozens of domain years remaining, it will be difficult for my clone, the Green Leaf Ancestor, to increase its strength further; it likely won't reach the level of a Top-tier Ancestor. Next, I will focus on comprehending and creating Ancestral Methods!"
Ye Tian decided.
Over dozens of domain years, Ye Tian's main body still hadn't created its Ancestral Method. Had he only wanted to create an ordinary Ancestral Method, he would have done so long ago, but the Ancestral Method he wanted to create was the Endless Ancestral Method, which encompassed all Ancestral Daos.
Although he clearly had significant insights and had even found the right path, he was still just one step away, unable to fully bring it into existence.
Another domain year passed, and Ye Tian's progress stalled.
"This won't do. No progress at all over such a long period—even if I'm only one step away, I must have taken the wrong direction in my comprehension!"
Ye Tian thought to himself.
The Endless Ancestral Method couldn't truly contain every single Ancestral Method. Theoretically, Ancestral Methods were infinite, so he had to use basic Ancestral Methods as a foundation to continuously evolve various Ancestral Methods, eventually forming the Endless Ancestral Method.
Creating the Endless Ancestral Method all at once was too difficult; he could first create individual basic Ancestral Methods and then fuse them to fully realize the Endless Ancestral Method.
Furthermore, creating these basic Ancestral Methods would allow some of the human race's peak Supreme-level Domain Ancestors or Soul Ancestors to fuse with them and become Ancestors themselves.
This way, the human race would give birth to a large number of Ancestors!
However, even with these cultivation methods, fusion would be difficult and might not be suitable for everyone, requiring an endless amount of time.
Moreover, others didn't have his ability to use Deduction infinitely or to shatter cloned bodies repeatedly; for others, shattering their body once meant death.
Thus, his path could not be replicated by others.
However, having a complete Ancestral Method provided an opportunity; one day, they would eventually become Ancestors.
"Let's start with the Gold Ancestral Method!"
Ye Tian decided.
His understanding of Ancestral Methods was already incredibly profound, even surpassing those of the Ancestors themselves.
Many Ancestors had obtained Ancestral Methods by chance and became Ancestors after fusing with them; while some had created their own, they were generally mediocre Ancestral Methods.
The most impressive was the Spacetime Ancestor, who had created the Spacetime Ancestral Method and thus had high potential; however, due to a short cultivation time, he couldn't surpass the Destruction Ancestor.
But if the Spacetime Ancestor were given endless ages to cultivate, he truly would surpass the Destruction Ancestor and become the number one Ancestor of the Destruction Holy Realm.
Yet, compared to the Endless Ancestral Method Ye Tian would create in the future, the Spacetime Ancestor's Spacetime Ancestral Method was only average.
Furthermore, Ye Tian's foundation was far beyond what the Spacetime Ancestor could compare to.
Three domain years later, Ye Tian was incredibly excited.
At this moment, he had already created a Gold Ancestral Method; although it was based on his own creation, others could also comprehend and cultivate it.
If this Gold Ancestral Method were broken into pieces, it could even allow the human race to give birth to several Half-step Ancestors.
Of course, Half-step Ancestors were of no use to the human race; if they were to achieve anything, they should become full Ancestors.
However, a single Gold Ancestral Method could only allow one peak Supreme-level Domain Ancestor or Soul Ancestor to become an Ancestor.
Next, every few domain years, Ye Tian was able to create another Ancestral Method.
Wood Ancestral Method, Water Ancestral Method, Fire Ancestral Method, Earth Ancestral Method, Light Ancestral Method, Dark Ancestral Method... one Ancestral Method after another was created by Ye Tian. If other Ancestors knew of this, they would surely be dumbfounded and find it unbelievable.
Even top-tier Ancestors like the Destruction Ancestor and the Holy Ancestor would be unable to create other Ancestral Methods if asked.
The Destruction Ancestor followed the path of the Destruction Ancestor; the Ancestral Method he created was the Destruction Ancestral Method. If he were asked to create a Gold Ancestral Method, he would be completely bewildered, as he simply didn't understand it.
Only Ye Tian, who followed the Endless Dao, could create so many Ancestral Methods.
Furthermore, since the Destruction Ancestor had already created one Destruction Ancestral Method, he couldn't continue to create a second one; if he tried, he would unconsciously end up back on the same Ancestral Method path.
Because of this, the Destruction Ancestor also had no way to help other Supreme-level Domain Ancestors become Ancestors.
Others who wanted to become Ancestors could only rely on themselves, not on an Ancestor.
Otherwise, many Holy Sects wouldn't have only one or two Ancestors.
But Ye Tian was too monstrous; having created so many Ancestral Methods now, it was enough to allow the human race to produce Ancestors one after another.
"Only the Space Ancestral Method and Time Ancestral Method are left!"
Ye Tian murmured.
Although he possessed a Space Ancestral Method, it belonged to someone else.
To create his own Space Ancestral Method without being influenced by the Space Ancestral Method of his clone, the Green Leaf Ancestor, Ye Tian's main body directly blocked its connection with the clone and erased the memory of that Space Ancestral Method from its mind before beginning the creation process.
Otherwise, once influenced, the creation of the Space Ancestral Method would not be successful.

Chapter 1473: Family Members Begin Choosing Ancestor Laws!

Chapter 1473: Family Members Begin Choosing Ancestor Laws
! [Requesting Subscription]
Creating a Space Ancestor Law was naturally much more difficult than creating other Ancestor Laws.
However, Ye Tian still had plenty of time, so he wasn't worried about running out...
In any case... his clone, Ancestor Qing Ye, had already grown to a level where he could rival the Destruction Ancestor, so there was no need to worry about safety.
In the years that followed, Ye Tian devoted himself wholeheartedly to creating the Space Ancestor Law.
One domain year! Two domain years! Three domain years! ...Unknowingly, thirteen domain years passed.
On this day, Ye Tian finally created the Space Ancestor Law.
Moreover, the Space Ancestor Law he created was much better than the one he had obtained from the Void Ancestor.
If one were to become an Ancestor using his Space Ancestor Law, they would definitely become a powerful Space Ancestor.
"Only the Time Ancestor Law is left. I'll continue creating!"
Ye Tian thought to himself.
It took Ye Tian thirteen domain years to create the Space Ancestor Law, and the Time Ancestor Law was even more terrifying than the Space Ancestor Law, making it even more difficult.
This time, it took Ye Tian a full eighteen domain years to finally create the Time Ancestor Law.
At this point, all the basic Ancestor Laws had been created.
Next, Ye Tian needed to fuse these basic Ancestor Laws into the Endless Ancestor Law.
This step was also very difficult and would likely take a very long time, but at least there was a clear direction, so he wouldn't fall into a bottleneck that couldn't be broken.
"Before going into seclusion, I need to pass these Ancestor Laws to Yue'er, Xingchen, and the others!"
Ye Tian thought.
His wife, son, daughter, and sister were all at the peak of the Supreme-level Domain Ancestor realm. Their cultivation could no longer progress; they could only continue to improve by practicing Ancestor Techniques and tempering their Ancestor Bodies.
They also needed to fuse an Ancestor Law to break through to the Ancestor realm. With their own comprehension and talent, it wasn't impossible for them to create their own Ancestor Laws, but the hope was slim. Even if they could truly create one, it would take an endless amount of time.
Instead of that, it was better to fuse his Ancestor Laws. In the future, they would still have the hope of growing to the Elite Ancestor realm.
Therefore, Ye Tian wanted to pass these Ancestor Laws to them.
"Yue'er, Xingchen, Xingyue, Xiao Yu, come here for a moment!"
Ye Tian sent a divine sense transmission to them.
*Whoosh! Whoosh! Whoosh!* Xiao Yue, Ye Xingchen, Ye Xingyue, and Ye Yu all tore through space and arrived before Ye Tian.
"Husband!"
"Father!"
"Brother!"
The four of them called out one by one.
Ye Tian looked at the four of them and said, "I have created some Ancestor Laws, all of which are top-tier. I want to ask for your opinions.
Will you choose to fuse with the Ancestor Laws I created to become Ancestors, or will you choose to create your own?"
"Some Ancestor Laws?"
The four of them widened their eyes, revealing looks of disbelief.
How precious were Ancestor Laws? In the Dark Forbidden Territory, countless monstrous geniuses were unable to create their own Ancestor Laws, and many couldn't even obtain a complete, masterless Ancestor Law, thus remaining unable to promote to the Ancestor realm for their entire lives.
Even some broken Ancestor Laws became treasures that many peak Supreme-level Domain Ancestors fought over, hoping to use such broken laws to become Half-step Ancestors.
Complete Ancestor Laws could no longer be created even by Ancestors. Therefore, if a complete, masterless Ancestor Law appeared, even Ancestors would fight and kill for it to secure a chance for their descendants to become Ancestors.
There were very few Ancestors in the Dark Forbidden Territory simply because Ancestor Laws were too rare and too difficult to create.
But now, Ye Tian said... he had created some Ancestor Laws, clearly more than one.
If these words were to spread, it would definitely cause a massive shock throughout the entire Dark Forbidden Territory, and all the Ancestors would have their eyes on Ye Tian.
"Husband, I choose to fuse with the Ancestor Law you created!"
Xiao Yue made her choice.
She had no confidence in herself. Other peak Supreme-level Domain Ancestors were unable to create Ancestor Laws, and she had always relied on Ye Tian to grow to this level. Where would she find the potential to create an Ancestor Law of her own? Therefore, being able to obtain an Ancestor Law that suited her was already excellent; she couldn't ask for more.
"Good. Choose one of these Ancestor Laws to fuse with. Ancestor Laws are very dominant; as long as you can successfully fuse with one, it will forcibly shift the path of your cultivation. Therefore, it doesn't matter much whether it perfectly suits you; the impact won't be that great.
Of course, it's naturally not as good as an Ancestor Law that perfectly suits you!"
Ye Tian said.
*Whoosh! Whoosh! Whoosh!* One Ancestor Law inheritance after another appeared before Xiao Yue.
Xiao Yue examined these Ancestor Laws and finally made a decision: "Husband, I choose the Light Ancestor Law!"
"Good, this Light Ancestor Law is yours, Yue'er!"
Ye Tian fused the Light Ancestor Law into Xiao Yue's soul. Once Xiao Yue fused with the Light Ancestor Law, even if others obtained this Light Ancestor Law in the future, they would not be able to become an Ancestor with it; they could only use it to comprehend Light-type Saint Techniques and Ancestor Techniques.
Ye Yu, Ye Xingchen, and Ye Xingyue also chose to fuse with Ancestor Laws instead of creating their own.
They also felt that the hope of self-creation was slim, so they didn't want to waste time.
Besides, they never dared to imagine becoming Ancestors before; being able to become Supreme-level Domain Ancestors was already satisfying, so they didn't have high demands.
"It's your turn, Xiao Yu!"
Ye Tian let Ye Yu pick second.
As for the two juniors, Ye Xingchen and Ye Xingyue, they would naturally pick third and fourth; the two of them certainly had no objections.
Ye Yu chose the Ice Ancestor Law without hesitation: "Brother, I choose the Ice Ancestor Law!"
Ye Tian nodded and fused the Ice Ancestor Law into Ye Yu's soul.
Subsequently, it was Ye Xingchen's turn.
Ye Xingchen pondered for a moment and finally chose the extremely powerful Space Ancestor Law.
In this way, after he became an Ancestor, his strength would be greater than that of ordinary Ancestors.
Ye Xingyue was not to be outdone and chose the Time Ancestor Law. It happened to be on the same level as her brother Ye Xingchen's choice, and since Time and Space were related and they were siblings, it was perfectly suitable.
Of course.
If they wanted to completely master the Time Ancestor Law and the Space Ancestor Law, it would likely take a very long time, but eventually, there would come a day when they could comprehend them thoroughly and become Ancestors.
Ye Tian's family had chosen their Ancestor Laws. As for the other Ancestor Laws, he would not give them to others for the time being, unless someone truly met his requirements; only then would he bestow these Ancestor Laws.
"It's time to continue my seclusion, fuse these Ancestor Laws, and create my own Endless Ancestor Law!"
Ye Tian entered the cultivation room and continued his seclusion to create.

Chapter 1474: The Endless Ancestor Method, Success in Creation!

Chapter 1474: The Endless Ancestor Method, Success in Creation
! [Requesting Subscriptions]
While Ye Tian's main body was in seclusion creating the Endless Ancestor Method, the progress of his clone, Qingye Ancestor, began to slow down.
After all, the Qingye Ancestor clone was raised by Ye Tian for the sake of speed; it couldn't compare to the foundation of his main body. Its potential was far inferior. Furthermore, the Qingye Ancestor clone had integrated the Space Ancestor Method of the Void Ancestor.
Back then, to pursue a rapid promotion to Ancestor, he naturally couldn't consider too much, nor did he have the time to slowly create an Ancestor Method. Otherwise, if someone else had been the first to promote to Ancestor, they might have targeted the Human Race or even his main body.
If that had happened, the Human Race wouldn't have its current prosperity.
Since he didn't promote through a self-created Ancestor Method, Qingye Ancestor's potential was limited and was now nearing its limit. Unless he obtained a better opportunity, he couldn't break through that limit.
And those Nirvana treasures could only increase cultivation; they couldn't help the Qingye Ancestor clone break its limits.
"The Qingye Ancestor clone is currently estimated to only reach the level of a powerful Elite Ancestor, second only to a Top Ancestor. Only by relying on the Dark Soul Domain can it contend with a Top Ancestor.
In the future, no matter how many Nirvana treasures are refined, the increase in strength will be limited!"
Ye Tian muttered.
Of course, the Qingye Ancestor clone could still progress, just many times slower than before, so he looked down on it a bit.
If other Ancestors knew of Ye Tian's progress speed, they would likely be incredibly jealous.
The progress speed Ye Tian looked down upon was something even Top Ancestors like the Saint Ancestor and Destruction Ancestor would envy.
....Domain year after domain year passed.
While the eyes of many Ancestors and factions were focused on the Dark Soul Domain, almost no one cared about a place like the Xuanxu Holy Realm.
Even if something happened here, no one would care.
One of Ye Tian's incarnations had been stationed in the Xuanxu Holy Realm, monitoring its changes at all times.
By now, the Xuanxu Holy Realm was many times larger than in the past. It had even birthed many rare resources and holy items, as well as treasures that only appeared in Ancestral Realms.
Additionally, the Celestial Realm within the Xuanxu Holy Realm had produced a large number of treasures. The Star Forbidden Tree had once again borne Star Forbidden Fruits, enough for many Invincible Domain Ancestors of the Human Race to temper their Invincible Domain Bodies to the extreme.
Although compared to the Dark Soul Domain, the resources of the Xuanxu Holy Realm were low-end and far inferior.
However, the potential here was very high, not lower than the Dark Soul Domain. In the future, it even hoped to become the fourth Dark Holy Land.
"The Xuanxu Holy Realm is about to become an Ancestral Realm. However, I can't let it become one yet, or it will surely attract the attention of the Ancestors.
My main body and Ancestor clone are both guarding the Dark Soul Domain. I can't manage the Xuanxu Holy Realm for now. I must suppress its promotion!"
Ye Tian thought.
He planned to wait until his main body created the Endless Ancestor Method and promoted to Ancestor before letting the Xuanxu Holy Realm evolve into an Ancestral Realm.
That way, he could withstand the prying eyes of other Ancestors. He could even explain that he obtained a treasure from the Dark Soul Domain that allowed the Xuanxu Holy Realm to promote. This would shift the Ancestors' attention to the Dark Soul Domain instead of the secrets of the Xuanxu Holy Realm.
On this day.
Something happened to the Human Race.
An Invincible Domain Ancestor promoted to the Supreme Level Domain Ancestor realm in the Xuanxu Holy Realm.
Consequently, many Invincible Domain Ancestors who couldn't promote in the Dark Soul Domain and felt it wasn't suitable for their cultivation returned to the Xuanxu Holy Realm one by one.
Gradually, the Dark Soul Domain was almost entirely populated by Human Soul Ancestors, while the Domain Ancestors returned to the Xuanxu Holy Realm.
Unknowingly, the 100-domain-year mark since the birth of the Dark Soul Domain was approaching. The Ancestors of various factions were becoming restless.
War Ancestor Realm.
The two Ancestors of the War Gate had also returned long ago, leaving only incarnations outside the Dark Soul Domain.
At this moment, the War Ancestor and Realm Ancestor were chatting with one of Ye Tian's incarnations.
"Myriad Law War Ancestor, the 100-domain-year mark is coming soon. The Destruction Ancestor will likely move against your Human Race's Qingye Ancestor. Give me the truth—how is Qingye Ancestor's strength now? With the help of part of the Dark Soul Domain's power, is there... hope of resisting the Destruction Ancestor? If not, we must give up territory in the Dark Soul Domain and join forces with the various Holy Gates of the Dark Holy Territory to resist the Ancestors of the Dark Destruction Domain.
As long as the benefits are large enough, they will still ally with us."
Ye Tian smiled and said, "War Ancestor, Realm Ancestor, rest assured. Qingye Ancestor's strength has reached the peak of the Elite Ancestor level, second only to Top Ancestors. With the boost from the Dark Soul Domain, he can definitely exert the combat power of a Top Ancestor. Blocking the Destruction Ancestor is no problem! However, even so, we must give up some territory, otherwise we won't be able to block all the Ancestors!"
Ye Tian never thought about ruling the entire Dark Soul Domain completely, but occupying the best area was no problem. Giving up other areas to other Holy Gates and the Ancestors of the Dark Destruction Domain wasn't a big issue either.
"That's good then!"
The War Ancestor and Realm Ancestor nodded slightly.
Although it was abnormal for Qingye Ancestor's strength to increase so quickly, they weren't surprised. After all, since Qingye Ancestor could promote to Ancestor in such a short time, having such strength was normal! Back then, the Saint Ancestor was the same.
However, they never imagined that Qingye Ancestor was actually Ye Tian's clone.
Ye Tian didn't reveal a thing, otherwise some secrets would be leaked.
Dark Soul Domain.
Ye Tian was at a critical moment; he was about to create the Endless Ancestor Method.
More years passed.
On this day.
Countless flashes of inspiration appeared in Ye Tian's mind. The essences of various Ancestor Methods merged together. Combined with dozens of domain years of comprehension and research, these insights finally fused into one.
The Endless Ancestor Method was finally created.
Boom!!!! Deep in his soul, Ancestor Method characters merged into a sphere, and endless Ancestor mysteries permeated out.
This sphere was... the inheritance of the Endless Ancestor Method, officially manifesting now.
The creation of the Endless Ancestor Method wasn't completely finalized yet; it was still evolving, manifesting many Ancestor mysteries, eventually evolving into three thousand Ancestor Method mysteries, and even more—infinite Ancestor Method mysteries.
It was like a collection of countless Ancestor Methods.
This was the true Endless Ancestor Method! This evolution lasted for trillions of years before finally completing, turning into the most perfect Endless Ancestor Method.
Now that the Endless Ancestor Method was created, Ye Tian only needed to fully comprehend and integrate it to become an Ancestor.
Since Ye Tian created the Endless Ancestor Method himself, even though it had evolved into a more perfect form, he could still quickly comprehend it and easily integrate it.
Therefore, it wouldn't be long before he could become an Ancestor! Read the version without underlines, please download Shitou Novels.

Chapter 1475: Condensing the Endless Ancestor Body, The Main Body Finally Becomes an Endless Ancestor

Chapter 1475: Condensing the Endless Ancestor Body, The Main Body Finally Becomes an Endless Ancestor
!
Outside the Dark Soul Domain.
One Ancestor after another emerged. These Ancestors were not... incarnations, but their true bodies descending here.
This was because in another few tens of thousands of years, the Dark Soul Domain would have existed for a hundred domain years.
At that time, the Dark Soul Domain would no longer restrict Ancestors from entering.
Furthermore, at that time, a second Ancestral World would be born within the Dark Soul Domain, and the Ancestral World would also produce more rare resources, even resources that were of great use to the Ancestors themselves.
The Ancestors didn't care about the previous resources, as those were of little help to them, but now it was different. What they were waiting for was... today.
For these opportunities and the territory of the Dark Soul Domain, they would even slaughter one another.
At this moment.
The Destruction Ancestor radiated an extremely dense aura of destruction, and the faintly revealed killing intent made many Ancestors tremble with fear.
At this time, various Ancestors were communicating in secret.
"The human race's Green Leaf Ancestor is likely finished. In a mere hundred domain years, how much could he possibly grow? Back then, the Dark Soul Domain was able to survive the crisis because the Destruction Ancestor was only an Elite Ancestor, but now the Destruction Ancestor possesses Top-tier Ancestor combat power. Green Leaf Ancestor still hasn't fully mastered the power of the Dark Soul Domain; at most, he can exert the combat power of an ordinary Elite Ancestor.
Once the Destruction Ancestor makes a move against Green Leaf Ancestor, I'm afraid Green Leaf Ancestor won't survive!"
"Who told Green Leaf Ancestor to dare kill a Supreme-level Domain Ancestor of the Destruction Saint Clan who was about to promote to Ancestor? Naturally, he enraged the Destruction Ancestor, the Space-Time Ancestor, and the others!"
"A Supreme-level Domain Ancestor of the All-Things Saint Sect who was about to promote to Ancestor also died at the hands of Green Leaf Ancestor. The All-Things Ancestor will likely make a move against Green Leaf Ancestor as well, right?"
"The All-Things Ancestor is merely an ordinary Ancestor and probably isn't a match for Green Leaf Ancestor, but he will definitely target the human race where Green Leaf Ancestor resides. For example, the human race's Myriad Law War Ancestor definitely has hope of promoting to Ancestor, and his combat power is terrifying. Perhaps the All-Things Ancestor will seek revenge by killing the Myriad Law War Ancestor."
"It's not very realistic for the All-Things Ancestor to want to kill the Myriad Law War Ancestor. The War Ancestor and the Domain Ancestor won't just stand by; they will definitely stop him!"
"They might not be able to stop him. Once they enter the Dark Soul Domain and many Ancestors engage in battle, in such a chaotic situation, anything could happen!"
....Time passed slowly, and the day for the Ancestors to enter the Dark Soul Domain drew closer and closer.
In the past, hundreds of millions of years were just the time for a nap to these Ancestors, but now, a mere ten thousand years seemed incredibly long.
On this day.
Abruptly.
The Dark Soul Domain shook. Someone was charging toward the Ancestor realm, and the commotion was incredibly massive, many times greater than when Green Leaf Ancestor broke through to the Ancestor realm.
"Who? Who is charging toward the Ancestor realm?"
One Ancestor after another was shocked.
At this critical juncture, someone was suddenly striking for the Ancestor realm; it was too strange.
"It's the human race's Myriad Law War Ancestor. No need to guess, he is the only one in the Dark Soul Domain qualified to strike for the Ancestor realm and capable of creating such a terrifying commotion!"
One Ancestor spoke up.
"There are only a few thousand years left before we enter the Dark Soul Domain. For the Myriad Law War Ancestor to break through now, he probably won't be able to fully enter the Ancestor realm. Isn't he afraid of his breakthrough process being interrupted?"
An Ancestor asked curiously.
Indeed, for a Supreme-level Domain Ancestor to charge into the Ancestor realm, without a million years, it was impossible to thoroughly break through.
Moreover, ordinary time formations simply couldn't withstand the aura of an Ancestor; it was impossible to break through inside a time formation.
A mere few thousand years was simply not enough time.
However, they had overlooked the existence of the Green Leaf Ancestor.
BOOM!!!! Green Leaf Ancestor mobilized the power of the Dark Soul Domain and began to accelerate time in the area where Ye Tian was in seclusion.
10,000 times! 100,000 times! Accelerating time by ten thousand times for Ye Tian, who was currently breaking through, and frantically mobilizing the energy of the Dark Soul Domain to assist Ye Tian's breakthrough came at a great cost.
At this moment, Green Leaf Ancestor's energy was being continuously consumed. To restore energy, massive amounts of Nirvana Treasures were being consumed and refined by Ye Tian.
Outside the Dark Soul Domain.
The Ancestors were all stunned; they also sensed Green Leaf Ancestor's actions.
"He actually accelerated the time of the Dark Soul Domain to fully assist the Myriad Law Domain Ancestor's breakthrough. Isn't he afraid that after a few thousand years, his state will be unstable?"
An Ancestor said in surprise.
While the many Ancestors were surprised, the Destruction Ancestor opened his eyes and looked toward the Dark Soul Domain.
"Hmph, Myriad Law War Ancestor, no matter how monstrous your talent or how deep your foundation, at most your combat power will rival an Elite Ancestor upon breakthrough. But the Myriad Law Domain Ancestor isn't the first person to break through to Ancestor in the Dark Soul Domain, so he can't borrow the power of the Dark Soul Domain. Thus, his combat power will only be that of an ordinary Elite Ancestor, nothing to fear!"
The Destruction Ancestor thought to himself.
However, he had underestimated Ye Tian.
Ye Tian not only had an incredibly deep foundation and had completed a second transformation at the Supreme-level Domain Ancestor level, but he also mastered several Ultimate Ancestral Techniques. His combat power was not... only that of an ordinary Elite Ancestor as they imagined.
In the blink of an eye, several hundred years passed in the outside world, but under the time acceleration, Ye Tian had spent a full several million years breaking through.
Finally, on this day, Ye Tian completely finished his breakthrough, condensed the Endless Ancestor Body, and stepped into the Ancestor realm.
Upon breaking through to the Ancestor realm, Ye Tian's strength increased by an unknown number of times. Furthermore, the Endless Ancestor Body far surpassed other Ancestor bodies, and could be called truly immortal and indestructible.
Although he didn't have time to refine that large amount of Nirvana Treasures now and couldn't rapidly increase his cultivation level.
But he did possess Ultimate Ancestral Techniques, and once he broke through to the Ancestor realm, he could fully exert the power of those Ultimate Ancestral Techniques. His combat power was even stronger than Green Leaf Ancestor borrowing the power of the Dark Soul Domain.
According to Ye Tian's estimation, his current strength was likely infinitely close to Top-tier Ancestor combat power.
Moreover, relying on the Endless Ancestor Body, even a Top-tier Ancestor couldn't kill him.
If given enough time, he could easily step into the Top-tier Ancestor combat power level.
At this time, with a few thousand years remaining in the outside world, Ye Tian had his clone, Green Leaf Ancestor, continue to accelerate time in this area. He began to frantically refine those Nirvana Treasures, striving to increase his cultivation a bit more.
BOOM BOOM BOOM!!!! Countless Nirvana Treasures were swallowed and refined by Ye Tian, and his cultivation rose bit by bit.
Unfortunately, no matter how much he practiced, he could only train for a few tens of millions of years more. He couldn't increase his strength too much; increasing it by thirty percent was already good, making him even closer to Top-tier Ancestor combat power.
But that was enough! When there were only a hundred years left, Ye Tian controlled his clone, Green Leaf Ancestor, to stop the time acceleration and instead refined a large number of Nirvana Treasures to recover his state.
Additionally, Ye Tian destroyed the Nirvana Time-Space; at the very least, he couldn't let... other Ancestors know about it, waiting to slowly cultivate the Nirvana Time-Space again in the future.
Soon, a hundred years passed.
The Ancestors were about to descend upon the Dark Soul Domain.

Chapter 1476: Battle of the Ancestors, Innate Ancestral Artifact!

Chapter 1476: Battle of the Ancestors, Innate Ancestral Artifact
!
Rumble!!! Somewhere in the Dark Soul Domain, an Ancestral Realm was slowly being nurtured. At the same time, the Primordial Ancestral Realm was also undergoing a transformation, giving birth to a large number of treasures.
Ye Tian and his clone, the Qing Ye Ancestor, were both in the Primordial Ancestral Realm, so they immediately collected the resources that were born. These resources were useful even to Ancestors.
It was here that the Dark Soul Domain's resistance toward Ancestors vanished.
Swish! Swish! Swish! One Ancestor after another descended upon the Dark Soul Domain. They did not go to the second Ancestral Realm, as it would take some time for that one to be fully born; their target was the Primordial Ancestral Realm.
At this moment, the Primordial Ancestral Realm was birthing a large number of treasures every second. For the Ancestors, seizing even a few of these treasures was a massive gain.
In an instant, the Ancestors descended upon the Primordial Ancestral Realm.
Some Ancestors went searching for resources, while others sought out the Qing Ye Ancestor.
"Qing Ye Ancestor, die!"
The Destruction Ancestor made his move against the Qing Ye Ancestor.
The World Ancestor wanted to help but was directly blocked by another Ancestor.
"World Ancestor, don't even think about helping the Qing Ye Ancestor!"
The Space-Time Ancestor blocked the World Ancestor.
As for the War Ancestor, his strength was too weak to intervene, and he didn't dare to block the Destruction Ancestor; otherwise, the Destruction Ancestor could easily kill him.
.... "The Destruction Ancestor really did make a move against me!"
Ye Tian thought to himself.
At this moment, the Saint Ancestor had the ability to stop the Destruction Ancestor, but he did not. Instead, he was busy collecting the treasures of the Primordial Ancestral Realm.
Thus, at this moment, Ye Tian could only rely on himself.
Currently, the true combat power of Ye Tian's clone, the Qing Ye Ancestor, was that of an Elite Ancestor, second only to Top-tier Ancestors. If he mobilized the power of the Dark Soul Domain, he could exert the combat power of a Top-tier Ancestor.
Moreover, Ye Tian possessed the Ultimate Ancestral Technique: Ancestral Armor, the Ultimate Ancestral Technique: Flowing Light, and the Ultimate Ancestral Technique: Tyrant Strength.
Furthermore, Ye Tian had later deduced his Time Ancestral Technique, the Eternal Ancestral Technique, to the level of an Ultimate Ancestral Technique.
Consequently, Ye Tian was extremely well-rounded, with almost no weaknesses.
At this time.
The Destruction Ancestor did not underestimate Ye Tian's clone, the Qing Ye Ancestor. After all, to be able to promote to an Ancestor at such a rapid speed—even more monstrous than the Saint Ancestor to a certain extent—he had to strike with full force to have any chance of heavily wounding the Qing Ye Ancestor.
He was confident he could slay the Qing Ye Ancestor within a short time.
Since the Saint Ancestor wasn't acting and the World Ancestor was blocked by the Space-Time Ancestor, no one could save the Qing Ye Ancestor.
Therefore, the Destruction Ancestor used his full strength to unleash his Ultimate Ancestral Technique—Destruction Ultimate Punch! Boom!!!!! A punch came crashing in, and he even wore an Innate Ancestral Artifact glove, allowing the power of this punch to reach a terrifying level.
"Tyrant Strength Ultimate Ancestral Technique!"
"Ancestral Armor Ultimate Ancestral Technique!"
The clone, Qing Ye Ancestor, also went all out and mobilized the power of the Dark Soul Domain to collide with the Destruction Ancestor's strike.
Boom!! The terrifying shockwave swept across the entire Primordial Ancestral Realm, causing it to tremble.
This was a collision of Top-tier Ancestor combat power! "What? An Ultimate Ancestral Technique!"
The Destruction Ancestor was shocked.
The Qing Ye Ancestor's attack was actually an Ultimate Ancestral Technique. Although its offensive power wasn't as high as his, it wasn't much weaker either.
Moreover, the Qing Ye Ancestor also possessed a defensive Ultimate Ancestral Technique. Thus, even if his attack was inferior, he wouldn't be injured.
On the contrary, the Destruction Ancestor did not have a defensive Ultimate Ancestral Technique, and after the collision just now, he actually felt a bit uncomfortable.
"I can't kill him!"
The Destruction Ancestor gave up.
He didn't have the ability to kill a Top-tier Ancestor. If the strength gap between Ancestors wasn't too large, it was impossible to kill one. After all, an Ancestor's life-saving capabilities were too strong; they weren't defective products like those of the Oblivion Race.
On the other side.
The All-Things Ancestor sought out Ye Tian's main body.
The human race was the greatest enemy of the All-Things Holy Sect because the human Qing Ye Ancestor had killed a Quasi-Ancestor of the All-Things Holy Sect just as he was about to promote.
Therefore, the All-Things Ancestor hated the human race deeply.
He knew he couldn't kill the Qing Ye Ancestor, but he had hope of killing Ye Tian.
No matter how monstrous Ye Tian's talent was or how strong his combat power had been, once he became an Ancestor, his combat power wouldn't immediately reach the Elite Ancestor level.
If ordinary Ancestors were divided into three tiers, Ye Tian would at most be in the second or third tier.
Besides, Ye Tian had just promoted to Ancestor, and his realm was still unstable, making this the best stage to kill him.
The All-Things Ancestor also knew very well that if Ye Tian were given some time to cultivate and raise his cultivation level, his strength would definitely step into the Elite Ancestor realm.
However, he had no idea of Ye Tian's true strength, because he couldn't even imagine it.
"Myriad Law Ancestor, today you are doomed!"
The All-Things Ancestor appeared before Ye Tian, his entire aura erupting.
"Not good, the All-Things Ancestor is actually an Elite Ancestor!"
The World Ancestor and War Ancestor both sensed it and were greatly shocked.
All along, the All-Things Ancestor had displayed the combat power of an ordinary Ancestor, at most at the third tier of ordinary Ancestors, similar to the War Ancestor.
But now, the All-Things Ancestor had revealed Elite Ancestor combat power. Although he was only a weaker Elite Ancestor, he was still much stronger than an ordinary Ancestor.
The War Ancestor wanted to support Ye Tian. If two ordinary Ancestors joined forces, they might be able to contend with the All-Things Ancestor for a while.
Moreover, Ancestors were very hard to kill, so there wasn't too much to worry about.
But the next scene caused the War Ancestor's expression to shake violently.
Swish! A golden crystal suddenly transformed into a barrier, enveloping Ye Tian and the All-Things Ancestor.
Seeing the barrier formed by this golden crystal, the War Ancestor cried out in shock, "A Barrier Ancestral Crystal!"
Such a thing was extremely precious even to Ancestors; even he didn't have one. Where did the All-Things Ancestor get a Barrier Ancestral Crystal? The All-Things Ancestor indeed didn't have one originally; he had obtained it through a trade with the Destruction Ancestor.
When the Destruction Ancestor learned that the All-Things Ancestor wanted to kill the Myriad Law Ancestor, he was immediately willing to trade.
Once a Barrier Ancestral Crystal deployed its barrier, it was very difficult for the outside world to break it. Unless a Top-tier Ancestor acted, it simply couldn't be shattered.
Furthermore, the Barrier Ancestral Crystal could suppress the opponent's strength by more than thirty percent.
"Myriad Law Ancestor, you can't get out now. Under the suppression of the Barrier Ancestral Crystal, your strength is suppressed by thirty percent. Moreover, you've just become an Ancestor, so I doubt you've even obtained a single Innate Ancestral Artifact.
But I, however, have an Innate Ancestral Artifact."
The All-Things Ancestor took out a silver longsword, which radiated an incredibly terrifying aura, somewhat similar to the aura of an Ancestor.
This was an Innate Ancestral Artifact, arguably the most powerful weapon in the Dark Forbidden Zone. Only the weapon-type Sacred Objects in the top few ranks of the Sacred Object List could barely compare to an Innate Ancestral Artifact.
"An Innate Ancestral Artifact! Myriad Law Ancestor, do not collide with that Innate Ancestral Artifact! That thing can cut through an Ancestor's body and inflict heavy damage!"
The War Ancestor hurriedly warned.
Ancestors usually didn't engage in true life-and-death battles, so they rarely brought out Innate Ancestral Artifacts.
Moreover, average Ancestors didn't even possess an Innate Ancestral Artifact.
For example, the War Ancestor was very poor and lacked sufficient strength; he only had one defective Innate Ancestral Artifact and a few top-tier Sacred Objects that were slightly inferior to Innate Ancestral Artifacts.
Within the War Gate, only the World Ancestor possessed an Innate Ancestral Artifact, and he only had one.
An Innate Ancestral Artifact could only enhance combat power by a few dozen percent, but it could cut through an Ancestor's body. If the strengths were similar, the impact of an Innate Ancestral Artifact wasn't huge.
But if one side was stronger and held an Innate Ancestral Artifact, they could very quickly slay a weaker Ancestor.
The War Ancestor and World Ancestor were panicking, but Ye Tian did not panic.
Looking at the All-Things Ancestor, Ye Tian smiled: "I just happened to be lacking an Innate Ancestral Artifact. I didn't expect you to deliver one, All-Things Ancestor!"
Boom!!!! An aura second only to a Top-tier Ancestor diffused from Ye Tian's body.
At this moment, many Ancestors were shocked beyond measure, revealing expressions of utter disbelief!

Chapter 1477: Slaying the Ancestor of All Things!

Chapter 1477: Slaying the Ancestor of All Things
!
"An elite Ancestor, and a top-tier elite Ancestor at that, second only to the combat power of a peak Ancestor... This is impossible! You've only just broken through to the Ancestor realm!"
The Ancestor of All Things was dumbfounded.
Who among them wasn't a monstrous genius? In the Dark Forbidden Zone, those strong enough to break through to the Ancestor realm were all peerless figures who had swept through their respective eras without rivals; they were true monsters.
Therefore, since everyone was a monster, everyone became an ordinary Ancestor after breaking through. Although there were differences in strength, the gap wasn't huge.
But what about Ye Tian? What kind of genius was this? To possess combat power second only to a peak Ancestor immediately upon breaking through—this was too exaggerated! "Ancestor Wanfa, I was just joking with you!"
The Ancestor of All Things chickened out.
So what if he possessed an Innate Ancestral Artifact? So what if he had the Barrier Ancestral Crystal? He still couldn't beat Ye Tian! He was only at the weaker level of elite Ancestors, while Ye Tian was at the level just below peak Ancestor combat power. The gap between the two was too vast.
"Ancestor of All Things, I am going to kill you. Let me tell you, this is no joke!"
Ye Tian's killing intent was laid bare, not hidden in the slightest.
"Ancestor Wanfa, do you really want to do this? Even if my strength is inferior to yours, it's not like I don't have the power to fight back. You don't have an Innate Ancestral Artifact. Although you can wound me, it will be difficult to obliterate my Ancestral Body. Killing me won't be easy!"
The Ancestor of All Things reminded him.
But in reality, he was still panicking; he was merely forcing himself to remain calm.
"Is that so? From what I know, the attacks of ordinary Ancestors are indeed difficult to obliterate an Ancestral Body. Only Innate Ancestral Artifacts and Ultimate Ancestral Techniques can cause significant damage to an Ancestral Body!"
Ye Tian spoke.
"Exactly. You don't have an Innate Ancestral Artifact, and since you've just broken through, it's impossible for you to have an Ultimate Ancestral Technique. Although I don't know how you possess the strength of an elite Ancestor, it will still be difficult for you to kill me.
How about we reconcile? Let's just forget everything that happened before!"
The Ancestor of All Things suggested.
"I indeed do not have an Innate Ancestral Artifact, but who told you I haven't mastered an Ultimate Ancestral Technique?"
Ye Tian sneered.
Boom!!!! Ultimate Ancestral Technique: Ancestral Armor, activated! Ultimate Ancestral Technique: Flowing Light, unleashed!
In an instant, Ye Tian charged toward the Ancestor of All Things.
Then, Ye Tian threw a punch at the Ancestor of All Things, employing the Ultimate Ancestral Technique: Overlord Strength.
For... Ancestors, other than Innate Ancestral Artifacts, other weapons were trash, far less powerful than an Ancestral Body. Even Saint Techniques weren't as powerful as a casual punch from an Ancestor.
Therefore, without an Innate Ancestral Artifact or an Ultimate Ancestral Technique, an Ancestor could choose to wear nothing and fight directly with their physical body; that was their strongest method.
"An Ultimate Ancestral Technique!!!!"
The Ancestor of All Things' pupils shrank violently as he immediately poured all his power into the Innate Ancestral Artifact longsword in his hand.
Boom!!!! The Innate Ancestral Artifact longsword collided with Ye Tian's Nine Extremes Ancestral Technique: Overlord Strength. The longsword was sent flying, and the punch landed directly on the Ancestor of All Things' body.
Crack!!! The Ancestor of All Things' physical body was shattered by the punch, but it healed in an instant.
Although the Ancestor of All Things recalled his Innate Ancestral Artifact, it couldn't pierce Ye Tian's Boundless Ancestral Body at all.
With the Boundless Ancestral Body combined with the Nine Extremes Ancestral Technique, and since the Ancestor of All Things' strength was already inferior to Ye Tian's, if he could have broken Ye Tian's defense with an Innate Ancestral Artifact, his strength would have reached peak Ancestor combat power long ago.
Bang! Bang! Bang! Ye Tian struck again and again, blowing apart the Ancestor of All Things' Ancestral Body repeatedly.
"Each strike actually obliterated one-thousandth—0.1%—of my Ancestral Body!!!"
The Ancestor of All Things was terrified.
This meant Ye Tian only needed a thousand attacks to kill him.
For... Ancestors, a thousand attacks wouldn't take long at all.
"Saint Ancestor, save me quickly!!!"
The Ancestor of All Things pleaded.
The Saint Ancestor frowned and spoke, "Ancestor Wanfa, spare the Ancestor of All Things!"
Ye Tian acted as if he hadn't heard and continued attacking the Ancestor of All Things.
Seeing that Ye Tian wasn't giving him face, the Saint Ancestor was also somewhat annoyed and prepared to break the barrier.
However, just as he moved, Ye Tian's clone, Ancestor Qingye, took action.
Boom!!!! Ancestor Qingye and the Saint Ancestor collided, neither gaining the upper hand.
"Ancestor Qingye, you are Ancestor Wanfa's clone, aren't you!"
The Saint Ancestor spoke.
The other Ancestors weren't surprised, simply because Ye Tian had just used the same Ultimate Ancestral Technique as Ancestor Qingye.
Ultimate Ancestral Techniques couldn't be taught; they could only be created by oneself. They naturally didn't believe that two people could create the exact same Ultimate Ancestral Technique.
Therefore, there was only one possibility: Ancestor Qingye was Ye Tian's clone.
Rumor had it that Ye Tian's clones were special, just like his main body, and it didn't matter how they died.
But now, this clone could even become an Ancestor without affecting the main body. This was too terrifying! "That's right!"
Ancestor Qingye spoke.
Once he acted, there was no way to hide it anymore, but he no longer needed to hide it. In the Dark Forbidden Zone, no one could threaten him anymore.
"As expected!"
The Ancestors thought to themselves.
"As expected of Ancestor Wanfa. I previously thought the Human Race was truly monstrous to produce two such terrifying geniuses, but now I know they are the same person.
Ancestor Wanfa, you sent your clone into the Dark Soul Realm; that is against the rules!"
The Saint Ancestor said.
"Against the rules? If you had the ability, you should have sent your clones into the Dark Soul Realm back then too!"
Ye Tian mocked.
Many Ancestors were fuming, but they couldn't do it.
"Ancestor Wanfa, the Ancestor of All Things cannot die. He is an Ancestor of our Dark Saint Realm. If he falls, the strength of our Dark Saint Realm will drop significantly!"
The Saint Ancestor said hurriedly.
"If one Ancestor dies, I will just train a few more Ancestors for the Dark Saint Realm!"
Ye Tian sneered.
"Are you really not going to give me face?"
The Saint Ancestor said angrily.
Ye Tian continued, "Saint Ancestor, do you really want to be my enemy? My clone can exert peak Ancestor combat power, and my main body will truly reach peak Ancestor combat power before long. Even after leaving the Dark Soul Realm, I will be a peak Ancestor.
Do you want to become my enemy for the sake of a mere weak elite Ancestor?"
The Saint Ancestor's expression changed. Only then did he realize that Ye Tian was not like those weak Ancestors from before, but a being truly equal to him.
The Ancestor of All Things wasn't his subordinate anyway; offending Ye Tian for his sake was indeed not worth it.
