Chapter 1478: The Huaxia Ancestral Realm!

Chapter 1478: Huaxia Ancestral Realm
!
The Progenitor of All Things was dead! The other Progenitors had not expected this at all. When the Progenitor of All Things brought out the Boundary Ancestral Crystal and the Innate Ancestral Artifact, they thought that Ye Tian—this newly ascended Progenitor—would fall.
However, they were wrong. The one who fell was the Progenitor of All Things.
A Progenitor! How long had it been since one had fallen? The number of Progenitors who had fallen in the Dark Forbidden Zone was far more than just one or two—it even exceeded double digits—but it had been a very long time since the last Progenitor fell. Thus, the fall of a Progenitor this time truly shocked them.
Particularly for the several newly ascended Progenitors, they realized that even Progenitors could fall.
For a moment, everyone was wary of Ye Tian.
His main body possessed top-tier elite Progenitor combat power and would definitely be able to promote to a top-tier Progenitor before long, while his clone possessed top-tier Progenitor combat power within the Dark Soul Domain.
How terrifying was such a Progenitor? He was even more fearsome than the Destruction Progenitor or the Saint Progenitor! Whoosh! Whoosh!!! The Battle Progenitor and the Realm Progenitor appeared beside Ye Tian one after another. Suddenly, the Battle Sect effectively possessed four Progenitors and held top-tier Progenitor combat power. In an instant, they surpassed the Dark Holy Sect and could be called the number one sect of the Dark Sacred Domain.
Of course.
The Battle Sect did not yet have top-tier Progenitor combat power in the outside world. After all, the combat power of the clone, Progenitor Qingye, was inferior to the main body in the outside world. Therefore, they needed to keep a low profile for the time being.
If Ye Tian's main body broke through to top-tier Progenitor combat power and then copied another body, it would be equivalent to two top-tier Progenitors, plus a clone capable of exerting top-tier Progenitor combat power in the Dark Soul Domain. That would be equivalent to three top-tier Progenitor combat forces.
At that time, the Battle Sect would have even greater confidence, and the human race would have even greater backing.
For now, Ye Tian was still unable to directly contend with so many Progenitors at once; if all those Progenitors joined forces, they would be no match for them.
Consequently, as these Progenitors searched for resources in the Original Ancestral Realm, Ye Tian did not stop them.
The other Progenitors left one by one to search for resources.
Ye Tian did not waste time either, searching for resources at extreme speed.
Progenitor Qingye also mobilized the power of the Dark Soul Domain to search for the resources of the Original Ancestral Realm.
Perhaps because a Progenitor had fallen, the Progenitors did not continue fighting afterward. Unless they encountered particularly precious resources, they only occasionally exchanged blows, and it would end quickly.
In the hundreds of millions of years that followed, the Dark Soul Domain was in a stage of resource explosion. A large number of Domain Ancestors flooded into the Dark Soul Domain to snatch resources and fight.
The Progenitors did not act; this was a rule among the Progenitors, not allowing interference in the affairs of Supreme-level Domain Ancestors.
Although the human race was powerful now, they could not contend against all the forces of the entire Dark Forbidden Zone. Therefore, they could only give up most of their territory and concentrate on resource-rich areas.
Gradually, the division of territory in the Dark Soul Domain became clear.
Almost every force occupied a territory, and even the experts of the Dark Destruction Domain occupied enough territory.
As for the local forces of the Dark Soul Domain, they were quite miserable. Because no Progenitor had been born among them, their status was too low. Many forces were wiped out or annexed by other forces.
As time passed, those local forces would cease to exist, gradually merging into the forces of the Dark Soul Domain and the Dark Destruction Domain.
In reality, the Dark Soul Domain had originally been controlled by the human race, and there weren't many local forces to begin with. Now, after this upheaval, the local forces naturally collapsed.
It could be said that the Dark Soul Domain had completely become the territory of the Dark Soul Domain, the Dark Destruction Domain, the Eternal Cult, and other forces.
They did not have the luck of the Dark Sacred Domain, which could control its own Dark Sacred Land.
Time passed slowly, and in the blink of an eye, three hundred million years had gone by.
At this point, the resource explosion stage of the Dark Soul Domain had ended. More resources might be born later, but it was almost impossible for resources to be born in such a concentrated manner as they were now.
Additionally.
The Original Ancestral Realm was also sealed off. After all, the previous battles had damaged the Original Ancestral Realm, and an Original Ancestral Realm of a Dark Sacred Domain had to be well-preserved so that more good resources could be obtained in the future.
If it wasn't sealed, the damage to the Original Ancestral Realm would be too great, which would affect its operation in the future and make it difficult for precious treasures to be born.
More importantly, no single force could completely occupy the Original Ancestral Realm; that was the real reason.
At this time, the second Ancestral Realm besides the Original Ancestral Realm was born.
According to the birth rules of the Dark Sacred Land, every interval of one Realm Year, the Dark Soul Domain would give birth to an Ancestral Realm. A total of ten Ancestral Realms could be born, though these ten Ancestral Realms did not include the Original Ancestral Realm.
For the sake of the Ancestral Realm, the Progenitors began to deliberate.
As soon as the meeting began.
Ye Tian demanded: "Our human race will occupy one Ancestral Realm!"
"On what grounds?"
The Destruction Progenitor said angrily.
The other Progenitors also disagreed one after another.
"On the grounds that my clone holds a portion of the authority of the Dark Soul Domain and can exert top-tier Progenitor combat power, and that I am about to promote to a top-tier Progenitor!"
Ye Tian's main body revealed an aura that was even more powerful than it had been three hundred million years ago.
During these three hundred million years, Ye Tian had also been secretly refining Nirvana treasures. Although the actual time spent practicing wasn't long, he had repeatedly used time acceleration arrays to cultivate. Thus, he had refined a massive amount of Nirvana treasures, and his strength was about to step into the level of top-tier Progenitor combat power.
"In at most one hundred million years, the Progenitor of Myriad Laws will inevitably promote to a top-tier Progenitor!"
The Destruction Progenitor and the Saint Progenitor were both wary.
But they could not kill Ye Tian, because he was incredibly close to top-tier Progenitor combat power and possessed an ultimate defensive Ancestral Technique. Such a Progenitor was too difficult to kill.
In addition, Ye Tian had a clone with top-tier Progenitor combat power, which made it impossible to kill him off.
"Agreed!"
"Agreed!"
The Destruction Progenitor and the Saint Progenitor discussed it and decided to give the human race one Ancestral Realm.
However, for the remaining Ancestral Realm slots, the human race would not be allowed to compete again.
Nevertheless, there were still nine Ancestral Realms left. There certainly wouldn't be enough to go around for so many forces, so it was inevitable that several forces would simultaneously control one Ancestral Realm, using it as a public world.
Subsequently, Ye Tian refined this Ancestral Realm and renamed it the Huaxia Ancestral Realm.
The human race originated from Huaxia, so using this name served as a way to remember the Huaxia of Earth.
Following this, a large number of human experts entered the Huaxia Ancestral Realm, and countless humans were moved here.
An Ancestral Realm was incredibly vast and could accommodate a very large population.
Furthermore, with the Huaxia Ancestral Realm as the core, the human race was distributed here.
Basically, humans from other regions of the Dark Soul Domain were almost all moved here to avoid being wiped out by other forces.
Before the Profound Void Sacred Realm was promoted to an Ancestral Realm, the Huaxia Ancestral Realm would serve as the core world of the human race for a period of time to come.

Chapter 1479: The Xuanxu Holy Realm is Finally About to Advance!

Chapter 1479: The Xuanxu Holy Realm is Finally About to Advance!
!
Time flowed by, and ten domain years passed.
By this time, all ten Ancestor Realms of the Dark Soul Domain had been born, and each had been partitioned.
Among them, the Destruction Holy Race occupied one Ancestor Realm, the Dark Holy Gate occupied one, and the War Gate occupied half of an Ancestor Realm.
Ye Tian occupied one Ancestor Realm in the name of the Human Race. Since the War Gate did not have a quota for this particular Ancestor Realm, they could continue to occupy their own share, and other forces could do nothing about it even if they disagreed.
Consequently, the War Gate seized an additional half of another Ancestor Realm.
For the War Gate, half an Ancestor Realm was sufficient; any more would be unnecessary.
As the various major powers each occupied their own territories within the Dark Soul Domain, the region gradually began to settle down.
At the very least, the Ancestors went into seclusion one by one to absorb and refine the resources they had obtained from the Primordial Ancestor Realm and the new Ancestor Realms.
Perhaps after a long period of time, their strength would increase once more.
For instance, some ordinary Ancestors who were very close to becoming Elite Ancestors might be able to break through their shackles and promote to Elite Ancestors. Likewise, top-tier Elite Ancestors like Jiezu might also have hope of breaking through their limits to reach top-tier Ancestor combat power.
Of course, the probability of such a breakthrough was relatively low.
Ye Tian, however, had utilized these ten domain years to refine countless Nirvana treasures, and he had long since broken through to top-tier Ancestor combat power.
This was a breakthrough for his true body; therefore, it was a genuine advancement.
Even in any part of the Dark Forbidden Zone, he could now exert top-tier Ancestor combat power, fearing neither the Destruction Ancestors nor the Holy Ancestors.
"The Dark Soul Domain has finally calmed down!"
Ye Tian murmured.
Over these ten domain years, the Dark Soul Domain had been extremely chaotic. Only the regions held by the Human Race remained peaceful, while the slaughter in other places had almost never ceased.
Now, the Dark Soul Domain was much better, roughly resembling the state of the Dark Holy Territory—local skirmishes were unavoidable, but the overall situation was stable.
Furthermore, the Dark Soul Domain imitated the practices of the Dark Holy Territory, constructing a large number of giant cities to manage the countless practitioners through these hubs.
However, the regions governed by the Dark Destruction Domain were not like this. They were frantically terraforming and cultivating a large number of races, forcing them to slaughter one another like raising Gu.
After all, many races of the Dark Destruction Domain grew through slaughter and destruction. It was only upon reaching the levels of Great Domain Ancestor, Invincible Domain Ancestor, Supreme-level Domain Ancestor, and Ancestor that they became almost like regular practitioners, increasing their strength through cultivation, as destruction could no longer provide much... improvement to their strength.
The Three Thousand Evil Races and the Destruction Holy Race only had their ordinary clansmen increase their cultivation by destroying domains and powerful worlds to absorb the power of destruction.
By conducting this "Gu-style" cultivation within a region of the Dark Destruction Domain, and given the recovery speed and resource generation rate of the Dark Soul Domain, they could mass-produce Domain Ancestors and experts above the level of Great Domain Ancestor.
This was the goal of the Ancestors from the Dark Destruction Domain. In reality, they also wanted to occupy the Dark Holy Territory, but the Dark Holy Territory had now become a monolithic block. The Destruction Ancestors could not easily invade it and could only occasionally launch an invasion war to cultivate their "Gu" through slaughter, sacrificing the majority of their Domain Ancestors to focus on nurturing experts at the Supreme level and above.
The Ancestors of the Dark Holy Territory were also aware of the cultivation methods of the Dark Destruction Domain and thus did not interfere. After all, the Domain Ancestors of the Dark Holy Territory could also temper themselves through these battles.
Ye Tian did not care about the domains occupied by the Dark Destruction Domain. The other party had sealed off that area, and for the time being, it would not affect other regions, which was enough.
"My true body has advanced to top-tier Ancestor combat power. Next, I can return to the Xuanxu Holy Realm and promote it to an Ancestor Realm!"
Ye Tian decided.
As for Xiao Yue and the others, they remained in the Huaxia Ancestor Realm.
Xiao Yue and the others had been: meditating on Ancestor Laws. With their comprehension and talent, it would likely take another hundred domain years before they had hope of completely integrating the Ancestor Laws and advancing to the Ancestor level.
This speed was not slow. After all, when other Supreme-level Domain Ancestors obtained Ancestor Laws, it would take them at least several hundred domain years to have any hope of a breakthrough.
Furthermore, the Ancestor Laws that Xiao Yue and the others were integrating were top-tier Ancestor Laws, which were much harder to merge. Therefore, achieving such a speed was quite excellent.
*Whoosh!* Ye Tian left the Huaxia Ancestor Realm. His departure was sensed by the avatars of other Ancestors, but they did not pay it much mind.
With a single thought, Ye Tian crossed a vast distance, traversing time and space to arrive at the Xuanxu Holy Realm.
If a Supreme-level Domain Ancestor wanted to fly there without the help of an Ancestor, it would take at least tens of millions of years at their fastest speed to reach the Xuanxu Holy Realm. It was... that exaggerated, because the distance was truly too vast.
If it were the speed of an Invincible Domain Ancestor, they might fly for an eternity and still be unable to cross such a staggering distance.
Therefore, in the Dark Forbidden Zone, aside from Ancestors, other Supreme-level Domain Ancestors were unable to traverse extremely long distances.
The Dark Soul Domain was considered relatively close to the Dark Destruction Domain, but the Dark Soul Domain itself was too far from other places.
The birth of a Dark Holy Land was random, so no one knew where one might appear. It was possible that one day, a Dark Holy Land might be born right next to the Dark Soul Domain.
Xuanxu Holy Realm.
Ye Tian returned and immediately duplicated his true body.
This way, the Xuanxu Holy Realm would be guarded by two top-tier Ancestor combat powers. Once the Xuanxu Holy Realm advanced to the Xuanxu Ancestor Realm, even if the Destruction Ancestors and Holy Ancestors came, he could block them and prevent them from probing the Xuanxu Ancestor Realm.
"Let the Xuanxu Holy Realm advance!"
Ye Tian no longer suppressed the origin of the Xuanxu Holy Realm. Under the stimulation of the Creation Primordial Well, the Xuanxu Holy Realm finally began its advancement.
*Rumble!!!!!* The volume of the Xuanxu Holy Realm began to skyrocket, doubling in size with every breath.
Endless territories were born, a sight that completely shocked the Human Race.
Consequently, one Supreme-level Domain Ancestor after another came to inquire about the situation.
"Lord Ancestor of Myriad Laws, what is happening to the Xuanxu Holy Realm?"
Facing the inquiries of these Domain Ancestors, Ye Tian gave a unified answer: "The Xuanxu Holy Realm is about to advance into the Xuanxu Ancestor Realm!"
"What? The Xuanxu Holy Realm is advancing to an Ancestor Realm? Does this mean our Human Race will possess two Ancestor Realms?"
Countless Domain Ancestors of the Human Race were stunned, followed by... wild joy! Once the Xuanxu Holy Realm was born as an Ancestor Realm, how many... rare resources would be produced! Perhaps the number of Supreme-level Domain Ancestors in the Human Race would increase again, and the strength of the Human Race would skyrocket.
The vast number of Invincible Domain Ancestors were even more excited upon hearing this news; they now had hope of advancing to the Supreme-level Domain Ancestor rank.
*Rumble!!!* The Xuanxu Holy Realm continued to expand. Given its condition, it would take roughly several million years to evolve into an Ancestor Realm.
At the same time, the entire Daoshan Domain was affected by the advancement of the Xuanxu Holy Realm and began to transform. The area of the Daoshan Domain continuously swallowed the Dark Forbidden Zone, and its territory expanded frantically.
This time, while the Daoshan Domain might not evolve to the size of a Dark Holy Land, it would at least be equivalent to a small-scale Dark Holy Land.

Chapter 1480: Scaring Away the Destruction Primordial Ancestor!

Chapter 1480: Scaring Away the Destruction Primordial Ancestor
!
The promotion of the Xuanxu Holy Realm to the Xuanxu Ancestral Realm was something that simply could not be hidden.
Although the Xuanxu Holy Realm was completely sealed off and under the sole control of the human race, there were a large number of factions outside the Xuanxu Holy Realm, and even branch divisions of the Dark Holy Region's forces.
Therefore, when the Xuanxu Holy Realm was promoted to an Ancestral Realm, these factions naturally found out immediately and promptly notified the powers within the Dark Holy Region.
Even if Ye Tian were to wipe out these faction branches with a single thought, he could indeed ensure that the news would not leak for a time, and he could even seal off the Daoshan Domain to prevent anyone from entering or leaving.
But that would only treat the symptoms, not the root cause.
If those branch divisions were destroyed, the Dark Holy Region would certainly send people to investigate, and it would still be exposed eventually.
Consequently, Ye Tian stopped caring.
If it was exposed, so be it. He had already advanced to top-tier Primordial Ancestor combat power, so he naturally did not fear other Primordial Ancestors, not even the two top-tier ones: the Holy Ancestor and the Destruction Primordial Ancestor.
....Dark Holy Sect.
At this moment, the Holy Ancestor was cultivating when he suddenly received a piece of intelligence.
"The Xuanxu Holy Realm has been promoted to an Ancestral Realm?"
The Holy Ancestor was shocked.
In the past, he wouldn't have even known what the Xuanxu Holy Realm was because he didn't pay attention to it.
But now, he knew the origin of the Xuanxu Holy Realm; it was the place of origin for the human race and the territory of the Primordial Ancestor of Myriad Laws.
It was said that the Xuanxu Holy Realm was initially just an ordinary small universe, which then promoted step by step until it reached the level of a Holy Realm.
Promoting to a Holy Realm was not difficult; he himself could nurture a world to promote to a Holy Realm, provided he spent some precious treasures.
But promoting to an Ancestral Realm—how was that possible? He couldn't do it at all, and neither could other Primordial Ancestors.
If it were possible to nurture an Ancestral Realm, he would have done so long ago.
A single Dark Holy Land could only give birth to one Original Ancestral Realm and ten Ancestral Realms; this was a restriction.
Places that were not Dark Holy Lands simply could not give birth to an Ancestral Realm.
For example, the headquarters of the Eternal Cult was actually just a treasure land within the Dark Forbidden Zone, but it was not an Ancestral Realm.
The Daoshan Domain was merely a domain; how could an Ancestral Realm be born there? This was abnormal! If this situation could be replicated, even if it took a long time, the Dark Holy Sect would be able to nurture one Ancestral Realm after another. What kind of concept was that? Once he controlled the resources of multiple Ancestral Realms, he could take another step forward.
Whoosh! The Holy Ancestor crossed a vast distance in a single step and descended outside the Xuanxu Holy Realm.
At the same time, other Primordial Ancestors arrived one after another. Even the Destruction Primordial Ancestor from the Dark Destruction Domain received the news immediately and arrived here.
...."It really is an Ancestral Realm!"
The Destruction Primordial Ancestor was shocked.
Just then, Ye Tian emerged from the Xuanxu Holy Realm.
"Fellow Primordial Ancestors, what brings you to my place?"
Ye Tian asked.
"Primordial Ancestor of Myriad Laws, your Daoshan Domain is just a domain. Why would an Ancestral Realm be born here, and specifically an Ancestral Realm promoted from a Holy Realm? I have never heard of a Holy Realm being able to promote to an Ancestral Realm!"
The Holy Ancestor questioned.
"I don't know either. It suddenly promoted, and I find it very strange as well!"
Ye Tian feigned ignorance.
"How about letting us go inside to take a look?"
The Destruction Primordial Ancestor suggested.
Boom!!!! A dense killing intent radiated from Ye Tian's body.
"Everyone, the Xuanxu Holy Realm is the origin of our human race. Naturally, no one is allowed to enter. Otherwise, if our human race has any secrets, wouldn't they be exposed to your investigation? Which faction doesn't have a few small secrets? Therefore, I refuse your suggestion."
"Furthermore, even if the Xuanxu Holy Realm has promoted to the Xuanxu Ancestral Realm and there really is some secret behind it, that is a matter for our human race. What does it have to do with you?"
Ye Tian said coldly.
The Destruction Primordial Ancestor said with a grim face, "Primordial Ancestor of Myriad Laws, the fact that a Holy Realm can promote to an Ancestral Realm is too significant. We must know the reason. If you have a way to elevate a Holy Realm to an Ancestral Realm, please sell this method to us. Otherwise, you will offend all the Primordial Ancestors!"
"Based on just you lot?"
Ye Tian said disdainfully.
The Holy Ancestor said, "Primordial Ancestor of Myriad Laws, it's better to hand over the method for nurturing an Ancestral Realm. Otherwise, with the Destruction Primordial Ancestor and me—two top-tier Primordial Ancestors—you won't be able to stop us.
This is not the Dark Soul Domain. If it were the Dark Soul Domain, you and your clone, the Qingye Primordial Ancestor, working together would be equivalent to two top-tier Primordial Ancestors. But here, your Qingye Primordial Ancestor clone can only exert elite Primordial Ancestor combat power. You cannot contend with us!"
The Holy Ancestor stepping in to deal with Ye Tian was equivalent to allying with the Destruction Primordial Ancestor.
At this time, even if the World Ancestor and the War Ancestor of the War Sect helped, they wouldn't be able to contend with so many Primordial Ancestors.
"Is that so?"
Ye Tian sneered.
Rumble!!!! Another Primordial Ancestor appeared, standing right beside Ye Tian.
This Primordial Ancestor was naturally Ye Tian's duplicate body, with identical combat power.
"This..."
The Destruction Primordial Ancestor and the Holy Ancestor were instantly dumbfounded upon seeing this duplicate body.
They knew Ye Tian possessed a special clone, but they thought there was only one, which was the Qingye Primordial Ancestor.
They never expected another clone to appear, and one with top-tier Primordial Ancestor combat power at that.
It was said that even if Ye Tian's clones died in battle, they could be condensed again.
This was equivalent to having a top-tier Primordial Ancestor clone that could never truly perish!
How could they fight this? Immediately, some Primordial Ancestors became extremely wary and left at once to avoid being caught in the crossfire and potentially killed.
Just then, a figure emerged; it was the World Ancestor.
Rumble!!! The aura of a top-tier Primordial Ancestor radiated from the World Ancestor. Although it was slightly weak, as he had just promoted, he was still a top-tier Primordial Ancestor.
Clearly, the World Ancestor had gained immense benefits from the Dark Soul Domain, allowing him to break through his shackles and advance to top-tier Primordial Ancestor combat power.
Now, the Dark Forbidden Zone had given birth to a total of four true top-tier Primordial Ancestors.
The Primordial Ancestor of Myriad Laws, the World Ancestor, the Destruction Primordial Ancestor, and the Holy Ancestor.
Among them, Ye Tian alone could be counted as two true top-tier Primordial Ancestor combat units. Combined with the World Ancestor, the War Sect's side was equivalent to three top-tier Primordial Ancestor combat units. If the Qingye Primordial Ancestor could exert top-tier combat power outside, it would be even more terrifying.
"Holy Ancestor, Destruction Primordial Ancestor, if you want to deal with our War Sect's Primordial Ancestor of Myriad Laws, then let's have a fight!"
The World Ancestor declared.
Three against two? And among the opponent's three top-tier combat units, one was not afraid of death. This was a fight they couldn't win.
Immediately, the Holy Ancestor said, "Hahaha, I was just joking!"
Clearly, the Holy Ancestor did not want to offend the War Sect. After all, his Dark Holy Sect was located in the Dark Holy Region. If he offended the current War Sect, the Dark Holy Sect's days would not be easy.
The Destruction Primordial Ancestor also lost his nerve. If Ye Tian and the others incited the Holy Ancestor to turn around and besiege him, there might actually be a chance they could keep him there forever.
Consequently, the Destruction Primordial Ancestor also left immediately.

Chapter 1481: The Six Great Forbidden Lands of the Dark Forbidden Zone, Ancestor...

Chapter 1481: The Six Great Forbidden Lands of the Dark Forbidden Zone, the Ancestors' Graves
!
As the Ancestors departed one by one, the crisis of the Profound Void Ancestral World naturally vanished.
At this time, the Realm Ancestor and the War Ancestor had not yet left.
In truth, the Realm Ancestor and the War Ancestor were extremely curious about the promotion of the Profound Void Holy World into the Profound Void Ancestral World. Of course, they did not directly inquire about the secrets of the Profound Void Ancestral World, but instead asked in a different way.
"Myriad Law Ancestor, the promotion of the Profound Void Holy World into the Profound Void Ancestral World—can this method be replicated?"
the Realm Ancestor inquired.
If this method could be replicated, then the War Gate could create one Ancestral World after another.
If that happened, how powerful would the War Gate become! "It cannot be replicated!"
Ye Tian replied, "In truth, this was a treasure I obtained from the Dark Destruction Domain back then. By integrating it into the Profound Void Holy World, I was able to allow the Profound Void Holy World to promote into the Profound Void Ancestral World!"
"A treasure obtained from the Dark Destruction Domain?"
The Realm Ancestor was shocked.
He did not think Ye Tian was lying. At Ye Tian's level, he was already at the most powerful tier of the Dark Forbidden Zone; there was no need to lie.
Therefore, he believed him.
"In that case, if the Destruction Ancestor knew the truth, he would probably regret it to death. A treasure they failed to discover was discovered by you!"
The War Ancestor laughed heartily.
The three of them chatted for a long time before dispersing.
In the days that followed, news of the Profound Void Holy World's promotion to the Profound Void Ancestral World spread. Furthermore, word got out that the Human Race's Myriad Law Ancestor possessed top-tier Ancestor combat power and even had a clone that also possessed top-tier Ancestor combat power.
This time, countless experts in the Dark Holy Domain, the Dark Destruction Domain, and the Dark Soul Domain were beyond shocked. Even the Eternal Cult and countless forces within the Dark Forbidden Zone were stunned by Ye Tian's strength.
Some even ranked Ye Tian among the top experts of the Dark Forbidden Zone. After all, with Ye Tian's main body and clone together, his combat power might even exceed that of the Holy Ancestor and the Destruction Ancestor.
Of course, without a true life-and-death struggle, no one knew whose true strength was superior.
What if the Destruction Ancestor and the Holy Ancestor were hiding their strength? That was also a possibility! In the blink of an eye, several million years passed.
On this day, the Profound Void Holy World finally completed its promotion into the Profound Void Ancestral World.
Just as the promotion finished, a massive amount of treasures were born, all of which belonged to the Human Race.
Moreover, Ye Tian only collected a portion of the top-tier resources of the Profound Void Ancestral World. He did not touch the rest, allowing the practitioners of the Human Race to search for them; whoever found them owned them, and they were free to compete for them.
Even some of the weak were lucky enough to obtain treasures, rising to prominence in a single bound.
Under these circumstances, many more experts and lucky geniuses were born within the Human Race.
Perhaps after a long period of time, the Human Race would see the birth of more Supreme-level Domain Ancestors.
After another period of time, Ye Tian's duplicated body left the Profound Void Ancestral World and began wandering through the Dark Forbidden Zone.
He had been an Ancestor for so long, yet he had hardly traveled through the Dark Forbidden Zone and truly didn't know much about it.
Therefore, this time he planned to learn more about the Dark Forbidden Zone.
As he traveled, he discovered that the Dark Forbidden Zone was truly vast, far exceeding his imagination. If one did not use the Ancestor's ability to traverse time and space and relied solely on flying, even an Ancestor would likely need millions of years to cross the entire Dark Forbidden Zone.
It was truly strange that such a massive Dark Forbidden Zone had only birthed three Dark Holy Lands to date.
Furthermore, there were places in the Dark Forbidden Zone that even Ancestors did not dare to enter.
For example, the forbidden land in front of Ye Tian.
At this moment, Ye Tian stood before a massive black mountain. This mountain sat right in the void of the Dark Forbidden Zone. The giant black mountain was equivalent to the volume of a Holy World, and it gave Ye Tian a very dangerous aura, as if he would perish upon entry.
"What place is this?"
Ye Tian was very curious. He did not enter immediately but instead contacted the Realm Ancestor.
"Realm Ancestor, I have discovered a massive black mountain in the Dark Forbidden Zone. What place is this?"
Ye Tian inquired.
Soon, the Realm Ancestor's Ancestor Avatar traversed time and space to arrive at Ye Tian's side. He looked at the giant black mountain before them with great trepidation and said, "This is the Calamity Black Mountain. Even Ancestors will perish if they enter. As far as I know, a total of three Ancestors have entered the Calamity Black Mountain. Two perished directly, and the other was an Elite Ancestor who perished shortly after coming out. Moreover, he was already maddened when he emerged. To make an Ancestor go mad, one can only imagine what terrifying things he encountered.
Myriad Law Ancestor, although you have a clone, I suggest you still do not go. Some attacks even ignore the connection between the clone and the main body, directly striking down the original self.
Ancestors also have Ancestor Avatars whose combat power is still very fearsome, yet no one dares to use an Ancestor Avatar to enter the Calamity Black Mountain precisely because... they worry about this problem."
Ye Tian also knew that his duplicated bodies were not omnipotent, which was why he hadn't been reckless; otherwise, he wouldn't have asked the Realm Ancestor.
At this time, the Realm Ancestor continued, "There are currently six places in the Dark Forbidden Zone that are forbidden lands for Ancestors. Even top-tier Ancestors do not dare to enter them.
There are also dozens of other places where ordinary Ancestors will perish upon entry, while top-tier Ancestors have a certain chance of survival."
Subsequently, the Realm Ancestor named those six true Ancestor Forbidden Lands.
The Calamity Black Mountain, the Destruction Swamp, the Boundless Wall, the Firmament Sword Tomb, the Illusory Dream World, and the Boundless Demon Sea.
These six great forbidden lands are known as the Ancestors' Graves, having claimed the lives of many Ancestors.
Before the birth of the first Dark Holy Land—the Dark Destruction Domain—the Dark Forbidden Zone had actually birthed the first batch of the most ancient Ancestors. Most of these ancient Ancestors... perished in these six forbidden lands.
Another portion of Ancestors disappeared; as for where they went, no one knows.
Some say they sealed themselves and entered a deep sleep, while others speculate they left the Dark Forbidden Zone.
When the Realm Ancestor mentioned leaving the Dark Forbidden Zone, Ye Tian was stunned and couldn't help but ask, "Isn't the Dark Forbidden Zone everything? Is it possible to leave the Dark Forbidden Zone? Could there be another world outside the Dark Forbidden Zone?"
"I'm not sure!"
The Realm Ancestor shook his head. "Rumor has it that every long period of time, a phantom portal appears in the Dark Forbidden Zone. Once an Ancestor enters that phantom dream, they disappear completely.
It is said that this phantom portal is... the passage to another world, but these are just rumors, and no Ancestor has ever returned.
We Ancestors have eternal lifespans. Unless we truly have no more room for improvement, only then would we think about leaving."
"So that's how it is!"
Ye Tian nodded.
He had thought that by breaking through to top-tier Ancestor combat power, the Dark Forbidden Zone would hold no more secrets for him. He hadn't expected the secrets to be even greater.
(End of Chapter)

Chapter 1482: Ten Realm Years, Strength Skyrockets!

Chapter 1482: Ten Realm Years, Strength Skyrockets
!
"So, there are more Ancestors in the Dark Forbidden Zone than the ones I've seen,"
Ye Tian asked curiously.
"Correct, there are indeed more than just these Ancestors. As for exactly how many there are, even I am not sure!"
The Realm Ancestor explained: "If an Ancestor hides, no one can find them.
Moreover, at the dawn of the Dark Forbidden Zone, no one knows exactly how many... good things were born.
It is said that before the Dark Destruction Zone was born, a significant portion of those sleeping Ancestors were Top Ancestors. Having lived through endless ages and reaching a point where they could no longer progress, yet unwilling to leave the Dark Forbidden Zone, they chose to enter a self-induced slumber to wait for new opportunities! The birth of the Dark Holy Land isn't of much value to them. After all, compared to the entire Dark Forbidden Zone, the Dark Holy Land is merely a treasure land. While it is highly valuable to... ordinary Ancestors, its value isn't necessarily high for those Top Ancestors.
The Saint Ancestor and the Destruction Ancestor belong to the weaker tier of Top Ancestors. If we were to classify the level above Top Ancestors as Supreme Ancestors, the Destruction Ancestor and Saint Ancestor are still very far from that level. Therefore, some treasures within the Dark Holy Land are still quite useful to them and can improve their cultivation, which is why they are so keen on fighting for the treasures and opportunities of the Dark Holy Land.
If they reach the limit of Top Ancestors and cannot promote to Supreme Ancestors, or if they find themselves unable to progress for a long time in the future, perhaps one day they too will enter a self-induced slumber, leave the Dark Forbidden Zone, or perhaps charge into the Six Great Forbidden Grounds to gamble for a chance!"
"So that's how it is!"
Ye Tian nodded.
Indeed, if a Top Ancestor remained unable to break through after living for too long, life would lose its meaning for such an Ancestor.
At that point, if they didn't want to seek death by entering the Six Great Forbidden Grounds, they could only sleep and wait for the long ages to pass before waking up. Perhaps then, a Supreme Ancestor would be born in the Dark Forbidden Zone, giving them hope for a breakthrough.
"Ancestor Wanfa, you have only recently broken through to the Ancestor realm, yet you already possess the combat power of a Top Ancestor. You can continue to cultivate. Once your strength approaches that of a Supreme Ancestor, you can go to some of the forbidden areas beneath the Six Great Forbidden Grounds. Although dangerous for Top Ancestors, there is still a high hope of survival, and you might obtain some opportunities.
For now, whatever you do, do not enter the Six Great Forbidden Grounds!"
The Realm Ancestor warned.
"I understand!"
Ye Tian nodded.
Afterward, the Realm Ancestor departed.
Ye Tian took a deep look at the Calamity Black Mountain before leaving the area.
In the following days, Ye Tian visited each of the Six Great Forbidden Grounds, but he only observed them from the outside without entering.
Just by observing from the exterior, he felt a terrifying aura of death, as if he would perish the moment he stepped inside.
...."I should still focus on increasing my Ancestor cultivation. It hasn't been long since I broke through to the Ancestor realm, so I can continue to improve. First, I'll nurture the Nihility Spacetime. By using the Profound Void Ancestral World to nurture the Nihility Spacetime and sealing its aura, other Ancestors shouldn't be able to sense it.
Besides, the Profound Void Ancestral World belongs entirely to the Human Race, and other Ancestors won't come here to investigate, so it should be very safe!"
Ye Tian thought to himself.
Although he didn't fear the Saint Ancestor or the Destruction Ancestor, if news of him nurturing a Nihility Spacetime leaked and caught the attention of some sleeping Top Ancestors, it wouldn't be good for him.
Therefore, it was better to be cautious for now.
Thus.
Ye Tian nurtured a top-tier Nihility Spacetime within the Profound Void Ancestral World, pouring a massive amount of resources into it to cultivate Nihility treasures.
Then, Ye Tian refined these Nihility treasures to continuously improve his cultivation.
In this way, Ye Tian's strength grew steadily.
One Realm Year after another passed by.
As his cultivation increased, he also attempted to create more Ultimate Ancestral Techniques.
For instance, defensive Ultimate Ancestral Techniques could be stacked.
Ye Tian had created the Ancestral Armor Ultimate Ancestral Technique, but he could also create a second defensive Ultimate Ancestral Technique, such as a Dao Robe Ultimate Ancestral Technique—condensing a robe to cover the body and block attacks, or other similar techniques.
The same applied to speed-type Ultimate Ancestral Techniques; a movement-type technique combined with a wing-type speed technique could also be stacked.
Similarly, for time-based Ultimate Ancestral Techniques, he could create one to accelerate his own time, which would significantly boost his speed, reaction time, and attack power.
Once he mastered more Ultimate Ancestral Techniques, his own strength would become even more formidable.
And so.
Ye Tian continuously created one Ultimate Ancestral Technique after another.
In the blink of an eye, ten 10 Realm Years had passed.
By this time, Ye Tian had created five 55 Ultimate Ancestral Techniques.
These five 55 Ultimate Ancestral Techniques were the Golden Wings, the Dao Robe, the Extreme Arm, the Dream Butterfly, and the Hand of Nihility.
Among them, the Extreme Arm technique allowed one arm to exert a terrifying effect, even more fearsome than the Tyrant Strength technique, and the two techniques had a slight stacking effect.
The Dream Butterfly technique was a time-based Ultimate Ancestral Technique that could rapidly accelerate his own time, making his speed and reactions incredibly fast. With increased speed, his attack power naturally became stronger. Thus, this technique was a huge help to Ye Tian's strength. If used in conjunction with the Eternal technique to freeze spacetime, the effect would be even better.
The Hand of Nihility was a Nihility-type Ultimate Ancestral Technique that Ye Tian created from scratch. It was only because he possessed the Ultimate Nihility Talent that he could create such a technique; it was likely the only one of its kind in the entire Dark Forbidden Zone.
With these five 55 new techniques, combined with his previous ones and the Nihility treasures he had refined over the ten 10 Realm Years, his strength had undergone a world-shaking transformation.
"My current strength is at least twenty times 20 greater than when I first broke through to the Top Ancestor level. I should have reached the peak of the Top Ancestor rank now. I could easily defeat the Destruction Ancestor or the Saint Ancestor!"
Ye Tian murmured.
If he used his duplicated bodies in coordination, he would be enough to kill the Destruction Ancestor and the Saint Ancestor.
Furthermore, his Green Leaf Ancestor clone's cultivation had also improved slightly. With the boost from several Ultimate Ancestral Techniques, it had barely reached the level of Top Ancestor combat power.
However, at that level, the power boost from the Dark Soul Realm had decreased significantly, and even with that boost, its combat power was far inferior to his main body.
"Yue'er and the others are about to break through to the Ancestor realm soon!"
Ye Tian murmured.

Chapter 1483: Human Ancestors Born One After Another!

Chapter 1483: Human Ancestors Born One After Another!
!
It had been many years since Ye Tian passed the Ancestor Methods to Xiao Yue and the others. Originally, they wouldn't have been able to fuse with the Ancestor Methods so quickly, but Ye Tian had frequently guided them over these years.
After all, these Ancestor Methods were created by Ye Tian himself, making him the person who understood them best. To help his family members become Ancestors faster, Ye Tian provided frequent guidance, which shortened the time required for them to become Ancestors by many times.
Otherwise, it would have taken them at least a hundred Domain Years to have any hope of fusing with an Ancestor Method and becoming an Ancestor.
Another Domain Year passed. On this day, Ye Tian's wife, Xiao Yue, was about to successfully fuse with the Light Ancestor Method.
Once the fusion was successful, Xiao Yue would become a Light Ancestor.
At this time.
Xiao Yue and the others had all returned to the Profound Void Ancestral World for secluded cultivation. With Ye Tian's true body protecting them, her breakthrough to the Ancestor realm would absolutely not be disturbed.
On this day.
Boom!!!!! Xiao Yue successfully fused with the Light Ancestor Method and was breaking through to the Ancestor realm. Countless amounts of energy surged into her body, and the entire Dao Mountain Domain and even the surrounding Dark Forbidden Zone were enveloped in Ancestral phenomena.
An event as significant as an Ancestor's breakthrough shook time and space, making it impossible to hide. Many Ancestors sensed it.
Immediately, the wills of various Ancestors descended upon the Profound Void Ancestral World across time and space. They did not dare to barge directly into the Profound Void Ancestral World, but they could perceive the situation.
"In the Profound Void Ancestral World, someone has broken through to the Ancestor realm. Who is it?"
The various Ancestors were incredibly shocked.
Wasn't Ye Tian the only monstrous talent in the human race? Even the Green Leaf Ancestor was just Ye Tian's clone.
Therefore, there shouldn't have been a second Supreme-level Domain Ancestor in the human race qualified to charge for the Ancestor realm! Although the human race currently had many Supreme-level Domain Ancestors, and even some at the peak of that level.
But these Ancestors knew very well how difficult it was to reach the Ancestor realm. One either had to create their own Ancestor Method or fuse with the masterless Ancestor Method of a fallen Ancestor.
However, there were only so many fallen Ancestors, and their Ancestor Methods had almost all been fused by others. Thus, obtaining a brand-new Ancestor Method was far too difficult.
As for creating one's own Ancestor Method, not everyone was as monstrously talented as Ye Tian.
Furthermore, even Ancestors themselves couldn't necessarily create a new Ancestor Method because they couldn't break free from their own Ancestral Path. Trying to create an Ancestor Method different from one's own Ancestral Path was simply too difficult.
Even the Saint Ancestor and the Destruction Ancestor had no way to create a second Ancestor Method, so they had no way to help others become Ancestors.
Consequently, they couldn't understand how the human race had suddenly birthed another Ancestor.
"Jie Zu, do you know who it is from the human race that broke through to the Ancestor realm?"
The Eternal Cult Leader asked curiously.
Jie Zu shook his head: "To be honest, I am also very shocked. Within the human race, only the Myriad Law Ancestor is an Ancestor of our Battle Sect, while the other humans are not... disciples of the Battle Sect. Therefore, I don't know much about the human race.
But from what I know, the other peak Supreme-level Domain Ancestors of the human race are not qualified to become Ancestors. Thus, there is only one possibility: the Myriad Law Ancestor obtained a masterless Ancestor Method and allowed a peak Supreme-level Domain Ancestor of the human race to fuse with it and step into the Ancestor realm."
"What incredible luck!"
The Destruction Ancestor said with a hint of jealousy. A complete, masterless Ancestor Method was something even he couldn't get his hands on.
Although he was confident he could kill a weaker Ancestor, that Ancestor wouldn't just produce an Ancestor Method for him. Unless an Ancestor was willing, it was impossible to obtain their Ancestor Method.
However, there weren't many Ancestors willing to produce one.
In the blink of an eye, several million years passed.
By this time, Xiao Yue had successfully broken through to the Ancestor realm. Although her combat strength wasn't particularly great, she was a true Ancestor.
After her successful breakthrough, Xiao Yue made an appearance and gave herself an Ancestral name: Moon Ancestor! Only then did the other Ancestors realize that the person who had broken through was the wife of the Myriad Law Ancestor, Ye Tian.
A husband and wife both being Ancestors—this was an incredibly rare occurrence.
Many Ancestors had never married, and some who had found their wives had long since fallen, or their strength was so low that they couldn't endure the long passage of time and had entered a self-imposed slumber.
Thus, these Ancestors were extremely envious of Ye Tian.
But there was nothing they could do; jealousy was useless.
The human race had birthed a new Ancestor, and combined with Ye Tian being equivalent to three Ancestors, it was as if they now possessed four Ancestors.
With Ye Tian's strength, the human race was almost comparable to the Destruction Saint Race.
Another half a Domain Year passed. On this day, the human race once again became the focus of many Ancestors.
Simply because the human race had birthed yet another Ancestor! Boom!!!! Ye Xingchen broke through and was stepping into the Ancestor realm. Countless amounts of forbidden energy surged into his body, helping him temper his physique and condense an Ancestral Body.
Soon, the Ancestors arrived again, each one dumbfounded.
"How can this be? How has the human race birthed another Ancestor? It's impossible to have luckily obtained another masterless Ancestor Method. There is definitely something wrong with the human race!!!"
The Spacetime Ancestor said in shock.
"Could it be that the human race has mastered a method to break through to the Ancestor realm without an Ancestor Method?"
One Ancestor speculated.
"Impossible. An Ancestor Method is the only way to become an Ancestor; otherwise, it cannot be done. Perhaps the human race's luck is truly just that good, and they obtained two masterless Ancestor Methods!"
Another Ancestor remarked.
At this point, many Ancestors were driven mad with jealousy. If it weren't for Ye Tian's immense strength, they truly would have barged into the Profound Void Ancestral World to investigate the human race's secrets.
Millions of years later, Ye Xingchen officially succeeded in his breakthrough, stepping into the Ancestor realm and calling himself the Star Ancestor.
Shortly thereafter, Ye Xingyue also broke through to the Ancestor realm, calling herself the Star-Moon Ancestor.
Ye Yu was slightly slower, but two Domain Years later, she also stepped into the Ancestor realm, calling herself the Rain Ancestor.
From that point on, all of Ye Tian's family members had stepped into the Ancestor realm.
With the human race birthing several Ancestors in succession, anyone could see that the human race was not normal.
Ye Tian had no way to explain. If he said he had created many Ancestor Methods, would others believe him? They wouldn't believe it at all! Even if they did believe it, the other Ancestors would only become more terrified, because if he could continuously create Ancestor Methods, it meant he could continuously create Ancestors. That was even more frightening! On this day.
Ye Tian and Jie Zu were chatting together.
Abruptly.
Jie Zu warned: "Myriad Law Ancestor, you must be careful of the Saint Ancestor!"
"Be careful of the Saint Ancestor? Why?"
Ye Tian frowned.
Jie Zu remained silent for a moment before finally saying: "The Saint Ancestor is not simple. Moreover, with your human race birthing Ancestors one after another, the Saint Ancestor will feel that your race holds a great secret that might be of huge help to his own strength. Even if it isn't helpful to him, if he masters your secret, he might be able to continuously create Ancestors, allowing the Dark Saint Sect to become a power that surpasses the Destruction Saint Race.
Therefore, he might make a move against you."
"I am not afraid of a mere Saint Ancestor!"
Ye Tian said confidently.
After all, his strength had reached the level of a top-tier Ancestor, and he was at the peak of that level. Ordinary top-tier Ancestors were far from being his match.
"No, the Saint Ancestor's own strength might not be that great, but he knows even more terrifying top-tier Ancestors!!!"
Jie Zu revealed a massive secret.

Chapter 1484: The Bone Beads of the Bone Sea Forbidden Zone!

Chapter 1484: The Bone Beads of the Bone Sea Forbidden Zone
! [Requesting Subscriptions]
"The Holy Ancestor knows even more terrifying top-tier Ancestors?"
Ye Tian said in shock.
"Yes!"
World Ancestor nodded. "Not many Ancestors know this secret. The Destruction Ancestor knows, a few Ancestors of the Dark Holy Gate know, and then there's me and the War Ancestor."
"Could it be a sleeping top-tier Ancestor?"
Ye Tian asked curiously.
World Ancestor said solemnly, "Exactly, it is indeed a sleeping top-tier Ancestor. According to our guesses, back when the Holy Ancestor was able to become the first Ancestor of the Dark Holy Domain and created his own Ancestor Law to do so, he must have received guidance from a top-tier Ancestor.
Otherwise, how could he have created his own Ancestor Law in a mere few dozen domain years?"
Ye Tian nodded. Even for a genius like him, with the Ultimate Ancestral Talent, it would take a long time to create an Ancestor Law.
The Holy Ancestor of the past was definitely not as monstrous as he was, yet he could create his own Ancestor Law in just a few dozen domain years; this was definitely abnormal.
After all, the cultivation system of the Dark Holy Domain had only just been established back then, and the Dark Destruction Domain could not have provided guidance for it. Therefore, becoming an Ancestor was even harder then. Creating an Ancestor Law was equivalent to creating something from nothing; one could imagine how immense the difficulty was! However, under such circumstances, the Holy Ancestor was able to create an Ancestor Law and become an Ancestor, which was naturally abnormal.
"World Ancestor, is there any evidence? If it's just a guess, I'm afraid it's not enough... right?"
Ye Tian said.
"Naturally, it's not based on guesswork alone!"
World Ancestor continued, "Once, when the Dark Destruction Domain invaded the Dark Holy Domain again, I had just promoted to Ancestor. The Holy Ancestor had just lost the power boost from the Dark Holy Domain, and the Dark Holy Domain was at its weakest. The Holy Ancestor was no match for the Destruction Ancestor, and the Destruction Ancestor brought out a terrifying treasure capable of slaying an Elite Ancestor. At that time, the Holy Ancestor was still an Elite Ancestor. Other Ancestors were busy in battle and didn't pay attention to the fight between the Holy Ancestor and the Destruction Ancestor, but I was different. I have a special method that allows me to perceive the battles and any slight fluctuations throughout the entire Dark Holy Domain.
At that moment, the strike from the treasure unleashed by the Destruction Ancestor was blocked by a single finger."
"I did not sense it wrongly; it was indeed a finger. Although it was fleeting, it was definitely a finger, and then it vanished.
Subsequently, the Destruction Ancestor retreated and did not dare to invade the Dark Holy Domain again.
Since then, the battles between the Dark Destruction Domain and the Dark Holy Domain have not involved Ancestors; they have all been minor skirmishes!"
"Previously, I was too weak to perceive the strength of that finger's owner, but I know now. That was definitely a top-tier Ancestor, and one many times more powerful than top-tier Ancestors like the Destruction Ancestor or the Holy Ancestor.
That person acted for the sake of the Holy Ancestor, so they likely have a deep relationship. Thus, I suspect he guided the Holy Ancestor and might even be the Holy Ancestor's master, the most ancient top-tier Ancestor of the Dark Forbidden Domain."
After World Ancestor finished speaking, Ye Tian began to take it somewhat seriously.
Although his current strength had reached the level of the highest top-tier Ancestor combat power and wasn't far from the limit of a top-tier Ancestor,
he was very clear that he was likely not yet invincible at the top-tier Ancestor level.
Some of the most ancient top-tier Ancestors likely had combat power that had reached a point where no further progress was possible.
He naturally wouldn't deliberately make an enemy of such a top-tier Ancestor, but the key was that those top-tier Ancestors might become his enemies.
After all, the Human Race had produced Ancestors one after another and cultivated an Ancestral World, and his own strength was comparable to a top-tier Elite Ancestor as soon as he broke through. All of this defied the understanding of the Ancestors.
All Ancestors knew he possessed a great secret; they just weren't confident in dealing with him.
But if one day those top-tier Ancestors united, he would truly be in some danger.
If not for World Ancestor's reminder this time, he really would have thought he was perfectly safe and nearly invincible.
"Although I feel I've reached the peak of a top-tier Ancestor, my strength can actually still improve a lot. But if I just cultivate slowly, the speed of improvement won't be very fast. My current rate of improvement is already very slow unless I obtain a great opportunity!"
Ye Tian thought to himself.
Great opportunities were rare. Currently, there were almost no opportunities in the Dark Forbidden Domain, except for those forbidden zones.
"The six major forbidden zones are too dangerous for me, but there are records of other forbidden zones where Ancestors have fallen, yet some have also escaped and survived.
Those Ancestors might not have obtained good things, but it doesn't matter if my duplicate bodies perish, as long as I don't encounter methods that can wipe out my original body through a duplicate body."
Ye Tian thought to himself.
In short, there was a sliver of risk, but the risk was not great.
Besides, he couldn't just stay huddled here cultivating forever. If he did, he would almost never be able to break the shackles of a top-tier Ancestor and charge into the level of a Supreme Ancestor.
In the following days, Ye Tian began to communicate with various Ancestors to gather information about the forbidden zones.
Those Ancestors might not reveal all the information, but they would at least disclose a little. Combined with the information from War Ancestor and World Ancestor, Ye Tian gained a better understanding of these forbidden zones.
Below the six major forbidden zones, there were dozens of forbidden zones that were dangerous even for Ancestors, but there were only eight that were considered very dangerous even for top-tier Ancestors. Other forbidden zones posed no danger to top-tier Ancestors, only to ordinary and Elite Ancestors.
Therefore, even if ordinary forbidden zones had good things, they had long since been scavenged.
Thus, Ye Tian's targets were those eight top-tier forbidden zones.
After some screening, Ye Tian chose one of them—the Bone Sea Forbidden Zone.
This forbidden zone contained many mysterious bones, which was how it got its name.
The Bone Sea Forbidden Zone was extremely dangerous. Even top-tier Ancestors did not dare to go deep; they only dared to linger on the outskirts for a few breaths. This way, they wouldn't perish. If they went even a little deeper or stayed a bit longer, they would likely be in danger.
Within the Bone Sea, there existed a special kind of creature—Bone Soldiers.
These Bone Soldiers were somewhat like the Bone Race of the three thousand evil races in the Dark Destruction Domain, but the difference in strength between the two was like heaven and earth.
An ordinary Bone Soldier possessed the combat power of an ordinary Ancestor, and there were many such Bone Soldiers, at least a thousand of them. There were also Bone Generals and Bone Kings.
Among them, Bone Generals possessed the combat power of an Elite Ancestor, and Bone Kings possessed the combat power of a top-tier Ancestor.
With so many Ancestor-level entities, once surrounded, even a top-tier Ancestor would have no chance of escaping.
As for what opportunities existed in the Bone Sea Forbidden Zone, only one is currently known: the Bone Beads.
Once, the Destruction Ancestor had sneaked into the Bone Sea Forbidden Zone, killed a Bone Soldier, and obtained a Bone Bead. According to the news revealed by the Destruction Ancestor, Bone Beads could increase one's cultivation, but no one dared to go in to hunt Bone Soldiers.
Because even the Destruction Ancestor had returned heavily injured and almost didn't make it back.
"Bone Beads can increase cultivation; they suit me. If my duplicate bodies can kill more Bone Soldiers and bring back some Bone Beads, then I can increase my strength in a short period of time!"
Ye Tian thought.

Chapter 1485: The Effect of the Bone Beads!

Chapter 1485: The Effect of the Bone Beads
!
In front of the Bone Sea Forbidden Zone.
Ye Tian did not hesitate for long before resolutely stepping into the Bone Sea Forbidden Zone.
Boom! Endless pressure surged forth, many times stronger than the pressure outside. If an ordinary Domain Ancestor entered this place, they would likely be crushed to pieces by the pressure in an instant.
In such a place, even a Progenitor would find it difficult to exert the same destructive power they possessed in the outside world.
Of course, while he was suppressed, the Bone Soldiers and Bone Generals within the Bone Sea Forbidden Zone were also suppressed, making it quite fair.
As soon as Ye Tian entered the Bone Sea Forbidden Zone, he immediately attracted the attention of the Bone Soldiers inside.
Suddenly, a large number of Bone Soldiers swarmed toward him.
Ten Bone Generals and over a thousand Bone Soldiers charged to surround and kill him, while the Bone Kings did not move.
The Bone Kings were likely too lazy to act. After all, if they had to act every time a Progenitor entered, they would be annoyed to death if Progenitors constantly sent avatars to harass them. Moreover, ten Bone Generals plus a thousand Bone Soldiers were enough to surround and kill a top-tier Progenitor.
If they truly couldn't win, the Bone Kings would naturally step in.
Ye Tian's goal this time was clear: kill a few Bone Soldiers, seize the Bone Beads, and then leave.
He wasn't greedy; otherwise, he wouldn't be able to obtain even a single Bone Bead.
"Kill!"
Ye Tian performed several Ultimate Ancestral Techniques. With the Ancestral Armor technique and the Dao Robe Ultimate Ancestral Technique, the two could be stacked, naturally causing his life-preserving capabilities to soar.
Immediately after, Ye Tian unleashed the Golden Wings Ultimate Ancestral Technique and the Streaming Light Ultimate Ancestral Technique, pushing his speed to the limit as he charged toward the Bone Soldiers. He then executed the Tyrant Strength Ultimate Ancestral Technique and the Extreme Arm Ultimate Ancestral Technique, throwing a punch at a Bone Soldier! With a loud boom, the Bone Soldier was shattered by Ye Tian's punch, leaving behind a Bone Bead.
Ye Tian immediately collected the Bone Bead.
At the same time, the thousand Bone Soldiers and ten Bone Generals attacked together. Even though Ye Tian was very fast, he was still hit by some of the attacks.
However, his defense was too powerful. With the two defensive Ultimate Ancestral Techniques stacked, the Dao Robe technique was broken, but the second layer, the Ancestral Armor technique, held firm. Consequently, he only suffered minor injuries, which were of little concern.
"Kill!"
Ye Tian struck back, shattering another Bone Soldier and obtaining a second Bone Bead.
"You seek death!!!"
Roars echoed from the depths of the Bone Sea Forbidden Zone.
Clearly, Ye Tian's killing of two Bone Soldiers had enraged the Bone Kings.
Rumble! Ten Bone Kings traveled from the depths of the Bone King Forbidden Zone. Each Bone King was incredibly powerful; in Ye Tian's eyes, they were all stronger than the Destruction Progenitor, at least three or four times as powerful.
There was no telling how many Bone Kings were here. Once surrounded by ten Bone Kings, it would be very difficult for him to escape.
Although he wasn't worried about the safety of his duplicated body, if the duplicated body fell, he wouldn't be able to bring the Bone Beads back.
Thus, while fleeing, Ye Tian killed one more Bone Soldier before quickly escaping the Bone Sea Forbidden Zone.
These Bone Kings did not dare to chase him out of the Bone Sea Forbidden Zone. There seemed to be some kind of restriction, though the exact nature of it was unclear.
"Three Bone Beads, not bad at all!"
Ye Tian said excitedly.
However, this was his first time entering the Bone Sea Forbidden Zone, and the Bone Kings had been careless, which allowed him to obtain three Bone Beads at once.
Next time, he would likely not have such an opportunity.
Because once he entered the Bone Sea Forbidden Zone again, the Bone Kings would surely take action immediately.
"Whatever, I'll refine these three Bone Beads first and see the effects!"
Ye Tian's duplicated body returned to the Mystic Void Ancestral Realm and handed the three Bone Beads to his original body.
Subsequently, Ye Tian's original body began to absorb and refine one Bone Bead.
Boom! Countless amounts of pure energy flooded into Ye Tian's Endless Progenitor Body, rapidly tempering it, nourishing his soul, and strengthening his Progenitor power.
"This effect..."
Ye Tian was shocked.
Compared to the effect of the Bone Beads, those Nirvana treasures were simply trash!
"Top-tier Progenitors don't dare to enter the Bone Sea Forbidden Zone because they could easily perish, and even if they do enter, it's very difficult to kill a single Bone Soldier.
Otherwise, the Progenitors would all take the risk.
But for me, my duplicated body isn't afraid of death. The Bone Sea Forbidden Zone is a treasure land for me, not a forbidden zone!"
Ye Tian murmured.
In the following days, Ye Tian continued to refine the Bone Beads.
His cultivation continued to rise, and his strength was also rapidly increasing.
It took him nearly ten thousand years to refine one Bone Bead. Now that thirty thousand years had passed, all three Bone Beads were completely refined.
At this moment, Ye Tian's strength had increased by ten percent.
Do not underestimate a ten percent increase in strength; to gain ten percent in just thirty thousand years—what if he had enough Bone Beads? Moreover, Ye Tian had already reached the pinnacle of top-tier Progenitor combat power. To be able to increase his strength by ten percent at such a level was truly terrifying!
"I must get more Bone Beads! Perhaps with my foundation, I can possess combat power comparable to a Supreme Progenitor while still at the top-tier Progenitor level!"
Ye Tian thought to himself.
Soon, Ye Tian's duplicated body arrived at the Bone Sea Forbidden Zone once again.
This time, as soon as Ye Tian entered the Bone Sea Forbidden Zone, ten Bone Kings moved out to surround and kill him.
All around him, there were also a large number of Bone Soldiers and Bone Generals assisting.
It could be said that Ye Tian was trapped in a heavy siege.
In the end, Ye Tian fought desperately. At all costs, he managed to kill one Bone Soldier and obtain a Bone Bead, escaping with a body that was nearly annihilated.
Such injuries would be fatal for an ordinary Progenitor because their Progenitor source would be almost exhausted.
But since this was a duplicated body, Ye Tian didn't care.
After obtaining another Bone Bead, Ye Tian's cultivation improved significantly.
However, Ye Tian knew very well that the next time he entered the Bone Sea Forbidden Zone, he would likely face not ten Bone Kings, but even more.
So, Ye Tian used his duplicated body to test the strength of the Bone Sea Forbidden Zone.
When Ye Tian entered the Bone Sea Forbidden Zone again, he indeed encountered twenty Bone Kings and was brutally killed.
"It's no use. If the duplicated body enters again, the result will still be death by siege. I can only resort to... another method!"
Ye Tian murmured.
His other method was... to duplicate the body of a Bone Race member and enter the Bone Sea Forbidden Zone with a Bone Race identity.
"I can't duplicate a Bone King. Bone Kings have high status in the Bone Sea Forbidden Zone; if a strange Bone King suddenly appeared, it would be easily recognized.
If I duplicate the body of a Bone Soldier, the possibility of exposure will be lower."
Ye Tian thought to himself.
Of course, even if he duplicated a Bone Soldier's body, he wouldn't appear in front of other Bone Soldiers. Instead, he would hide and investigate the situation of the Bone Race.
After all, if the Bone Soldier he duplicated met the original person, he would be exposed immediately.
Ye Tian had fought those Bone Soldiers for a long time, so he could naturally duplicate their bodies.
Ye Tian randomly chose a Bone Soldier and prepared to begin the duplication.
However.
When he performed the duplication, an accident occurred.
Boom! The duplicated Bone Soldier body was instantly annihilated.
It was forcibly annihilated by the source of the Dark Forbidden Domain.
Bone Soldiers were not allowed to appear in the Dark Forbidden Domain.
This was the reason why Bone Soldiers, Bone Generals, and Bone Kings did not dare to come out; they would be annihilated the moment they emerged.

Chapter 1486: Turning into a Bone Soldier, Infiltration!

Chapter 1486: Turning into a Bone Soldier, Infiltration
!
"Bone Soldiers are not allowed to exist in the Dark Forbidden Domain. I didn't expect it to be like this!"
Ye Tian said in surprise.
He had thought that the Bone Sea Forbidden Land was what restricted those Bone Soldiers, Bone Generals, and Bone Kings. He hadn't expected that it wasn't the Bone Sea Forbidden Land restricting them; they could actually leave the Bone Sea Forbidden Land. However, the sole price of leaving was... instant annihilation.
Consequently, they did not dare to come out.
"It seems I cannot replicate a Bone Soldier in the Dark Forbidden Domain. In that case, my main body will go to the Bone Sea Forbidden Land, thrust one hand into it, and then replicate the Bone Soldier body so that it appears directly inside the Bone Sea Forbidden Land. That should work fine."
Ye Tian thought to himself.
And so.
Ye Tian's main body arrived at the Bone Sea Forbidden Land. He instantly thrust one hand into the Bone Sea Forbidden Land and replicated a Bone Soldier's body.
In the next instant, Ye Tian withdrew his hand.
The Bone Soldier body appeared within the Bone Sea Forbidden Land and immediately moved away from that area. Soon, a powerful divine sense swept over to investigate. Finding no trace of an outsider, it paid no further mind.
Some Bone Kings sensed Ye Tian's Bone Soldier body, but they didn't care, as it was a genuine Bone Soldier.
...."I must be careful next. Otherwise, if this Bone Soldier body falls, it will be easily discovered if I try this method again!"
Ye Tian thought to himself.
Thus, he did his best to control his aura and did not enter the depths of the Bone Sea Forbidden Land. He only wandered the outskirts to understand the situation here.
The Bone Sea Forbidden Land contained massive bone mountains. On each bone mountain, there were Bone Soldiers cultivating, and even some Bone Generals.
Therefore, Ye Tian did not dare to approach these bone mountains. After sensing the auras of the Bone Soldiers and Bone Generals from a distance, he would move far away.
There were no Bone Kings in the outer perimeter, and he didn't know why the Bone Kings didn't guard the outskirts.
In the blink of an eye, ten years passed.
Ye Tian didn't encounter any trouble during these ten years. After all, he was extremely cautious, and these Bone Soldiers rarely perished; most were constantly in bitter cultivation.
There were fewer Bone Soldiers in the outer perimeter, while there were more Bone Soldiers and Bone Generals in the interior of the Bone Sea Forbidden Land. However, if he approached, it would be easy to run into the actual Bone Soldier he had replicated.
It wasn't that he hadn't thought about replicating a deceased Bone Soldier, but that would be even more dangerous.
Because the Bone Soldiers of the Bone Sea Forbidden Land likely all knew which of their comrades had died in battle. If one suddenly reappeared, it would be strange if they weren't investigated. His replicated body might even be discovered by the Bone Kings the moment it appeared, leading to the discovery of the problem.
That was why he didn't dare choose a deceased Bone Soldier as a replication template.
"I can't obtain much intelligence on the outskirts of the Bone Sea Forbidden Land. I should head deeper!"
Ye Tian decided.
Although this decision was risky, at worst, this replicated body would just perish, and he would have to find other ways to obtain Bone Beads later.
Thus, Ye Tian cautiously ventured deep into the Bone Sea Forbidden Land.
Ye Tian's luck seemed good; without much trouble, he easily entered the depths of the Bone Sea Forbidden Land.
At this time, he saw a massive bone mountain. This bone mountain was covered with buildings.
Ye Tian directly approached this bone mountain and entered it.
This bone mountain seemed to be a trading mountain. Many Bone Soldiers and Bone Generals were trading here, and there were even some shops.
Seeing this bizarre scene, Ye Tian found it somewhat hard to believe.
It was just a small forbidden land, yet it actually had a place for trade. This was just like the Ancestors of the Dark Forbidden Domain; with so few Ancestors living in one area, how could it develop into a place of trade? "The number of Bone Soldiers here is likely very large, far beyond my imagination!"
Ye Tian realized.
Sure enough, he saw many, many Bone Soldiers. Just the number of Bone Soldiers he could see right now was in the thousands.
Among them, some Bone Soldiers seemed to recognize him and greeted him, but he did not respond, fearing he would say the wrong thing.
But those Bone Soldiers didn't seem to care, as if they didn't have much of a friendship.
If this were the outside world, the Ancestors would perceive everything with a single thought, and he would likely be discovered quickly.
But here, things were heavily suppressed. Even an Ancestor couldn't know everything. Divine sense couldn't probe very far, and there were many Bone Soldiers. Many Bone Soldiers stayed in their residences or were even constantly in seclusion, so their auras wouldn't spread out.
Therefore, as long as Ye Tian's Bone Soldier body didn't come into close contact with that specific Bone Soldier, it wouldn't be easily discovered.
The greater possibility was that the Bone Soldier was currently cultivating, hadn't come out, and wasn't sensing the outside situation. Thus, Ye Tian would not be exposed for the time being.
However, over a long period, he would definitely be exposed.
Soon, Ye Tian arrived at a shop.
The owner of the shop was a Bone General. Seeing Ye Tian arrive, he said, "Xiao Zai, I heard you were injured while following the Bone Kings to besiege an Ancestor of the Dark Forbidden Domain. I didn't expect you to recover so quickly! What, have you come to my place to buy some treasures?"
"Just looking!"
Ye Tian said indifferently.
"These are newly arrived goods, take a look!"
This Bone General took out a treasure orb. Inside the orb were various treasures.
Ye Tian didn't know what these treasures were. Moreover, he knew nothing about this place and had no local currency, so he naturally wouldn't actually buy anything.
He currently wanted Bone Beads, but even more, he wanted to know the situation here.
He felt that this place was far from simple. Having so many Bone Soldiers, Bone Generals, and Bone Kings comparable to Ancestors was too abnormal! Furthermore, this Bone General mentioned the Dark Forbidden Domain, indicating they knew about the situation outside.
"Sigh, I don't know what's up with that Ancestor lately. He's entered several times, and I almost died!"
Ye Tian lamented.
The Bone General nodded: "Indeed, this didn't happen in the past. The Dark Forbidden Domain is very weak, and those Ancestors are few in number and value their lives more. I didn't expect a top-tier Ancestor to enter our base multiple times and kill several Ancestor-level Bone Soldiers. However, that top-tier Ancestor still died!"
Clearly, the Bone Race of the Bone Sea Forbidden Land thought Ye Tian's replicated body was his main body, completely unaware that it was merely a replicated body.
Ye Tian continued to chat with this Bone General, gathering intelligence through indirect means. Although he made the Bone General feel suspicious several times in the middle—feeling that Ye Tian's speech was somewhat abnormal—the other party didn't doubt Ye Tian's identity. He only thought that Ye Tian's frequent injuries hadn't fully healed, making him a bit muddled.
But in the end, Ye Tian still obtained some useful intelligence.
For example, this shop occasionally went to get stock. As for where they got the stock, he wasn't entirely sure, but it was definitely not the Bone Sea Forbidden Land.
This indicated that the Bone Sea Forbidden Land was connected to another place.
Second, the Bone Ancestors comparable to Ancestors were called Ancestor-level Bone Soldiers, Ancestor-level Bone Generals, and Ancestor-level Bone Kings, and they were called the War Bone Race.
Third, the War Bone Race had once entered the Dark Forbidden Domain, but they couldn't enter now. Moreover, the War Bone Race desperately needed the resources of the Dark Forbidden Domain. It was said that the resources of the Dark Forbidden Domain were of great help to the War Bone Race, significantly enhancing their cultivation and strength.
Just as Bone Beads were of great help to Ye Tian.
But he couldn't fish for any more intelligence, because if he continued to probe indirectly, he feared something would go wrong.
Thus, he hurriedly left the place.


Chapter 1487: Harvesting Eighteen Bone Beads!

The Bone Soldiers and Bone Generals would chat normally; they didn't believe any Ancestor could infiltrate this place, so they were completely unguarded and talked about everything.
Gradually, Ye Tian learned about the situation.

Every Bone Mountain treasure land would produce resources that were extremely precious to the Bone Race.
Therefore, the Bone Sea Forbidden Land was a treasure land for the Bone Race, which was why they stayed here, occasionally coming across precious resources.
Furthermore, whoever discovered a precious resource owned it; even the Bone Kings could not seize their treasures.

Every Bone Race member could leave this place at any time, and a new Bone Race member would take their place.
From this, it was evident that there were many Ancestor-level Bone Race members, their numbers likely exceeding Ye Tian's imagination.
If so many Bone Race members were to all appear in the Dark Forbidden Domain, the major factions wouldn't be able to stop them and would be wiped out in an instant.

Bone Stones were divided into many grades, and the Bone Stones used by these Ancestor-level Bone Soldiers were Ancestral Bone Stones. They could restore combat consumption and slowly increase cultivation, so they were used as currency.

The risk of a Bone Soldier being exposed was smaller, but their strength was too weak, making it unrealistic to try and kill other Bone Soldiers.

But even so, if Ye Tian wanted to instantly kill a Bone Soldier, he still couldn't do it.
Moreover, once a battle broke out, it would inevitably attract the attention of other Bone Race members, making it impossible to keep hidden.
Ye Tian's current plan was... to obtain enough Bone Beads or other resources that would be of great help to him, allowing his own strength to reach a terrifying level so that he would no longer... need to use this sneaky method.
At that time, he would sweep through the Bone Sea Forbidden Land with absolute strength, slaughtering large numbers of Bone Soldiers to obtain Bone Beads.

Clearly, that Bone Soldier's injuries were not light, and he was still: healing.

These Bone Soldiers were stunned, but he was not. He continued to snatch resources at extreme speed.

And Ye Tian, relying on his terrifying speed and powerful strength, had snatched many treasures.

Not all Bone Race resources were very effective for him; some resources overlapped with those in the Dark Forbidden Domain, so their effects were poor.
Currently, he only knew that Bone Beads were of great help to Ancestors.

A fake Bone Soldier had mixed into the Bone Sea Forbidden Land, disguised himself as a Bone Soldier, and purchased many Bone Beads, and they hadn't even noticed.

Xuanxu Ancestral Realm.
