At that point, he would be in danger.

Chapter 1489: The Strongest Emperor Artifact!

Chapter 1489: The Strongest Emperor Artifact!
!
Currently, there were twenty-five Bone Kings in the Bone Sea Forbidden Land. The weakest among them was comparable to a Destruction Ancestor, while the most powerful had reached the peak of a top-tier Ancestor. Yet, they were still no match for Ye Tian; otherwise, they wouldn't be so helpless against him.
At this moment, these twenty-five Bone Kings were extremely nervous.
"Everyone, what should we do? That top-tier Ancestor from the Dark Forbidden Domain is far too powerful. He likely possesses combat power nearing that of a Strongest Ancestor. A Strongest Ancestor of the Dark Forbidden Domain is comparable to a Bone Emperor, and if a Bone Emperor were to forcibly descend here, they would have to pay a massive price.
But if we leave him be...
Then after some time passes and that top-tier Ancestor refines those Bone Beads, his strength will surge, and we won't be able to stop him. Those Ancestor-level Bone Soldiers and Bone Generals will likely be slaughtered by him in massive numbers, becoming the opportunities for his growth," one Bone King said.

The other Bone Kings chimed in one after another.
Evacuate? What a joke. They had paid an incredibly heavy price to establish the Bone Sea Forbidden Land. This was their hope. Improving their combat power was almost hopeless.
By the same token, the Bone Race was the same; they also had to rely on the resources of the Dark Forbidden Domain to quickly increase their strength.
Because the Bone Sea Forbidden Land was born within the Dark Forbidden Domain, although its rules differed from those of the Dark Forbidden Domain, it was still influenced by them. Consequently, the resources born here had a significant effect on them. Over a long period of time, they could still increase their strength somewhat.
However, they could not withstand the rules of the Dark Forbidden Domain. Once they entered the Dark Forbidden Domain itself, they would surely die.
But the Dark Forbidden Domain would experience Great Calamities time and again, just as the Realm Worlds would.
During a Great Calamity, the origin of the Dark Forbidden Domain would fall into chaos and its rules would weaken. They would only need to pay a certain price to enter the Dark Forbidden Domain, plunder its resources, and thereby strengthen the Bone Race.
Last time, they had broken into the Dark Forbidden Domain and obtained immense benefits.
The Dark Forbidden Domain was relatively young, so its strength was weak, and it didn't have many Ancestors... it was unable to compete with them. Only other places with foundations similar to theirs could pose a threat.
The Bone Race's discovery of the Dark Forbidden Domain was a massive opportunity for them.
Last time, the Bone Race plundered the resources of the Dark Forbidden Domain, leading to the birth of several Bone Emperors.
Therefore, how could they possibly abandon such a great opportunity? Even if it meant paying the price of a large number of Bone Soldiers, they could not abandon the Bone Sea Forbidden Land. Once abandoned, they would have no hope of entering the Dark Forbidden Domain again, or they would have to pay an even more staggering price.
"Then let us call for reinforcements!"
The Bone Kings reached a decision.
As for having a Bone Emperor guard this place, that was the final resort. Unless they were driven into a desperate situation, they would not employ such a method.
After all, once they did so, the price the Bone Emperor would pay would be too great. Their strength would plummet, and it might even affect their origin, preventing them from making any progress for countless ages.
Thus, requesting some Bone Kings to guard this place was something that could be done.
Soon.
The Bone Race dispatched another twenty Bone Kings, including one extremely powerful top-tier Bone King who was not even weaker than the combat power Ye Tian had previously displayed.
The Bone Race felt that by dispatching so many Bone Kings to guard the Bone Sea Forbidden Land, even if Ye Tian dared to enter again, they would be certain to suppress and kill him.
...At this time, Ye Tian was in the Profound Void Ancestral World refining Bone Beads.
This time, he had obtained many Bone Beads. After refining them, his strength continued to rise.
Nearly a million years passed, and he had refined all thirty-plus Bone Soldier Beads, allowing his strength to increase significantly once more.
But at this point, Ye Tian felt that his cultivation had still not reached its limit.
Consequently, Ye Tian continued to refine those two Bone General Beads.
The energy contained within a Bone General Bead naturally far exceeded that of a Bone Soldier Bead. The effect of these two Bone General Beads was likely comparable to those thirty-plus Bone Soldier Beads.
After all, Ye Tian had refined many Bone Soldier Beads, so their effectiveness would naturally decrease, whereas he had never refined a Bone General Bead before. Once he refined them, his strength would likely increase by a large margin.
By then, his strength would definitely allow him to kill a Bone General in a single strike, or even heavily injure a Bone King in one blow.
If it were a top-tier Ancestor like the Destruction Ancestor, he could kill them within a few moves.
"Refine!"
Ye Tian spent a full million years to completely refine the two Bone General Beads, and his strength surged tremendously.
Without treasures like Bone Beads, simply absorbing and refining Nirvana treasures was of no use to Ye Tian anymore. Bitter cultivation also held no meaning unless he could create a more powerful ultimate ancestral technique, or perhaps an ancestral technique above the ultimate level; otherwise, his cultivation would not be able to increase his strength.
"I still have to target the Bone Beads!"
Ye Tian thought to himself.
One day.
Ye Tian duplicated his body and sent the duplicate into the Bone Sea Forbidden Land once again.
When Ye Tian descended upon the Bone Sea Forbidden Land, forty-five Bone Kings appeared and joined forces to besiege him, with a large number of Bone Generals assisting them.
Otherwise, if the forty-five Bone Kings failed to stop him, wouldn't he be able to charge into their home base? At that time, even more Bone Soldiers would perish, and there was even a possibility that he might damage the Bone Race's most important treasure—the Gate! Therefore, the large number of Bone Generals forming a formation was able to withstand Ye Tian's offensive.
However, they still underestimated Ye Tian's determination.
Ye Tian attacked the Bone Generals desperately, not caring about his own injuries in the slightest.
In the end, at the cost of being heavily injured and on the verge of death, Ye Tian killed six Bone Generals, took their Bone Beads, and escaped from the Bone Sea Forbidden Land.
If it were a real top-tier Ancestor possessing strength like Ye Tian's, they would never act so recklessly. Even if they truly wanted to deal with the Bone Sea Forbidden Land, they would surely combine the strength of all Ancestors to invade, rather than using such a life-risking method.
It was only because Ye Tian did not worry about the death of his duplicate body that he dared to disregard his life so completely.
After obtaining the six Bone General Beads, Ye Tian began secluded cultivation to refine them, and his strength continued to improve.
Meanwhile, the Bone Kings of the Bone Sea Forbidden Land had fallen into a predicament.
They were well aware that forty-five Bone Kings were still unable to quickly kill Ye Tian.
Of course, they believed that Ye Tian's strength had definitely reached the absolute limit of a top-tier Ancestor and could not be improved further. Therefore, even if he obtained six Bone General Beads, he would definitely be unable to break through the shackles and become a Strongest Ancestor.
Thus, they still did not invite a Bone Emperor to guard the place. Instead, they mobilized another dozen or so Bone Kings and brought along a Strongest Emperor Artifact.
Even the Bone Race did not possess many Strongest Emperor Artifacts. By deploying one this time, it could be said they placed immense importance on the Bone Sea Forbidden Land.
With so many Bone Kings plus a Strongest Emperor Artifact, once Ye Tian entered the Bone Sea Forbidden Land again, they would absolutely be able to suppress and kill him.

Chapter 1490: Twenty Ultimate Defensive Ancestral Techniques!

Chapter 1490: Twenty Ultimate Defensive Ancestral Techniques
!
Xuanxu Ancestral Realm.
Ye Tian's cultivation continued to rise, and his combat power grew stronger and stronger, as if there were no end to it.
However, Ye Tian knew very well that he was fast approaching the limit of a top-tier Ancestor.
Furthermore, even the Bone General Bone Beads were no longer providing a significant boost to his strength. Perhaps after refining these six Bone General Bone Beads, refining more would only yield a third or even a fifth of the original effect.
"With my current cultivation and strength, if I were to refine Bone Soldier Bone Beads, the effect would likely be negligible,"
Ye Tian thought to himself.
This was just like Nirvana treasures; if one refined too many, further refinement would have no effect.
It was similar to how an ordinary person develops resistance after taking too much of a certain medicine; the same applied to Ancestors.
"Regardless, I'll refine all six Bone General Bone Beads first, and then continue to snatch more!"
Ye Tian murmured.
Millions of years passed. Under Ye Tian's full effort, all six Bone General Bone Beads were completely refined.
By this time, Ye Tian's strength had received a massive boost, becoming much more powerful than before.
Consequently, Ye Tian once again used a duplicate body to break into the Bone Sea Forbidden Land.
....Bone Sea Forbidden Land.
As soon as Ye Tian entered, he sensed a large number of Bone King auras.
"Sixty Bone Kings! The Bone Race actually dispatched so many experts!!!"
Ye Tian was surprised.
Boom!!!! Sixty Bone Kings crossed over and surrounded Ye Tian, attacking him from all sides.
During the battle, one of the Bone Kings sacrificed a bone sword.
The moment this bone sword appeared, Ye Tian felt the aura of death.
"What kind of weapon is this?"
Although Ye Tian did not panic, he was shocked.
It didn't matter if the duplicate body died, but he had never seen such a terrifying weapon in the Dark Forbidden Domain.
He was certain that the Holy Ancestor and the Destruction Ancestor definitely did not possess such a thing; otherwise, they would have used it the last time they dealt with him.
Had they used such a weapon, he definitely wouldn't have been able to contend with the Destruction Ancestor last time and would have been instantly killed.
"Die, Ancestor of the Dark Forbidden Domain!"
The Bone King roared.
Boom!!!! The bone sword transformed into a beam of light and pierced toward Ye Tian.
At this moment, time and space were frozen. Even a powerful force could not break the spatial-temporal lock; it was as if no power could contend with this... bone sword.
"Break for me!!!!"
Ye Tian roared inwardly, mobilizing all his power and activating one Ultimate Ancestral Technique after another. Only then did he manage to break free from the constraints.
However, he still could not dodge the bone sword.
Puchi!!!! The bone sword pierced through Ye Tian's body, but it did not kill him; it only heavily wounded him.
After unleashing this strike, that Bone King's aura became incredibly weak, clearly the price for using the bone sword.
But at this moment, Ye Tian was on the verge of death and could not take the opportunity to kill this Bone King.
The other Bone Kings seized the chance and immediately attacked Ye Tian, while one Bone King escorted the weakened one away from the battlefield.
Before long, Ye Tian's duplicate body was blasted apart and killed.
...."I didn't expect that after becoming so powerful, I would still be killed,"
Ye Tian said speechlessly.
He also understood very well that the reason he was killed was not because there were a dozen more Bone Kings, but because of that... bone sword.
That was definitely a powerful weapon used at the level of a Supreme Ancestor. Only such a weapon could heavily wound him to the point where even recovery-type Ancestral Techniques couldn't heal his injuries in time.
Ye Tian did not continue to send duplicate bodies. If he couldn't block that... bone sword, no matter how many times he sent a duplicate, he wouldn't be able to obtain bone beads and would only be killed over and over again.
"I must strengthen my defense!"
Ye Tian thought.
He had always felt his defense was very strong, yet even with two defensive Ultimate Ancestral Techniques stacked, he was still pierced by the bone sword.
"Two defensive Ultimate Ancestral Techniques can't contend with that bone sword, but what if there were three or even four?"
Ye Tian pondered.
Defensive Ultimate Ancestral Techniques were easy to stack, whereas offensive ones were indeed difficult, if not impossible, to stack.
Therefore, if he could create stackable defensive Ultimate Ancestral Techniques, he might be able to withstand the attack of that... bone sword.
"In the coming years, I will focus on creating defensive Ultimate Ancestral Techniques!"
Ye Tian decided.
He had plenty of experience in creating Ultimate Ancestral Techniques, and with his current cultivation level, the speed at which he could create them was naturally faster.
According to Ye Tian's estimation, he could create at least two to three defensive Ultimate Ancestral Techniques per Realm Year.
As he progressed, he might even be able to create more.
Although activating Ultimate Ancestral Techniques consumed a lot of energy—and unleashing multiple ones at once would drain a large portion of his Ancestral Power—as long as he could block a single strike from the bone sword, he could kill several Bone Generals in a short amount of time.
Time flowed slowly as Ye Tian continued to create defensive Ultimate Ancestral Techniques.
Meanwhile, the Bone Kings of the Bone Race, seeing that no Ancestor had entered the Bone Sea Forbidden Land for a long time, assumed that Ye Tian had suffered heavy losses. They believed that the death of his clone must have come at a great cost, requiring a long time to recover, and thus they all breathed a sigh of relief.
As time passed, some Bone Kings returned to the Bone Race.
In the blink of an eye, ten Realm Years had passed.
By now, the Bone Kings in the Bone Sea Forbidden Land had already forgotten about Ye Tian.
However, no one knew how many... defensive Ultimate Ancestral Techniques Ye Tian had created during this long period.
"Hahaha, eighteen defensive Ultimate Ancestral Techniques! It's a pity I can't seem to create any more; it's as if some unseen force is limiting me from creating more defensive Ultimate Ancestral Techniques!"
Ye Tian murmured.
Because of this limitation, he had only created eighteen new ones. Adding the two he already knew, that made a total of twenty defensive Ultimate Ancestral Techniques.
Most of these defensive Ultimate Ancestral Techniques were shield-type techniques that could be fused and stacked.
Now, with twenty defensive Ultimate Ancestral Techniques, even a strike from that... bone sword wouldn't be able to hurt him, let alone the attacks of the Bone Kings.
If he kept all twenty defensive Ultimate Ancestral Techniques active, although he could only fight for a short... while before exhausting his Ancestral Power, he would likely be invincible during that time.
"This time, I must obtain enough bone beads, and maybe even a few Bone King Bone Beads!"
Ye Tian thought to himself.


Chapter 1491: Sweeping Through the Bone Sea Forbidden Land!

Chapter 1491: Sweeping Through the Bone Sea Forbidden Land
!
Bone Sea Forbidden Land.
It was very peaceful here. Bone soldiers and bone generals were cultivating, and even the Bone Kings were in meditation. There was no sense of tension, as if they had forgotten about Ye Tian's previous invasion of the Bone Sea Forbidden Land.
Furthermore, there were only thirty Bone Kings remaining here now; the other Bone Kings had already returned to the Bone Race.
On this day.
Ye Tian arrived at the Bone Sea Forbidden Land once again. As soon as he entered, his incompatible aura was naturally detected by the Bone Kings; no matter how he tried to hide, it was useless.
"Damn it, that Ancestor has actually come again!!!"
The Bone Kings roared in anger.
Boom!!!! Thirty Bone Kings moved to intercept Ye Tian, while a large number of bone generals formed battle arrays to block him. As for the bone soldiers, they fled as far away as they could.
Additionally, some bone soldiers returned to the Bone Race to seek reinforcements. Otherwise, relying solely on these Bone Kings, they would be unable to do anything to Ye Tian and might even lose more of their kinsmen.
Rumble!!!! Thirty Bone Kings besieged Ye Tian. They did not use the bone sword because it had already been sent back to the Bone Race.
After all, that was a Supreme Imperial Artifact and did not belong to them. Last time it was a temporary loan; it was impossible for it to be kept here indefinitely.
Without the Supreme Imperial Artifact, how could they deal with Ye Tian? Very quickly, Ye Tian discovered that they did not have that... bone sword, and he became instantly exhilarated.
Immediately, he began to deal with those bone generals.
"Kill!"
A battle array was blasted apart, and bone generals were heavily wounded one after another.
Then, with a squeeze of his hand, Ye Tian crushed a bone general into powder, leaving behind only a single bone bead, which he instantly collected.
Bang bang bang!!!! The bone generals had no power to fight back at all. They were blown apart one by one, turning into bone beads.
The Bone Kings were beyond furious. Bone generals were the high-level combat power of the Bone Race; losing even one was a significant loss, yet they were losing so many now.
Suddenly.
A Bone King was heavily wounded by a full-strength strike from Ye Tian. He was sent flying, the bones on his body cracking as if he were falling apart.
Although the cracks in the bones healed instantly, the injuries did not recover nearly as fast.
Next, Ye Tian aimed directly at this Bone King, attacking him with all his might. Under the successive attacks, this Bone King could no longer hold on and was in a state of being heavily wounded and near death.
The other Bone Kings wanted to stop him, but they couldn't.
Ye Tian's current strength was too powerful; it was simply not something they could withstand.
Moreover, at this moment, Ye Tian had deployed three defensive Ultimate Ancestral Techniques, completely ignoring the attacks of these Bone Kings as he desperately sought to slay one.
"Sha Bai, run!"
The other Bone Kings shouted urgently.
Sha Bai was the heavily wounded and dying Bone King.
However, his speed was too slow.
Ye Tian's speed was much faster than his—whenever he tried to flee, Ye Tian would intercept him.
Finally.
Under a punch from Ye Tian, this bone body completely shattered and could no longer heal, turning into a single bone bead.
This bone bead bore golden patterns and was far larger than an ordinary bone bead.
This was a Bone King's bone bead! With the fall of a Bone King, the bone generals were terrified, and even several Bone Kings panicked.
Bone Kings also feared falling. It was said that since they broke into this place, only a few had fallen when the Bone Sea Forbidden Land was first established, or during the Great Calamity of the Dark Forbidden Domain when they clashed with other powerful forces.
As for clashing with the Ancestors of the Dark Forbidden Domain, almost no Bone King had ever fallen.
But now, a Bone King had fallen at the hands of an Ancestor from the Dark Forbidden Domain.
"No one is allowed to flee! Besiege him with everything you have and wait for reinforcements to arrive!"
A Bone King commanded.
The bone generals had no choice and did not dare to flee. They desperately tried to stop Ye Tian, fearing that he would invade the Gate. Once the Gate was destroyed, they would be... the sinners of the Bone Race! Even though they knew very well that Ye Tian craved bone beads and that staying here meant death for the bone generals, they had to block Ye Tian even if it meant using their lives to pile up a defense.
Rumble!!!! One bone general after another continued to fall, and the Bone Kings were constantly injured, completely unable to contend with Ye Tian.
At this moment, they were also extremely anxious, wanting reinforcements to arrive as soon as possible.
Otherwise, the Bone Sea Forbidden Land would likely suffer the slaughter of a large number of bone generals and even Bone Kings.
Just then.
One Bone King after another passed through the Gate and arrived at the Bone Sea Forbidden Land. One of the Bone Kings held a bone sword—it was the Supreme Imperial Artifact of the Bone Race.
"Kill that Ancestor!"
The arriving Bone Kings roared in anger.
The Bone King holding the bone sword said nothing and began to activate the sword, vowing to use this... Supreme Imperial Artifact to blast Ye Tian to death.
Last time, they had... used this... Imperial Artifact to heavily wound Ye Tian, leaving him on the verge of death, and ultimately he was unable to contend with them and was killed in the siege.
They were certain they could achieve the same result this time. After all, a top-tier Ancestor could not contend with a Supreme Imperial Artifact.
Kill! The bone sword turned into a streak of light and lunged toward Ye Tian.
At this moment.
Ye Tian instantly activated those defensive Ultimate Ancestral Techniques.
A total of twenty defensive Ultimate Ancestral Techniques turned into layers of protective shields to guard Ye Tian.
Crack!!!! The bone sword pierced down, and layer after layer of shields were punctured.
But when it pierced through the tenth layer of shields, it finally came to a halt.
Ye Tian had blocked a strike from the Supreme Imperial Artifact.
Meanwhile, the Bone King who had activated the Supreme Imperial Artifact was now incredibly weak.
Ye Tian performed the Flowing Light Ultimate Ancestral Technique and approached that Bone King. Two Bone Kings tried to protect the weakened one, but unfortunately, they couldn't stop Ye Tian and were directly blasted away.
As for that incredibly weak Bone King, he had no power to resist and was killed by a single strike from Ye Tian.
A second Bone King had fallen! As for the Supreme Imperial Artifact, it also fell into Ye Tian's hands.
"Impossible! The Supreme Imperial Artifact actually couldn't wound him?"
The Bone Kings were filled with terror.
In their eyes, even an ordinary Supreme Ancestor level combatant wouldn't be able to take a hit from a Supreme Imperial Artifact without being injured!
In reality, to block that strike, Ye Tian had indeed consumed one-tenth (10%) of his Ancestral Power; only then did he manage to block the Supreme Imperial Artifact.
Next, Ye Tian deactivated some of the defensive Ultimate Ancestral Techniques; otherwise, he wouldn't be able to maintain his combat strength for long.
Soon, ten minutes passed.
During this time, Ye Tian slaughtered a large number of bone generals and killed yet another Bone King, meaning he had killed three Bone Kings in total.
Meanwhile, more Bone Kings from the Bone Race were arriving as reinforcements, and perhaps even more powerful members of the Bone Race would descend.
Coupled with the fact that the Ancestral Power in Ye Tian's body was severely depleted and his combat strength was declining sharply, if he fought much longer, his power would likely be exhausted.
Consequently, Ye Tian attempted to leave.
"Leave our race's Supreme Imperial Artifact behind!!!!"
Those Bone Kings went into a frenzy, but Ye Tian ignored them completely.
Whoosh! Protected by twenty layers of defensive Ultimate Ancestral Techniques, Ye Tian broke through the encirclement and left the Bone Sea Forbidden Land.
And at the moment he left, he seemed to sense a suffocating aura, and even the bone sword he had stowed away seemed as if it wanted to break through space and depart.
But once Ye Tian returned to the Dark Forbidden Domain, the bone sword settled down, and only a faint, indistinct roar of fury echoed out, shaking the entire Bone Sea Forbidden Land.

Chapter 1492: Attempting to Trade with the Bone Clan!

Chapter 1492: Attempting to Trade with the Bone Clan
!
"Hahaha, the harvest this time is simply too massive!!!"
Ye Tian was incredibly excited.
Three Bone King beads and one hundred and twenty-three Bone General beads.
What did this signify? It was equivalent to him killing three Top Ancestors and over a hundred Elite Ancestors in this single excursion.
And how many were there in the entire Dark Forbidden Domain... at least on the surface, there weren't even a hundred Elite Ancestors; at most, there were no more than ten.
It had to be said that the Bone Clan was incredibly powerful. This level of loss wouldn't shake their foundation, but for him, it was a monumental gain.
Once he refined all these bone beads, his strength would definitely rise to the absolute pinnacle of the Top Ancestor level.
And his pinnacle as a Top Ancestor would likely be comparable to an ordinary Supreme Ancestor.
"Refine!"
One by one, the bone beads were absorbed and refined by Ye Tian, tempering his body and strengthening his Ancestral power. His cultivation continued to rise, and his strength grew steadily.
In the blink of an eye, a hundred million years passed.
By this time, Ye Tian had finished refining all of the hundred-plus Bone General beads, and it was becoming difficult for his strength to increase further.
"There are still two Bone King beads left. Let's continue refining!"
Ye Tian thought to himself.
Boom!!!! The energy from the Bone King beads surged into Ye Tian's body, frantically tempering his Ancestral physique.
Under these circumstances, Ye Tian began to progress again, but the speed of improvement remained slow.
Ye Tian knew very well that his strength had reached the pinnacle of the Top Ancestor level. Even after refining these two Bone King beads, it would be difficult for his strength to increase by much...
In the blink of an eye, another few tens of millions of years passed.
Ye Tian had completely refined these two Bone King beads, but his cultivation could no longer progress even a single bit. His combat power had reached an absolute limit.
"I can't progress any further!"
Ye Tian murmured.
Even if he obtained more Bone King beads, he wouldn't be able to increase his strength.
Unless he could break through this shackle and promote to the Supreme Ancestor level.
However, he was well aware that the transition from Top Ancestor to Supreme Ancestor was not something that could be crossed simply by increasing cultivation. It surely involved some secret. Otherwise, there wouldn't be a total lack of legends regarding Supreme Ancestors in the Dark Forbidden Domain.
Even Ancestors like the Realm Ancestor only knew of ancient Ancestors in deep slumber, but those... ancient Ancestors were also only at the Top Ancestor realm. No Ancestor had ever stepped into the Supreme Ancestor level.
If there truly were Supreme Ancestors, they would have swept through the Bone Sea Forbidden Land long ago.
Since his cultivation could not improve and his Ultimate Ancestral Techniques were already at the peak of what Ancestral Techniques could be, he had no way to continue improving them. Once an Ultimate Ancestral Technique is created, it is the limit; that is why it is called "Ultimate."
With neither cultivation nor Ancestral Techniques able to improve, he had no way to increase his strength. He didn't even know how to go about increasing it.
Even if his Copying Talent was incredible, without a method to increase his strength, he naturally couldn't progress.
"When I left the Bone Sea Forbidden Land before, the Bone Clan dispatched a terrifying powerhouse. That aura definitely surpassed a Top Ancestor. Even a Supreme Ancestor might not be able to defeat them. That person was definitely comparable to a top-tier Supreme Ancestor.
Therefore, the Bone Clan must know the secret of how to break through to the Supreme Ancestor level!"
Ye Tian thought.
But would the Bone Clan tell him this secret? Suddenly.
Ye Tian took out a bone sword.
This... bone sword was a Supreme Imperial Weapon of the Bone Clan. He had already refined it, but he was unable to unleash its full power.
After all, this was a bone sword of the Bone Clan and was not suited for him.
However, to the Bone Clan, the value of this Supreme Imperial Weapon was definitely high. Perhaps he could use this... Supreme Imperial Weapon to exchange for the secret of reaching the Supreme Ancestor level.
Ye Tian did not bring this... Imperial Weapon with him, but instead sent a duplicated body to the location.
Even if this duplicated body perished in the Bone Sea... the Bone Sea Forbidden Land.
As soon as Ye Tian stepped into this place, he immediately drew the attention of the Bone Kings in the Bone Sea Forbidden Land.
At this moment.
The Bone Kings did not attack Ye Tian. The other Bone Generals and Bone Soldiers all retreated to the center of the Bone Sea Forbidden Land.
At the same time, arrays rose up one after another, protecting the center of the Bone Sea Forbidden Land.
Clearly, they did not dare to fight Ye Tian anymore, fearing the loss of too many clansmen.
Ye Tian went deep into the Bone Sea Forbidden Land and locked eyes with the Bone Kings.
"I am here to negotiate!"
Ye Tian spoke.
"Ancestor of the Dark Forbidden Domain, what do you want to negotiate?"
A Bone King spoke.
The reason he replied to Ye Tian was not... because he actually wanted to talk, but to stall for time, waiting for a Bone Emperor to descend.
"I want to trade with the Bone Clan. I will return your clan's Supreme Imperial Weapon, and in exchange, you tell me how to step into the Supreme Ancestor level. How about it?"
Ye Tian said.
"We will consider it!"
The Bone King replied.
But deep down, the Bone King sneered: "You want to break through to the Supreme Ancestor realm? Simply wishful thinking!"
A Supreme Imperial Weapon was indeed very precious, and the Bone Clan did not want to lose it, but that didn't mean they had no way to snatch it back.
Once the Great Calamity of the Dark Forbidden Domain arrived, the Bone Emperor could enter the Dark Forbidden Domain. At that time, suppressing Ye Tian would be easy.
Even if Ye Tian's clones could be condensed again and again, if his original body perished, he would be dead for good.
At that time, Ye Tian's original body wouldn't be able to run.
So, they only needed to wait for a while. There was absolutely no need to trade with Ye Tian.
But he wouldn't tell Ye Tian this.
"He's here!"
The Bone Kings thought excitedly.
Rumble!!!! A Bone Emperor descended, his aura instantly sealing off the Bone Sea Forbidden Land.
At the same time, the Bone Kings moved, attempting to intercept Ye Tian and prevent him from escaping.
However, Ye Tian had no intention of leaving. He looked directly at this Bone Emperor.
Crack!!!! A hundred-meter-tall Bone Emperor wearing golden battle armor appeared before Ye Tian, emitting a terrifying aura.
However, Ye Tian also felt the suppression of this world upon this Bone Emperor.
Clearly, this Bone Emperor could not exert his full strength within the Bone Sea Forbidden Land.
"The Bone Sea Forbidden Land only allows Bone Kings to act at most. This Bone Emperor must have paid a price to force his way in!"
Ye Tian guessed.
Boom!!!! The Bone Emperor attacked, giving Ye Tian no chance to negotiate.
However, the opponent didn't seem prepared to kill Ye Tian, but rather wanted to capture him.
After all, killing Ye Tian would only destroy a clone, which was of little significance. If he could capture Ye Tian, he might be able to study the secrets of the clones through this body or use a secret technique to kill Ye Tian across space.
A bone finger pierced through the air, its power several times stronger than that Supreme Imperial Weapon.
Moreover, such an attack wasn't just a one-off. Previously, that Bone King could only activate the Supreme Imperial Weapon for a single attack. Thus, the gap between the two was massive.
Swish swish swish!!!! One Ultimate Ancestral Defense Technique after another was instantly deployed. Coupled with the fact that Ye Tian's strength was much greater than before, the power of these Ultimate Ancestral Defense Techniques was naturally even stronger.
Crack!!!! Layer after layer of defensive shields were pierced, but in the end, the Bone Emperor only pierced through thirteen layers of defensive shields before his power was spent.
"Your Excellency, if you continue to attack, I will also take action. When that time comes, you won't be able to protect these Bone Generals and Bone Kings. As for me, I am merely a clone and do not fear death.
Shall we negotiate, or continue the slaughter?"
Ye Tian said coldly.
The Bone Emperor stopped and looked directly at Ye Tian, saying, "You are very strong. Your realm is only equivalent to a Bone King, but no Bone King could withstand a single blow from me without being injured. Your strength is not much different from a weaker Bone Emperor, and in terms of defense, you are comparable to some powerful Bone Emperors."
"Thank you for the praise!"
Ye Tian smiled.
The Bone Emperor said in a heavy voice, "What do you want to negotiate?"
"A Supreme Imperial Weapon in exchange for the secret of reaching the Supreme Ancestor level. The Supreme Ancestors of our Dark Forbidden Domain are equivalent to your Bone Emperors. Although the paths we walk are different, there might be similarities in some areas. Therefore, I want to know how to break through the bottleneck!"
Ye Tian requested.
The Bone Emperor fell silent and did not answer immediately...
"Not enough... the Supreme Imperial Weapon is only temporarily in your hands. When the day of the Great Calamity comes, my clan will still have a way to take it back!"
The Bone Emperor said.
"Is that so?"
Ye Tian sneered. "If I attack this Bone Sea Forbidden Land again and again, how many... clansmen will your Bone Clan lose? Unless you guard this place forever, once you leave, I will even do my best to destroy that—Gate!"
At the mention of the Gate, the Bone Emperor's expression changed drastically, and his aura began to turn violent.
"You dare!!!"
The Bone Emperor roared in rage.
"If you don't agree to this trade, I will dare!"
Ye Tian said with a smile.


Chapter 1493: One Punch Heavily Injures the Holy Ancestor!

Chapter 1493: One Punch Heavily Injures the Holy Ancestor
!
The Bone Emperor was hesitant; he was indeed afraid.
He could not guard this place forever. Not only would it be a great burden on himself, but it would also be a heavy burden on the Bone Sea Forbidden Ground.
Guarding it for a few thousand years was fine, but any longer would be dangerous.
And a mere few thousand years was practically nothing to beings of their level. Once he left and Ye Tian came to cause trouble, the Bone Sea Forbidden Ground would not only suffer heavy losses, but if Ye Tian managed to destroy the Gate, it would be disastrous.
Although a top-tier Ancestor might not necessarily be able to destroy the Gate—the probability was very, very low—the Bone Emperor did not dare to gamble.
Furthermore, if the Bone Race members in the Bone Sea Forbidden Ground were all killed, even if the Gate wasn't destroyed, it would still mean the destruction of the Bone Race's foundation in the Dark Forbidden Domain.
Therefore, he absolutely could not completely offend Ye Tian.
"Fine, I agree to this deal!"
The Bone Emperor agreed.
He had no choice but to agree, otherwise, the Bone Race would suffer heavy losses.
As for whether Ye Tian would reach the level of an Ultimate Ancestor after obtaining the method to do so, he wasn't worried. Reaching the level of an Ultimate Ancestor was not that simple; it wasn't something that could be achieved just by having monstrous talent.
Immediately, the two made a Life Oath. Although it might not be absolutely binding, it at least had some effect.
Moreover, the Bone Emperor did not dare to violate it, otherwise, the Bone Race would not be able to withstand Ye Tian's desperate retaliation.
Afterward.
Ye Tian returned to the Profound Void Holy Realm and brought back the Ultimate Emperor Artifact.
This item wasn't of much use to him, so it was better to use it for the trade.
"This Ultimate Emperor Artifact is yours!"
Ye Tian tossed the Ultimate Emperor Artifact over.
At the same time, the Bone Emperor handed over a bead, which contained the secrets of how a top-tier Ancestor could break through to the level of an Ultimate Ancestor.
"Pleasure doing business with you!"
Ye Tian smiled.
"Hmph!"
The Bone Emperor snorted coldly, not feeling pleased at all.
Whoosh! Ye Tian left the Bone Sea Forbidden Ground and likely wouldn't return in the future, while the Bone Emperor also passed through the Gate and left the Bone Sea Forbidden Ground.
Back in the Profound Void Ancestral Realm.
Ye Tian carefully browsed the information recorded in the bead and gradually understood the key to breaking through to the Ultimate Ancestor level.
Whether it was an Ultimate Ancestor or a Bone Emperor, they actually belonged to the same level; it was just that the names were different.
A top-tier Ancestor was almost the limit of the world within the Dark Forbidden Domain. No matter how one practiced, it was impossible to break through; this was the restriction of the Dark Forbidden Domain.
Never mind that Ye Tian had comprehended many Ultimate Ancestral Techniques; even if he created hundreds or thousands of them, he still wouldn't be able to break through.
No one could break the shackles within a single world.
However, if one left the Dark Forbidden Domain, they could break the shackles and become an Ultimate Ancestor.
It was just like how if a Bone King of the Bone Race entered the Dark Forbidden Domain during its Great Catastrophe, they would have a chance to break the shackles and become a Bone Emperor.
In the endlessly distant past, the Bone Race had given birth to several Bone Emperors within the Dark Forbidden Domain.
New Ancestors like Ye Tian did not know about such things, and neither did the Realm Ancestor or War Ancestor, but... those ancient Ancestors who were in deep slumber knew.
But outside of the Great Catastrophe period, even a Bone Emperor would not dare to step into the Dark Forbidden Domain, otherwise, they would surely die.
Similarly, if Ye Tian dared to step into a world similar to the Dark Forbidden Domain, he would be instantly obliterated. He could only go there when that other world entered its own Great Catastrophe.
But to go there, one must use a Gate.
Controlling a Gate was the only way to travel to other worlds.
The Bone Race controlled a Gate. How they obtained it was unknown; only the Bone Emperors of the Bone Race would know.
"To control a Gate and also know when the world on the other side enters a Great Catastrophe before being able to cross over... both of these conditions are extremely harsh!"
Ye Tian murmured.
Furthermore, to make the breakthrough, one's true body must go in person.
The reason the Bone Race dared to reveal this secret was that they weren't afraid of him using their Gate to break through.
After all, if his true body went over, it would be exactly what the Bone Race wanted. At that time, the Bone Race would definitely dispatch multiple Bone Emperors to kill him.
Besides, if the Bone Race's side hadn't entered a Great Catastrophe, he wouldn't dare to go over. Going over would mean... death.
"Based on the Bone Race's situation, the six forbidden grounds of the Dark Forbidden Domain should be bases established by six powerful worlds. Once the Dark Forbidden Domain enters a Great Catastrophe, the experts of these forces will enter the Dark Forbidden Domain to snatch resources and attempt to break through to the level of an Ultimate Ancestor."
Ye Tian speculated.
However, based on the current situation, it would likely be a very long time before the Dark Forbidden Domain entered its next Great Catastrophe.
He couldn't stand being unable to improve his cultivation and strength for such a long period.
"I must find an ancient Ancestor to ask about the situation!"
Ye Tian murmured.
But who should he look for? He didn't know a single ancient Ancestor, and he didn't even know where they were.
The Dark Forbidden Domain was so vast; it wasn't just a small place like the Bone Sea Forbidden Ground. If a top-tier Ancestor hid themselves in slumber, he wouldn't be able to find them.
Suddenly.
Ye Tian thought of the Holy Ancestor.
The Holy Ancestor was very likely the disciple of an ancient Ancestor and definitely had a way to contact that ancient Ancestor.
In the past, the Holy Ancestor's strength was not much different from his.
But now, Ye Tian didn't think much of the Holy Ancestor's strength; he could kill him within a few moves.
"Then I'll take a trip to the Dark Ancestral Realm!"
Ye Tian's duplicated body tore through time and space, instantly arriving at the Dark Holy Domain.
Immediately, the Realm Ancestor, War Ancestor, and other Ancestors sensed him.
"Ancestor of Ten Thousand Laws!"
"Ancestor of Ten Thousand Laws!"
One by one, the Ancestors greeted Ye Tian.
"I'm looking for the Holy Ancestor!"
Ye Tian responded to these Ancestors.
"Ancestor of Ten Thousand Laws, why are you looking for the Holy Ancestor?"
The Realm Ancestor was curious.
"To ask him about something!"
Ye Tian said with a smile.
The Realm Ancestor was curious but didn't ask further.
At this moment, Ye Tian arrived outside the Dark Ancestral Realm.
The Holy Ancestor naturally knew Ye Tian had arrived, but he felt an ill omen, as if he were already in a dangerous situation.
"Holy Ancestor, come out!"
Ye Tian said.
BOOM!!!! The Holy Ancestor walked out of the Dark Ancestral Realm, his gaze fixed on the Ancestor of Ten Thousand Laws, speaking with some wariness: "Ancestor of Ten Thousand Laws, what do you want with me?"
"I want to find the ancient Ancestor behind you. Tell me where he is."
Ye Tian questioned in a commanding tone.
"What Ancestor behind me? I don't know what you mean, Ancestor of Ten Thousand Laws."
The Holy Ancestor shook his head.
"Speak, or die!"
Ye Tian threatened.
"Die?"
The Holy Ancestor said coldly, "Ancestor of Ten Thousand Laws, even if you have a top-tier Ancestor clone plus your true body, you can't do anything to me even if you work together!"
"Is that so?"
Ye Tian struck.
He threw a single punch, using nearly eighty percent of his strength.
The Holy Ancestor's expression changed drastically. An Innate Ancestral Artifact-level defensive armor appeared on his body, and he exerted his full strength to perform an Ultimate Ancestral Technique to resist Ye Tian.
However, it was useless!!! CRACK!!!!!! Under the punch, the Innate Ancestral Artifact cracked, and the Holy Ancestor's physical body was nearly blown apart. The terrifying power annihilated countless amounts of his life force.
With this one punch, the Holy Ancestor was heavily injured and on the verge of death! At the same time, the entire Dark Ancestral Realm cracked, and countless living beings were annihilated by the shockwaves of the strike.
It could be said that the Dark Holy Sect was heavily damaged by the aftershocks and was on the verge of being wiped out.
At this moment.
The Realm Ancestor was shocked, and the Ancestors who were secretly watching were also dumbfounded.
To heavily injure the Holy Ancestor with one punch—what kind of combat power was this? If he struck a few more times, the Holy Ancestor would likely be killed! Stone reminds you: Three things for reading—collect, recommend, and share! ,

Chapter 1494: Three Great Calamities, the Third Dark Era

Chapter 1494: Three Great Calamities, the Third Dark Era
"How is it possible? How can you possess such terrifying strength?"
The Holy Ancestor spoke in disbelief.
He was a top-tier Ancestor, and not one who had just broken through. His strength was immense.
In the Dark Forbidden Zone, a top-tier Ancestor was the... limit. Even the strongest among them shouldn't be able to heavily injure him in a single strike.
But Ye Tian had done it. A single blow had left him severely wounded. If Ye Tian attacked a few more times, he feared he would be killed outright.
"Could it be that you have stepped into the realm of a Supreme Ancestor?"
The Holy Ancestor asked in horror.
But he immediately dismissed the thought, saying, "Impossible. You couldn't have reached the level of a Supreme Ancestor. No one in the Dark Forbidden Zone can reach that level!"
"I naturally haven't reached the level of a Supreme Ancestor."
Ye Tian stared at the Holy Ancestor. "But killing a top-tier Ancestor like you only takes a few moves."
The Holy Ancestor was terrified. Once, he had looked down upon everything; aside from the Destruction Ancestor, he feared no one.
But now, he was afraid of Ye Tian.
How long had it been? Ye Tian had grown from an ant to a level where even he had to look up.
"Ancestor of Myriad Laws, what exactly do you want?"
The Holy Ancestor asked.
Ye Tian gazed at him and said, "I said before, I am looking for the ancient Ancestor behind you. Don't deny it, or you die!"
The Holy Ancestor dared not deny it any longer and hurriedly asked, "What exactly do you want with my Master?"
Master? Ye Tian had already suspected as much, and now he finally had a definitive answer from the Holy Ancestor's mouth.
As expected, that ancient Ancestor was the Holy Ancestor's Master.
Ye Tian said, "Rest assured, I am only looking for your Master to ask some questions, not to cause him trouble. After all, I don't even know him. There is no enmity between us, so there's no need to deal with him!"
"I need to contact my Master. If he is unwilling to see you, there is nothing I can do. After all, I do not know his exact location!"
The Holy Ancestor said.
"No problem!"
Ye Tian nodded.
Subsequently.
The Holy Ancestor began to contact his Master, waiting slowly.
Before long, the Holy Ancestor replied, "Master is willing to see you, but only through an incarnation!"
"That's fine!"
Ye Tian agreed.
At that moment.
An incarnation of an Ancestor appeared before Ye Tian. It took the form of a middle-aged man wearing a simple, ancient black robe. His aura was extremely powerful.
Through this incarnation, Ye Tian roughly judged the other party's strength. He had indeed reached the peak of the top-tier Ancestor realm. Although much weaker than Ye Tian, he was far stronger than the Holy Ancestor.
"Greetings, Ancestor of Myriad Laws!"
The Black-Robed Ancestor was polite.
"May I ask how to address your Excellency?"
Ye Tian said indifferently.
The Black-Robed Ancestor said, "Call me Baipo!"
"Ancestor Baipo, I would like to inquire about some matters. I wonder if that is possible?"
Ye Tian asked politely.
"No problem!"
Ancestor Baipo agreed.
Immediately, Ye Tian and Ancestor Baipo isolated themselves from the prying eyes of other Ancestors and began to communicate privately.
Ye Tian also knew that if he hadn't threatened the Holy Ancestor, this Ancestor Baipo would certainly not have appeared.
"Ancestor Baipo, I want to know what the Great Calamity is all about."
Ye Tian asked.
"You know about the Great Calamity as well?"
Ancestor Baipo was somewhat surprised.
"Indeed!"
Ye Tian nodded. "I learned of it from the Bone Race in the Bone Sea Forbidden Land. The Bone Race came from the other side of the Gate. They stay in the Bone Sea Forbidden Land and can only enter the Dark Forbidden Zone during a Great Calamity. Currently, they dare not set foot in the Dark Forbidden Zone. Furthermore, based on the information I have, the Dark Forbidden Zone has experienced Great Calamities before. Forces like the Bone Race have invaded, yet no such information has been passed down in the Dark Forbidden Zone. I presume ancient Ancestors like you must know many secrets."
Ancestor Baipo said in great shock, "I didn't expect the Ancestor of Myriad Laws to know so much and even obtain information from the Bone Race. It truly surprises me. Some information can indeed be told to you. The Dark Forbidden Zone has indeed experienced Great Calamities. As far as I know, there have been three in total, and I have only experienced one."
"In terms of Domain Years, 120,000 Domain Years make one Domain Epoch. 108 Domain Epochs count as one Dark Era Year. After nine Dark Era Years, a Great Calamity arrives. We are currently in the third Dark Era Year. There are still six Dark Era Years left before the next Great Calamity."
As soon as Ancestor Baipo finished speaking, Ye Tian was startled and said, "Dark Holy Lands!"
"Exactly. Each time a Dark Holy Land is born, it represents the passing of one Dark Era Year. Three Dark Eras have passed since the last Great Calamity. Therefore, the Ancestor of Myriad Laws does not need to worry too much about the next Great Calamity."
Ancestor Baipo said with a smile.
"Then what is the deal with the Gate? Passing through the Gate allows one to enter other worlds similar to the Dark Forbidden Zone. In the Dark Forbidden Zone, one cannot break through to become a Supreme Ancestor. Ancestor Baipo should know about this, right?"
Ye Tian asked.
"I do indeed know!"
Ancestor Baipo nodded. "It seems you know this as well, which surprises me. Even among our batch of Ancestors who survived one Great Calamity, only a very few vaguely know a little about it."
Ye Tian shared the information he knew: "According to what I know, one cannot break through to a Supreme Ancestor in the Dark Forbidden Zone. Only by entering other worlds can one break through. However, if another world is not undergoing a Great Calamity, anyone entering it will be erased by that world's laws. One must wait until the other world enters a Great Calamity to cross over. Only then is there hope of reaching the Supreme Ancestor realm. I want to know one thing: does any Ancestor in the Dark Forbidden Zone control a Gate?"
"No!"
Ancestor Baipo said with certainty, "I can tell you for sure that no Ancestor in the Dark Forbidden Zone controls a Gate. After all, we have only gone through three Great Calamities, while some worlds have even survived ten or even a hundred. Compared to other worlds, the Dark Forbidden Zone is still too young and thus cannot compete with other powerful worlds. If we controlled a Gate, perhaps we would have hope of giving birth to a Supreme Ancestor. But based on the information I currently have, not a single Supreme Ancestor has been born yet. Of course, this is just what I know. Some Ancestors passed through unstable Gates and disappeared thereafter. Perhaps those Ancestors became Supreme Ancestors, but it is more likely they perished upon crossing."
"Unstable Gates? What are those?"
Ye Tian was curious.
Ancestor Baipo did not hide it; this was information that could be easily discovered, so there was no harm in telling Ye Tian.
Thus, he said, "In the Dark Forbidden Zone, shortly after every Dark Era, a Gate appears. This Gate only appears for a short time and then dissipates; it does not exist eternally. We have yet to find a way to make such a Gate permanent. Some Ancestors, unable to withstand the ravages of time and wishing to promote to Supreme Ancestor, would risk entering another world. If that world happened to be in a Great Calamity, they might luckily survive. But the probability is too low. I dare not gamble!"
"So, you also have no way to enter other worlds to pursue Supreme Ancestor combat power?"
Ye Tian frowned.
"Yes, no way!"
Ancestor Baipo shook his head. "We are too weak. If a force like the Bone Race were willing to share the method of establishing a permanent Gate, then we would have hope of becoming Supreme Ancestors. But they certainly wouldn't be willing. After all, once they hand over such a method, we would have a way to enter their world, potentially threatening their home world."
Ye Tian was somewhat disappointed.
Suddenly, Ye Tian asked again, "Do you know which force is the weakest—far weaker than the Bone Race—yet possesses a forbidden land in our Dark Forbidden Zone?"
"What do you intend to do?"
Ancestor Baipo was curious.
"Just tell me."
Ye Tian said.
Baipo, also fearing Ye Tian would cause trouble for his disciple, spoke: "According to what I know, the Bone Race is at a middle-tier level among these forces. The weakest force is called the Haitian Holy Sect. This is a sect of exotic beasts. They possess a forbidden land in our Dark Forbidden Zone called the Haitian Forbidden Land. However, it is no less dangerous than the Bone Sea Forbidden Land because this forbidden land is covered by seawater with powerful corrosive properties. Only the exotic beasts of the Haitian Holy Sect can survive in it. Once we Ancestors enter, our strength is reduced by more than half, and we cannot even sustain long-term combat. Furthermore, at least a thousand exotic beasts are stationed inside that forbidden land, with six or seven among them having strength comparable to top-tier Ancestors. According to my guesses, this force does not have many beasts comparable to the Supreme Ancestor realm—at most one or two."
"Thank you!"
Ye Tian thanked him.


Chapter 1495: Wiping Out the Sea-Sky Forbidden Zone, Occupying a Gate!

Chapter 1495: Wiping Out the Sea-Sky Forbidden Zone, Occupying a Gate
!
Ye Tian had obtained a considerable amount of intelligence from the mouth of the Hundred Souls Ancestor, though the Hundred Souls Ancestor feigned ignorance regarding certain details.
Ye Tian was well aware that the Hundred Souls Ancestor certainly hadn't revealed everything. Only one piece of information was truly useful to Ye Tian: the intelligence regarding the Sea-Sky Forbidden Zone.
Perhaps to the Hundred Souls Ancestor, this information was of little use, but to Ye Tian, it was incredibly valuable.
The Sea-Sky Holy Sect was weak, and consequently, the strength of the Sea-Sky Forbidden Zone was also weak.
He could completely wipe out the strange beasts in the Sea-Sky Forbidden Zone, then use his Duplication Talent to copy one of them. Through that... beast, he could enter the world where the Sea-Sky Holy Sect was located, thereby entering another realm to seek the secrets of breaking through.
This method was not applicable to the Bone Sea Forbidden Zone because the Bone Race was too powerful; they could dispatch a Bone Emperor to descend at any moment.
If he dared to duplicate a fallen Bone King, he would definitely be discovered.
However, the strange beasts within the Sea-Sky Forbidden Zone were different. Their numbers were very sparse. If he charged to the other side of the gate, slaughtered those beasts, and wiped them out in a short period, the Sea-Sky Holy Sect wouldn't be able to react in time.
"Although the seawater of the Sea-Sky Forbidden Zone will restrict a portion of my strength, I am too powerful. Suppressing a fraction of it is nothing."
With this thought, Ye Tian sent his duplicated body toward the Sea-Sky Forbidden Zone.
Swish! In an instant, Ye Tian arrived outside the Sea-Sky Forbidden Zone.
Then, he stepped into the Sea-Sky Forbidden Zone and was enveloped by countless gallons of seawater. This water constantly eroded his physical body and suppressed about thirty percent of his strength.
A mere thirty percent suppression was nothing; he remained invincible among top-tier Ancestors.
"An outside Ancestor has broken in, kill him!"
The strange beasts of the Sea-Sky Holy Sect rushed over.
These beasts came in all sorts of bizarre shapes, but every one of them was massive in size.
From the aura on their bodies, Ye Tian roughly judged their strength. Most were at the level of ordinary Ancestors, with a few elite Ancestors, and only five comparable to top-tier Ancestors—even weaker than the strength the Hundred Souls Ancestor had disclosed.
Ye Tian did not reveal his full strength immediately. Otherwise, if these beasts became terrified, they might immediately send for reinforcements, which would make it easy for him to be exposed.
Therefore, he initially displayed very weak strength, barely reaching the level of a top-tier Ancestor.
Consequently, Ye Tian allowed himself to be "injured" by their attacks on purpose, while constantly drawing closer to the location of the gate during the battle.
The Sea-Sky Forbidden Zone was not as vast as the Bone Sea Forbidden Zone. From this, it was evident that the Sea-Sky Holy Sect's strength was inferior to the Bone Race, which was why the forbidden zone they opened in the Dark Forbidden Domain was not large.
These strange beasts were completely unaware of Ye Tian's objective; they had no idea his target was the gate.
"There are two beasts stationed at the edge of the gate. One... beast is comparable to an elite Ancestor, and the other's strength is likely on par with a top-tier Ancestor, but not a powerful one—just an average top-tier Ancestor. Against such a top-tier Ancestor, even if my strength is suppressed, I can kill them in just a few moves."
Ye Tian thought to himself:.
"It's about time!"
Ye Tian suddenly erupted with full power. Layers of Ultimate Defensive Ancestral Techniques were displayed, and the attacks of those strange beasts were all blocked, unable to harm Ye Tian in the slightest.
Several beasts were instantly blasted into blood mist, perishing on the spot, allowing Ye Tian to charge out directly toward the gate.
At this moment, those beasts finally realized that Ye Tian was a pig eating a tiger, intentionally disguising his strength, and that his target was their gateway.
"Quickly, go for help! This Ancestor wants to destroy... the gate!"
The beasts roared one after another.
The two beasts guarding the gate immediately understood and prepared to traverse the gate to seek reinforcements.
However, they were too late.
At that moment, Ye Tian performed an Ultimate Ancestral Technique—the Eternal Ultimate Ancestral Technique. This was a Time Ultimate Ancestral Technique, which, combined with the Dream Butterfly Ultimate Ancestral Technique, directly froze time and space.
If these two beasts' strength were comparable to Ye Tian's, they would certainly have the power to break through the space-time freeze, but their strength was lacking. Thus, they were directly pinned down. They might have been able to break the space-time lock, but it would require a bit of time.
And Ye Tian would not give them that time.
At this moment, Ye Tian rushed over at maximum speed. With the boost of two speed-type Ultimate Ancestral Techniques, he charged directly to the gateway, where no one could stop him.
Upon reaching the gate, Ye Tian crushed the beast comparable to an elite Ancestor with one hand, killing it in a single blow.
Then.
Ye Tian sent the other beast flying with a single punch.
He stood right there at the gate, not allowing any beast to pass through.
This place belonged to him now! "Damn it, he doesn't want to destroy the gate; he wants to occupy our gate! Charge through with everything you've got!"
The strange beasts spared no expense to perform forbidden arts, lunging toward Ye Tian one after another.
And at this time.
Ye Tian's main body arrived and stepped into the Sea-Sky Forbidden Zone.
If it were the Bone Sea Forbidden Zone, Ye Tian's main body would not dare to enter, but he dared to enter the Sea-Sky Forbidden Zone.
The gate could not transmit messages, so the events happening here could not pass through. Under normal circumstances, the Sea-Sky Holy Sect on the other side of the gate would not send beasts over, so they wouldn't know immediately.
Therefore, it was very safe for his main body to enter here.
Moreover.
With his current strength, even if a beast comparable to the Strongest Ancestor truly descended, he could easily leave.
As Ye Tian's main body entered the Sea-Sky Forbidden Zone, he coordinated with his duplicated body to begin a massacre of these beasts.
For those weaker beasts, Ye Tian killed almost one with every strike.
In a short while, only five beasts remained.
The strength of these five beasts was comparable to top-tier Ancestors, but they were still no match for Ye Tian. The strongest among them was comparable to a very powerful top-tier Ancestor, yet its strength was still much weaker than Ye Tian's.
Soon, the other four beasts had been killed by Ye Tian, leaving only this last powerful beast.
This beast had many life-saving methods and was quite powerful, so it managed to hold out for a long time.
But in the end, this beast was still killed by Ye Tian.
Of course, Ye Tian's consumption was also quite high.
It had to be said that if the strength of the Sea-Sky Forbidden Zone had been any greater, it would have been much more difficult for him to wipe out these beasts.
"The beasts of the Sea-Sky Forbidden Zone have been completely wiped out by me. The Sea-Sky Holy Sect in the other world will definitely not be able to sense their deaths."
Ye Tian murmured.
He dispelled the duplicated body and then accelerated time.
Soon, the duplication ability could be used again.
This time, Ye Tian duplicated that strongest beast.
Boom!!!! A massive beast, resembling an ape but possessing six arms, appeared.
Compared to the previous beast, the one Ye Tian duplicated was identical, even down to the soul.
Back then, the Bone Race members Ye Tian duplicated were recognized by the origin of the Dark Forbidden Domain as genuine Bone Race members, which was why they had obliterated the duplicated bodies.
Clearly, even the origin of the Dark Forbidden Domain could not distinguish the truth of Ye Tian's duplicated bodies.
Therefore, this duplicated body could definitely enter the gate without being recognized.
Afterward, Ye Tian plundered all the resources of the Sea-Sky Forbidden Zone, creating the illusion that the zone's resources had been raided.
Next, Ye Tian acted to heavily injure the duplicated body, putting it in a state of being near death. Otherwise, if it had no injuries at all while passing through the gateway, it would be suspected by the Sea-Sky Holy Sect.
This duplicated body not only had a heavily damaged physical body, but even its soul was in a state on the verge of collapsing, though it wouldn't actually shatter.
"That should be about enough!"
Ye Tian thought to himself:.

Chapter 1496: The Way to Break the Shackles!

Chapter 1496: The Way to Break the Shackles
!
The duplicate beast body passed through the gate, pretending to seek reinforcements, while Ye Tian's original body quickly left the Haitian Forbidden Land.
Although he felt that the Haitian Sacred Sect was not particularly powerful, he had to be careful in case the intelligence was incorrect. Therefore, he had to remain cautious.
....Haitian Sacred Sect, Base.
When Ye Tian's duplicate body passed through the gate, appearing heavily injured and on the verge of death, it was immediately discovered by the Haitian Sacred Sect beasts guarding the other side.
"An Ancestor has invaded!"
Ye Tian immediately called out.
"What happened?"
One powerful beast after another appeared, questioning Ye Tian for information.
At the same time, some beasts gave Ye Tian special healing substances and life-saving items to consume, preventing him from falling.
Ye Tian reported the situation truthfully, saying that a powerful Ancestor had invaded, one whose strength was comparable to a Supreme Ancestor. They were simply no match, and almost everyone had been blasted to death.
He had paid a massive price to escape back.
Soon, a beast comparable to a Supreme Ancestor appeared and personally headed over.
Meanwhile, Ye Tian returned to the Haitian Sacred Sect to recover. The sect did not suspect him at all; even this world recognized him and did not attempt to erase him.
Furthermore, since all the beasts within the Haitian Forbidden Land had perished, it was almost impossible for him to be discovered.
It could be said that Ye Tian's plan was a success.
Haitian Sacred Sect.
Ye Tian had been back for some time. He even had several servants; after all, as a powerful beast comparable to a Top Ancestor, his status in the Haitian Sacred Sect was naturally high.
During this time, he used his servants to inquire about recent events. Since he had been guarding the Haitian Forbidden Land and was unfamiliar with the situation here, it was perfectly normal to ask.
Through these inquiries and the records of the Haitian Sacred Sect, he gradually came to understand this sacred land.
This world was not dominated by the Haitian Sacred Sect alone; there were three major Sacred Sects, of which the Haitian Sacred Sect was the weakest.
Beasts comparable to Ancestors were called Sacred Beasts here, and they were divided into Ordinary Sacred Beasts, Elite Sacred Beasts, Top Sacred Beasts, and Supreme Sacred Beasts.
The Haitian Sacred Sect possessed two Supreme Sacred Beasts, while the entire world possessed ten. It was naturally much stronger than the Dark Forbidden Domain.
There were even more Top Sacred Beasts; the Haitian Sacred Sect alone had over seventy.
In total, the Haitian Sacred Sect had several thousand Sacred Beasts, which was equivalent to several thousand Ancestors.
From this, it was clear how powerful the Haitian Sacred Sect was; even ten Dark Forbidden Domains combined could not contend with a single Haitian Sacred Sect.
And the Haitian Sacred Sect was still one of the relatively weaker forces.
Ye Tian had now infiltrated the world of the Haitian Sacred Sect, which they referred to as the Sacred Domain.
The Sacred Domain was infinitely vast. Aside from Sacred Beasts, ordinary beings could not cross the entire domain, a situation similar to the Dark Forbidden Domain.
Ye Tian currently had two goals.
The first goal was to seek a breakthrough and step into the Supreme Ancestor realm.
The second goal was to obtain the method for constructing a Gate. Although the Haitian Sacred Sect was weak, it controlled a Gate, and he wanted to master the construction method so that a Gate could exist eternally.
"I'll complete the first goal first. Once that's done, it will be easier to achieve the second!"
Ye Tian thought to himself.
After all, the Gate was the most important asset of the Haitian Sacred Sect. The construction method was bound to be in the hands of those two Supreme Sacred Beasts and would be very difficult to obtain.
Ye Tian currently only knew that by entering another world, one could break the shackles of a Top Ancestor and promote to the Supreme Ancestor realm.
But as for the specific method of breaking through, Ye Tian was still unclear.
Logically, the Top Sacred Beasts of the Haitian Sacred Sect should know.
However, Ye Tian was a fake Top Sacred Beast and did not possess the memories of that beast.
He didn't rush to learn this information at first, but instead focused on healing while gathering general knowledge.
During this period, various Sacred Beasts came to visit and offer their regards.
Of course, since he had nearly lost the Haitian Forbidden Land, the punishment from the Sacred Sect arrived as well, deducting several Sacred Beast Years' worth of his stipend.
A Sacred Beast Year was equivalent to a Dark Era, so this was considered a relatively heavy punishment.
After several hundred million years, another group of Sacred Beasts was stationed in the Haitian Forbidden Land. To prevent its loss, three of the highest-ranking Top Sacred Beasts of the Haitian Sacred Sect were sent to guard it, and one Supreme Sacred Beast went into secluded cultivation right at the edge of the Gate. If anything happened, they could descend upon the Haitian Forbidden Land immediately.
This showed how much importance they placed on the Gate and the Forbidden Land.
As time passed, Ye Tian gradually became familiar with some of the Sacred Beasts of the Haitian Sacred Sect, ensuring he wouldn't make any mistakes.
With increasing familiarity, Ye Tian discovered that the Sacred Domain was somewhat similar to the Dark Forbidden Domain; at the very least, the creatures here possessed various talents, and the Sacred Beasts possessed Sacred Talents.
However, this duplicate body did not contain the Copy Talent, so he couldn't check the talents of other Sacred Beasts. But from the Sacred Beasts in the Haitian Forbidden Land, Ye Tian had seen a uniform array of Sacred Talents, and one even possessed an Ancestral Talent—the very body Ye Tian had copied.
However, these talents were of no use to Ye Tian.
After becoming acquainted with the Sacred Beasts of the Haitian Sacred Sect, Ye Tian, using the identity of the Sacred Beast named He Yuan, frequently interacted with others, even displaying a longing for the Supreme Sacred Beast rank.
Through various means, he discussed topics like Supreme Sacred Beasts, the Great Calamity of the Dark Forbidden Domain, and breakthroughs with other Top Sacred Beasts. Gradually, he uncovered the secrets of the breakthrough.
Just as Ye Tian had guessed, all Top Sacred Beasts knew how to charge toward the Supreme Sacred Beast rank.
Thus, he finally obtained this secret.
"I didn't expect it to be so difficult for a Top Sacred Beast to break through to a Supreme Sacred Beast!"
Ye Tian murmured.
According to what he learned, for a Top Sacred Beast to break through to a Supreme Sacred Beast, they must enter another world during a Great Calamity and comprehend the rules of that world. Once their comprehension reaches a certain level, they must create a "Sacred Beast Body" technique. Once this Sacred Beast Body reaches perfection, the stimulation between the two different Sacred Beast Bodies allows them to break the shackles and promote to a Supreme Sacred Beast. The two Sacred Beast Bodies then fuse into one, becoming a Supreme Sacred Beast Body.
Creating a Sacred Beast Body was difficult enough, but to cultivate it to the perfection stage required an immense amount of resources—specifically, resources from the other world. This necessitated plundering countless resources to elevate oneself.
Furthermore, the act of charging toward the Supreme Sacred Beast rank itself required a sea of resources.
Because it was so difficult, the Haitian Sacred Sect only had two Supreme Sacred Beasts to this day.
"So that's it. For a Top Ancestor to charge toward the Supreme Ancestor rank, they must comprehend the rules of another world, create an Ancestor Law that fits that world, condense an Ancestor Body, and then cultivate that Ancestor Body to the peak of the Top Ancestor realm. Only then can they break the shackles, fuse the two Ancestor Bodies, and step into the Supreme Ancestor realm!"
Ye Tian realized.
For other Ancestors, completing such a breakthrough would be incredibly difficult.
But for him, it didn't seem difficult at all!

Chapter 1497: The Primordial Ancestor Law Compatible with the Holy Realm!

Chapter 1497: The Primordial Ancestor Law Compatible with the Holy Realm
!
Knowing the key to breaking through to the Strongest Primordial Ancestor, Ye Tian began to comprehend the rules of the Holy Realm within the Sea-Sky Holy Sect.
For him, the rules of this unfamiliar Holy Realm were vastly different from those of the Dark Forbidden Zone. Furthermore, the comprehension of this body was inferior to his original body, and he could not use the "Evolution" ability to comprehend the rules; everything had to rely on himself.
Therefore, it would be extremely difficult for Ye Tian to create a Primordial Ancestor Law belonging to the Holy Realm.
Most importantly, it was too difficult for the two worlds to communicate.
Ye Tian currently had no way to contact his duplicated body, so it was unclear exactly when he would be able to create a Primordial Ancestor Law.
Holy Realm, Sea-Sky Holy Sect.
In the blink of an eye, several domain years had passed.
By this time, Ye Tian's duplicated body had already integrated into the Sea-Sky Holy Sect under the identity of He Yuan. Not a single... Holy Beast suspected him; he was virtually no longer at risk of exposure.
Additionally, Ye Tian occasionally obtained some fragmented Holy Laws from the Sea-Sky Holy Sect.
Holy Laws were similar to the Primordial Ancestor Laws of the Dark Forbidden Zone; only by merging with a Holy Law could one become a Holy Beast.
Ye Tian could not merge with the Holy Laws, but he could use them as a reference to understand and master the rules of this world, which was a huge help in creating his own Primordial Ancestor Law.
With the status of this body, it was not difficult to obtain some fragmented Holy Laws, and he could even manage to get some complete Holy Laws.
Unlike the Dark Forbidden Zone, there were many Holy Laws in the Holy Realm. Although they were still very precious, they were not difficult to obtain.
Because Holy Beasts in the Dark Holy Realm frequently fell and died, there were many masterless Holy Laws.
Furthermore, some of the strongest Holy Beasts could also create other Holy Laws, enriching the number of Holy Laws in the Holy Realm.
Therefore, there were many Holy Laws here, and the difficulty of obtaining them was naturally low.
Unfortunately, the Holy Laws here were not suitable for the human race; otherwise, Ye Tian would have prepared to bring a batch of Holy Laws back to the human race to create a batch of Primordial Ancestors.
Profound Void Ancestral World.
Ye Tian's original body could not progress and could only continuously create Ultimate Ancestral Techniques, occasionally creating Primordial Ancestor Laws.
He walked the path of the Endless Primordial Ancestor, so creating a Primordial Ancestor Law for a single path was possible. Although he had created some before, some paths had not been created yet, as the Endless Primordial Ancestor extended into many paths.
Theoretically, he could create countless Primordial Ancestor Laws.
Of course, this was quite difficult.
Perhaps at the beginning, he could create some Primordial Ancestor Laws, but later on, it became more and more difficult, even requiring countless domain years to create a single one.
In the blink of an eye, a hundred domain years passed. Ye Tian created three Primordial Ancestor Laws and placed them in the Human Race Holy Temple. Only Supreme-level Domain Ancestors with very significant contributions were eligible to exchange for them and merge to become Primordial Ancestors.
After that, another hundred domain years passed, and he created one more Primordial Ancestor Law. Clearly, creating Primordial Ancestor Laws was much harder than before.
Later on, Ye Tian needed many domain years to create a single Ancestral Law.
Domain years passed one after another. Unknowingly, the first domain cycle of the Third Dark Calendar passed.
The first domain cycle lasted for a full twelve [units], and Ye Tian had effectively cultivated for 120,000 domain years. But the total number of Primordial Ancestor Laws he created was only twenty-three. Now, it would likely take one or even several domain eras to create a single Primordial Ancestor Law.
Several more domain eras passed. Although Ye Tian created more Ultimate Ancestral Techniques, his overall strength did not improve much. However, the strength of the human race improved significantly, and it had now become the number one power in the Dark Forbidden Zone.
In terms of the number of Primordial Ancestors alone, the human race had already exceeded double digits. This was naturally thanks to the Primordial Ancestor Laws Ye Tian created, which increased the number of human Primordial Ancestors. There are currently thirteen Primordial Ancestors.
This was only because Ye Tian did not give out Primordial Ancestor Laws casually; one had to make a great contribution to exchange for them. Otherwise, the number of human Primordial Ancestors would have surely exceeded twenty.
Additionally, under Ye Tian's cultivation, his wife, son, daughter, and sister—the four of them—had all stepped into the Elite Primordial Ancestor realm and were only one step away from being Top-tier Primordial Ancestors.
If the duplicated body could bring back enough resources from the Sea-Sky Holy Sect, it would be enough to push their strength to Top-tier Primordial Ancestor combat power.
....Sea-Sky Holy Sect.
Ye Tian's duplicated body was still bitterly cultivating and comprehending to create a Primordial Ancestor Law. Unfortunately, the original body was not here, so the difficulty of creation increased countless times. Thus, he had not yet created a single Primordial Ancestor Law.
In fact, if he were creating an ordinary Primordial Ancestor Law, he might have succeeded already.
But what Ye Tian wanted to create was an Endless Primordial Ancestor Law that fit the rules of the Holy Realm, so the difficulty was very high.
He also followed a path similar to the Dark Forbidden Zone, starting by creating basic Primordial Ancestor Laws for Gold, Wood, Water, Fire, Earth, Time, Space, and so on... and then combining them to create the Endless Primordial Ancestor Law.
Now, after several domain eras, he still had not created a single Primordial Ancestor Law, but he was close to actually succeeding.
He was currently creating a Gold Primordial Ancestor Law. This law was not ordinary; it was definitely at the top tier among Primordial Ancestor Laws.
Unlike the Gold Primordial Ancestor Law of the Dark Forbidden Zone, this law was completely compatible with the Holy Realm. However, Ye Tian also based it on the original body's physical structure and cultivation path, making it extremely suitable for the original body, though perfect compatibility was impossible.
After all, the original body was a creature of the Dark Forbidden Zone, while this was a Primordial Ancestor Law transformed from the rules of the Holy Realm, so it naturally could not be perfectly compatible.
One day.
Ye Tian's duplicated body laughed aloud because the Gold Primordial Ancestor Law had been successfully created. This was a good start.
"It took five domain eras to create one Primordial Ancestor Law. Creating twelve Primordial Ancestor Laws certainly cannot be done in sixty domain eras, but it can definitely be done within the time of one Dark Calendar!"
Ye Tian thought.
Subsequently.
Ye Tian entered another long period of bitter cultivation, almost ignoring external affairs.
Even when some Holy Beasts invited Ye Tian to certain treasure lands or ruins to hunt for treasures, Ye Tian declined them all.
After all, it was not easy for this duplicated body to enter the Holy Realm. There would not be such a good opportunity next time. Therefore, this duplicated body absolutely could not fall. As long as there was a hint of danger, he would not do it.
Domain years passed one after another. In the blink of an eye, 107 domain eras had passed since the last birth of the Dark Soul Realm, equivalent to more than ten million domain years. What a long period of time.
Over such a long period, Ye Tian not only created the twelve basic Primordial Ancestor Laws of the Holy Realm but also merged them to create the Endless Primordial Ancestor Law compatible with the Holy Realm.
In other words, Ye Tian's first goal was accomplished.
"First, apply to enter the Sea-Sky Forbidden Land to guard it for a period. Once my duplicated body enters the Sea-Sky Forbidden Land, I can connect with the original body and share memories and information. At that time, the original body will also obtain the Endless Primordial Ancestor Law of the Holy Realm. Then, I'll send the Holy Realm resources accumulated by the duplicated body over the long years to the original body. Then, the original body can impact the realm of the Strongest Primordial Ancestor!"
Ye Tian thought to himself.
