Yet this time, the Blood Mist Alliance had not dispatched many foreign experts. For example, they hadn't paid much attention to the competition for the first Origin Rule Calamity Crystal.
If anyone were to come here, they would find that many Ultimate-level foreign experts had gathered.
Within the blood-colored mist, figures sat upon thrones. There were about dozens of them, all at the Ultimate Ancestor level, with no shortage of second-tier experts among them.

Suddenly.
Boom!!!!
A terrifying figure emerged, clearly surpassing the second tier and reaching the third tier, infinitely close to the level of an Invincible Ancestor.
"Greetings, Lord Baigui!"
"Greetings, Lord Baigui!"
"Greetings, Lord Baigui!"
One by one, the foreign experts stood up and bowed respectfully.
True Emperor Baigui, one of the three Vice Alliance Leaders of the Blood Mist Alliance, a third-tier Ultimate True Emperor.
"True Emperor" corresponded to the Ancestor level; it was their title for it.
An Ultimate True Emperor was an Ultimate Ancestor; only the name was different, while the path was similar.
True Emperor Baigui looked at the many True Emperors and spoke: "Our Blood Mist Alliance has completely digested another foreign world and destroyed all Gates not belonging to the alliance, gaining 100% control over that world. Now, our Blood Mist Alliance has sufficient strength to invade the Sacred Domain World. This Sacred Domain World has already passed its 'newbie period.' Unlike some newborn foreign worlds where we cannot completely transform them due to the protection of rules, the Sacred Domain World does not have this issue. Once we gain complete control here, we can begin the transformation to make this world adapt to our Blood Mist Alliance. At that time, our Blood Mist Alliance will have one more foreign world."
"Lord Baigui, when do we strike?" an Ultimate True Emperor asked.
"Wait a bit longer. During the late stages of the Great Calamity, when the source of the Sacred Domain World is weak, it will be easier for us to attempt the transformation. Furthermore, let them slaughter more living beings to clear out the Sacred Domain World for us; there's no rush to act. None of these forces have third-tier Ultimate True Emperors; once I take action, they won't be able to stop me at all. Moreover, in a while, another third-tier Ultimate True Emperor will arrive. With two third-tier Ultimate True Emperors combined with over ten second-tier Ultimate True Emperors, no force will be able to contend with us!" True Emperor Baigui said.
"Yes!"
The many True Emperors responded one by one.
At this time, the other foreign powers and the native Ultimate Sacred Beasts of the Sacred Domain World were not necessarily aware of the Blood Mist Alliance's ambitions and were still searching for Origin Rule Calamity Crystals.
Ye Tian was also unaware of the Blood Mist Alliance's plans, but even if he knew, he wouldn't be worried.
After all, no matter how bad the situation got, the Blood Mist Alliance currently had no way to invade the Dark Forbidden Zone.
Besides, given his rate of progress, by the time the Great Calamity hit the Dark Forbidden Zone, he might have already advanced to the third tier of the Ultimate Ancestor level and wouldn't fear the Blood Mist Alliance at all.
In the blink of an eye, another few billion years passed, and the second Origin Rule Calamity Crystal appeared.


Chapter 1508: The Blood Mist Alliance Strikes!

Chapter 1508: The Blood Mist Alliance Strikes!

When the second Origin Rule Calamity Crystal appeared, Ye Tian received the news relatively early. Thus, he arrived at the scene immediately, heavily injured three Supreme Ancestors, and ultimately snatched this Origin Rule Calamity Crystal.
After seizing this Origin Rule Calamity Crystal, Ye Tian returned to the Sea Sky Holy Sect to observe it.
"So this is an Origin Rule Calamity Crystal!"
Ye Tian carefully sensed the rules upon it. They indeed belonged to the rules of the Sanctuary World, and they were the most fundamental origin rules. Comprehending an Origin Rule Calamity Crystal was naturally better and faster than cultivating within the Sanctuary World itself, and the crystal contained powerful origin power.
Ye Tian could sense that if he refined this Origin Rule Calamity Crystal, it would be enough to raise his cultivation level slightly and even temper his Supreme Ancestor Body.
However, compared to the benefits brought by creating a Supreme Ancestral Technique, a mere Origin Rule Calamity Crystal was nothing.
Yet, not just anyone could create a Supreme Ancestral Technique.
For instance, in the Sanctuary World, over such a long period of time, there had only been one second-tier Supreme Holy Beast.
"It is more cost-effective to use this Origin Rule Calamity Crystal in the future to comprehend and create a Supreme Ancestral Technique or to give it to the Human Race!"
Ye Tian thought to himself.
Consequently, he sent the Origin Rule Calamity Crystal back to the Dark Forbidden Zone. Through the hands of a Human Ancestor, it passed through the door and was delivered to his main body.
Following that, every so often, an Origin Rule Calamity Crystal would be born within the Sanctuary World.
However, his luck was poor afterward, and the subsequent Origin Rule Calamity Crystals were all snatched away by other Ancestors.
As time passed, a total of nearly thirty Origin Rule Calamity Crystals were born in the Sanctuary World.
"I only managed to snatch two!"
Ye Tian sighed.
He also wanted to seize more Origin Rule Calamity Crystals, but once other Ancestors obtained one, they could return to their respective foreign worlds at the fastest possible speed. He had no way to pursue them.
After all, the other foreign worlds had not yet reached the time of their Great Calamity. If he pursued them there, he would be directly obliterated by the foreign world's power.
Unless he was willing to copy the body of a powerhouse from that foreign world to give chase, but that would expose his ability, so it wasn't worth it.
Nevertheless, among so many Supreme Ancestors, being able to snatch two Origin Rule Calamity Crystals was already quite good.
He did not keep either of these two Origin Rule Calamity Crystals for himself; he sent them both back to his human main body.
At this time, the Great Calamity of the Sanctuary World had reached its late stages. Except for the territories of the three Great Holy Sects, all other regions had become a void. Not a single resource remained; everything had been plundered. Countless worlds had been reduced to fragments, and the living beings within them had naturally all perished.
Myriad Beasts Holy Sect.
Wan Yuan Holy Beast was somewhat flustered at this moment because this Great Calamity was far too different from those in the past.
In the past, the True Emperors of the Blood Mist Alliance would collect resources on a large scale and would even be attacking the three Great Holy Sects by now. The three Great Holy Sects would have to unite with other foreign worlds to keep the Blood Mist Alliance in check.
But now, the Blood Mist Alliance had hardly made a move. Even for collecting resources, they had only dispatched a few Supreme True Emperors. This was not the style of the Blood Mist Alliance.
Furthermore, through investigation, the Blood Mist Forbidden Land of the Blood Mist Alliance had been shrouded. Even Supreme-level powerhouses could not peer inside, and no one knew what they were doing.
Under such circumstances, all Supreme-level foreign powerhouses knew the Blood Mist Alliance had some issues, but the other foreign powerhouses weren't worried. Their bases were not in the Sanctuary World; at worst, they could just withdraw. They weren't afraid of the Blood Mist Alliance at all.
But the Myriad Beasts Holy Sect was afraid!
The Sanctuary World was the very foundation of the Myriad Beasts Holy Sect. They couldn't just run away.
"I hope the Blood Mist Alliance just has problems at their headquarters and lacks the strength to participate in this calamity, rather than it being some kind of conspiracy!"
Wan Yuan Holy Beast thought secretly.
However, not long after, a Holy Beast from the Myriad Beasts Holy Sect sent word that a large number of True Emperors from the Blood Mist Alliance were attacking, including many Supreme True Emperors.
Shortly after the message arrived, that Holy Beast went silent. Clearly, they had been discovered and obliterated by the True Emperors of the Blood Mist Alliance.
……
One of the three Great Holy Sects of the Sanctuary World, the Gilded Holy Sect.
This sect was even stronger than the Sea Sky Holy Sect, possessing three Supreme Holy Beasts, and its other Holy Beasts were far more numerous than those of the Sea Sky Holy Sect.
But suddenly, many True Emperors of the Blood Mist Alliance arrived here. It was all too abrupt, leaving the Gilded Holy Sect no time to react.
Hum!!!!
Countless rays of light swept across the region occupied by the Gilded Holy Sect. Countless worlds were annihilated, and countless beings perished. Even many Holy Beasts had no power to resist and were instantly killed.
·········Asking for flowers··· ·····
If the Ancestors in the Dark Forbidden Zone saw this scene, they would likely fall into despair.
After all, Holy Beasts with combat power comparable to Ancestors had become like ants at this moment.
"Blood Mist Alliance, you've gone too far!!!!!"
The three Supreme Holy Beasts of the Gilded Holy Sect shouted in rage.
They didn't think about fighting to the death with the Blood Mist Alliance because they knew they couldn't win. Instead, they tried their best to break through the encirclement to unite with the Myriad Beasts Holy Sect and then with other foreign forces to contend with the Blood Mist Alliance.
However, a giant hand reached across time and space, instantly grabbing one of the Supreme Holy Beasts.
With a gentle squeeze, that Supreme Holy Beast was crushed.
Of course, this Supreme Holy Beast still hadn't perished, but before he could fully heal and recover, another strike landed. This time, every trace of the Supreme Holy Beast's life was completely wiped out, erased entirely from the world.
... .. 0
There was no power to resist!
"A third-tier Supreme True Emperor!!!"
The other two surviving Supreme Holy Beasts cried out in despair.
They had never seen such a powerhouse; in the past, the Blood Mist Alliance had never dispatched such an expert!
Why would such a powerhouse appear in the late stages of the Great Calamity? This wasn't normal!
However, they couldn't escape either.
Soon, they also died at the hands of that third-tier Supreme True Emperor of the Blood Mist Alliance—the White Turtle True Emperor.
The destruction of the Gilded Holy Sect naturally reached the Myriad Beasts Holy Sect and the Sea Sky Holy Sect.
Immediately, Ye Tian had all the human powerhouses withdraw from the Sea Sky Forbidden Land. Then, Ye Tian's copied body, taking his clone He Yuan Holy Beast, evacuated the Sea Sky Holy Sect at once. He abandoned the Sea Sky Holy Sect.
He knew very well that since the Blood Mist Alliance had wiped out the Gilded Holy Sect in an instant, their next target would likely be the Sea Sky Holy Sect.
He had no way to contend with the Blood Mist Alliance, so he didn't want to lose his clone or his copied body.
The powerhouses of the Blood Mist Alliance could enter the Sea Sky Forbidden Land through the door, so the humans naturally couldn't stay to guard it. They had to evacuate to avoid losses.
It must be said that Ye Tian's decision was very clear.
Soon, the Blood Mist Alliance arrived at the Sea Sky Holy Sect and destroyed it with a wave of a hand.
And at this time, Ye Tian arrived at the Myriad Beasts Holy Sect and.


Chapter 1509: Authority of Heaven and Earth!

Chapter 1509: Authority of Heaven and Earth!

Ye Tian knew he was an invader, but that didn't stop him from cooperating with the Myriad Beasts Holy Sect. After all, even the Myriad Beasts Holy Sect had no way to contend with the Blood Mist Alliance.
Therefore, it was the Myriad Beasts Holy Sect that truly and urgently needed other forces to cooperate with them. Ye Tian's arrival would only make the Myriad Beasts Holy Sect overjoyed.
As for Ye Tian occupying the Hai Tian Holy Sect, it wasn't a significant issue at all.
Swish! Swish! Swish!!!
One after another, Supreme-level foreign experts descended upon the Myriad Beasts Holy Sect. Clearly, they had all received transmissions from the Myriad Yuan Holy Beast. Coupled with the threat of the Blood Mist Alliance, they had no choice but to unite; otherwise, they would be harvested one by one by the Blood Mist Alliance.
Moreover, unless those foreign forces destroyed their Gates now and completely severed their connection with the Sanctuary World, the Blood Mist Alliance would eventually build Gates in the future to link to their own foreign worlds, and they would face invasion from the Blood Mist Alliance as well.
So, to protect their Gates, they had to unite and resist the Blood Mist Alliance.
Unless it was a desperate situation, these foreign experts would not easily give up on the Sanctuary World.
In almost a few moments, a large number of Supreme-level foreign experts gathered at the Myriad Beasts Holy Sect.
Just at the second tier of the Supreme level, thirteen experts had gathered here, and there were dozens more at the first tier of the Supreme level.
With so many foreign experts present, the Myriad Yuan Holy Beast breathed a slight sigh of relief.
Boom!!!!!
The Supreme True Emperors of the Blood Mist Alliance arrived, nearly surrounding the Myriad Beasts Holy Sect.
"Blood Mist Alliance, what exactly do you want to do?"
The Myriad Yuan Holy Beast questioned.
The White Turtle True Emperor smiled and said, "No special thoughts. Our goal is simple: to destroy the Sanctuary World and take complete control of it. I know you Supreme-level beings are not from the Sanctuary World. If you leave now, our Blood Mist Alliance will not act against you. Otherwise, we will treat you as part of the Sanctuary World and wipe you all out!"
After saying this, the White Turtle True Emperor displayed his strength.
The pressure of a Tier 3 Supreme True Emperor spread out, causing the expressions of the many experts present to change drastically.
"A Tier 3 Supreme True Emperor!!!!"
Ye Tian was also incredibly surprised.
Such an expert was only one step away from being an Invincible Ancestor. He was no match for the opponent and simply couldn't win.
The Myriad Yuan Holy Beast also panicked. He looked around and saw many foreign experts hesitating.
The Blood Mist Alliance had sent too many Supreme True Emperors this time, and with a Tier 3 Supreme True Emperor descending, they were clearly prepared to destroy the Sanctuary World at any cost.
They were not creatures of the Sanctuary World; there was no need for them to risk their lives for it.
Although losing the Sanctuary World meant they couldn't enter it again in the future, they at least wouldn't perish. There was still hope of finding other foreign worlds, and some forces were connected to more than one, so they didn't need to fight to the death.
Immediately, one foreign expert after another departed, and as expected, the Blood Mist Alliance did not stop them.
Before long, the number of foreign experts at the Myriad Beasts Holy Sect had significantly decreased.
Following this trend, other foreign experts, seeing the situation was dire, would not stay either.
By then, the Myriad Beasts Holy Sect would have no hope of survival.
No matter how one looked at it, the Myriad Beasts Holy Sect seemed to be in a desperate situation.
Ye Tian did not leave, because there was no need to.
His clone, the He Yuan Holy Beast, would definitely be treated as a creature of the Sanctuary World by the Blood Mist Alliance, so they wouldn't let it leave.
As for Ye Tian's own duplicated body, if it perished, it would only be a loss of some energy; the cost wasn't high.
Therefore, he would not leave.
"Blood Mist Alliance, do you truly intend to destroy our Sanctuary World?"
The Myriad Yuan Holy Beast roared.
"Correct!" The White Turtle True Emperor sneered. "If those foreign experts hadn't left, your combined strength might have actually caused us some trouble, and perhaps you could have even killed a few Supreme True Emperors of our Blood Mist Alliance. But now, almost all the foreign experts are gone. With your meager strength, you are far from being able to contend with us."
Just as the White Turtle True Emperor was about to make a move, the aura on the Myriad Yuan Holy Beast changed.
Suddenly, he took out at least ten Origin Rule Tribulation Crystals and swallowed them all at once.
These were Origin Rule Tribulation Crystals belonging to the Sanctuary World, not foreign ones, so they weren't of much help to the Myriad Yuan Holy Beast's cultivation.
However, swallowing so many at once seemed useless; it couldn't possibly allow him to step into the third tier of the Supreme Holy Beast level.
Yet, the aura on the Myriad Yuan Holy Beast became more and more terrifying, while cracks spread across his body, and a deathly aura emanated from him.
At the same time, the rules of heaven and earth underwent a change.
The He Yuan Holy Beast didn't feel much, but Ye Tian's duplicated body felt the surrounding rules suppressing him...
"Not good, retreat quickly!!!"
The White Turtle True Emperor cried out in terror.
"Tribulation Power, Disperse!"
The Myriad Yuan Holy Beast spoke.
In an instant, several Supreme True Emperors of the Blood Mist Alliance were covered by a terrifying rule. Their bodies were directly annihilated, leaving not a single trace behind.
The Myriad Yuan Holy Beast himself was not faring well either; a portion of his body was permanently annihilated.
"You actually mastered a sliver of the Sanctuary World's Authority? How do you know such a secret technique?"
The White Turtle True Emperor was terrified.
The Authority of Heaven and Earth could be used to drive, modify, and perfect the rules of a world. It might seem like it doesn't help much in increasing one's combat power.
However, the Myriad Yuan Holy Beast was able to modify the rules, changing the rules of a designated area back to the state before the Great Tribulation occurred, which was equivalent to erasing the Tribulation.
Without the Great Tribulation, how could foreign experts dare to invade the Sanctuary World? They would be erased by the world itself.
And those Supreme True Emperors just now were exactly like that. The area they were in had the Tribulation erased, and without the protection of the Tribulation environment, they were directly wiped out by the Sanctuary World.
Never mind these Tier 1 Supreme True Emperors; even a Tier 3 Supreme True Emperor who was infinitely close to the Invincible True Emperor realm could not contend with the power of the Sanctuary World.
"Hahaha, even if I sacrifice this life, I will deal a heavy blow to your Blood Mist Alliance!!!!"
The Myriad Yuan Holy Beast went mad.
He knew he couldn't survive. With his strength, he naturally couldn't perform such a secret technique without paying with his life.
A Tier 2 Supreme True Emperor who failed to escape in time was directly erased by the world.
As these Supreme True Emperors fled, the Myriad Yuan Holy Beast pursued them, and one by one, the Supreme True Emperors of the Blood Mist Alliance fell.
At this moment, the Myriad Yuan Holy Beast knew he couldn't hold on much longer and descended directly upon the Blood Mist Forbidden Land.
No one dared to stop him, and no one could.
"Shatter for me!"
The Myriad Yuan Holy Beast exhausted all his strength, striking at the Tier 2 Gate.
However, even with his full effort, he couldn't destroy the Tier 2 Gate.
With his final strike, the Myriad Yuan Holy Beast sacrificed his life to break off a corner of the Tier 2 Gate.
Subsequently, the Myriad Yuan Holy Beast perished.
Only then did the White Turtle True Emperor dare to appear here. Another Tier 3 Supreme True Emperor also stood to the side, both of their faces incredibly grim.


Chapter 1510: The Second Supreme Ancestral Technique!

Chapter 1510: The Second Supreme Ancestral Technique!

"The Second-stage Gate has been slightly damaged. If we want to repair it, it will take a very long time. Until it is fixed, we cannot transform the Sacred Domain. Transforming the Sacred Domain must use the Second-stage Gate as its foundation," the White Turtle True Emperor said angrily.
"There’s no other way. We won't be able to completely occupy the Sacred Domain during this Great Calamity. We can only wait for the next one!"
another third-tier Supreme True Emperor said helplessly.
In short, the Blood Mist Alliance had miscalculated this time.
Originally, they felt that a mere Sacred Domain didn't have many powerful experts. By threatening other foreign forces, they believed they could completely wipe out the three major Sacred Sects within the Sacred Domain. Once the three major sects were destroyed, they planned to use a supreme treasure to radiate across the entire Sacred Domain, locate all the hidden Sacred Beasts, and slaughter them all.
Then, they would begin the process of transforming the Sacred Domain, continuously expanding the Blood Mist Forbidden Zone to cover countless territories.
Although they wouldn't be able to completely transform the Sacred Domain during this single Great Calamity, they could have at least transformed nearly half of it.
Once half was transformed, they could have resisted the rules of the Sacred Domain and seized a portion of its authority.
At that point, even outside the period of a Great Calamity, the True Emperors of the Blood Mist Alliance could enter the Sacred Domain without being erased by its rules.
If that happened, the Sacred Domain would effectively fall into their hands.
But now, all of this had been ruined.
Of course, they could still execute this plan again during the next Great Calamity and ensure its perfect completion, but delaying it by an entire Great Calamity cycle was a massive loss for the Blood Mist Alliance.
Once the White Turtle True Emperor returned, he would definitely be punished by the Leader of the Blood Mist Alliance.
"Forget it. Things have come to this. Repairing the Second-stage Gate takes too long; we won't be able to fix it before this Great Calamity in the Sacred Domain ends!" the White Turtle True Emperor sighed.
……
Ten Thousand Beasts Sacred Sect.
Ye Tian was still somewhat surprised that the Wanyuan Sacred Beast possessed such means, sacrificing its own life to dismantle the Blood Mist Alliance's plan and kill many of their Supreme True Emperors.
He could sense that if the Wanyuan Sacred Beast had targeted him, his duplicate body would have been instantly annihilated as well.
After all, his duplicate body was a creature of the Dark Forbidden Domain. Once the power of the calamity receded, he would also be erased by the rules of the Sacred Domain.
*If I also mastered this kind of technique, I would truly have nothing to fear from other foreign forces in the Dark Forbidden Domain.*
Subsequently, Ye Tian wanted to trade for this secret technique with the few surviving Supreme Sacred Beasts of the Ten Thousand Beasts Sacred Sect. Unfortunately, the other Supreme Sacred Beasts of the sect did not possess this technique at all; they didn't even know the Wanyuan Sacred Beast had such a secret skill.
Thus, Ye Tian could only give up on the idea.
With the Blood Mist Alliance suffering heavy losses, the experts from other foreign forces began to return one after another, continuing their search for Source Rule Calamity Crystals within the Sacred Domain.
Ye Tian returned to the Sea-Sky Sacred Sect. Although it had been turned into ruins and all the disciples of the Sea-Sky Sacred Sect had perished, he didn't particularly care about that.
He rebuilt a base, set up arrays, and with the Heyuan Sacred Beast as the core, established a new Sacred Sect. He no longer used the name Sea-Sky Sacred Sect, but instead named it the Profound Void Sacred Sect.
In the blink of an eye, more years passed.
By this time, the Great Calamity of the Sacred Domain had finally come to an end.
Before the calamity ended, the foreign experts departed one after another, passing through the gates to leave the Sacred Domain and return to their own foreign worlds. Otherwise, if they left too late, they might accidentally be erased by the Sacred Domain's rules, which would be a foolish way to die.
-----------------
Ye Tian's duplicate body returned to the Dark Forbidden Domain, while his clone, the Heyuan Sacred Beast, stayed behind to guard the Profound Void Sacred Sect and the forbidden area, keeping watch over the gate.
On the other side, the Sea-Sky Forbidden Zone in the Dark Forbidden Domain was once again managed by the human race. A large number of human experts were stationed there, and the place was transformed into a forbidden zone suitable for human cultivation.
Not long after, the fifth Dark Era of the Dark Forbidden Domain arrived, and the fifth Dark Sacred Ground was born.
This meant that in four more Dark Eras, the Dark Forbidden Domain would face its own Great Calamity.
For Ye Tian, the duration of four Dark Eras was still quite long; he had enough time to increase his strength.
With his abilities and talents, reaching the third tier of a Supreme Ancestor should not be a problem.
"Over such a long time, I have continuously searched for Ancestral Talents. Every Original Ancestral World within the Dark Sacred Grounds has an Ancestral Talent race. Combined with my last trip to the Sacred Domain, where my duplicate body copied many, many Ancestral Talents, all these talents have now been fused. This has allowed me to give birth to many Ultimate Ancestral Talents. For now, I don't need to worry about Ultimate Ancestral Talents. It is time to create several Supreme Ancestral Techniques and strive to step into the third tier of the Supreme Ancestor realm."
Ye Tian murmured to himself.
Soon after, he took out a Source Rule Calamity Crystal from the Sacred Domain and began to comprehend the rules of that world.
Then, his duplicate body began to burn Ancestral Talents, activating the Evolutionary Trait to deduce the Space Ultimate Ancestral Technique—Void Slash.
Void Slash was once an Ancestral Technique, but after he fused numerous Space Ancestral Talents into an Ultimate Space Ancestral Talent, he had recently deduced this technique to the level of an Ultimate Ancestral Technique.
Therefore, he only needed to create a version of Void Slash that was compatible with the rules of the Sacred Domain. Then, he could attempt to fuse the two versions of the Ultimate Ancestral Technique Void Slash to form a single Supreme Ancestral Technique: Void Slash.
Using the Evolutionary Trait to comprehend and create the Void Slash Ultimate Ancestral Technique, his progress was incredibly fast.
Before long, the duplicate body's Ancestral Talents were burned out, and it completely shattered.
Next, Ye Tian spent some resources to condense another duplicate body and once again used it to activate the Evolutionary Trait to create the Ultimate Ancestral Technique Void Slash.
"Such incredible speed. Back then, it took me ten Domain Years to create an Ultimate Ancestral Technique, but it took nearly an entire Dark Era to fuse two Ultimate Ancestral Techniques into a Supreme Ancestral Technique. Although that was created by the Heyuan Sacred Beast, whose talent is somewhat inferior, even if my main body were to create and fuse them, it would take at least dozens of Domain Epochs. Now, by sacrificing duplicate bodies and repeatedly activating the Evolutionary Trait, I estimate that in at most one Domain Epoch, I can fuse the two Ultimate Ancestral Techniques of Void Slash." Ye Tian thought with full confidence.
In a very short amount of time, an Ultimate Ancestral Technique compatible with the rules of the Sacred Domain was created by Ye Tian.
Next, he began to fuse the two versions of the Ultimate Ancestral Technique Void Slash, which was the real challenge.
As his duplicate bodies collapsed and were annihilated time and time again, finally, after many annihilations and the consumption of a vast amount of resources, approximately one Domain Epoch passed. Ye Tian finally fused the two Ultimate Ancestral Techniques of Void Slash, resulting in the Supreme Ancestral Technique: Void Slash.
When the Supreme Ancestral Technique Void Slash was created, Ye Tian's physical body fused with it, undergoing a massive transformation.
BOOM!!!!!
Ye Tian's physical body transformed, as countless resources were turned into energy to facilitate the process.
After a long time, the physical transformation was complete, and Ye Tian's strength had become even more powerful.
Possessing two major Supreme Ancestral Techniques, Ye Tian's current strength was likely very close to that of a third-tier Supreme Ancestor expert.


Chapter 1511: The Third Level of the Supreme Ancestor!

Chapter 1511: The Third Level of the Supreme Ancestor!

In just one domain epoch, Ye Tian had mastered another Supreme Ancestral Technique. At this rate, it wouldn't take long for him to step into the third level of the Supreme Ancestor.
"I have already mastered two Supreme Ancestral Techniques. For the third one, I'll choose the Eternal Supreme Ancestral Technique!"
Ye Tian decided.
This Supreme Ancestral Technique was a Time Supreme Ancestral Technique, which required comprehending another Eternal Ultimate Ancestral Technique.
Thus, Ye Tian continued to contemplate the Origin Rule Calamity Crystal of the Sanctuary Heaven and Earth, repeatedly using his duplicated bodies to trigger the derivation trait, causing them to collapse time and again.
Under these circumstances, Ye Tian quickly created another Eternal Ultimate Ancestral Technique that aligned with the rules of the Sanctuary Heaven and Earth.
Next, he began to fuse the two Eternal Ultimate Ancestral Techniques to create an Eternal Supreme Ancestral Technique.
This time, he took a bit longer.
As for the reason, Ye Tian knew it well.
Using the same Sanctuary Heaven and Earth to create Supreme Ancestral Techniques would become increasingly difficult unless he switched to a different foreign heaven and earth.
However, Ye Tian currently only had the Origin Rule Calamity Crystal of the Sanctuary Heaven and Earth, making it easiest to comprehend its rules. Even if it took some time, it didn't matter much.
After two domain epochs, Ye Tian successfully fused the two Eternal Ultimate Ancestral Techniques into one Supreme Ancestral Technique.
With this, Ye Tian had mastered three Supreme Ancestral Techniques at once, and his strength skyrocketed.
Furthermore, over these years, Ye Tian continuously refined resources from the Sanctuary Heaven and Earth. His cultivation rose steadily, and his physical body underwent three transformations. Combined with the amplification of the three Supreme Ancestral Techniques, his strength was far greater than when he had first broken through to the Supreme Ancestor level.
However, Ye Tian was still a bit short of the third level of the Supreme Ancestor.
In reality, the limit for every Supreme Ancestor was different.
In terms of actual combat power, Ye Tian wasn't far from the third level, but he was still far from his own limit.
Once he truly reached the third level of the Supreme Ancestor, he would be much more powerful than other third-level experts.
In the following years, Ye Tian continued to create Supreme Ancestral Techniques.
To create the fourth Supreme Ancestral Technique, Ye Tian spent nearly ten domain epochs.
And to create the fifth, he spent thirty domain epochs.
After spending another sixty domain epochs, Ye Tian finally created the sixth Supreme Ancestral Technique.
Meanwhile, the Dark Forbidden Realm had passed its sixth Dark Era. Only three Dark Eras remained before the fourth great tribulation of the Dark Forbidden Realm would arrive.
......
"Now I have mastered six Supreme Ancestral Techniques: Tyrant Strength, Streamer, Sacred Armor, Void Slash, Eternal, and God-Suppressing. Combined with the countless resources I've refined from the Sanctuary Heaven and Earth, my cultivation has risen high enough. With my current strength, although I haven't reached my limit, I am even more powerful than an average third-level Supreme Ancestor. I can now be considered at the third level of the Supreme Ancestor!"
Ye Tian thought to himself.
He wasn't sure if this level of strength was enough to protect the human race, but he wanted to improve even more.
The threats facing the Dark Forbidden Realm were no less than those of the Sanctuary Heaven and Earth. Even the Bone Race might be stronger than the Myriad Beast Saint Sect of the Sanctuary Heaven and Earth.
And the Bone Race wasn't actually the greatest threat to the Dark Forbidden Realm; the real threats were the forces behind the six major forbidden zones.
Even now, Ye Tian had not attempted to enter those six forbidden zones. The top ancestors of the Dark Forbidden Realm also knew very little about them.
Calamity Black Mountain, Destruction Swamp, Boundless Wall, Firmament Sword Tomb, Illusory Dream World, and Infinite Demon Sea.
These were the six forbidden zones, and also six major powers.
They were likely no weaker than the so-called Blood Mist Alliance. It was just that the Dark Forbidden Realm was a newly born forbidden realm, protected by the Supreme Rules and unable to be modified.
The Sanctuary Heaven and Earth was targeted by the Blood Mist Alliance because its protection period had ended.
But the Dark Forbidden Realm was too young, so there was no immediate worry about it being occupied.
However, without enough strength, it would still be destroyed. Those powerful forces definitely did not want to see the Dark Forbidden Realm rise.
"I must understand the general strength of those six major forces; otherwise, I will be very passive when the great tribulation of the Dark Forbidden Realm arrives!"
Ye Tian murmured.
Seeking information from the top ancestors of the Dark Forbidden Realm yielded almost nothing.
He thought of one power—the Bone Race!
The Bone Race had entered the Dark Forbidden Realm many times, so they should logically know about these six major forces.
Thus, Ye Tian arrived at the Bone Sea Forbidden Zone, intending to trade with the Bone Race again and inquire about the six major forces.
--------------
Bone Sea Forbidden Zone.
The Bone Race was very pleased with Ye Tian's arrival.
But since Ye Tian was powerful, the Bone Race naturally didn't want to offend him.
Soon, a Bone Emperor of the Bone Ancestor condensed a wisp of consciousness and descended upon the Bone Sea Forbidden Zone.
"Ancestor of Myriad Laws, why have you come here again?"
The Bone Emperor said with some annoyance.
"Bone Emperor Cang Yu, I wish to trade some resources with your Bone Race and also ask about the forces behind the six forbidden zones of the Dark Forbidden Realm," Ye Tian said.
"Not interested in trading!"
Bone Emperor Cang Yu refused.
"What if it's an Origin Rule Calamity Crystal?" Ye Tian took out an Origin Rule Calamity Crystal from the Sanctuary Heaven and Earth and said, "You should be interested in such a good thing, right?"
"An Origin Rule Calamity Crystal? This isn't from your Dark Forbidden Realm. Where did you get it?"
Bone Emperor Cang Yu said in shock.
"Regardless of where it came from, you must be interested. I want to use this Origin Rule Calamity Crystal to trade for one from your foreign heaven and earth. This is a mutually beneficial trade!" Ye Tian said with a smile.
Since he had two Origin Rule Calamity Crystals from the Sanctuary Heaven and Earth, trading one wouldn't affect him much. If he could exchange it for one from the Bone Race's world, it would be a great deal!
Bone Emperor Cang Yu stared at the crystal in Ye Tian's hand and nodded. "This Origin Rule Calamity Crystal is indeed one our Bone Race doesn't have. We are willing to trade."
Subsequently.
Bone Emperor Cang Yu descended in person to the Bone Sea Forbidden Zone and completed the trade with Ye Tian.
"Bone Emperor Cang Yu, can you tell me about the six forbidden zones?"
Ye Tian asked.
"I can tell you, but what treasure can you offer in exchange?" Bone Emperor Cang Yu asked.
"How about my friendship?"
Ye Tian revealed his pressure.
Boom!!!!!
The pressure belonging to the third level of the Supreme Ancestor spread out, making Bone Emperor Cang Yu tremble.
He could sense that Ye Tian could easily kill him in an instant, even preventing him from escaping.
"The third level of the Supreme Ancestor? How is this possible? You were clearly only at the level of having just broken through to the Supreme Ancestor before. How could you have stepped into the third level so quickly???" Bone Emperor Cang Yu was stunned.
Only a few Dark Eras had passed. For Supreme-level beings, a few Dark Eras wasn't a long time.
Many Supreme-level foreign experts had gone through multiple great tribulations without being able to improve their strength much, yet Ye Tian's progress was too illogical.
Knowing Ye Tian's strength, Bone Emperor Cang Yu's attitude changed, and he immediately answered Ye Tian's question.
"Alright, I can tell you the general situation of those six forces!" Bone Emperor Cang Yu said.


Chapter 1512: Super-Rank Power!

Chapter 1512: Super-Rank Power!

The Cangyu Bone Emperor slowly revealed the powers behind the six great forbidden zones of the Dark Forbidden Domain, while Ye Tian listened intently.
The Cangyu Bone Emperor said, "The powers behind the six forbidden zones of the Dark Forbidden Domain are stronger than our Bone Race. The gates established by those six forbidden zones are Second-Tier Gates!"
"What, Second-Tier Gates!"
Ye Tian was incredibly surprised.
He knew very well what a Second-Tier Gate represented; the gate established by the Blood Mist Alliance was a Second-Tier Gate.
Although he didn't know how to establish a Second-Tier Gate, any power capable of doing so was bound to be immensely powerful.
The Sanctuary Heaven and Earth only had one Second-Tier Gate, yet the Dark Forbidden Domain actually possessed six. This was simply unbelievable.
Immediately, he asked, "Why are there six Second-Tier Gates in the Dark Forbidden Domain? I have been to other foreign heavens and earths, and the one I visited before only had one Second-Tier Gate."
The Cangyu Bone Emperor did not answer directly, but said evasively, "The Dark Forbidden Domain seems to be somewhat different from other foreign heavens and earths. As for how it is different, I am not sure, but it is significant enough for six powerful forces to open Second-Tier Gates."
Ye Tian didn't know if the Cangyu Bone Emperor truly didn't know or was intentionally withholding information, but he didn't press further.
The Cangyu Bone Emperor continued, "Those six foreign powers are capable of establishing Second-Tier Gates and possess many Supreme-level existences, even those of the third tier. There are even rumors that there are Invincible-level existences among those six major powers. Of course, we have never been to the foreign realms of those six powers, so we cannot know more detailed information. However, based on several interactions, the most powerful among them should be Calamity Black Mountain, followed by the Firmament Sword Tomb. The other four major powers are likely comparable to each other."
Subsequently, the Cangyu Bone Emperor provided a piece of information that surprised Ye Tian.
Calamity Black Mountain once deployed six third-tier Supreme-level existences to fight a great war against other forces right within the Dark Forbidden Domain.
As for why the battle broke out, the Bone Race did not know, because they were too weak to dare approach.
Of course, this was the Cangyu Bone Emperor's way of putting it.
"Ancestor of Ten Thousand Laws, I might as well provide you with some data!" the Cangyu Bone Emperor said. "Among the many foreign heavens and earths, major powers are divided into grades. Those without Supreme-level existences aren't worth mentioning. Any power that possesses Supreme-level existences but lacks a second-tier Supreme-level existence is called an Unnamed Rank power, meaning they aren't even qualified to have their names known, representing weakness. A power that possesses a second-tier Supreme-level existence and has more than three Supreme-level existences in total is called a Named Rank power, indicating they have potential worth noting. A power that possesses a third-tier Supreme-level existence and has more than ten Supreme-level existences is called a Great Rank power. And a power that possesses an Invincible-level existence is called a Super-Rank power. Above Super-Rank powers, it is said there are also Saint-Rank powers and Eternal-Rank powers. Those six major powers belong to the Super-Rank category; their strength is unfathomable!"
Unnamed Rank, Named Rank, Great Rank, Super-Rank...
Such a classification was very apt and simple, but it also presented the truth of the law of the jungle: without strength, one didn't even have the qualification to be remembered.
"According to this classification, our Human Race can only be considered an Unnamed Rank power!"
Ye Tian thought to himself.
Although he had reached the third tier of the Supreme Ancestor level, the Human Race had no other Supreme Ancestors besides him, so they didn't even count as a Named Rank power.
Furthermore, the Human Race's foundation was too shallow; not only was he the only Supreme Ancestor, but even ordinary Ancestors were incredibly scarce.
Of course, this was also because the Human Race had not yet survived a single Great Tribulation. It was said that once a tribulation was passed, providence would skyrocket, and cultivation would become much easier.
Once they survived a Great Tribulation, the Human Race would have the chance to give birth to many Ancestors.
Afterward, Ye Tian spoke with the Cangyu Bone Emperor for a while longer before departing.
Although he now had a general understanding of the strength of the six major powers, the pressure had actually increased.
Six Super-Rank powers, each possessing at least one Invincible-level existence, and each power having more than just one or two third-tier Supreme-level existences comparable to him.
Such powers would be very difficult for him to contend with.
"It seems I must raise my strength to a level nearly invincible among the Supreme-level before the Great Tribulation of the Dark Forbidden Domain arrives."
Ye Tian thought secretly.
Having learned the strength of the six major powers, he no longer had any intention of barging into the six forbidden zones.
At the very least, for now, only the Bone Race knew of his strength, and the Bone Race had no way to contact the people of those six major powers. Therefore, those six powers did not yet know that a third-tier Supreme Ancestor had been born in the Dark Forbidden Domain.
If they knew, the six major powers might dispatch even more Supreme-level existences during the Dark Forbidden Domain's Great Tribulation.
Therefore, there were benefits to hiding his strength and keeping a low profile.
...
Trading for a Source Rule Tribulation Crystal from the Bone Race this time brought many benefits to Ye Tian. At the very least, he could easily create several more Supreme Ancestral Techniques.
After all, it was becoming increasingly difficult for him to fuse Ultimate Ancestral Techniques that harmonized with the rules of the Sanctuary Heaven and Earth, requiring a long time. However, fusing with a Source Rule Tribulation Crystal that harmonized with the Bone Race's world was much easier.
"For the next Ultimate Ancestral Technique, I'll choose the Extreme Arm Ultimate Ancestral Technique!"
Ye Tian decided.
Thus, with the help of the Bone Race's Source Rule Tribulation Crystal, he began to comprehend the Extreme Arm Ultimate Ancestral Technique that harmonized with the Bone Race's world rules. It didn't take long for him to successfully create the Extreme Arm Ultimate Ancestral Technique.
Next, he began to fuse the two types of Extreme Arm Ultimate Ancestral Techniques.
In the blink of an eye, one Domain Epoch passed.
"I've finally succeeded in the fusion. I didn't expect that fusing an Ultimate Ancestral Technique harmonized with the Bone Race's world rules for the first time would be so easy. With the Evolution characteristic plus the Copying Body, if I have enough different Source Rule Tribulation Crystals from various worlds, I'm afraid I could skyrocket my strength to a terrifying degree in a short time!"
Ye Tian thought.
Successfully creating the Extreme Arm Supreme Ancestral Technique was equivalent to possessing a seventh Supreme Ancestral Technique, causing Ye Tian's body to undergo another transformation and his strength to increase once more.
Next, Ye Tian began attempting to create an eighth Supreme Ancestral Technique.
This time, the Ultimate Ancestral Technique he chose was the Golden Body Ultimate Ancestral Technique. Having an extra Supreme Defensive Ancestral Technique would at least make his life-preserving capabilities stronger.
To create the eighth Supreme Ancestral Technique, Ye Tian spent one and a half Domain Epochs.
For the ninth Supreme Ancestral Technique, Ye Tian still chose a defensive Supreme Ancestral Technique, which took him two Domain Epochs this time.


Chapter 1513: Twelve Supreme Ancestral Techniques!

Chapter 1513: Twelve Supreme Ancestral Techniques!

Nine supreme ancestral techniques—this number was an absolutely staggering figure for many supreme-level existences.
Generally, even a third-tier Supreme Primordial Ancestor would be unable to master nine supreme ancestral techniques.
Under normal circumstances, once one's cultivation reached a point where it was difficult to improve further, mastering four or five supreme ancestral techniques would be equivalent to the third tier of a Supreme Primordial Ancestor.
Yet, Ye Tian had mastered a full nine supreme ancestral techniques; this number was truly terrifying.
In the years that followed, besides refining countless resources to accumulate cultivation, Ye Tian spent the rest of his time comprehending and creating supreme ancestral techniques.
Long years passed, and one domain epoch after another went by.
Finally, the Dark Forbidden Domain passed its seventh Dark Era.
By this time, Ye Tian's strength had surged. Not only had his cultivation reached a level where further progress was difficult, but he had also mastered a total of twelve supreme ancestral techniques.
Twelve supreme ancestral techniques allowed Ye Tian's strength to far surpass that of an ordinary third-tier Supreme Primordial Ancestor, reaching an incredible level, though he was still definitely no match for an Invincible Ancestor.
"It's becoming harder and harder to fuse ultimate ancestral techniques that are compatible with the Sacred Domain and the Bone Clan worlds. It's taking more and more time. Now, creating just one more supreme ancestral technique would take at least an entire Dark Era, and there are only two Dark Eras left until the Great Calamity."
Ye Tian frowned.
Therefore, he could no longer continue practicing in such a step-by-step manner.
"I must obtain Source Rule Calamity Crystals from other foreign worlds!"
Ye Tian thought to himself.
However, Source Rule Calamity Crystals were incredibly precious; how could other factions possibly trade them to him?
Even if he traded item for item, exchanging one Source Rule Calamity Crystal for another, it wouldn't be easy. After all, no faction wanted to see another grow stronger.
Those factions would rather slowly collect Source Rule Calamity Crystals over long ages than trade them away.
Furthermore, Source Rule Calamity Crystals would eventually be consumed; they couldn't be used indefinitely.
Additionally, once experts from many factions obtained a Source Rule Calamity Crystal, they might refine it directly to increase their cultivation instead of using it for comprehension.
"Trading with the Bone Clan again probably won't work. Their world's Source Rule Calamity Crystals are useless to me now, and even if they have crystals from other foreign worlds, they won't trade them. If I ask, they'll likely just say they don't have any," Ye Tian thought.
He thought for a moment and prepared to trade with other Nameless-grade or Named-grade foreign powers in the Dark Forbidden Domain.
If these factions were unwilling, he would destroy their forbidden lands and their gates.
There were dozens of forbidden lands in the Dark Forbidden Domain, which meant there were dozens of foreign powers. Factions like the Bone Clan were ranked relatively high.
There were also many foreign powers behind forbidden lands that were only equivalent to the level of the Sea Heaven Sacred Sect. He could easily threaten them.
Of course, these weaker factions might not necessarily have Source Rule Calamity Crystals; it would require a bit of luck.
"If they don't have Source Rule Calamity Crystals, then I'll just rob them of some resources. I'm sure they'll be willing to give them up!" Ye Tian said coldly.
......
Golden Sun River Forbidden Land.
This was a base established by a foreign power called the Golden Sun River Palace. It resembled a massive river and was one of the bottom ten among the dozens of forbidden lands in the Dark Forbidden Domain. It wasn't very dangerous, and even top-tier ancestors could enter and leave safely.
This forbidden land produced a treasure called Golden Sun River Beads, which were one of the treasures born from the collision of rules.
Any base established by a foreign power would produce some treasures under the collision of rules between two different worlds. Exactly what treasures would be born depended on luck.
Golden Sun River Beads could be used to restore energy and heal wounds, making them decent items.
On this day.
Ye Tian arrived at the Golden Sun River Forbidden Land, but he had no interest in the Golden Sun River Beads. He was here for the Golden Sun River Palace.
Boom!!!
Ye Tian stepped inside, causing a disturbance in the rules.
Immediately, the experts of the Golden Sun River Palace took notice and launched an attack on Ye Tian at once.
Hands covered in scales reached out across the void, striking toward Ye Tian.
Hmph!
Ye Tian snorted coldly, and a terrifying force directly shattered those hands.
"Get lost!!!"
Ye Tian shouted, and the entire void of the Golden Sun River Forbidden Land shattered. One by one, the experts of the Golden Sun River Palace were heavily injured and spat out blood.
"A Supreme Primordial Ancestor!!!!"
The experts of the Golden Sun River Palace were horrified.
They only had a few top-tier River Ancestors stationed here, who were only equivalent to top-tier ancestors. How could they be a match for Ye Tian?
· ·········Seeking Flowers··· ·····
Immediately, they wanted to go for reinforcements.
Ye Tian did not stop them, letting them seek help.
After all, he wanted to speak with the Supreme River Ancestor of the Golden Sun River Palace. These top-tier River Ancestors were not qualified to talk to him.
Soon.
The Supreme River Ancestor of the Golden Sun River Palace crossed through the gate and arrived at the Golden Sun River Forbidden Land.
Rumble!!!
A figure with a human torso and a fish tail flew out from the gate.
The experts of the Golden Sun River Palace were similar to a merman race, living in river water, which was why the Golden Sun River base was like a river.
"Lord River Ancestor Lingze, a Supreme Primordial Ancestor from the Dark Forbidden Domain is attacking!!!"
... .. 0
The top-tier River Ancestors cried out for help.
River Ancestor Lingze saw Ye Tian and originally intended to threaten him, but the more he looked, the more something felt wrong.
Terror!
True, absolute terror!
He had never seen such a terrifying expert. Although the aura on Ye Tian's body was concealed, the slight trace of aura he emitted made Lingze feel as if he were facing a true nightmare.
Clearly, Ye Tian was no ordinary Supreme Primordial Ancestor.
"Respected Excellency, I believe there might be some misunderstanding between us?" River Ancestor Lingze said with a smile.
Ye Tian said coldly, "Misunderstanding? I am a Supreme Primordial Ancestor of the Dark Forbidden Domain, and you are a foreign power, an invader. Do you really think there's a misunderstanding?"
Ye Tian approached River Ancestor Lingze, no longer suppressing his cultivation aura.
Immediately, River Ancestor Lingze finally understood Ye Tian's level of strength.
The third tier of the Supreme Primordial Ancestor realm!
Heavens, the entire Golden Sun River Palace didn't even have a second-tier Supreme River Ancestor; they only had a few first-tier Supreme River Ancestors.
To the Golden Sun River Palace, an expert like Ye Tian was absolutely an existence they had to look up to.
It was only because Ye Tian was not an expert from their foreign world; otherwise, they would have all knelt and surrendered immediately. How would they dare to offend him?
"Respected powerhouse, since you didn't strike immediately, I assume you didn't come to destroy this base? If there is anything you need, please just say it!" River Ancestor Lingze asked.
"I want to trade for a Source Rule Calamity Crystal from your Golden Sun River Palace!"
Ye Tian demanded.


Chapter 1514: Only One Dark Era Left!

Chapter 1514: Only One Dark Era Left!

"Origin Rule Calamity Crystal?"
Upon hearing the name of this treasure, Lingze River Ancestor's expression shifted instantly. He then said helplessly, "My Lord, where would we get an Origin Rule Calamity Crystal? They are far too precious. Our Jinyang River Palace failed to seize a single Origin Rule Calamity Crystal in the Dark Forbidden Domain, and in our own foreign world, our strength isn't particularly great, so we couldn't compete with others. We did manage to snatch one once, but news of it leaked by accident, so we refined it immediately for fear of it being stolen by other powerful forces."
"A force like our Jinyang River Palace is too weak. We don't even have a single second-tier Supreme River Ancestor. We could be wiped out at any moment; how could we possibly keep an Origin Rule Calamity Crystal in stock?"
"No Origin Rule Calamity Crystals?" Ye Tian was somewhat disappointed.
Judging that Lingze River Ancestor was likely telling the truth, he decided not to pursue the crystals with them.
"Since you don't have Origin Rule Calamity Crystals, then let's trade for some resources. If you dare to refuse, then don't expect this base to continue existing, and I will destroy this gate as well!" Ye Tian threatened.
Faced with Ye Tian's threat, Lingze River Ancestor naturally did not dare to refuse and agreed to the trade.
Thus, Ye Tian brought out many resources and treasures, demanding that Lingze River Ancestor mobilize resources from their main headquarters. If the resources weren't delivered, Lingze River Ancestor wouldn't be allowed to leave.
Of course, Ye Tian wasn't interested in an equal exchange; it was essentially a trade where he gave one portion of resources for ten of theirs. Otherwise, how could it be called a "Great Calamity Trade"?
Soon, countless resources were sent from the Jinyang River Palace, and the trade with Ye Tian was completed.
Afterward.
Ye Tian left the Jinyang River Forbidden Area and continued to other forbidden areas.
After Ye Tian departed, Lingze River Ancestor murmured, "During the last Great Calamity, the Dark Forbidden Domain hadn't even given birth to a single Supreme Progenitor. Now, before this Great Calamity has even arrived, a third-tier Supreme Progenitor has suddenly emerged. How did he do it?"
To become a Supreme Progenitor, one must fuse Progenitor Laws. This requires going to other foreign worlds to create Progenitor Laws or obtaining Origin Rule Calamity Crystals from other foreign worlds to use them to comprehend foreign world rules, thereby creating a Progenitor Law that fits those rules.
Therefore, it was absolutely impossible for Ye Tian to become a Supreme Progenitor relying solely on himself.
Clearly, Ye Tian had someone behind him, or a powerful organization.
"To be able to easily create a third-tier Supreme Progenitor... is it one of those six Beyond-Famous grade forces? Or has an even more powerful force intervened in the Dark Forbidden Domain?"
Lingze River Ancestor speculated.
However, this matter had nothing to do with him. Jinyang River Palace was too weak and had no desire to get involved in anything.
Over the following days, Ye Tian continuously visited various forbidden areas, specifically seeking out weak forces to "trade" with.
These forces did not dare to resist Ye Tian's arrival at all.
After trading with these forces, Ye Tian obtained a massive amount of foreign world resources. These were not only helpful to him but also to the Progenitors of the human race, helping them reach the level of top-tier Progenitors faster.
Through multiple trades, Ye Tian finally managed to acquire two Origin Rule Calamity Crystals, replacing the ones he had previously used.
After obtaining the two new Origin Rule Calamity Crystals, Ye Tian returned to closed-door cultivation to comprehend and create Supreme Ancestral Techniques.
It must be said that with the new Origin Rule Calamity Crystals, Ye Tian's speed in fusing ultimate ancestral techniques was incredibly fast, but it was still somewhat affected. It wasn't as fast as the very first time he used an Origin Rule Calamity Crystal to create a Supreme Ancestral Technique.
For the thirteenth Supreme Ancestral Technique, Ye Tian spent a full two Realm Eras to create it successfully, which wasn't particularly fast.
For the fourteenth Supreme Ancestral Technique, Ye Tian spent a full six Realm Eras.
To create the fifteenth Supreme Ancestral Technique, Ye Tian spent twenty Realm Eras.
Subsequently, he spent sixty Realm Eras on the sixteenth Supreme Ancestral Technique.
At this point, he switched to the other Origin Rule Calamity Crystal for comprehension and creation.
As a result, it took him three Realm Eras to create the seventeenth Supreme Ancestral Technique. Clearly, the difficulty of creation and fusion had increased again.
Unknowingly, the Dark Forbidden Domain passed its eighth Dark Era, leaving only one Dark Era of time remaining.
By now, Ye Tian had created a total of nineteen Supreme Ancestral Techniques. His strength was incredibly terrifying, far surpassing that of an ordinary third-tier Supreme Progenitor...
Now, Ye Tian found that for every new Supreme Ancestral Technique he created, the increase in his strength was very, very weak.
Unless he found a way to break through to become an Invincible Progenitor, it would be impossible for his strength to increase significantly!
However, he did not know how to become an Invincible Progenitor, and likely many third-tier Supreme experts didn't know either.
Furthermore, becoming an Invincible Progenitor was likely even harder than becoming a Supreme Progenitor.
He had previously threatened some Nameless-grade forces to learn the secrets of reaching the Invincible Progenitor level, but none of them knew.
Therefore, he temporarily set aside the idea of pushing for the Invincible Progenitor stage.
"There is only one Dark Era of time left. Even if I go trade for more Origin Rule Calamity Crystals, it would be difficult to create many more Supreme Ancestral Techniques, and I wouldn't be able to increase my strength much. It would be better to help my family members create Progenitor Laws that fit foreign world rules and then pass them on, helping them push toward becoming Supreme Progenitors!" Ye Tian thought to himself.
Indeed, through his research, Ye Tian now knew that becoming a Supreme Progenitor didn't necessarily require creating one's own foreign Progenitor Law. Just like becoming a Progenitor, one could fuse an ownerless Progenitor Law.
Becoming a Supreme Progenitor was the same. If one obtained two Progenitor Laws from a fallen Supreme Progenitor, they could fuse those two laws to push for the Supreme Progenitor level.
In fact, because of the experience left behind by the Supreme Progenitor, the difficulty of fusing to become a Supreme Progenitor was actually lower.
For instance, most of those Nameless-grade forces had luckily become Supreme Progenitors by stumbling upon the treasures or inheritances of fallen Supreme Progenitors.
Otherwise, many Nameless-grade forces were too weak and couldn't snatch Origin Rule Calamity Crystals. During a Foreign World Great Calamity, they could only stay for one Realm Year. How could they possibly create a Progenitor Law in such a short time?
Thus, inheriting two Progenitor Laws from a fallen Supreme Progenitor gave one a certain chance of becoming a Supreme Progenitor.
It was a "certain chance," not a certainty. If the compatibility between the Progenitor Law and oneself was not high, the chance of success would not be great.
Furthermore, a Supreme Progenitor created this way would be very weak, inferior to one who achieved it through their own efforts. But no matter how weak, a Supreme Progenitor was still a Supreme Progenitor.


Chapter 1515: Relatives Become Supreme Primordials!

Chapter 1515: Relatives Become Supreme Primordials!

Creating Primordial Laws was not difficult for Ye Tian. Moreover, the Primordial Laws practiced by his relatives—Xiao Yue, Ye Xingchen, Ye Xingyue, and Ye Yu—were all created by him. Therefore, he understood their laws perfectly. He only needed to create corresponding Primordial Laws based on their bodies and Primordial Bodies combined with Otherworld rules.
Previously, Ye Tian had already created a batch of Primordial Laws and fused them to create his own Endless Primordial Law.
Now, he only needed to modify them slightly to make them compatible with his family members before passing these Otherworld Primordial Laws to them.
When the time came, they would follow the steps, using the Otherworld Primordial Laws to ascend to the Primordial realm once more on a second path. After reaching the level of Top-tier Primordials, they would combine the two Primordial Laws and fuse them to become Supreme Primordials.
In just a few dozen realm years, Ye Tian created Primordial Laws that were perfectly suited to his relatives' Primordial Bodies.
Subsequently, Ye Tian taught the four Primordial Laws to them one by one, guiding their cultivation and providing a massive amount of resources.
Under Ye Tian's guidance and the supply of vast resources, Xiao Yue and the others used the Otherworld Primordial Laws to step into the Primordial realm again on their second path. Shortly after, they returned to the Top-tier Primordial level.
With both Primordial Laws elevated to the Top-tier Primordial level, their strength increased significantly, already surpassing other Top-tier Primordials.
Next, they pushed both Primordial Laws to the absolute limit of the Top-tier Primordial level. They only needed to fuse the two laws to break through to the Supreme Primordial realm—the realm that countless Primordials dreamed of.
With Ye Tian's guidance, even though they hadn't created the laws themselves, it wouldn't take them too long to advance to the Supreme Primordial realm.
If Ye Tian hadn't helped, it might have taken them several Dark Eras to reach that level.
But with his guidance, it wouldn't even take one Dark Era.
As time passed, countless cultivators throughout the Dark Forbidden Zone began to grow anxious because news of the Great Calamity was spreading.
The current Dark Forbidden Zone was no longer what it once was. The number of Primordials had increased tenfold, and the Human Race had even more, reaching triple digits. Among them were those who had advanced by creating their own Primordial Laws, as well as those who used the laws Ye Tian had created.
With hundreds of Primordials, such a number was enough to make any force find it difficult to compete.
The Human Race no longer took other forces seriously; their only goals were the other Otherworld Heavens and Earths.
Furthermore, the Human Race possessed the Saint Realm Heaven and Earth as a resource point, allowing them to obtain many resources. Consequently, the Human Primordials had ample resources, and one by one, they ascended to the Top-tier Primordial level. Some had even surpassed the Destruction Primordial and the Saint Ancestor.
Finally, with less than ten realm epochs remaining before the Great Calamity, Ye Tian's wife, Xiao Yue, was the first to advance to the Supreme Primordial realm.
Following her, Ye Xingchen, Ye Xingyue, and Ye Yu successively advanced to the Supreme Primordial realm.
At this point, the Human Race possessed four Supreme Primordials.
If categorized by power, the Human Race could at least be rated as a Ranked-tier force. Moreover, with a powerhouse like Ye Tian present, as long as he did not fall, even those Renowned-tier forces would not dare to offend the Human Race.
...
On this day.
The heads of many forces outside the Human Race held a meeting together. The leaders were the Destruction Saint Clan and various Saint-Gate level forces from the Dark Holy Lands, such as the Saint Ancestor.
The current strengths of the Destruction Primordial, Spacetime Primordial, World Ancestor, and Saint Ancestor were also much greater than in the past. They had reached the peak of the Top-tier Primordial realm, not inferior to those ancient Primordials.
Unless it was a Top-tier Primordial possessing a Supreme Ancestral Artifact, they could not be easily crushed.
Supreme Ancestral Artifacts were like the Supreme Imperial Weapons of the Bone Clan; their value was incredibly high. Even for a Supreme Primordial, they were quite precious.
Ye Tian had wiped out the Sea-Sky Holy Sect and, combined with the various materials he had collected, had only managed to refine a few Supreme Ancestral Artifacts in total.
Therefore, aside from the Human Race, other forces in the Dark Forbidden Zone did not possess Supreme Ancestral Artifacts. To them, such items were legends and not counted as regular combat power.
"Destruction Primordial, what is the main purpose of this meeting? The Great Calamity is approaching. Although none of us have experienced it, based on the limited intelligence available, the calamity is terrifyingly horrific. Even for Primordials, it is a narrow escape from death. We must be prepared!" a Top-tier Primordial asked.
The Destruction Primordial smiled and said, "What preparation? When the Great Calamity arrives, our strength will be like that of ants. Unless we hide, but even then, it is easy to be found; it almost entirely depends on luck. If your luck is good, you can survive by hiding. If your luck is bad, you die instantly!"
"Perhaps if we unite, we might have a chance to survive!" an Elite Primordial suggested.
"Unite? No matter how we unite, we cannot contend with a single Supreme Primordial. And when the Great Calamity comes, do you know how many Supreme Primordial-level experts there will be? Even those ancient Primordials who survived one calamity still don't dare to show their faces, fearing their hiding spots will be exposed. Uniting is useless. Currently, there are only two ways!" the Destruction Primordial said.
"What ways?"
The many Primordials were curious.
The Destruction Primordial said, "The first way is to seek refuge with an Otherworld force. If they accept us, we have a hope of surviving. The second way is to find a place we believe is very hidden, such as a special spacetime node, and then use ultimate concealment-type Ancestral Techniques. If luck is on our side, we won't be discovered. But Supreme Primordials are very powerful; whether we can hide from them, I cannot say for sure."
Seek refuge? Hide?
They had thought of these two methods, but no one had spoken them aloud.
Now, the Destruction Primordial had said it.
"Neither of these two methods seems very reliable!" a Primordial remarked.
"Naturally they aren't reliable, but there's no other way. Who told us to be too weak to advance to the Supreme Primordial realm?" the Saint Ancestor sighed.
"What about the Human Race?"
Suddenly, a Primordial asked.
The Human Race?
Currently, the Human Race had many Primordials and was the most powerful force. The Myriad Law Primordial was even more mysterious and had almost stopped interacting with them; they hadn't seen him for a very long time.
Rumor had it that the Myriad Law Primordial had reached the Supreme Primordial realm, but it couldn't be confirmed.
"World Ancestor, the Myriad Law Primordial is one of the Primordials of our War Gate. Has he actually advanced to the Supreme Primordial realm? Does the Human Race have the confidence to survive this calamity?" the Spacetime Primordial looked at the World Ancestor and asked.
The World Ancestor smiled bitterly. "The Myriad Law Primordial stopped contacting us much a long time ago. Although he was once a member of the War Gate, his core is with the Human Race. The Human Race is so powerful now, how would we dare to treat him as just a member of the War Gate anymore? Therefore, we don't know much about the Human Race or the Myriad Law Primordial."
The Saint Ancestor said, "World Ancestor, you can contact the Myriad Law Primordial and ask how the Human Race plans to deal with this calamity. If the Human Race is confident in surviving, I am willing to join them!"
"Yes, yes, yes, we are also willing to join the Human Race!"
One Primordial after another spoke up quickly.
With the Great Calamity approaching, they were all afraid of death and wanted to live.
"I'll ask then," the World Ancestor said helplessly.


Chapter 1516: The Great Calamity of the Dark Forbidden Domain is Here!

Chapter 1516: The Great Calamity of the Dark Forbidden Domain is Here!

With a single thought, Jie Zu traveled instantly to the outskirts of the human race's Profound Void Ancestral World. Today, the Profound Void Ancestral World had already surpassed a standard Ancestral World, reaching the level of a Supreme Ancestral World. Both its cultivation environment and resources far exceeded those of naturally born Ancestral Worlds.
This place had completely developed into the core of the human race, while the human ancestral worlds within those Dark Holy Lands had become branch locations.
Furthermore, through Ye Tian's refinements, even an Ancestor would find it difficult to pry into the slightest detail of the Profound Void Ancestral World.
When a thought from Jie Zu arrived, the human Ancestors naturally sensed it.
"Jie Zu, what business brings you here?"
A human Ancestor asked.
"I wish to see the Myriad Law Ancestor!" Jie Zu stated.
"Very well, I will go and inquire. As for whether Lord Myriad Law Ancestor will see you, I cannot guarantee it!" the human Ancestor replied.
After all, even these human Ancestors had not seen the Myriad Law Ancestor for a long time.
Soon, the human Ancestor went to see the Myriad Law Ancestor.
In truth, Ye Tian naturally knew Jie Zu had arrived. Since he was not currently in a state of total secluded meditation, he was aware of the situation in the outside world.
He could even roughly guess Jie Zu's purpose, which was why he hesitated over whether to meet him.
"Forget it, I might as well see him."
Ye Tian's avatar appeared outside the Profound Void Ancestral World to meet Jie Zu.
"Myriad Law Ancestor!"
Jie Zu said respectfully.
This was the first time he had seen the Myriad Law Ancestor in a very long time.
At this moment, he was somewhat alarmed.
Because the aura on the Myriad Law Ancestor's body far surpassed his imagination; it was simply not an aura that a top-tier Ancestor could possess.
A Supreme Ancestor!
Jie Zu realized it instantly.
Clearly, Ye Tian had indeed stepped into the Supreme Ancestor realm, just as the rumors suggested.
"Jie Zu, why have you sought me out?" Ye Tian asked.
Jie Zu said, "Myriad Law Ancestor, the Ancestors of our Dark Forbidden Domain are currently holding a meeting to discuss how to deal with the Great Calamity. As their representative, I wish to ask if the human race has the capability to withstand the calamity. If the human race is capable, everyone wishes to join the human race and become a subordinate force."
"Jie Zu, go back and tell them that the human race does not have the capability to withstand the Great Calamity!" Ye Tian spoke plainly.
"Myriad Law Ancestor, is the human race truly unable to withstand the calamity?" Jie Zu asked seriously.
Ye Tian said, "Once the calamity arrives, the Battle Sect can come to the human territory for refuge, but other forces cannot."
"Why?"
Jie Zu wanted to know the reason.
"Because the human race cannot protect all forces!" Ye Tian sighed. "You do not know how powerful those foreign forces are. Supreme Ancestors are divided into three levels: the first level, the second level, and the third level. Above the Supreme Ancestors are the Invincible Ancestors. Six of the foreign forces possess Invincible Ancestors, and these six forces are the ones behind the six Great Forbidden Lands. The human race is no match for them. If we truly tried to protect all forces, we would have to face all those opponents. When the calamity arrives, those foreign forces must slaughter and clear the entire Dark Forbidden Domain. With my ability, protecting this area of the human race is my limit."
"I understand. Thank you, Myriad Law Ancestor!"
Jie Zu said gratefully.
Subsequently, this thought of Jie Zu's returned to his main body.
...
"Jie Zu, what did the Myriad Law Ancestor say?"
One Ancestor after another asked, appearing incredibly urgent.
Jie Zu sighed. "The human race says they cannot protect us. They are also not certain they can survive the calamity. If they accept us, they would have to face threats from even more foreign forces, so they have declined!"
"Damn the human race!"
"I shouldn't have expected the Myriad Law Ancestor to agree!"
"Forget it, I'll just find a safe place to hide!"
Afterward, the Ancestors departed one by one.
Some Ancestors even headed toward the various Forbidden Lands, attempting to join those foreign forces.
However, those Ancestors never appeared again.
As time passed, the Great Calamity of the Dark Boundary grew closer and closer.
On this day.
Ye Tian recalled the human race from various Dark Holy Lands. One Ancestor after another took action, either personally bringing back humans from various territories or opening space-time gates to let the humans travel through them to the Daoshan Boundary Domain.
The number of humans in the entire Dark Forbidden Domain was too vast; it took a long time to relocate them all.
To settle these humans, the human Ancestors built a massive number of worlds in the areas surrounding the Daoshan Boundary Domain.
It took several boundary years to finally complete the migration of the entire human race.
At this point, the territory centered around the Profound Void Ancestral World was the human race's sole domain; all other territories were abandoned.
Some small forces, unaware of the situation, were excited to see the human race abandon so many territories and even Ancestral Worlds. They rushed to occupy these Ancestral Worlds and territories, not knowing that when the calamity descended, these lands would be of no use at all.
While the human race was preparing, the Ancestors of other forces were also preparing.
They all abandoned their organizations because they simply couldn't protect them, and each went into hiding.
If they were lucky, some Ancestors might still survive.
Calamity Black Mountain.
One Ancient Ancestor after another, radiating the aura of calamity, appeared. Ancient Ancestors were equivalent to Ancestors, and the Ancient Ancestors of Calamity Black Mountain not only possessed powerful physical bodies but were also skilled in curses. Even from a vast distance, they could curse someone to death using just a single strand of hair.
Even if the opponent possessed many clones and a main body, as long as they had one clone, they could instantly kill all of the opponent's clones.
Thus, the Ancient Ancestors of Calamity Black Mountain were very powerful and terrifying.
Before long, three third-level Supreme Ancient Ancestors crossed over from the other side of the Rank Two Gate.
Dozens of Supreme Ancient Ancestors and tens of thousands of ordinary Ancient Ancestors—Calamity Black Mountain had mobilized a great deal of power this time.
Moreover, they could dispatch even more experts at any time.
Besides Calamity Black Mountain, other foreign forces were also ready, waiting for the Great Calamity of the Dark Forbidden Domain to arrive.
BOOM!!!!
The Great Calamity of the Dark Forbidden Domain arrived. The rules of the entire Dark Forbidden Domain underwent a subtle change, no longer repelling foreign experts.
Having already experienced a Great Calamity in the Holy Domain Heaven and Earth, Ye Tian was naturally very familiar with the changes of the calamity.
"...Activate the grand array!"
Ye Tian commanded.
Instantly, within the human territory, countless grand arrays were activated. Myriad Domain Ancestors stood as guardians of the formations at their respective posts, while the many Ancestors of the human race also maintained the arrays.
Ye Tian had already issued orders forbidding any Ancestor from going out to snatch Source Rule Tribulation Crystals.
Meanwhile, Ye Tian produced a duplicated body. His main body sat in wait within the human race, while his duplicated body went out to seize Source Rule Tribulation Crystals. If any foreign experts invaded the human race, this duplicated body could return to provide support at any time.


Chapter 1517: Slaying Supreme-level Beings!

Chapter 1517: Slaying Supreme-level Beings!

Dark Forbidden Domain.
Dozens of forbidden lands, from each of which a large number of foreign powerhouses emerged, entering various parts of the Dark Forbidden Domain to wipe out countless living beings.
Even the Three Thousand Evil Tribes of the Dark Destruction Domain were like ants before these foreign powerhouses, possessing no power to resist at all.
The Three Thousand Evil Tribes lived for destruction, but now, they were being destroyed by foreign powerhouses.
Dark Destruction Domain, Dark Sacred Domain, Dark Soul Domain...
Countless beings in one Dark Sacred Land after another were wiped out, and endless resources were taken by these foreign powerhouses.
The entire Dark Forbidden Domain was filled with slaughter; or rather, the creatures of the Dark Forbidden Domain were being massacred. Even ordinary Ancestors would be easily struck down if discovered by foreign powerhouses.
In a short time, almost all ordinary creatures in the Dark Forbidden Domain were killed, and many Ancestors had also fallen.
Outside the Daoshan Realm.
An Ancestor wanted to flee into the Human Race's territory, but was blocked by the Human Race's grand array.
"Ancestor Wanfa, save me!"
One Ancestor cried out for help.
However, the Human Race's Ancestors had no intention of saving him.
After all, the most important thing for the Human Race was to survive this Great Tribulation. Once they passed it, the Human Race was almost certain to rise and soar.
Therefore, nothing else mattered; surviving the Great Tribulation was the only priority.
This Ancestor had no connection to the Human Race, so they naturally wouldn't offend a foreign power for his sake.
Boom!!!!
A Supreme-level foreign powerhouse descended and killed that Ancestor with a single hand.
This Supreme-level foreign powerhouse looked at the Human Race's territory in this area of the Daoshan Realm, saw the densely packed arrays, hesitated for a moment, and did not act immediately, instead summoning other foreign powerhouses.
