Previously, although Ye Tian had broken into many forbidden lands, there were some he had never entered. Thus, the powers behind those forbidden domains had no idea of Ye Tian's strength.
Foreign powerhouses who knew of Ye Tian's strength wouldn't dare invade the Human Race's territory after making even a slight inquiry.
But foreign powers ignorant of Ye Tian's strength, seeing the Human Race's territory, assumed the resources here were abundant and naturally wanted to invade.
This Supreme-level foreign powerhouse belonged to a Great Name-level foreign power—Chaotian Pavilion.
Soon, powerhouses comparable to Supreme Ancestors arrived outside the Human Race's territory.
In a short while, nine Supreme-level beings gathered here, including one at the second tier of the Supreme level.
"Long Mo, why have you summoned us here?"
A Supreme-level being from Chaotian Pavilion asked.
The Supreme-level powerhouse named Long Mo spoke: "This is the territory of the Human Race, the strongest power in the Dark Forbidden Domain. I suspect they have Supreme Ancestors among them, so I did not act immediately!"
"The Human Race? This power didn't exist during the last Great Tribulation. It must be a newly risen power. Within the span of a single Great Tribulation era, it's difficult to even leave the Dark Forbidden Domain. Even with opportunities, birthing one Supreme Ancestor is likely the limit! And any Supreme Ancestor born would likely have inherited a legacy to advance, making their combat power weak and not worth mentioning!"
"Exactly, what does a mere Human Race amount to? With our Chaotian Pavilion's strength, we can easily wipe them out!"
"Let's act quickly. If the six Ultra Name-level powers like Calamity Black Mountain take action, we won't even get a scrap of the benefits!"
These Supreme-level beings discussed briefly and decided to attack the Human Race.
Rumble!!!!!
One Supreme-level aura after another spread out, enveloping the entire Human Race territory.
Under the pressure of these Supreme-level beings, the arrays began to tremble.
These Supreme-level powerhouses didn't want to wipe out the Human Race all at once, otherwise, many resources would be destroyed along with them, which would be a great loss.
Therefore, they planned to first kill the Human Race's Ancestors, then wipe out the souls of countless clansmen with a single thought. That way, they could collect the Human Race's resources and treasures without damaging them.
However, just as they were attacking the Human Race's arrays, a towering figure appeared outside the territory.
Ye Tian stood there, his gaze fixed on the powerhouses from Chaotian Pavilion.
Their attacks were directly blocked by Ye Tian, failing to even touch the Human Race's arrays.
In the next moment.
Ye Tian struck. Combining the Tyrant Strength Supreme Ancestral Technique with the Extreme Arm Supreme Ancestral Technique, he threw a punch.
This punch seemed to extinguish everything, causing the Supreme-level beings of Chaotian Pavilion to fall into terror.
"Run!"
They were terrified.
Ye Tian's strike was too terrifying, exceeding their imagination. They had never seen such a terrifying powerhouse; even a third-tier Supreme-level being probably wouldn't have such a powerful aura.
Crack, crack, crack!!!!
One Supreme-level being after another had their bodies shattered by Ye Tian's punch, completely annihilated.
In the blink of an eye, only one second-tier Supreme-level being remained.
This Supreme-level being wanted to tear through space-time to escape, but Ye Tian had already sealed it.
Unable to escape through space-time, he could only rely on speed. However, how could his speed match Ye Tian's? He was easily overtaken.
"Eternal Supreme Ancestral Technique!"
Terrifying time rules enveloped this second-tier Supreme-level being from Chaotian Pavilion. Under the time-type Eternal Supreme Ancestral Technique, time was frozen. Although he could perceive the solidification of time, he couldn't react. His entire body was as if pinned, uncontrollable.
In the next moment.
Ye Tian's palm descended, directly slaying this Supreme-level being.
With this, the Supreme-level beings of Chaotian Pavilion were completely wiped out.
This was naturally a massive loss for Chaotian Pavilion; it was unknown how long it would take for them to recover their strength.
After slaying these Supreme-level beings from Chaotian Pavilion, Ye Tian collected the treasures on their bodies.
"Oh? There are actually three Source Rule Calamity Crystals!"
Ye Tian was somewhat surprised.
These Source Rule Calamity Crystals were naturally not from the Sacred Domain Heaven and Earth, but from other foreign worlds. They were carried by these Supreme-level beings, who never expected to fall in the Dark Forbidden Domain; otherwise, they would never have brought these three crystals to their deaths.
With these three foreign Source Rule Calamity Crystals, Ye Tian had made a huge profit.
Ye Tian's action of slaying the Supreme-level beings of Chaotian Pavilion did not attract much attention, as there were no other Supreme-level beings in this area. Thus, the news did not leak.
In the following days, Supreme-level beings would occasionally attack the Human Race's territory, only to be slain by Ye Tian.
Gradually, the news leaked, and the Human Race's strength was exposed.
And for some unknown reason, the Supreme-level beings of the six Ultra Name-level powers were not keen on searching for opportunities, but were instead looking for something.
Ye Tian was also curious about this intelligence.
"What exactly are those six major powers looking for? Could it be that the mysterious treasure is the true goal of the six major powers!"
Ye Tian thought to himself.


Chapter 1518: Calamity Beast! The True Goal of the Six Great Powers!

Chapter 1518: Calamity Beast! The True Goal of the Six Great Powers!

Ye Tian couldn't figure it out for the time being, so he stopped thinking about it.
It was a good thing that those six super-tier powers weren't making a move against the human race.
Although he didn't fear the Supreme-level beings who had currently entered the Dark Forbidden Zone, the six super-tier powers did, after all, possess Invincible-level beings. If he killed too many of their Supreme-level experts, an Invincible-level being would inevitably descend upon the Dark Forbidden Zone.
In that case, even if he could escape, the human race wouldn't be able to.
Therefore, he didn't want to provoke the six super-tier powers for the time being.
As time passed, the first Origin Rule Calamity Crystal appeared in the Dark Forbidden Zone.
The Dark Forbidden Zone was the human race's home base, and Ye Tian was extremely familiar with it. Combined with his great strength, he was able to arrive at the destination in time to seize the Origin Rule Calamity Crystal.
Although Ye Tian didn't manage to snatch the first Origin Rule Calamity Crystal, he did get his hands on the second one.
Unbeknownst to many, more than twenty Origin Rule Calamity Crystals had already been born in the Dark Forbidden Zone, and Ye Tian had snatched six of them, which was definitely a very large number.
During this period, Ye Tian also encountered Supreme-level experts from the six super-tier powers. They had also snatched some Origin Rule Calamity Crystals, but since they were primarily searching for something, most of their manpower didn't participate in the scramble for the crystals. Thus, the six powers hadn't snatched many.
Currently, in the Dark Forbidden Zone, except for the human race and the Battle Gate, almost all other forces had been wiped out. Only a few Ancestors remained hidden and were lucky enough to still be alive.
One Dark Holy Land after another had long since been destroyed, and the entire Dark Forbidden Zone had become incredibly empty.
One day.
Somewhere in the Dark Forbidden Zone, a Supreme-level foreign expert was investigating the area and suddenly sensed a special space-time node.
"There should be an Ancestor from the Dark Forbidden Zone hiding here, right?"
This foreign expert thought to himself.
So, he attacked that space-time node.
*Crack!!!*
This patch of space-time shattered instantly, revealing a figure—it was a Top-tier Ancestor.
If Ye Tian were here, he would have recognized this Ancestor's identity: Ancestor Hundred Souls, the master of the Saint Ancestor.
At this moment, Ancestor Hundred Souls looked desperate.
This place was very well-hidden, with no resources or treasures in the surrounding area. It just so happened that there was a concealed space-time node here. By hiding inside, as long as no Ancestor was in the vicinity, it would be very difficult to detect this node.
And given how vast the Dark Forbidden Zone was, even a Supreme Ancestor couldn't investigate a very large area. Therefore, he still had a high probability of avoiding this great calamity again.
But he didn't expect that his luck would be so bad this time that he would actually be discovered.
"Hahahaha, a Top-tier Ancestor! By killing you, I can obtain the resources on your body. You Top-tier Ancestors are each incredibly wealthy; killing one of you is more profitable than slaughtering an entire territory!"
The foreign expert said excitedly.
Ancestor Hundred Souls didn't want to die. As an ancient Ancestor, he had lived for a long time and possessed many trump cards, giving him a glimmer of hope for escape.
Immediately, he sacrificed a bead.
This bead was a Primordial Ancestral Object he had once discovered by accident. It could cause space-time vibrations and isolate a patch of space-time, buying him a chance to escape.
*Buzz!!!!*
As the bead was sacrificed, this patch of space-time began to vibrate, isolating him from the foreign expert.
Then, he began to flee.
However, an accident occurred.
The space-time vibration caused a resonance in a certain special space-time, and a terrifying aura emanated from that unknown space-time.
This wisp of aura not only made Ancestor Hundred Souls feel chilled to the bone, but even the Supreme-level foreign expert trembled all over.
"What is this..."
He felt death; the owner of that aura far exceeded his imagination.
*Crack!*
Space-time shattered, and a claw reached out from the depths of space-time. Ancestor Hundred Souls bore the brunt of it and was instantly killed.
The foreign expert wanted to flee, but he was stared down by a pair of pupils, as if he were directly imprisoned.
Then, the claw grabbed him and squeezed gently, turning the foreign expert into ashes.
......
"It's appeared!"
A man with three eyes and golden wings on his back was holding a compass, the needle pointing to where the claw had appeared.
This man was an Illusion Ancestor from the Illusory Dream World, one of the six super-tier powers. He was skilled in illusions and was named Illusion Ancestor Zi Ling, a third-tier Supreme Illusion Ancestor.
*Whoosh!*
The man broke through space-time and shuttled over.
At the same time, one Illusion Ancestor after another from the Illusory Dream World shuttled through space-time, descending upon the place where Ancestor Hundred Souls had fallen.
Additionally, the other five major powers also sensed it and descended upon the location one after another.
The experts from the six super-tier powers tacitly refrained from fighting each other. With a glance at one another, they decided to cooperate.
"Let's cooperate. The Calamity Beast is extremely powerful. Even if it's only a First Calamity Beast, it's comparable to the weakest Invincible-level beings. We must unite to have a chance of killing it."
"Fine, then let's cooperate. We'll decide how to distribute the benefits after the Calamity Beast is killed!"
"No problem!"
"We agree as well!"
After choosing to cooperate, the six super-tier powers joined forces to attack that unknown space-time.
*Boom!!!!*
The unknown space-time barrier was torn apart, and the eyes of many experts fell upon a massive figure.
It was a terrifying beast so massive it was beyond imagination. Infinite rules permeated its surroundings, and the aura on its body crushed even Supreme Ancestors.
It could be said that any Supreme-level being facing this Calamity Beast might be instantly killed.
... ..... 0
Consequently, the Supreme-level beings from each power immediately deployed battle arrays, and six battle arrays surrounded the Calamity Beast.
The slaughter began!
As soon as the fighting started, they realized they had underestimated the Calamity Beast's strength.
"Not good, this Calamity Beast is one of the stronger ones even among First Calamity Beasts. We won't be able to kill it; we must request reinforcements!"
The Supreme-level beings thought to themselves.
Requesting reinforcements was a last resort; they didn't want to do it.
Because once they requested reinforcements, it meant the benefits they would receive would be reduced.
After all, even within the same power, no one wanted to share the benefits with others. If they had a way to solve it themselves, no one would be willing to call for help.
But now, they had no choice but to call for help; otherwise, not only would they fail to kill the Calamity Beast, but they would also lose manpower.
Soon, the battle spread over a very long distance. Additionally, Ye Tian had many thought incarnations searching for Origin Rule Calamity Crystals in the Dark Forbidden Zone, and one of them sensed the battle fluctuations and noticed the area.
Thus, Ye Tian's true body shuttled over and saw the experts of the six major powers besieging the Calamity Beast.
The moment he saw the Calamity Beast, Ye Tian was also shocked.
The rules emanating from this Calamity Beast were actually the rules of the Dark Forbidden Zone. It was clearly a creature of the Dark Forbidden Zone, yet the Dark Forbidden Zone actually possessed such a terrifying creature.
"What on earth is this creature?"
Ye Tian was filled with curiosity.
But he had guessed it: the true goal of the six super-tier powers was likely this creature and...


Chapter 1519: A Great Discovery, the Appearance of an Eternal Ancestral Talent!

Chapter 1519: A Great Discovery, the Appearance of an Eternal Ancestral Talent!

"Copy Talent!"
Ye Tian immediately used his Copy Talent to investigate the creature's talents.
This creature was called a Calamity Beast, and it possessed multiple Ultimate Ancestral Talents.
However, one specific talent shocked Ye Tian beyond measure, because it wasn't an Ultimate Ancestral Talent, but something called an Eternal Ancestral Talent.
This was the first time he had ever seen an Eternal Ancestral Talent.
[Eternal Ancestral Talent: Calamity]
Without a second thought, Ye Tian directly copied all those Ultimate Ancestral Talents, and he copied this Eternal Ancestral Talent as well.
However, while copying this Eternal Ancestral Talent, Ye Tian clearly felt his Copy Talent struggling. It took ten seconds to successfully copy this Eternal Ancestral Talent.
This would have been impossible in the past, as he usually copied any talent in an instant, yet copying the Eternal Ancestral Talent took ten seconds.
Clearly, the Copy Talent had its limits, and copying an Eternal Ancestral Talent was currently close to that limit.

Unless the Copy Talent could be upgraded again, there was no hope of breaking this limit.
Due to time constraints, he couldn't fuse the Eternal Ancestral Talent: Calamity right now, so he didn't yet know its use. He could only wait until he returned to slowly learn more about it.
Ye Tian's arrival naturally couldn't be hidden from the Supreme-level experts of the six super-renowned powers.
"Ancestor of Myriad Laws, how about helping us hold back this Calamity Beast?"
One Supreme-level expert said.
Although only one expert at the third tier of the Supreme Ancestor realm had arrived, and his help wouldn't be massive, having another Supreme Ancestor to stall for time and share the burden was still good.
As for whether Ye Tian would perish, that was none of their concern.
However, Ye Tian did not act immediately.
"Everyone, tell me what a Calamity Beast is and what its uses are. I know you came specifically for it, so it must be of great value. If you provide me with information, I will help you," Ye Tian said.
It was just a bit of information, so the six super-renowned powers didn't hide it and told Ye Tian directly.
Immediately, a stream of information entered Ye Tian's mind.
There wasn't much content; after all, these six powers wouldn't reveal too much to him, only giving him some basic information.
For example, the origin of the Calamity Beast.
A Calamity Beast is a creature born at the moment an exotic world is completely destroyed. An exotic world does not exist forever; after ten thousand great tribulations, it will completely collapse and be destroyed, and that is when a Calamity Beast is born.
After absorbing the energy of an exotic world's destruction, the Calamity Beast falls into a deep sleep. After long ages, a new exotic world will be born in this region, starting the cycle anew.
A Calamity Beast that has experienced one world destruction is a One-Calamity Beast; if it has experienced two, it is a Two-Calamity Beast; and three makes it a Three-Calamity Beast.
The Dark Forbidden Zone had been destroyed once before, thus giving birth to a Calamity Beast. This beast had been sleeping and was very difficult to find.
If left undisturbed, it would sleep until the day the Dark Forbidden Zone was destroyed again.
But now, it had been disturbed.
Calamity Beasts were of great value because they contained Origin Rule Calamity Crystals. Killing one would yield many of these crystals.
As for exactly how many Origin Rule Calamity Crystals could be obtained, the six powers didn't say.
But Ye Tian guessed the amount must be significant, otherwise, it wouldn't have attracted these six super-renowned powers.
"Ancestor of Myriad Laws, you've received the information. Hurry and help us stop it!"
The exotic experts shouted one after another.
"Alright!"
Ye Tian replied.
Immediately, he attacked the Calamity Beast.
Of course, Ye Tian wouldn't show his full strength, only displaying power slightly greater than an average third-tier Supreme Ancestor.
Even so, it surprised the six super-renowned powers.
Because Ye Tian had been cultivating for such a short time, yet possessed such strength, if he had enough opportunities, there might be a sliver of hope for him to promote to an Invincible Ancestor.
As Ye Tian attacked the Calamity Beast, it noticed him and slammed its tail toward him.
The power and speed of this tail strike were terrifying. Furthermore, the Calamity Beast was a creature that ignored time and space; even though Ye Tian was proficient in the Time-Space Ancestral Path and Time-Space type Supreme Ancestral Skills, it was difficult to dodge this blow.
Boom!!!!
The Calamity Beast's tail strike slammed into Ye Tian.
Just as the Supreme-level experts of the six powers thought Ye Tian would be killed in one hit, several defensive Supreme Ancestral Skills appeared on his body.
Golden Body Supreme Ancestral Skill!
Holy Armor Supreme Ancestral Skill!
Primordial Chaos Astral Shield Supreme Ancestral Skill!
One-Element Shield Supreme Ancestral Skill!
……
Six defensive Supreme Ancestral Skills were activated simultaneously. Combined with his own physical defense and a defensive Supreme Ancestral Object, the stacked defenses finally withstood the blow...
Of course, all six layers of defense shattered, the defensive Supreme Ancestral Object was damaged, and Ye Tian's body sustained minor injuries.
But at the very least, he blocked it, merely being sent flying.
"What!!!"
"What!!!"
The Supreme-level exotic experts were dumbfounded, unable to believe that Ye Tian had actually blocked a strike from the Calamity Beast and only suffered minor injuries.
How was this possible?
The Calamity Beast was incredibly powerful. If they hadn't formed a battle array to attack collectively and share the damage, they would have been heavily injured.
Yet Ye Tian was just one person; how could he withstand a strike from the Calamity Beast?
"This human Supreme Ancestor has cultivated six defensive Supreme Ancestral Skills. How afraid of death is he?"
One Supreme-level exotic expert remarked.
Others might not have noticed in that split second, but he did; those six defensive Supreme Ancestral Skills were the reason Ye Tian survived.
"What, six defensive Supreme Ancestral Skills? How terrifying. So that means he sacrificed speed, soul defense, and other Supreme Ancestral Skills to specialize in defense and a single offensive skill. I see!"
The other Supreme-level exotic experts suddenly understood and no longer doubted.
A Supreme Ancestor with such amazing defensive power, though reaching the third tier, had major flaws and could easily be targeted. It was only because the Calamity Beast wasn't good at soul attacks; otherwise, an equivalent Invincible Ancestor could have killed Ye Tian with a single soul attack.
Unfortunately, they would never know how many Supreme Ancestral Skills Ye Tian knew. In fact, he didn't just have six defensive skills, but ten.
If he hadn't wanted to hide his strength, the Calamity Beast wouldn't have even been able to break through all his defenses, let alone injure him.
However, Ye Tian alone couldn't kill the Calamity Beast because its defense was truly terrifying.
As time passed, Ye Tian and the experts of the six powers finally received reinforcements. By this time, the Supreme-level experts were heavily injured, and Ye Tian also pretended to be badly hurt.
Boom!!!!
One after another, third-tier Supreme-level experts arrived, all belonging to the six super-renowned powers. These reinforcements were all at the third tier, numbering twenty-five in total.
With twenty-five more third-tier Supreme-level experts, the group was filled with confidence in surrounding and killing the Calamity Beast.


Chapter 1520: Tribulation Blood! Transaction!

Chapter 1520: Tribulation Blood! Transaction!

Ka ka ka!!!
Under the siege of numerous supreme-level experts, the Tribulation Beast gradually began to show signs of fatigue.
The Tribulation Beast was not without intelligence; its intelligence was simply very low.
Thus, seeing itself at a disadvantage, it attempted to flee.
Many experts pursued it relentlessly, but the Tribulation Beast's defense was too terrifying. If it hadn't lacked powerful offensive techniques, the many supreme-level experts present would not have been able to defeat it at all.
The Tribulation Beast could not leave the Dark Forbidden Domain, so it could only flee within its boundaries, unable to shake off these experts from the outer realms.
Finally, in a silent stretch of the void.
The Tribulation Beast fought for its life, engaging in a desperate struggle with the many supreme-level beings.
Boom!!!!
A battle formation was torn apart. Six supreme experts of the first tier were blasted to death, and other supreme experts were heavily injured.
Of course, this Tribulation Beast was also heavily wounded again by the other supreme experts, making its injuries even more severe.
Subsequently, one battle formation after another collapsed, rendering them unusable.
Consequently, everyone began attacking the Tribulation Beast with their individual strength.
Before long, the number of fallen supreme experts from the outer realms reached double digits, and many more were severely injured.
These supreme experts were on the brink of death and dared not intervene further, distancing themselves one by one.
In the end, only the third-tier supreme experts from the six super-tier forces remained to besiege the Tribulation Beast.
Compared to the beginning, the Tribulation Beast's current strength was less than a third of its peak, and its injuries were incredibly heavy. Its scale-covered body was in a wretched state, with countless scales shattered, and the Tribulation Beast's blood flowed continuously, unable to heal.
"Give it one more push!"
The supreme experts roared.
At this moment, every supreme expert was extremely excited. Once the Tribulation Beast fell, the benefits would be immense.
Ye Tian was also among them, keeping a low profile and not deliberately showing off his strength.
Moreover, the current goal of the six super-tier forces was to slay the Tribulation Beast, so they naturally wouldn't bother with him.
Not long after, the Tribulation Beast's strength dropped to an extremely low level. Its body was riddled with holes, and it could no longer recover from its wounds or withstand the attacks of the supreme experts.
Finally, it succumbed to its heavy injuries and perished.
The moment the Tribulation Beast died, its physical body began to disintegrate.
A large number of Origin Rule Tribulation Crystals flew out, along with a mass of black blood that radiated a terrifying aura.
The supreme experts immediately rushed to snatch that mass of black blood; this was their true target.
Of course, the Origin Rule Tribulation Crystals were also their targets, but their primary objective was naturally the black blood, followed by the crystals.
Every supreme expert craved this mass of black blood. Ye Tian naturally knew it was a treasure and stopped hiding his strength.
Boom!!!!
Ye Tian displayed his full combat power, grabbing the black blood at maximum speed before beginning to snatch the Origin Rule Tribulation Crystals.
In the void, giant hands reached out to grab the crystals one by one, with the majority falling into Ye Tian's hands.
At this moment, how could these supreme experts not understand!
Ye Tian hadn't been injured at all; he had hidden his strength. His true power might not equal the Tribulation Beast's peak, but he possessed at least a third of its strength.
Meanwhile, they were all heavily injured with greatly reduced combat power. How could they compete with Ye Tian?
"Ancestor of Myriad Laws, hand over the Tribulation Blood! That is not something you can snatch!!!!"
The supreme experts surrounded Ye Tian, threatening him.
"Get lost!"
Ye Tian said coldly.
The six super-tier forces wasted no more words and attacked Ye Tian together.
At this moment, Ye Tian displayed nearly invincible strength, almost sweeping everything aside.
However, he did not kill the supreme experts of the six super-tier forces. After all, with his current strength, he was not yet enough to contend with these six forces. If he killed these supreme experts and the six invincible powerhouses behind them took action, he would have no choice but to hide and wait for the Great Tribulation to pass.
Therefore, unless it was absolutely necessary, he would not seek his own death.
In the void of the Dark Forbidden Domain.
One by one, the supreme experts were heavily injured, either lying down, kneeling, or trembling as they all stared at Ye Tian.
"Ancestor of Myriad Laws, you are truly remarkable to have created so many supreme ancestral techniques. No wonder your strength is so terrifying. But as long as you haven't become an Invincible Ancestor, you have no right to be an enemy of the super-tier forces!" one supreme expert said.
Ye Tian sighed, "I didn't want to be your enemy either; it was you who insisted on being mine. I am curious, what use does this so-called Tribulation Blood have? Why do you all want to fight for it?"
"That is a secret!"
The supreme experts of the six super-tier forces seemed unwilling to speak.
Ye Tian smiled and said, "If you tell me, perhaps I can trade the Tribulation Blood with you!"
Trade the Tribulation Blood?
The supreme experts of the six super-tier forces were somewhat moved. If they could trade for it, that would naturally be for the best.
"What do you want?"
A representative of the six super-tier forces asked.
Ye Tian pondered for a moment and said, "I want to know how to break through to become an Invincible Ancestor. Your six super-tier forces should have invincible-level beings, so you should know this secret, right? Each of you communicate with me; whoever offers a price that interests me, I will give the Tribulation Blood to them!"
Immediately, the supreme experts communicated with Ye Tian, stating their offers.
In reality, one portion of Tribulation Blood could at most be consumed by one person. If it were divided, the effect would be lost, as this was only the blood of a First-Tribulation Beast.
Ultimately, a third-tier supreme expert from the Firmament Sword Tomb proposed a trade that Ye Tian found hard to refuse.
The manufacturing method for a Tier-2 Gate, the secret of how a supreme expert breaks through to become an invincible one, and additionally, ten Origin Rule Tribulation Crystals. These ten crystals were not from the same outer realm heaven and earth, but belonged to ten different ones, which were very difficult to collect.
"Supreme expert of the Firmament Sword Tomb, Wuhai Sword Ancestor, we can make the trade!"
Ye Tian chose Wuhai Sword Ancestor.
Seeing Ye Tian trade with Wuhai Sword Ancestor, the other supreme experts were incredibly envious.
The key profound secret of a supreme expert breaking through to an invincible one wasn't much, but the manufacturing method for a Tier-2 Gate was extremely rare. Few among the supreme experts knew it. While some present did know, they had sworn oaths not to reveal it. Therefore, only a manufacturing method obtained by chance could be used for trade.
Coincidentally, Wuhai Sword Ancestor had once wiped out a force and obtained a Tier-2 Gate manufacturing method, which he now used for the trade.
Ye Tian handed the Tribulation Blood to Wuhai Sword Ancestor, and in return, he received the Tier-2 Gate manufacturing method, the secret of breaking through to an Invincible Ancestor, and the ten Origin Rule Tribulation Crystals.
"Farewell!"
Ye Tian departed.
Meanwhile, Wuhai Sword Ancestor quickly retreated under the protection of the other supreme experts from the Firmament Sword Tomb. Several battles broke out during the process, but in the end, Wuhai Sword Ancestor successfully returned to the Firmament Sword Tomb.
Of course, the other forces were not without gains; they also harvested some Origin Rule Tribulation Crystals and materials from the Tribulation Beast.
Xuanxu Ancestral Realm.
After Ye Tian returned, he immediately began to study the secrets in his mind regarding how to break through to become an Invincible Ancestor. Such secrets were like a legacy; they could only be obtained through inheritance and could not be spoken or written down.
Soon, Ye Tian finished receiving the inheritance and finally understood how a Supreme Ancestor should break through to become an Invincible Ancestor.


Chapter 1521: Physical Tribulation! Absorbing Tribulation Power to Temper the Body!

Chapter 1521: Physical Tribulation! Absorbing Tribulation Power to Temper the Body!

The Supreme Ancestor and the Invincible Ancestor may seem only one realm apart, but the gap in their strength is immense, like the difference between heaven and earth.
Take a One-Tribulation Tribulation Beast, for example. A One-Tribulation Tribulation Beast is comparable to a weaker Invincible Ancestor, yet even so, it required so many Supreme Ancestors to join forces, and many of them lost their lives, just to kill it.
If it were a normal Invincible Ancestor, even that many Supreme Ancestors joining forces would have ended in defeat and death.
This is the power of an Invincible Ancestor!
And the difficulty of breaking through from a Supreme Ancestor to an Invincible Ancestor is more than a hundred times harder than a Top-tier Ancestor breaking through to a Supreme Ancestor.
Among the many exotic domains, the number of Supreme Ancestors is not small; every exotic domain has some to a greater or lesser extent, with the exception of new exotic domains.
But exotic domains that possess Invincible ones are far too few. Only an Invincible one at the level of an Invincible Ancestor can be considered truly free from the shackles of an exotic domain, possessing an infinite future and no longer being a frog at the bottom of a well.
According to the information provided by the Wuhai Sword Ancestor, a Supreme Ancestor must satisfy three conditions to become an Invincible Ancestor.
First is one hundred Origin Rule Tribulation Crystals. If one does not have one hundred Origin Rule Tribulation Crystals, even if other conditions are met, the breakthrough is very likely to fail. Furthermore, the deeper one's foundation, the more Origin Rule Tribulation Crystals need to be prepared.
Often, even a single Origin Rule Tribulation Crystal is difficult to collect; trying to collect one hundred is simply too difficult.
But in reality, this is the easiest condition to fulfill. After all, if one is powerful enough, even if they only accumulate one Origin Rule Tribulation Crystal per Great Tribulation, one hundred Great Tribulations would be enough to collect them all.
The second condition is even harder: absorbing Tribulation Power and using the power of an exotic domain's Great Tribulation to undergo a tribulation for oneself.
At this time, a Supreme Ancestor faces two choices. One is to take the path of Physical Tribulation, which is to use the body to absorb Tribulation Power, tempering the body with that power to condense an Invincible Body. The second is Soul Tribulation, to condense an Invincible Undying Soul.
Tribulation Power is terrifying. Ordinary Supreme Ancestors wouldn't dare to absorb and refine it, and to absorb enough Tribulation Power, one must experience many Great Tribulations.
Basically, undergoing Physical Tribulation or Soul Tribulation more than five times gives a high probability of breaking through to the Invincible Ancestor realm.
However, trying to undergo a tribulation more than five times is incredibly difficult.
"Could it be that Tribulation Blood is related to undergoing tribulations?"
Ye Tian speculated.
If Tribulation Blood could help a Supreme Ancestor quickly complete five or more tribulations and do so relatively safely, then it would truly be a priceless treasure, enough to make any Supreme Ancestor fight to the death for it.
The third condition is the most difficult, yet for some Supreme Ancestors, it is also the easiest.
During non-tribulation periods, one enters an exotic domain and uses their body or soul to withstand the exotic rules. Through the stimulation of the exotic rules, they allow themselves to undergo a qualitative change, thereby ascending to the Invincible Ancestor realm.
However, this is incredibly risky; one could die with the slightest mistake.
Supreme Ancestors are almost unable to contend with the rules of an exotic domain. Even if they step into an exotic domain for just one second, they likely won't be able to withstand it and will die instantly.
But if one has enough life-saving items and enters and exits the exotic domain's rules repeatedly to slowly adapt, there is a certain hope of ascending to the Invincible Ancestor realm.
These are all three conditions.
"Hard! It's too hard! No wonder so many Supreme Ancestors have no way to ascend to become Invincible ones!"
Ye Tian murmured.
Currently, he had quite a few Origin Rule Tribulation Crystals in his possession.
Although that Tribulation Beast was only a One-Tribulation Tribulation Beast, it possessed over ten thousand Origin Rule Tribulation Crystals. Because of his great strength, he had managed to seize more than five thousand of them.
However, his foundation was too deep, so the number of Origin Rule Tribulation Crystals he needed would definitely far exceed other Supreme Ancestors. One hundred crystals would certainly not be enough; he would need to prepare at least 2,000.
If not for killing the One-Tribulation Tribulation Beast this time, he feared it would have taken him countless ages to accumulate so many Origin Rule Tribulation Crystals.
Origin Rule Tribulation Crystals seem very precious, but in reality, they are only useful to Supreme Ancestors. For those Invincible ones, they likely aren't of much use and can at most be used as currency.
Ye Tian now satisfied the first condition, leaving only the second and third.
"Absorb Tribulation Power!"
Ye Tian sensed the Great Tribulation power permeating the Dark Forbidden Domain. This power was incredibly chaotic and terrifying, making it fundamentally difficult to absorb and refine.
Suddenly.
He thought of the talent he had copied from the Tribulation Beast. Among them was an Eternal Talent: Tribulation. Perhaps this talent was related to Tribulation Power.
Consequently.
Ye Tian began to integrate the Eternal Talent: Tribulation to see what use this talent had.
After a long time, Ye Tian finally completely integrated the Eternal Talent: Tribulation.
At this moment, he finally knew the use of this talent.
"It's actually for absorbing Tribulation Power to temper the physical body!"
Ye Tian said in surprise.
He finally knew why Tribulation Beasts were all so powerful. They could repeatedly absorb Tribulation Power to temper their bodies; even while sleeping, they were invisibly absorbing Tribulation Power to increase their strength.
If a Tribulation Beast were allowed to survive multiple Great Tribulation Eras, how terrifying would its strength become!
"The Eternal Talent: Tribulation is a talent specifically for the physical body. It seems I can only take the path of Physical Tribulation," Ye Tian thought to himself.
In fact, the path of an Ancestor was already biased toward the physical body, so the Eternal Talent: Tribulation was indeed very suitable for him.
Boom!!!!!
Ye Tian activated the Eternal Talent: Tribulation, absorbing the Tribulation Power from the world at an incredible speed.
This Tribulation Power entered Ye Tian's physical body, quickly tempering it.
As time slowly passed, before long, Ye Tian's physical body had grown much stronger, and he felt the rules of the Dark Forbidden Domain pressing down on him.
At this moment, Ye Tian had a moment of realization.
His physical body was about to undergo a tribulation!
He was an existence that could be called invincible among Supreme Ancestors, and his Endless Ancestor Body was also incredibly powerful, so the power of his physical tribulation was naturally far beyond that of other Supreme Ancestors.
Boom!!!!
The rules of the Dark Forbidden Domain transformed into rule flames, rule wind blades, rule lightning... constantly attempting to annihilate Ye Tian's physical body. But such a tribulation did not cause his body to perish; instead, it grew stronger and stronger.
Not long after, Ye Tian's physical body had passed its first Physical Tribulation.
Next, he continued to cultivate, striving to complete two Physical Tribulations before the Great Tribulation of the Dark Forbidden Domain passed.
In that case, his strength would see a massive increase.
Finally, as the Great Tribulation of the Dark Forbidden Domain was about to end, Ye Tian finally welcomed his second Physical Tribulation and successfully passed it, his physical strength skyrocketing.


Chapter 1522: After the Great Tribulation!

Chapter 1522: After the Great Tribulation!

If one were to consider physical body tribulation crossing as a realm, it would stand above the third-tier paramount powerhouses.
Thus, Ye Tian was now a Physical Body Second Tribulation Realm paramount powerhouse. Every time the physical body crossed a tribulation, its strength would skyrocket. It was precisely because of this that a Paramount Ancestor would become so incredibly powerful after becoming an Invincible Ancestor.
Above the Physical Body Fifth Tribulation Realm or the Soul Fifth Tribulation Realm, one could travel to foreign domains to confront foreign laws head-on. Relying on various life-saving items, one would attempt to make the physical body undergo a qualitative change time and again, at least ensuring they would not perish under the suppression of foreign laws. Only then would they be considered qualified.
Afterward, one would use a hundred Origin Rule Tribulation Crystals to charge toward the realm of an Invincible One, such as an Invincible Ancestor.
Once successful, one would be a true Invincible One.
These three steps became increasingly difficult with each stage. Many paramount powerhouses did not know how many Great Tribulation Eras they had to endure or how many life-threatening dangers they had to face. Even with the support of major forces, there was only a sliver of hope to promote to the Invincible One realm.
If others knew that Ye Tian had raised his physical body to the Second Tribulation Realm in such a short time, they would find it absolutely unbelievable!
Because for any paramount powerhouse, the absorption of tribulation force was extremely slow, making it almost impossible to improve. However, Ye Tian had obtained the Eternal Talent: Tribulation, which allowed him to quickly absorb and refine tribulation force, thus raising his physical body to the Second Tribulation Realm in a short period.
If he visited a few more foreign domains undergoing a Great Tribulation, he could definitely raise his physical body to the Ninth Tribulation Realm.
Soon, the Great Tribulation of the Dark Forbidden Domain passed.
From beginning to end, the Invincible Ones of the six super-tier forces did not descend upon the Dark Forbidden Domain, allowing Ye Tian to breathe a sigh of relief.
From the information gathered from the six forces, it seemed Invincible Ones could enter foreign domains during non-tribulation periods. Their strength was terrifying, and the Invincible Ones of the six super-tier forces were definitely not newcomers to the realm; thus, they were certainly much stronger than Tribulation Beasts.
Therefore, he was definitely no match for those Invincible Ones.
But now, since the Invincible Ones had not come, it was likely they had no interest in a few thousand Origin Rule Tribulation Crystals, or perhaps they were occupied with other matters or were in secluded cultivation, which was why they had not descended upon the Dark Forbidden Domain.
Now that the Great Tribulation of the Dark Forbidden Domain was over, even if an Invincible One came, he would no longer be afraid.
After all, during a non-tribulation period, even if an Invincible One came, their strength would inevitably be suppressed severely, perhaps even becoming weaker than him. Coming here would be seeking death.
In this Great Tribulation, the Human Race's strength suffered almost no losses, but other forces were nearly annihilated, with only a few Ancestors remaining.
Whoosh! Whoosh! Whoosh!
One by one, the Ancestors of the Human Race emerged from human territory, crossing time and space to reach various regions of the Dark Forbidden Domain, only to see a landscape of desolation and silence.
In the short term, those treasure lands and domains of the Dark Forbidden Domain likely would not be born. It would take a certain amount of time for these domains, worlds, treasure lands, and Dark Holy Lands to emerge.
Therefore, the practitioners of the Human Race would likely have to live within human territory for the coming years. Although it would be crowded, it was sufficient for the time being.
Moreover, the Ancestors of the Human Race could create worlds in the surrounding territories and even accelerate the evolution of domains, so the Human Race did not lack territory.
On this day.
Ye Tian summarized and organized the entire evolutionary path of the Human Race from Ancestor to Paramount Ancestor and Invincible Ancestor. He used special means to seal this knowledge within the Human Race Holy Temple. Any Supreme Domain Ancestor would be eligible to inherit this secret knowledge, ensuring they would not take the wrong path and fail to promote to Paramount or Invincible Ancestor in the future.
In the following time, the Human Race produced several Supreme Domain Ancestors at regular intervals. Successive Supreme Domain Ancestors with deep foundations even promoted to Ancestors, all by creating their own Ancestor Methods.
Because everyone's comprehension had skyrocketed after surviving the Great Tribulation; even Ye Tian's comprehension had improved significantly. This was the benefit of surviving a Great Tribulation.
It was foreseeable that before long, the Human Race would produce a large number of Ancestors, and Supreme Domain Ancestors would truly be as numerous as the hairs on an ox.
Additionally, since Ye Tian had obtained many Origin Rule Tribulation Crystals this time and did not need them all himself, he could place them in the Human Race Holy Temple for the top Ancestors to slowly contemplate.
It was unlikely that a Paramount Ancestor would be born in a short time, but over long ages—even if one was not born in a single Great Tribulation Era (nine Dark Calendars)—after several Great Tribulation Eras, Paramount Ancestors would definitely emerge, and their numbers would only increase.
...
With the Great Tribulation gone from the Dark Forbidden Domain, Ye Tian could no longer absorb tribulation force. Not knowing which foreign domain would undergo a Great Tribulation next, he began to focus on creating Ultimate Ancestral Techniques and then fusing them into Paramount Ancestral Techniques.
He already had several Origin Rule Tribulation Crystals from other foreign domains, obtained by killing paramount powerhouses from those worlds.
Furthermore, he could continue to trade for Origin Rule Tribulation Crystals. With his current strength, he could easily trade for foreign Origin Rule Tribulation Crystals.
Thus, he did not lack foreign Origin Rule Tribulation Crystals.
As time passed, Ye Tian created more and more Paramount Ancestral Techniques. Although their effects on him were weakening, creating more still enhanced his strength.
Occasionally, he would help his wife and son create Ultimate Ancestral Techniques, guiding them to fuse two Ultimate Ancestral Techniques to comprehend and create a Paramount Ancestral Technique, saving them countless years of time.
Domain year after domain year passed. The Dark Forbidden Domain slowly became prosperous. Densely packed domains were born, ensuring the entire Dark Forbidden Domain was no longer empty.
Moreover, many taboo creatures were born, but they only served as resources for the Human Race, being hunted or raised in captivity by human experts.
At the same time, countless humans were distributed among super-large and large domains, and even small domains were filled with human presence.
Additionally, Ye Tian spent time building a Space-Time Gate at the level of a Paramount Ancestral Artifact. It could project countless Space-Time Gate phantoms, allowing humans to travel easily throughout the Dark Forbidden Domain. Otherwise, even a Supreme Domain Ancestor would find it difficult to cross such vast territories.
Unknowingly, the Human Race had produced many Ancestors and countless Supreme Domain Ancestors.
Ye Tian now possessed nearly forty Paramount Ancestral Techniques, to the point where they could no longer amplify his physical body. There was no longer any need to continue creating them.
At this point, aside from crossing physical body tribulations, he had no other way to increase his strength.
Thus, he began to look for ways to find out which foreign domain was about to undergo a Great Tribulation.


Chapter 1523: Seeking the Great Tribulation of an Otherworldly Realm!

Chapter 1523: Seeking the Great Tribulation of an Otherworldly Realm!

When a great tribulation will occur in an otherworldly realm is a very hidden matter. Unless one has established a base in another otherworldly realm and mastered its secrets, it is very difficult to know when that realm will enter a great tribulation; otherwise, it is nearly impossible to predict.
For example, he did not know when the Bone Race's realm would enter its great tribulation.
The only otherworldly realm whose tribulation date he knew was the Sanctuary Realm, but there were still several Dark Eras of time remaining. He did not want to wait too long. After all, he did not wish to encounter the current situation again during the next Dark Forbidden Zone tribulation, where the entire Dark Forbidden Zone was looted clean.
He wanted the human race to completely control the Dark Forbidden Zone and sweep through all the forbidden lands, making the various major forces afraid to enter the Dark Forbidden Zone again.
Thinking it over, Ye Tian came up with two methods.
The first method was to use the same approach he used to enter the Sanctuary Realm: first wipe out the bases of those forces in the Dark Forbidden Zone, then copy the body of one of the otherworldly experts to enter their realm to gather information and confirm how much time remained before their next great tribulation.
The second method was to directly threaten these forces, demanding they inform him when their tribulation arrived, or else he would directly destroy their bases.
But Ye Tian calculated that the second method was likely unrealistic.
After all, no one wanted a force far stronger than themselves to enter their realm; in that case, the entire force would likely be occupied or wiped out.
Therefore, once he used the second method, these forces would likely abandon the Dark Forbidden Zone and directly destroy their gates.
After all, if they destroyed the gate, they could simply wait for an illusory gate to appear again, fix it, enter another otherworldly realm, and open a new gate. That way, they would not be threatened by the Dark Forbidden Zone.
After all, the current Dark Forbidden Zone was very powerful, and many small forces had already actively abandoned this place. Currently, the number of forbidden lands in the Dark Forbidden Zone had already decreased by about a dozen.
For example, the otherworldly force that had attacked Ye Tian back then—the Chaotian Pavilion—destroyed its gate shortly after those supreme experts fell, and the forbidden land where the Chaotian Pavilion was located vanished directly.
After thinking for a while, Ye Tian made his decision: "Then I will adopt the first method!"
------------------
Not long after, Ye Tian directly targeted an otherworldly force slightly weaker than the Bone Race—the Wind-Rain Sect.
In an instant, he wiped out the Wind-Rain Sect's base in the Dark Forbidden Zone, then copied the body of one of the Wind-Rain Sect experts and passed through the gate into the otherworldly realm where the Wind-Rain Sect was located.
The otherworldly realm where the Wind-Rain Sect was located was called the Universal Realm. The Wind-Rain Sect occupied an incredibly massive world within the Universal Realm and was the most powerful force there, possessing six supreme experts.
Ye Tian entered the Universal Realm in the guise of a Wind-Rain Sect expert. He immediately called for help and used a perfect reason to explain why he had survived.
That was, Ye Tian had spared him to bring back a message: the Wind-Rain Sect must pay a portion of resources and disclose the time of the great tribulation's arrival before they would be allowed to continue maintaining their base in the Dark Forbidden Zone.
After Ye Tian said this, he thought the Wind-Rain Sect would consider it for a while, but to his surprise, the several supreme experts of the Wind-Rain Sect began to deliberate immediately.
"What should we do? An incredibly powerful supreme ancestor has been born in the Dark Forbidden Zone, far exceeding an ordinary third-tier supreme ancestor. Once we tell him the time of our world's great tribulation, if he breaks in, none of us will be able to stop him. When the time comes and he wipes out our Wind-Rain Sect, everything will be over!"
"We cannot tell him about the time of our Universal Realm's tribulation. Even if he makes a life-bound oath, we cannot believe him. For an expert like him, no oath is effective."
"Abandon this gate. When the Universal Realm's illusory gate descends again, we will fix it and rebuild an eternal gate. Although it will cost many resources and materials, at least the Wind-Rain Sect will not face any threat!"
"Mm, then let us abandon this gate!"
All six supreme experts of the Wind-Rain Sect agreed to abandon the gate.
Subsequently, the six supreme experts arrived before the Wind-Rain Sect's gate and attacked it together.
A first-tier gate was not very sturdy. Top-tier ancestor-level peak experts could damage the gate, and a single strike from a supreme expert could destroy it. With the six experts acting together, they directly smashed the gate into countless cracks, making it almost unusable.
They continued to attack because what they wanted was to completely destroy the gate, meaning it would vanish entirely.
Boom! Boom! Boom!!!!
One attack after another fell, and soon this first-tier gate turned into countless fragments and vanished.
· ········· Seeking flowers ··· ·····
Seeing this, Ye Tian's copied body could not help but marvel inwardly: "How decisive!"
It had to be said, this was indeed the best method.
"I wonder if I can communicate with the main body in the Dark Forbidden Zone?"
Ye Tian's copied body tried to make contact.
Back in the Sanctuary Realm, he had tried to make contact but failed, only succeeding once the copied body reached the supreme expert level.
But things were different now. The main body's strength was much greater, second only to the Invincibles. Thus, the connection was deep. Perhaps even if this copied body only rivaled a top-tier ancestor, it could still sense the main body!
Time passed slowly, and in the blink of an eye, hundreds of thousands of years went by.
... ..... 0
On this day, the copied body established a sliver of connection with the main body and could transmit some simple messages, but that was enough.
By this time, Ye Tian's copied body already knew the timing of the Universal Realm's great tribulation. Calculating by the nine Dark Eras of the Dark Forbidden Zone, only five Dark Eras had passed in the Universal Realm, and there were still four Dark Eras before the great tribulation would arrive. Thus, there was still plenty of time.
Ye Tian not only transmitted the time but also, through the connection between the main body and the copied body, mapped out the coordinates of the Universal Realm in the following days.
This way, when the Universal Realm's great tribulation was about to arrive in the future, he could build a gate to travel there and absorb and refine those tribulation forces.
"The Universal Realm still has four Dark Eras before its great tribulation. It is not the best target. Let's keep looking!"
Ye Tian abandoned this copied body, letting it disintegrate on its own, and then set his sights on a second otherworldly force.
In this way, Ye Tian tried again and again, finally finding an otherworldly realm very close to its great tribulation.
The force in this otherworldly realm was called the Xiyue Tribe. They had also destroyed their gate, but that did not matter. Ye Tian already knew the coordinates of this otherworldly realm. He prepared to build a gate connecting to this realm, and a second-tier gate at that.
He already had the method to build a second-tier gate. He only needed to wait for the first Dark Era of the Dark Forbidden Zone to pass. At the moment the illusory gate appeared, he would completely fix it, modify the coordinates, and establish a second-tier gate connecting to that otherworldly realm.


Chapter 1524: The Second-Order Gate, Successfully Constructed!

Chapter 1524: The Second-Order Gate, Successfully Constructed!

"The first Dark Era of the Dark Forbidden Domain has passed!"
Ye Tian murmured to himself.
Shortly after, an illusory gate appeared somewhere within the Dark Forbidden Domain. This illusory gate was the target Ye Tian had been waiting for.
An illusory gate would not exist for very long. Therefore, before it could dissipate, one had to completely stabilize it and then prepare countless precious materials to forge it into a physical gate.
Ye Tian possessed the construction methods for not only a First-Order Gate but also a Second-Order Gate.
The cost of building a Second-Order Gate was ten times that of a First-Order Gate, but with Ye Tian's wealth and resources, he naturally had the capability to construct one.
The location of an illusory gate could not be changed. Consequently, the Human Race had to establish a branch base at its location, or they could even move their headquarters there.
However, the Human Race was bound to possess many gates in the future, so there was no need to relocate the headquarters. Dispatching a few Ancestors to guard the site would suffice for daily operations.
At the site of the illusory gate, Ye Tian brought out countless materials and began smelting them, integrating them into the illusory structure.
Time flowed slowly, and in the blink of an eye, ten thousand years had passed.
By now, the illusory gate had transformed into a tangible, real gate, brimming with a powerful aura. This was a Second-Order Gate forged entirely from countless materials, yet it was still missing one final component: Origin Rule Tribulation Crystals.
A First-Order Gate did not require Origin Rule Tribulation Crystals, but a Second-Order Gate required ten. This was the reason why ordinary forces could not build Second-Order Gates—the price was simply too high. Even a typical Great-name level force would find it difficult to produce ten Origin Rule Tribulation Crystals.
Only Super-name level forces could easily bring out ten Origin Rule Tribulation Crystals without feeling the slightest bit of heartache.
Swish! Swish! Swish!
Under Ye Tian's control, the Origin Rule Tribulation Crystals merged into the Second-Order Gate one by one. Gradually, the gate began to take its final shape and was on the verge of completely connecting to another world.
Suddenly.
Ye Tian forcibly modified the channel, inputting the world coordinates of the Xiyue Clan, thereby linking to the world where the Xiyue Clan resided.
After all, his goal was to enter the Xiyue Clan's world.
According to his intelligence, the Xiyue Clan's world had only one-tenth of a Dark Era remaining before it entered its Great Tribulation period. Thus, after building this Second-Order Gate, he wouldn't have to wait very long.
As the coordinates were modified, the Second-Order Gate began to pierce through to the Xiyue Clan's world.
Within the Xiyue Clan's world.
Boom! ! ! ! !
The void split open, and a Second-Order Gate slowly took form.
The appearance of a Second-Order Gate could not possibly be hidden from the Xiyue Clan.
Swish! Swish! Swish!
One after another, the powerhouses of the Xiyue Clan arrived at the scene. Seeing the Second-Order Gate, they attempted to destroy it.
However, their attacks were completely useless.
"Stop attacking. This is a Gate. It has just pierced into our world. Under the protection of the rules of the other world, we cannot destroy it while it is forming. We can only hope to destroy the gate after it has fully materialized," a supreme powerhouse of the Xiyue Clan spoke.
After a long time, the Second-Order Gate was completely formed, signifying that the Dark Forbidden Domain and the Xiyue Clan's forbidden land were now fully connected.
At that moment, the rules emanating from the Second-Order Gate began to influence the surrounding area, transforming it into a forbidden zone.
"Not good, this is a Second-Order Gate!"
The expressions of the Xiyue Clan powerhouses changed drastically.
The Xiyue Clan's world did not possess a Second-Order Gate, but that did not mean they failed to recognize one.
The entire Xiyue Clan possessed a total of thirteen supreme powerhouses, including three who were at the second level. Their strength was quite formidable.
At this moment, these supreme powerhouses gathered together, intent on destroying the Second-Order Gate.
An additional First-Order Gate meant little to the Xiyue Clan, but if a Second-Order Gate appeared, the Xiyue Clan's future days would be difficult!
Boom! ! ! ! !
The many supreme powerhouses attacked the Second-Order Gate, attempting to destroy it before the opposing force could descend. Once the other side dispatched a group of supreme powerhouses, they would have no hope of destroying such a gate.
Just then, a hand reached through from the other side of the gate, transforming into a colossal hand that easily blocked the attacks of all the supreme powerhouses.
In the next instant.
Ye Tian's figure stepped through the Second-Order Gate, officially entering the Xiyue Clan's world.
While remaining within the forbidden zone, he would not be affected by the rules of the Xiyue Clan's world.
Furthermore, a Second-Order Gate allowed supreme powerhouses to pass through freely without paying any price. He had descended here with his full combat power. . . . . . . . . .
"Ancestor of Myriad Laws!"
"Ancestor of Myriad Laws!"
"Ancestor of Myriad Laws!"
The supreme powerhouses of the Xiyue Clan cried out in disbelief.
Retreat! Retreat! Retreat!
The Xiyue Clan's supreme powerhouses hurriedly backed out of the forbidden zone, not daring to take a single step inside.
Currently, the Xiyue Clan's world was not in its Great Tribulation period, so Ye Tian could not step out of the forbidden zone.
At this moment, the Xiyue Clan's supreme powerhouses were extremely bewildered.
Wasn't the Ancestor of Myriad Laws a supreme ancestor of the Dark Forbidden Domain? How did he suddenly build a Second-Order Gate and arrive in the Xiyue Clan's world?
Setting aside how Ye Tian obtained the construction method for a Second-Order Gate, even if he was lucky enough to find it, how did he obtain the coordinates for the Xiyue Clan?
One usually had to personally step into the Xiyue Clan's world and spend a vast amount of time calculating the coordinates based on the position of the Dark Forbidden Domain!
For the Dark Forbidden Domain to possess the coordinates of the Xiyue Clan's world seemed illogical no matter how they looked at it!
"Ancestor of Myriad Laws, what do you intend to do?"
One of the Xiyue Clan's supreme powerhouses asked.
"It's simple. I'm establishing a base on your side. You were able to establish a base in the Dark Forbidden Domain, so why can't I?" Ye Tian sneered.
The Xiyue Clan supreme powerhouse said, "We have already destroyed that gate in the Dark Forbidden Domain and will no longer travel to your domain!"
"That is because you fear me. Otherwise, how could you possibly destroy a First-Order Gate you built yourselves?" Ye Tian mocked.
Then, Ye Tian added, "Rest assured, my Human Race is currently weak and has no interest in invading your world. I only wish to use your world for cultivation. As long as you do not disturb me, I won't bother with you."
"We hope the Ancestor of Myriad Laws is a man of his word!"
The Xiyue Clan supreme powerhouse replied.
Subsequently, all of the Xiyue Clan's forces in this area were withdrawn. They no longer provoked Ye Tian, as they simply could not afford to.
Especially since the Great Tribulation of the Xiyue Clan's world was approaching. If they provoked Ye Tian and he slaughtered his way into the Xiyue Clan's headquarters, no one would be able to stop him.
Time passed slowly.
Finally, the Great Tribulation of the Xiyue Clan's world arrived.


Chapter 1525: Physical Body Five-Tribulation Realm Supreme Powerhouse!

Chapter 1525: Physical Body Five-Tribulation Realm Supreme Powerhouse!

As the Great Tribulation of the Xiyue Clan descended, Ye Tian did not invade the Xiyue Clan's world.
Perhaps he could have plundered some resources during this tribulation, or even snatched some Origin Rule Tribulation Crystals, but he no longer looked down upon such small gains.
Instead of spending time searching for resources, he would rather focus on his cultivation.
This time, his goal was to put all his effort into cultivation and strive to cross several more Physical Body Tribulations.
Thus, Ye Tian's true body descended upon the Xiyue Clan's world.
When the Great Tribulation arrived, Ye Tian built a cultivation site in an area outside that forbidden land, where he activated his Eternal Talent: Tribulation to absorb the tribulation power.
During the previous Great Tribulation of the Dark Forbidden Domain, he had obtained the Eternal Talent: Tribulation, but by then, the tribulation had already been underway for a long time. Consequently, he didn't have enough time to cultivate, which was why he had only crossed two Physical Body Tribulations.
But this time was different. He had been here absorbing tribulation power since the very beginning of the Xiyue Clan's Great Tribulation, so his progress would certainly be greater.
Of course, the Physical Body Tribulations became increasingly difficult as they progressed. Especially after the fifth Physical Body Tribulation, the amount of tribulation power required to complete another one was immense.
However, many Physical Body Tribulation Realm supreme powerhouses would attempt to break through to the Invincible Realm once they completed their fifth Physical Body Tribulation. There was no need to pursue a higher realm, as the time and energy required were too great, and it was easy for accidents to occur, leading to their fall in a foreign world.
Since Ye Tian did not plunder resources or fight for Origin Rule Tribulation Crystals, the Xiyue Clan and other foreign forces did not come looking for trouble with him. Any supreme powerhouse who truly sought trouble with him would surely be doomed.
Time flew by like a shuttle.
On this day.
With the help of the Eternal Talent: Tribulation, Ye Tian finally began his third Physical Body Tribulation.
Ye Tian's physical body endured an unimaginable impact. Countless lightning wind-blades were born from every cellular world, attempting to destroy his body. However, Ye Tian's physical body was too powerful; in the end, the tribulation failed to destroy him and instead made his body even stronger.
"Physical Body Three-Tribulation Realm!"
Ye Tian said with joy.
However, he also felt that his absorption and refinement of the tribulation power were too crude.
No matter how powerful the Eternal Talent: Tribulation was, it was only a talent. For example, no matter how powerful an Ancestral Talent was, it could not compare to a created Ancestral Technique. One had to create and comprehend techniques derived from the talent's power to push that power to its limit.
If he could create a secret technique that complemented the Eternal Talent: Tribulation, he might be able to absorb and refine tribulation power even faster, which would speed up his cultivation significantly.
Over the years, Ye Tian had been attempting to create such a secret technique.
Furthermore, he repeatedly used his copied bodies to overdraw his Ancestral Soul and activate his deduction abilities. As a result, the process of creating this secret technique went very smoothly, and he was now at the final threshold.
He needed to absorb and refine tribulation power while simultaneously attempting to modify this secret technique to finally perfect it.
Only during a Great Tribulation could he quickly perfect it. Otherwise, relying solely on his usual meditation, he wouldn't be able to comprehend much at all. Without practical cultivation, it was impossible to create such a secret technique.
And this Great Tribulation of the Xiyue Clan's world was a perfect opportunity.
Finally, as the Great Tribulation approached its later stages, Ye Tian finally created a secret technique that could rapidly absorb and refine tribulation power. Its effectiveness was at least ten times greater than simply using the Eternal Talent: Tribulation alone.
This secret technique could barely be considered an Invincible-level secret technique, and Ye Tian named it the Tribulation Transformation Secret Technique!
Through the Tribulation Transformation Secret Technique, Ye Tian's speed in absorbing and refining tribulation power surged, using the power to rapidly temper his physical body.
Finally, he ushered in his fourth Physical Body Tribulation. Once he crossed it, he would be a Physical Body Four-Tribulation Realm supreme powerhouse.
Before long, Ye Tian successfully crossed the tribulation and entered the ranks of the Physical Body Four-Tribulation Realm powerhouses.
"According to my cultivation speed, by the time the Xiyue Clan's Great Tribulation ends, I should be confident in stepping into the Physical Body Five-Tribulation Realm!"
Ye Tian said with full confidence.
Without the Tribulation Transformation Secret Technique, he naturally wouldn't be able to achieve this, but now it was possible.
Just like that, the Xiyue Clan's Great Tribulation was gradually coming to an end. Various foreign forces returned to their own worlds, while Ye Tian continued to absorb tribulation power to temper his body, preparing to charge into the Physical Body Five-Tribulation Realm.
Perhaps in the eyes of the Xiyue Clan, Ye Tian was an eccentric. After all, they did not know the secrets of supreme powerhouses striving for the Invincible Realm, and they had no idea that one needed to absorb tribulation power to temper the body.
Otherwise, they would have known just how terrifying Ye Tian was.
In such a short time, Ye Tian had stepped into the Physical Body Four-Tribulation Realm. For any other supreme powerhouse, this wouldn't be possible even after countless Great Tribulation Eras.
Finally, when only tens of millions of years remained in the Xiyue Clan's Great Tribulation, Ye Tian ushered in his fifth Physical Body Tribulation. Without much pressure, he crossed this tribulation very easily and stepped into the Physical Body Five-Tribulation Realm.
After entering the Physical Body Five-Tribulation Realm, Ye Tian felt a sensation—or rather, he sensed a vague barrier of shackles.
That was the barrier between a supreme powerhouse and an Invincible One.
At this point, if he entered a foreign world that was not in a period of Great Tribulation and repeatedly attempted to clash his physical body against the rules of that foreign world, and if he could adapt to those rules and cause a qualitative change in his body, then there would be hope of breaking those vague shackles and stepping into the Invincible Realm.
However, Ye Tian did not have that intention for now.
A mere Physical Body Five-Tribulation Realm was nothing. His goal was higher; he wanted to charge into the Invincible Realm with a perfect foundation.
"The Xiyue Clan's world is currently of little value to me. It's time to find a second foreign world that is about to enter a Great Tribulation!"
Ye Tian thought to himself.
Ye Tian returned to the Dark Forbidden Domain and once again used his copied bodies to infiltrate other foreign worlds to figure out the dates of their Great Tribulations.
Soon, he discovered another foreign world that was about to enter a Great Tribulation.
This foreign world was named the Mingheng World, and its strength was not very great, similar to the Xiyue Clan's world.
More importantly, the supreme powerhouses of the Mingheng World were not very decisive and had not immediately destroyed their Rank One Gate, and the timing of their Great Tribulation was also grasped by Ye Tian.
Thus, Ye Tian waited silently. Once the Mingheng World's Great Tribulation arrived, his true body would forcibly enter the Mingheng World through the Rank One Gate. That way, he could directly occupy this Rank One Gate and turn it into his own, just like the Rank One Gate of the Sea Sky Holy Sect.
After a dozen or so Domain Eras, the Great Tribulation of the Mingheng World arrived.
On this day.
Ye Tian left the Mystic Void Ancestral World and arrived at the forbidden land leading to the Mingheng World.


Chapter 1526: Preparing to Negotiate with Super-Famous Level Forces

Chapter 1526: Preparing to Negotiate with Super-Famous Level Forces

As soon as Ye Tian entered the Mingheng World, he immediately began to take action against the Mingtian Alliance that guarded the gate.
Although he had suffered backlash from forcibly traversing the Tier 1 Gate, was wounded by the laws, and had consumed a significant amount of power, his strength remained incredibly terrifying. He far surpassed ordinary third-tier powerhouses, and thus, he easily destroyed the Mingtian Alliance and slaughtered their supreme powerhouses.
Afterward, Ye Tian began to refine the gate, turning it into his own, and then established a base within the Mingheng World.
This way, even after the great calamity of the Mingheng World passed, he could dispatch human powerhouses to guard the base, ensuring that this Tier 1 Gate would not be snatched back.
Having finished all this, Ye Tian began to absorb and refine Calamity Power to temper his physical body.
He was currently a powerhouse in the Physical Body Five-Calamity Realm. His goal this time was not overly ambitious; he only needed to reach the Physical Body Six-Calamity Realm. After all, after the Five-Calamity Realm, every subsequent stage was incredibly difficult, requiring far more Calamity Power and time than before.
Therefore, he did not expect to be able to raise his strength to the Physical Body Seven-Calamity Realm in one go.
Time passed slowly, and in the blink of an eye, the great calamity of the Mingheng World reached its late stages.
On this day.
Ye Tian finally tempered his physical body to a new limit, ushering in his sixth physical body calamity.
Boom!!!!
After his body underwent repeated cycles of destruction and recovery, and after surviving the most terrifying lightning calamity, it finally completed a qualitative change, stepping into the Physical Body Six-Calamity Realm.
"This tribulation was relatively easy; I only suffered a few minor injuries. It seems I am still far from my limit!"
Ye Tian thought to himself.
Everyone has a limit. Many people lack a sufficient foundation and cannot even reach the Physical Body Five-Calamity Realm; attempting a forced breakthrough would only result in death.
Thus, no matter how powerful a force was, or how many resources and how much time they had, once they touched their own limit, they could no longer continue to undergo physical body calamities.
For example, most Invincible Ones were only at the Physical Body Five-Calamity Realm back then and did not dare to attempt the sixth calamity because the fifth was their limit.
But for Ye Tian, passing the sixth physical body calamity was not even difficult, so he could continue using Calamity Power to temper his body.
Next, Ye Tian cultivated in the Mingheng World for another period of time. It wasn't until the great calamity of the Mingheng World was about to end that he left. As for the base in the Mingheng World, Ye Tian dispatched several human Ancestors to guard it.
After all, the Mingheng World had suffered heavy losses during this calamity, and he had killed many of its supreme powerhouses. They wouldn't dare to move against the human base!
Therefore, dispatching a few Ancestors to guard it was sufficient.
---------------
Time flew by.
Five Dark Eras had already passed in the Dark Forbidden Zone. During this time, Ye Tian entered multiple foreign worlds, and even visited the Holy Region World during another of its great calamities. Using the Calamity Power of these foreign worlds, he continuously tempered his physical body.
However, the further he progressed, the harder it became to temper his body. To this end, he had refined his Calamity-Neutralizing Secret Technique several times, yet the great calamity of a single foreign world was no longer enough to raise him by a full calamity realm.
Now, by utilizing the Calamity Power from multiple great calamities, he had barely managed to raise his realm to the Physical Body Seven-Calamity Realm, making his strength much greater than before.
In terms of actual combat power, he was definitely not weaker than an ordinary Invincible Ancestor.
However, moving from the Physical Body Seven-Calamity Realm to the Eight-Calamity Realm was too difficult. He had already visited two foreign worlds and still hadn't reached the Eight-Calamity Realm.
Clearly, relying solely on pure Calamity Power to reach the Physical Body Eight-Calamity Realm was too difficult.
"If I could obtain Calamity Blood, perhaps I could raise my cultivation faster!"
Ye Tian thought.
After all, it was difficult for ordinary supreme powerhouses to absorb Calamity Power directly; they could only rely on Calamity Blood. This showed the value of Calamity Blood. Even the blood of a One-Calamity beast might be enough to push him directly from the Seven-Calamity Realm to the Eight-Calamity Realm.
"It's a pity about that portion of Calamity Blood from before!"
Ye Tian couldn't help but sigh.
However, if given the choice again, he would still choose to trade that Calamity Blood for the construction method of a Tier 2 Gate and the secret knowledge of how to become an Invincible One. Otherwise, he still wouldn't know how to strike for the Invincible Ancestor level, and he wouldn't have been able to reach his current Physical Body Seven-Calamity strength.
But the problem at hand was how to obtain another portion of Calamity Blood.
Calamity Beasts were extremely powerful. A One-Calamity beast was comparable to a weaker Invincible Ancestor. If it were a beast of two, three, or more calamities, even an Invincible Ancestor wouldn't dare provoke it; to do so would be seeking death.
Whenever a foreign world was destroyed, a Calamity Beast would be born.
Perhaps the Holy Region World had a Calamity Beast, but it might not be a One-Calamity beast, or it might have already been slain.
However, many foreign worlds had experienced multiple destructions. In those cases, if the Calamity Beast hadn't been killed, it would be absolutely terrifying. Even Super-Famous Level forces wouldn't dare provoke such a beast.
The reason the Dark Forbidden Zone was targeted was that it had only experienced one world destruction. That Calamity Beast was only a One-Calamity beast. The six Super-Famous Level forces knew this information, which was why they dared to plot against it. Otherwise, they wouldn't have the courage to lay a finger on a Calamity Beast!
……
The Dark Forbidden Zone.
Today, the Human Race already possessed over several thousand Ancestors. Their strength could be described as incredibly formidable, and their clansmen were spread throughout the entire Dark Forbidden Zone. Among other forces, only the Battle Gate had some room to survive; the others had no living space at all.
At the same time, the number of forbidden lands in the Dark Forbidden Zone had dwindled. Previously, there were dozens, but now only about a dozen remained, including the base forbidden lands of the six Super-Famous Level forces.
This was naturally due to Ye Tian, which led many foreign forces to abandon the Dark Forbidden Zone.
This was a good thing; at least in the future, the Dark Forbidden Zone would not suffer invasions from multiple foreign forces.
Once the Dark Forbidden Zone was free of any foreign gates, the Human Race could completely control the entire zone and focus all their efforts on invading other foreign worlds.
"It's time to show my hand to the six Super-Famous Level forces. At the very least, I need to trade for some knowledge or resources. If nothing else, I must destroy their Tier 2 Gates!"
Ye Tian thought.
On this day.
Ye Tian arrived at the forbidden land of the "Illusory Dream World," a Super-Famous Level force. He intended to capture members of this forbidden land to use as leverage for negotiations. Otherwise, he had nothing of value to trade with a Super-Famous Level force.
As for whether he would offend the Illusory Dream World, he didn't care in the slightest.


Chapter 1527: Initial Clash with the Invincible!

Chapter 1527: Initial Clash with the Invincible!

Illusory Dream World, Forbidden Land.
