Ye Tian entered this place and immediately sensed the situation of this forbidden land, as well as the strength of the members of the Illusory Dream World guarding it.
Five Supreme Beings and thousands of Ancestors.
"It seems the Illusory Dream World values the Dark Forbidden Domain quite highly, actually dispatching so many experts!"
Ye Tian said with slight surprise.
At this moment.
The Supreme Beings of the Illusory Dream World also saw Ye Tian, and their expressions changed drastically one after another.
"Ancestor of Myriad Laws!"
It wasn't that they didn't know Ye Tian's strength; it was precisely because they knew his strength that they had dispatched five Supreme Beings, one of whom had even reached the third level.
But they also knew very well that relying on just five Supreme Beings, they couldn't possibly stop Ye Tian, and even relying on the formations here would be useless.
Of course, they didn't know Ye Tian's purpose; if he hadn't come to fight, there was no need to be nervous.
However—
Ye Tian directly attacked!
Boom!!!!
The power of the Physical Body Seven Tribulations Realm erupted in full, and a terrifying aura and pressure crushed all the experts here.
Those members of the Illusory Dream World below the level of Supreme Being didn't even have the ability to move, and the five Supreme Beings were also trembling all over, their hearts filled with incomparable horror.
"Physical Body Seven Tribulations Realm! How is this possible?"
They simply couldn't believe it.
After all, the Illusory Dream World had previously clashed with Ye Tian in the Dark Forbidden Domain. Although Ye Tian's strength was far greater than an ordinary third-level Supreme Being, he definitely hadn't crossed a single physical body tribulation back then; otherwise, his aura couldn't have been hidden.
Once a Supreme Being reaches the third level, it becomes very difficult to increase their strength. They can only cross physical body tribulations or soul tribulations, gradually advancing toward the realm of the Invincible.
However, absorbing tribulation power to temper the physical body was too slow and time-consuming.
Many third-level Supreme Beings spent thousands of Great Calamity Eras and still found it difficult to cross five physical body tribulations to gain the qualification to charge for the Invincible realm.
But from the last time Ye Tian hadn't crossed a tribulation until now, only a few Dark Calendar periods had passed, and he had suddenly crossed seven physical body tribulations. This was too abnormal!
Ye Tian was already very powerful to begin with, and now that he had crossed seven physical body tribulations, one could imagine to what extent his strength had increased.
Thus, the moment Ye Tian attacked, the five Supreme Beings of the Illusory Dream World wanted to flee, having no intention of fighting at all.
Unfortunately, their strength was too weak; they couldn't escape at all.
"Five Elements Sealing!"
This was one of Ye Tian's Supreme Ancestral Techniques, which had also evolved step by step from a Saint Technique. Now that it had reached the level of a Supreme Ancestral Technique, even Supreme Beings would find it difficult to break through the lock of the Five Elements Sealing.
Buzz!!!!
This entire forbidden land area was directly locked down, making it impossible for these Supreme Beings and those below them to escape.
"Seal!"
The Five Elements Sealing continued to shrink, turning into individual seals that suppressed the power of each expert. Even the five Supreme Beings were quickly sealed, their full strength unable to be exerted, meaning they had no way to escape.
"Ancestor of Myriad Laws, what are you doing? Do you want to start a war with our Illusory Dream World? The strength of the Illusory Dream World is far beyond your imagination. You are seeking death!"
One Supreme Being said angrily.
"Oh, the strength of the Illusory Dream World is far beyond my imagination? I have already reached the Physical Body Seven Tribulations Realm, do I still need to fear your Illusory Dream World?" Ye Tian sneered.
That Supreme Being threatened, "Our Illusory Dream World possesses three Invincible Illusion Ancestors, and our leader is far beyond ordinary Invincible Ancestors. Compared to our Illusory Dream World, you are simply an ant!"
"Oh, thank you for informing me of the Illusory Dream World's strength!" Ye Tian said with a smile.
"You... did that on purpose!" That Supreme Being was stunned, then became furious. He had unintentionally revealed the strength of the Illusory Dream World. Although it wasn't a huge deal, he was very annoyed.
"Go and inform the Illusory Dream World that I want to make a deal with them!" Ye Tian released a top-tier Illusion Ancestor and let him go to inform the Illusory Dream World headquarters.
The other party immediately traversed the Rank 2 Gate, leaving this forbidden land and heading toward the world where the Illusory Dream World was located.
Not long after.
A terrifying aura forcibly traversed the Rank 2 Gate, attempting to cross the domains.
Clearly, the opponent was an Invincible who surpassed the Supreme Beings—an Invincible Illusion Ancestor of the Illusory Dream World.
After all, Supreme Beings could easily pass through a Rank 2 Gate, and only Invincibles needed to pay a price to cross one.
Crack!!!
The void vibrated!
A figure forcibly crossed the Rank 2 Gate and descended upon this forbidden land.
"Pupil Ancestor, save us!"
The Illusion Ancestors of the Illusory Dream World cried out for help.
Pupil Ancestor, one of the three giants of the Illusory Dream World, in the realm of an Invincible Illusion Ancestor, possessed incomparable strength.
However, by forcibly descending this time, his strength had dropped by at least thirty percent, but he still possessed the combat power of an Invincible Illusion Ancestor.
At this moment, seeing Ye Tian holding so many Illusion Ancestors of the Illusory Dream World captive, he was instantly enraged.
Immediately, he wanted to use illusion techniques to attack Ye Tian and kill him outright.
Countless illusions swept in, but Ye Tian held firm to his heart and let out a furious roar: "Begone!"
Countless illusions shattered!
At this time, Pupil Ancestor released a pupil technique attack, which transformed into a sharp blade and slashed toward Ye Tian. It looked like an ordinary pupil technique, but it was extremely terrifying, capable of slashing not only the physical body but also the soul.
However.
Ye Tian threw a punch. With the power of the Extreme Arm Supreme Ancestral Technique combined with the Tyrant Strength Supreme Ancestral Technique, plus the power attached to the Physical Body Seven Tribulations Realm, the power of this punch was terrifying to the extreme.
The void in front of him was directly annihilated by the punch, and even Pupil Ancestor's pupil technique attack was shattered. However, this attack also left a bloodstain on Ye Tian's fist, counting as a wound to Ye Tian.
"You actually possess Invincible Ancestor combat power!"
Pupil Ancestor was extremely surprised.
Although a Supreme Being of the Physical Body Seven Tribulations Realm was powerful, they were definitely still far from the Invincible level. But now Ye Tian possessed Invincible Ancestor combat power; clearly, his foundation was too deep, and he had created many, many Supreme Ancestral Techniques at the Supreme Being level, which allowed him to possess such formidable combat power.
Moreover, those at the Physical Body Seven Tribulations Realm had a seventy to eighty percent chance of promoting to an Invincible; unless their luck was extremely poor, they wouldn't die during the breakthrough process.
He couldn't kill such an expert. Even if the leader arrived, once the Ancestor of Myriad Laws fled into the Dark Forbidden Domain, even if those Invincibles didn't fear the rules of the Dark Forbidden Domain, most of their strength would still be suppressed. At that time, they wouldn't be able to do anything to Ye Tian and might even face the risk of falling.
"I cannot offend the Ancestor of Myriad Laws!" Pupil Ancestor thought to himself.
Thus, Pupil Ancestor stopped attacking and instead asked, "Ancestor of Myriad Laws, what do you want? How can you release these members?"
Ye Tian pondered for a moment and stated his demands.


Chapter 1528: The Six Levels of the Invincible Ones

Chapter 1528: The Six Levels of the Invincible Ones

"One portion of Tribulation Blood!"
Ye Tian demanded an exorbitant price.
"Impossible!" Tong Zu immediately refused.
One portion of Tribulation Blood—how could that be possible!
The value of these members was not necessarily worth a portion of Tribulation Blood. They were merely Supreme Beings; they could be cultivated given enough time. Unless it was a junior he personally favored, he would never be willing to pay the price of a portion of Tribulation Blood. Otherwise, these Supreme Beings simply weren't worth it.
After all, Tribulation Blood was too precious. One had to slay a Tribulation Beast to obtain a single portion.
However, Tribulation Beasts were far too powerful. Even he only dared to target beasts of the first or second tribulation. Once a Tribulation Beast reached the third tribulation level, even he would be no match for it, unless their Leader personally took action.
Therefore, the Illusory Dream World could not possibly pay the price of a portion of Tribulation Blood for these Supreme Beings.
Ye Tian didn't truly expect Tong Zu to pay a portion of Tribulation Blood to ransom these Supreme Beings; he was merely testing the waters.
"I want a type of treasure that contains a large amount of Tribulation Power. Does your Illusory Dream World possess such a treasure?" Ye Tian asked.
Tong Zu really didn't want to deal with Ye Tian, but since the Supreme Beings of the Illusory Dream World were in Ye Tian's hands and he had no way to deal with him, he could only answer: "Aside from treasures like Tribulation Blood, there is another type—Tribulation Stones. They are a resource occasionally born when a foreign world is destroyed. Compared to Tribulation Blood, Tribulation Stones are naturally much more numerous, but their value is far lower. Tribulation Stones also contain terrifying Tribulation Power, which should satisfy your requirements."
"Let me see one!"
Ye Tian demanded.
"Fine, I happen to have a few Tribulation Stones on me!"
Tong Zu took out a Tribulation Stone from his storage treasure and tossed it to Ye Tian.
The Tribulation Stone was six-sided, black, and contained incredibly dense Tribulation Power. If an ordinary Ancestor were to even glance at it, their mind or even their physical body might be affected by the stone's power; the Tribulation Power it contained was simply too terrifying.
Without activating his Tribulation Transformation Secret Technique or invoking his Eternal Talent 'Tribulation,' Ye Tian attempted to refine the Tribulation Stone using his own strength. He found it very difficult to refine; instead, the stone's Tribulation Power began to invade his physical body, wreaking havoc within.
Under such circumstances, there was no way to utilize the Tribulation Stone.
"Tong Zu, Supreme Beings shouldn't be able to use Tribulation Stones to temper their bodies for tribulations, right?" Ye Tian inquired.
"It is possible, but it requires many precious auxiliary items and secret techniques. Even then, the speed is much slower than the Tribulation Power during a Great Tribulation. However, a Great Tribulation only lasts for a short time, whereas with Tribulation Stones, one can refine Tribulation Power continuously. It's just a massive waste of resources and time. In short, Tribulation Blood cannot be given to you; only Tribulation Stones are available. As for whether you want them or not, that is your business!" Tong Zu said coldly.
"I want the Tribulation Stones, but their value is far inferior to Tribulation Blood. You must provide a sufficient quantity of Tribulation Stones to ransom these Supreme Beings. Additionally, I need detailed cultivation data regarding the Invincible Ones," Ye Tian demanded.
"You are too greedy!" Tong Zu snorted, but he did not refuse Ye Tian.
The two continued to negotiate, eventually settling on the number of Tribulation Stones, and Tong Zu also agreed to give Ye Tian the cultivation data for the Invincible Ones.
10,000 Tribulation Stones, plus a set of cultivation data.
Tong Zu had the Illusory Dream World prepare for a while before handing these two items over to Ye Tian.
Ye Tian did not go back on his word. Otherwise, if the Illusory Dream World decided to retaliate at all costs, the Human Race and the Dark Forbidden Domain would not be able to withstand their vengeance. Being able to extort so many good things from the Illusory Dream World was already enough.
When Ye Tian left this forbidden land of the Illusory Dream World, he saw the forbidden land vanish, and that Second-Tier Gate disappeared without a trace.
It was clear that the Illusory Dream World had also abandoned the Dark Forbidden Domain, not wishing to suffer any more such losses.
Human Race, Profound Void Ancestral Realm.
Ye Tian returned and began to browse the cultivation data on the Invincible Ones from the Illusory Dream World.
Supreme Beings were divided into three levels—one, two, and three—and their strength improvement was closely related to Supreme Ancestral Techniques. Above the third level was the Physical Body Tribulation Realm or the Soul Tribulation Realm, followed by the Invincible One realm. The classification of an Invincible One's strength was quite complex.
First, the weakest Invincible Ones were those who had just broken through. They still used Supreme Ancestral Techniques and did not possess a single Invincible Ancestral Technique.
Next were the Invincible Ones who had mastered one Invincible Ancestral Technique. Such Invincible Ones were naturally much stronger than those who had just broken through; their strength would undergo an earth-shattering transformation.
As for how to comprehend an Invincible Ancestral Technique? Ye Tian didn't know before, but now he understood.
· ········· Seeking Flowers ··· ·····
Merging an Ultimate Ancestral Technique from one foreign realm with an Ultimate Ancestral Technique from another, combining the rules of two foreign realms to form a Supreme Ancestral Technique—that was the origin of Supreme Ancestral Techniques. However, Invincible Ancestral Techniques were not formed through fusion; rather, they were comprehended from the rules of the Eternal World, and there was only an extremely low probability of comprehending one.
"Eternal World?"
Ye Tian didn't know what such a place represented, but did the word 'Eternal' have something to do with Eternal Talents?
The Illusory Dream World hadn't revealed too much information, leaving him somewhat confused. Clearly, the Illusory Dream World had withheld it on purpose.
Basically, these two levels of Invincible Ones were referred to as Sixth-Grade and Fifth-Grade Invincible Ones. They belonged to the bottom tier of Invincible Ones, yet the majority of Invincible Ones resided within these two levels.
... ..... 0
A Fourth-Grade Invincible One had to master at least three Invincible Ancestral Techniques, and their cultivation had to far exceed that of an ordinary Invincible One to be called such.
A Third-Grade Invincible One required a perfected Invincible Tribulation Body, mastery of multiple Invincible Ancestral Techniques, and the requirement of having ascended as an Invincible One through the sixth tribulation of either the physical body or the soul. Only such an Invincible One could be called Third-Grade.
As for Second-Grade Invincible Ones, the requirements were even higher. If an Invincible One ascended through the Physical Body Tribulation Realm, they were required to have their physical body feed back into their soul, allowing the soul to also undergo tribulation cultivation. By crossing tribulations repeatedly until the soul reached the same level of tribulation, they would become a Second-Grade Invincible One.
As for First-Grade Invincible Ones, that involved the fusion of the Physical Body Tribulation Realm and the Soul Tribulation Realm into one, becoming an Eternal Tribulation Realm Invincible One. That was a First-Grade Invincible One.
"Invincible Ancestors, six grades. The classification is more detailed and has more levels than that of Supreme Ancestors. According to this classification, Tong Zu is likely only a Sixth-Grade Invincible One. As for the Leader of the Illusory Dream World, perhaps they are also just a Sixth-Grade Invincible One, albeit with profound cultivation, infinitely approaching the Fifth-Grade," Ye Tian speculated.
Of course.
There were still many things Ye Tian didn't understand, but he could continue to extort the other five super-grade forces, using the same method to make them provide a certain amount of Tribulation Stones and data.
"That's the plan. No rush to cultivate yet. I'll continue to extort these super-grade forces. They've taken resources from the Dark Forbidden Domain time and again; it's time for some payback!"
Ye Tian thought to himself.


Chapter 1529: Refining Tribulation Stones, Physical Body Nine Tribulations Realm!

Chapter 1529: Refining Tribulation Stones, Physical Body Nine Tribulations Realm!

Following the super-tier power known as the Illusory Dream World, Ye Tian chose the Boundless Wall as his next target.
On this day, Ye Tian arrived at the forbidden land of the Boundless Wall within the Dark Forbidden Domain. Using his formidable strength, he directly captured the strongest experts of the Boundless Wall, thereby threatening this super-tier power. By using these experts as leverage, he obtained ten thousand Tribulation Stones from the Boundless Wall, along with a set of cultivation records, which included information regarding the Eternal Heaven and Earth.
According to the intelligence gathered from the Boundless Wall, the Eternal Heaven and Earth was an otherworldly realm similar to the Dark Forbidden Domain and the Saint Realm, but it was countless times more advanced—it was a realm that truly existed eternally.
Existing eternally meant that the Eternal Heaven and Earth faced no Great Tribulations and would never be destroyed. It remained in existence forever, guarded by countless powerful experts, such that no one dared to invade an Eternal Heaven and Earth.
The Eternal Heaven and Earth was a place many experts dreamed of reaching, but it was not a place of absolute safety; it also harbored slaughter, competition, and more.
However, if one wished to become a truly powerful being, they had to travel to an Eternal Heaven and Earth; this was an unavoidable fact.
But how could a realm become an Eternal Heaven and Earth? Naturally occurring Eternal Heavens and Earths were almost non-existent. They were upgraded step-by-step from ordinary realms. An otherworldly realm would face destruction once every ten thousand Great Tribulation Eras, which was why ten thousand Great Tribulation Eras were referred to as one Kalpa-Era. After enduring one hundred thousand Kalpa-Eras, an otherworldly realm would completely vanish, ceasing to exist entirely.
However, if a Supreme One was born before an otherworldly realm was completely annihilated, they could cause the realm to ascend, extending the limit of one hundred thousand Kalpa-Eras to several hundred thousand.
If it ascended three times, that otherworldly realm could become an Eternal Heaven and Earth.
In other words, an otherworldly realm had to give birth to three Supreme Ones to become an Eternal Heaven and Earth. This was an incredibly difficult feat.
Therefore, Eternal Heavens and Earths were extremely rare. Experts from ordinary otherworldly realms generally could not find them, and many did not even know the name "Eternal Heaven and Earth."
For instance, Ye Tian had not known about the Eternal Heaven and Earth before. If he hadn't learned of its existence from the Illusory Dream World and the Boundless Wall this time, it likely would have taken him a vast amount of time to hear about it.
It had to be said that Ye Tian's luck was quite good, learning about the Eternal Heaven and Earth before even becoming an Invincible.
However, Ye Tian discovered that he did not know how to travel to an Eternal Heaven and Earth.
"It seems I can only learn the method through other super-tier powers," Ye Tian thought to himself.
Ye Tian's third target was the Boundless Demon Sea. Using the same method, he invaded their forbidden land, captured their strongest experts, extorted ten thousand Tribulation Stones, and obtained the method to enter an Eternal Heaven and Earth.
"One must actually become an Invincible to enter an Eternal Heaven and Earth?"
This was the answer Ye Tian received.
Ordinary people, even Supreme Ancestors, could not find the location of an Eternal Heaven and Earth. Rumor had it that they existed in a special space-time, and only a Tier-3 Gate could cross between otherworldly realms to reach one.
However, no power possessed a Tier-3 Gate. Even in an Eternal Heaven and Earth, Tier-3 Gates were incredibly rare and not something an ordinary power could obtain, so one could not rely on them.
But once one became an Invincible, they would vaguely sense the existence of a special place. That special place would be the Eternal Heaven and Earth closest to them. By following that sensation and crossing through various otherworldly realms, one could reach it.
Subsequently, Ye Tian extorted a fourth super-tier power—the Destruction Swamp.
From the Destruction Swamp, Ye Tian obtained another ten thousand Tribulation Stones. The intelligence he gathered was similar to that of the other powers, proving that they had not lied.
At this point, Ye Tian ceased his extortions. He did not go to the forbidden lands of the Firmament Sword Tomb or the Calamity Black Mountain.
This was because these two powers were very formidable, much stronger than the other six super-tier powers. Not only did they have more Invincibles, but their leaders had reached the combat power of a Level 5 Invincible—and they were no ordinary Level 5 Invincibles.
Therefore, extorting these two powers would likely invite a retaliation. If their leaders crossed through a Tier-2 Gate to attack him, even if he hid in the Dark Forbidden Domain, the opponent might still be able to defeat him despite the layers of suppression...
Consequently, he did not dare to take the risk. Unless his strength increased significantly again, rising from the Physical Body Seven Tribulations Realm to the Nine Tribulations Realm, he wouldn't be certain of blocking the attacks of these two super-tier powers.
Besides, he had harvested forty thousand Tribulation Stones this time and gained a lot of intelligence, giving him a clear understanding of future cultivation. He had already gained immensely and had no need to continue risking himself.
In the Mystic Void Ancestral Realm.
Ye Tian took out a Tribulation Stone and performed the Tribulation Transformation Secret Technique to absorb and refine the tribulation power contained within.
BOOM!!!!
Countless amounts of tribulation power surged into Ye Tian's body. Refined by his Tribulation Transformation Secret Technique, it rapidly tempered his physical body.
"Such incredible speed!"
Ye Tian was beyond surprised.
For other experts in the Physical Body Tribulation Realm, Tribulation Stones weren't of much use. The tribulation power within the stones was much harder to refine than the power found during a Great Tribulation—the difficulty was at least dozens of times higher. But for Ye Tian, under the effects of the Tribulation Transformation Secret Technique and his Eternal Talent 'Tribulation,' there was no difference regardless of the type of tribulation power. Since the power within the Tribulation Stones was many times more concentrated, the tempering effect on his physical body was far superior.
It had to be said that Tribulation Stones were indeed priceless treasures for Ye Tian.
Time flew by like a shuttle.
Ye Tian continuously refined the Tribulation Stones one by one. As a large number of stones were consumed, his physical body grew stronger and stronger.
Finally, after consuming seven thousand Tribulation Stones, Ye Tian finally faced his eighth Physical Body Tribulation.
During this tribulation, Ye Tian was significantly injured, but he still managed to pass the eighth Physical Body Tribulation, becoming an expert of the Physical Body Eight Tribulations Realm. His strength was now much greater than before.
Afterward, Ye Tian continued to refine the remaining stones. He still had over thirty thousand Tribulation Stones left and hoped to use them to temper his body to the Physical Body Nine Tribulations Realm.
In the blink of an eye, dozens of cosmic epochs passed.
Finally, Ye Tian had nearly exhausted all thirty thousand plus Tribulation Stones, and he successfully triggered his ninth Physical Body Tribulation. At the cost of being heavily wounded, he successfully crossed it, becoming an expert of the Physical Body Nine Tribulations Realm.


Chapter 1530: Finally Breaking Through, Invincible Ancestor!

Chapter 1530: Finally Breaking Through, Invincible Ancestor!

"It's the limit!"
Ye Tian had a feeling that the Physical Nine Tribulations Realm should be the limit; there was simply no such thing as a Tenth Tribulation Realm.
Moreover, no matter how he used Tribulation Stones to temper his body, he could not progress even a single bit; at the level of the Physical Tribulation Realm, he had already reached the pinnacle.
At this point, his only option was to head to a foreign world and use its rules to influence his body. By repeatedly contending against the rules of the foreign world, he could force his body to undergo a qualitative change, and then, with the help of a large number of Origin Rule Tribulation Crystals, step into the Invincible Realm.
Of course, exposing the physical body to the rules of a foreign world, especially during a non-Great Tribulation period, could turn one into ashes in an instant if one wasn't careful, and even many protective treasures might not be effective.
Furthermore, Ye Tian didn't have any life-saving treasures on him.
As for trading for treasures from other super-tier forces, that was also unrealistic.
"I'll start by using a duplicate body to resist the rules of the foreign world and give it a try. Even if I fail, it'll only be the loss of one duplicate body!"
Ye Tian thought to himself.
---------------
This time, Ye Tian chose to enter the Xiyue Tribe World. He had constructed a Second-Tier Gate between the Xiyue Tribe World and the Dark Forbidden Domain, so entering the Xiyue Tribe World at his current level required no cost.
*Whoosh!*
Ye Tian passed through the Second-Tier Gate and arrived at the base in the Xiyue Tribe World.
Inside the base, Ye Tian looked out at the Xiyue Tribe World, sensing the rules of the outside world.
At this time, the Xiyue Tribe World was not in a Great Tribulation period. Once he entered, he would inevitably face the impact of the rules. Ordinary powerhouses, even those at the third level of the Supreme Realm, would be turned to ashes in an instant with no chance of survival.
Ye Tian was currently a powerhouse in the Physical Nine Tribulations Realm, but whether he could withstand the rules of the Xiyue Tribe World was still unknown.
At this moment.
Some Ancestors of the human race were also here. They all looked toward Ye Tian, waiting for him to enter the Xiyue Tribe World.
They knew Ye Tian was going to attempt to enter the Invincible Realm, so they all wanted to observe. Perhaps in the distant future, they too would have a chance to strike for the Invincible Realm!
Ye Tian had no worries. After all, this was just a duplicate body with no risk to his life, so he naturally didn't hesitate at all.
*Boom!!!*
Ye Tian left the base and stepped into the Xiyue Tribe World.
Immediately, the rules of the Xiyue Tribe World sensed Ye Tian as a foreign intruder, and endless rules crushed down upon him.
*Crack!!!!*
Ye Tian's body cracked. Even with his body at the Physical Nine Tribulations Realm, he couldn't withstand the rules of the foreign world. His body fractured instantly, endless blood flowing out only to be annihilated.
Ye Tian exerted all his strength to cast various defensive Supreme Ancestral Techniques, but they shattered one after another. These techniques couldn't protect him at all because this was a test by the rules against the very foundation of the physical body, something no Supreme Ancestral Technique could block.
Soon, Ye Tian's body could no longer withstand the suppression of the rules. He returned to the base just in time, so this duplicate body wasn't completely annihilated, though it was on the brink of death.
Inside the base.
Ye Tian's duplicate body sat there, sensing the condition within his body to comprehend the gains from this confrontation with the rules of the Xiyue Tribe World.
Soon, he had some small gains.
For example, some parts of his body had turned directly to ash during the confrontation; clearly, those parts could not evolve and needed to be discarded. Meanwhile, some parts had actually undergone slight changes and become stronger, so those areas needed focused tempering.
Afterward, Ye Tian entered the Xiyue Tribe World again to confront the rules once more, but this time the confrontation was very brief before he returned to the base.
Through repeated confrontations, Ye Tian gained a deeper understanding of the mysteries of the physical body.
But eventually, this duplicate body collapsed, unable to be restored.
Shortly after, Ye Tian spent more resources to condense another duplicate body and entered the Xiyue Tribe World again, comprehending the mysteries of the physical body through repeated struggles against the world.
One Realm Era!
Ten Realm Eras!
A hundred Realm Eras!
...
Ye Tian didn't know how many duplicate bodies he had condensed, but many resources from the Dark Forbidden Domain and those seized from other foreign worlds were almost entirely exhausted by him.
However, he finally succeeded.
Through countless condensations of duplicate bodies and countless confrontations with foreign world rules to comprehend physical mysteries, he successfully organized an evolution path suited to himself, allowing his body to undergo a qualitative change under the influence of foreign rules without being harmed.
On this day.
Under the influence of the Xiyue Tribe World's rules and Ye Tian's control, the duplicate body's physical form constantly changed. Some parts were discarded and replaced with a brand-new body. Through these repeated changes, the rules of the Xiyue Tribe World could no longer harm Ye Tian's body.
Moreover, with the consumption of countless resources, Ye Tian's body grew stronger and stronger.
Finally, the body underwent a qualitative change.
*Rumble!!!!*
Countless rules of the Xiyue Tribe World merged into Ye Tian's body, helping it complete its final qualitative change.
It was at this moment that Ye Tian took out a large number of Origin Rule Tribulation Crystals.
Ten!
A hundred!
A thousand!
In the end, Ye Tian consumed over three thousand Origin Rule Tribulation Crystals to achieve a complete breakthrough.
At the moment of breakthrough, Ye Tian's body completely transformed into an Invincible Tribulation Body, and his cultivation stepped into the Invincible Ancestor realm.
Of course, this was the breakthrough of Ye Tian's duplicate body, not his original body.
With the breakthrough of this duplicate body, Ye Tian found that he could permanently solidify this body to become a new clone, but the clone in the Haitian Forbidden Land had to be disbanded.
For Ye Tian, the Heyuan Sacred Beast clone in the Haitian Forbidden Land was too weak and couldn't help him much, so it was better to just disband it.
Thus, Ye Tian disbanded the Heyuan Sacred Beast clone and solidified this duplicate body into a permanent clone.
This way, Ye Tian could let this Invincible Ancestor clone attempt to head to the Eternal World, while his original body could remain in the Dark Forbidden Land to ensure the safety of the Dark Forbidden Domain.
After the duplicate body broke through, Ye Tian finally let his original body attempt it.
Not long after, his original body also completely stepped into the Invincible Ancestor realm.
Thus, Ye Tian was finally considered a true Invincible Ancestor. His strength far surpassed ordinary Invincible Ancestors; even the leader of the Boundless Wall was no longer his match, and his strength was likely infinitely close to a Fifth-Tier Invincible Being.


Chapter 1531: Instantly Killed by a Calamity Beast!

Chapter 1531: Instantly Killed by a Calamity Beast!

After breaking through to become an Invincible Ancestor, Ye Tian's perception broke through the shackles of the Dark Forbidden Domain, and he could even vaguely sense the regions beyond it.
"That is..."
Ye Tian sensed the aura of the Source, but it was an unowned Source, and an incredibly chaotic one at that.
At this moment, Ye Tian clearly realized that he could tear through the void of the Dark Forbidden Domain and travel to the regions outside.
This was an instinct.
Back when he was a Physical Calamity Realm powerhouse, no matter how strong he was, he never had this feeling. This was an ability unique to Invincible beings.
Immediately, Ye Tian's Invincible Ancestor clone tore through the Dark Forbidden Domain and stepped into the region beyond.
*Whoosh!*
As Ye Tian stepped into the ocean of chaotic Source, he immediately realized where he was.
The Source Sea!
The Source Sea was the origin of all Sources. Foreign worlds were born from the Source Sea and annihilated within it. Aside from Invincible beings and those above them, no other living creatures could survive in the Source Sea, nor could they even reach it.
The Source Sea rejected all beings below the Invincible level. Even a powerhouse, even with the help of an Invincible being, could not traverse foreign worlds to reach the Source Sea; they would be directly repelled.
Standing in the Source Sea, although Ye Tian could survive, his strength was heavily suppressed, as if he had instantly become an ordinary being, unable to exert any powerful offensive force.
Of course, the same applied to other beings.
Ye Tian instinctively tried to absorb the Source within the Source Sea, but found he couldn't. The Source here was not only chaotic but also acted as a single entity; a mere Invincible being could not absorb the Source of the Source Sea at all.
It was at this moment that Ye Tian sensed carefully and actually felt a calling—a call coming from the Eternal Heaven and Earth.
"Too far!"
Ye Tian shook his head.
If he traveled through the Source Sea, his current speed was too slow, and the Eternal Heaven and Earth was too far away. It would likely take an incredibly long time to reach it.
Therefore, traveling through the Source Sea while his strength was still relatively low was not a wise choice. Furthermore, the Source Sea was not necessarily without danger, and he didn't dare to cross it recklessly.
However, having vaguely sensed the location of the Eternal Heaven and Earth, he could tear through the void from various foreign worlds into the Source Sea to map out a route.
Basically, the positions of foreign worlds connected to one another within the Source Sea were not too distant, so it was possible to find a route given enough time. Then, he could traverse through foreign worlds one by one and eventually reach the Eternal Heaven and Earth.
Moreover, an Invincible being did not need to rely on Second-Order Gates. As long as they knew the coordinates of another foreign world, they could tear open a temporary gate themselves to reach it.
For example, the Invincible beings of the six Super-Famous level forces wouldn't need a gate if they wanted to enter the Dark Forbidden Domain. They could directly tear through the barriers between two foreign worlds with their true bodies to cross over, though it would consume some of their power.
After becoming an Invincible Ancestor, Ye Tian went into seclusion for a period to stabilize his realm.
Afterward, he began refining various resources to increase his cultivation, but found the progress too slow.
It was as if those resources had suddenly become useless to him.
Upon careful thought, Ye Tian understood.
An Invincible Ancestor had almost surpassed the scope of a single foreign world itself, so the resources born within that world had very little effect on him. Now, aside from Calamity Stones and Calamity Blood, other resources were of no use to him.
If he could enter the Eternal Heaven and Earth, many of the resources there should still be of great help to him.
"The Calamity Stones in my hands are exhausted. To significantly increase my cultivation, a mere few tens of thousands of Calamity Stones are definitely not enough. First-Calamity blood probably won't help much either. Only the blood from a Second-Calamity beast or an even stronger one can significantly boost my cultivation!"
Ye Tian muttered.
Calamity Stones were too difficult to find. Unless he could endure long ages, waiting for foreign worlds to face the end of their Calamity Eras and be destroyed, he wouldn't be able to collect enough. Other Invincible beings might be able to wait, but his cultivation speed was too fast. The time he had spent cultivating didn't even amount to a fraction of theirs, so he didn't have the patience to wait.
Therefore, he currently had only one option: to hunt Calamity Beasts and obtain their blood to increase his cultivation. This blood could even help the human race produce more Physical Calamity Realm powerhouses.
It was difficult for powerhouses to find Calamity Beasts, but it wasn't so hard for an Invincible being.
One day.
Ye Tian condensed an Invincible Ancestor duplicate body and tore through the barrier between the Dark Forbidden Domain and the Yuanmo Heaven and Earth. He descended into the Yuanmo Heaven and Earth because it was currently in the midst of a Great Calamity, so his duplicate's strength would not be suppressed.
Next, Ye Tian's thoughts transformed into individual thought-clones, heading to various parts of the Yuanmo Heaven and Earth to search for the Calamity Beast's location.
After reaching the Invincible Ancestor level, his detection range and mastery over the void far exceeded those of a powerhouse. Thus, he had a ninety percent chance of finding the Calamity Beast's hiding place before the Great Calamity ended.
Time passed slowly.
Finally, as the Great Calamity of the Yuanmo Heaven and Earth was nearing its end, Ye Tian found the Calamity Beast's sleeping place.
Then, Ye Tian's duplicate body descended, tearing through the space-time node with a single strike and discovering the Calamity Beast.
*Boom!!!*
The Calamity Beast's slumber was disturbed. It woke up and glared at Ye Tian in rage.
Then, the beast attacked.
It was relatively easy to identify the strength of a Calamity Beast. A First-Calamity beast had only one Calamity Mark, but this beast possessed 1,795 marks, meaning it was a 1,795-Calamity beast.
This meant that the Yuanmo Heaven and Earth had been destroyed at least 1,795 times, leading to the birth of such a beast.
Ye Tian didn't know exactly how powerful a 1,795-Calamity beast was, but he was about to find out.
The Calamity Beast fixed its gaze on Ye Tian, and he found himself unable to move.
Then, the beast lunged with a claw.
With a *bang*, Ye Tian's duplicate body was instantly killed without any power to resist.
Back in the Dark Forbidden Domain.
Ye Tian's main body sensed the fall of his duplicate and exclaimed in shock, "The Calamity Beast of the Yuanmo Heaven and Earth is actually this powerful!!!"
He finally understood why the Invincible beings of the six Super-Famous level forces didn't hunt Calamity Beasts themselves—because they were too terrifying.
This was a beast that had only survived over a thousand Calamity Eras; how terrifying would one be if it had survived a hundred thousand?.


Chapter 1532: A Thirty-Seven Calamity Calamity Beast!

Chapter 1532: A Thirty-Seven Calamity Calamity Beast!

"Fortunately, I sent a duplicate body. If my main body had gone looking for the Calamity Beast, I would definitely be dead!"
Ye Tian felt a surge of relief.
Other Invincible Ones did not possess duplicate bodies like his. They could only enter otherworld realms in their true forms to search for Calamity Beasts. If they were unlucky enough to encounter a relatively powerful Calamity Beast, they wouldn't even have time to escape.
For instance, the Calamity Beast from just now possessed strength far superior to Ye Tian's. A single glance had pinned his body in place, rendering him unable to move.
According to Ye Tian's estimation, that Calamity Beast's strength was at least comparable to a Third-tier Invincible Ancestor. Compared to it, his strength as a Sixth-tier Invincible Ancestor was practically like that of an ant.
"I have no choice but to give up on the Yuanmo Realm!"
Ye Tian murmured.
He selected another otherworld realm. In any case, the fall of a duplicate body only meant a loss of some resources, which was nothing significant. If he got lucky and encountered a relatively weak Calamity Beast—for example, one below the ten-calamity level—he would have a certain hope of slaying it.
As an Invincible Ancestor, Ye Tian could easily enter various otherworld realms without worrying about being obliterated by their foreign laws.
Each otherworld realm was connected to many others, and countless such realms linked together to form an otherworld realm network.
Therefore, within a very short period, he could find many otherworld realms and determine what stage they were in. Once these realms entered a Great Calamity period, he would enter them to search for Calamity Beasts.
Essentially, every short interval, an otherworld realm would enter a Great Calamity period, and Ye Tian would take action.
It had to be said that weak Calamity Beasts were still very rare. The birth of a One-Calamity Beast in the Dark Forbidden Zone was an incredibly rare occurrence. It was precisely because it was so rare that the supreme experts of the six super-tier forces had set their sights on it.
However, the Invincible Ones looked down on a mere One-Calamity Beast, which was why they hadn't come to the Dark Forbidden Zone to hunt it.
A Calamity Beast that had experienced too few Calamity Eras was not only weak in strength but also contained very little Calamity Power in its Calamity Blood. Naturally, it wasn't of much help to Invincible Ones.
Ye Tian tried time and time again, repeatedly encountering powerful Calamity Beasts. Most of those he met were over a thousand calamities, and occasionally he even encountered those over ten thousand calamities.
Of course, there was one time he encountered a beast of over a hundred calamities, but he was still far from being its match. The opponent's combat power was at least comparable to a top-tier Fifth-tier Invincible Ancestor and could easily inflict heavy injuries on him.
There were also several otherworld realms that surprisingly had no Calamity Beasts. Clearly, the beasts had been hunted, and since a new Calamity Era hadn't passed yet, no new Calamity Beast had been born.
He discovered that these realms had many "Gates," even several Second-tier Gates. Obviously, various forces were keeping a close eye on these special realms, waiting for them to enter a new Calamity Era and birth a new Calamity Beast before striking.
Unknowingly, the Dark Forbidden Zone had already passed six Dark Calendars, with only three remaining before the arrival of the Great Calamity.
Regarding the Great Calamity of the Dark Forbidden Zone, he was no longer worried. Instead, he continued his search for Calamity Beasts.
Finally, on this day, Ye Tian found a Calamity Beast that wasn't overwhelmingly powerful.
A Thirty-Seven Calamity Calamity Beast. Its strength was only equivalent to a Sixth-tier Invincible Ancestor, but it was comparable to the very peak of that tier, not much weaker than a Fifth-tier Invincible Ancestor.
Ye Tian was naturally not its match, but he was able to leave easily.
A Thirty-Seven Calamity Calamity Beast was quite rare, and its strength was relatively weak, meaning there was hope of hunting it.
However, he couldn't hunt it alone.
Even if his main body, duplicate body, and Invincible Ancestor avatar all attacked together, they wouldn't be able to kill a Thirty-Seven Calamity Calamity Beast.
"I can only find people to cooperate with!"
Ye Tian thought to himself.
Currently, only two forbidden lands of super-tier forces remained in the Dark Forbidden Zone: the Firmament Sword Tomb and the Calamity Black Mountain.
As for the other four super-tier forces, they had long since destroyed their Second-tier Gates. Although Ye Tian knew which otherworld realms their headquarters were located in, he didn't want to go looking for them.
The more Invincible Ones involved in the cooperation, the smaller his own harvest would be.
Therefore, he only planned to cooperate with the Firmament Sword Tomb and the Calamity Black Mountain. These two forces were powerful enough; only by cooperating with them would there be hope of slaying that Calamity Beast.
If he cooperated with the other four super-tier forces, they might not be able to handle that beast.
------------
Dark Forbidden Zone, Firmament Sword Tomb Forbidden Land.
Ye Tian arrived here and directly asked the supreme experts guarding the place to contact their Invincible One.
Soon, an Invincible One from the Firmament Sword Tomb descended.
Upon his arrival, the Invincible One was incredibly surprised to see that Ye Tian had reached the Invincible Ancestor realm.
"I didn't expect that not long after this Dark Forbidden Zone was born, an Invincible Ancestor would emerge, and one who achieved it in such a short time. It's truly unexpected!" the Firmament Sword Tomb Invincible One—Shangxu Sword Ancestor—spoke.
"Just good luck!"
Ye Tian said with a smile.
Shangxu Sword Ancestor added, "Since an Invincible One has been born in your Dark Forbidden Zone, our Firmament Sword Tomb will naturally show respect. We will withdraw this Second-tier Gate immediately."
He assumed this was Ye Tian's purpose and spoke preemptively.
However, Ye Tian shook his head and said, "Shangxu Sword Ancestor, my purpose in coming to you is not that. Rather, I wish to cooperate with your Firmament Sword Tomb to slay a Calamity Beast!"
"Slay a Calamity Beast?" Shangxu Sword Ancestor was slightly startled. "Calamity Beasts are very powerful. Many are even comparable to Fourth-tier, Third-tier, or even Second-tier Invincible Ones. We wouldn't dare go looking for them; there's a ninety percent chance of being killed instantly."
Ye Tian quickly said, "Shangxu Sword Ancestor, I have intelligence on the beast's strength. This time, we are dealing with a Thirty-Seven Calamity Calamity Beast. I am not its match alone. I wonder if your Firmament Sword Tomb is interested?"
"A Thirty-Seven Calamity Calamity Beast?"
Shangxu Sword Ancestor became interested.
Although a Calamity Beast of this level was powerful and infinitely close to a Fifth-tier Invincible One, there was at least a hope of slaying it.
"I... our Firmament Sword Tomb agrees!" Shangxu Sword Ancestor consented.
"I will also seek cooperation from the Calamity Black Mountain," Ye Tian added.
"No problem!" Shangxu Sword Ancestor nodded. "The leader of our Firmament Sword Tomb is in an Eternal Realm and cannot be contacted for the time being. Cooperating with the Calamity Black Mountain will give us a greater certainty of slaying that beast. However, can you ensure your intelligence is correct?"
"Naturally. I went there personally; how could it be false? When the time comes, I will strike first, and you can follow behind. If the intelligence is wrong, you can withdraw immediately!" Ye Tian guaranteed.
"Then I have no issues!"
Shangxu Sword Ancestor said.
Subsequently, Ye Tian contacted the Calamity Black Mountain. After speaking with their Invincible One, they were also willing to take action.
After all, the value of a Thirty-Seven Calamity Calamity Beast far exceeded that of a One-Calamity Beast. Even for Invincible Ones, it held great value.
Ye Tian chose a date and united eight Invincible Ones from the two super-tier forces, Firmament Sword Tomb and Calamity Black Mountain. Adding in Ye Tian's two Invincible-level combatants—his duplicate body and his Invincible Ancestor avatar—it was equivalent to a total of ten Invincible Ones being deployed.


Chapter 1533: Slaying the Calamity Beast, A Massive Harvest!

Chapter 1533: Slaying the Calamity Beast, A Massive Harvest!

The Cloud Mist World.
Ye Tian and the other Invincible Ones descended upon this place, but the others were secretly preparing their retreat, faintly tearing at the world barrier to ensure they wouldn't lack the time to escape.
These were necessary preparations; after all, one could never be too careful when hunting a Calamity Beast.
"Ancestor of Myriad Laws, to think you are an Invincible One with the ability to create clones. As far as I know, aside from a few special Invincible Ones, others have no way of condensing a clone," remarked the Ancestor of Dragon Calamity, the Vice Mountain Lord of the Calamity Black Mountain.
"It's just a mere clone, of no great use!"
Ye Tian replied evasively, not revealing much.
The Ancestor of Dragon Calamity did not press further; their mission this time was to hunt the Calamity Beast.
The primary combatants this time were not Ye Tian, but rather the Ancestor of Dragon Calamity from the Calamity Black Mountain and the Ancestor of Ten Thousand Origin Swords from the Firmament Sword Tomb. These two Invincible Ones were much stronger than Ye Tian. Although Ye Tian could possess top-tier 5th-grade Ancestor combat power—which was indeed terrifying for someone who had just broken through to become an Invincible Ancestor—the gap between a newly ascended Invincible Ancestor and a true 5th-grade Invincible Ancestor was immense. It wouldn't be an exaggeration to call it a hundredfold difference.
Some Invincible Ones, despite not having created an Invincible Ancestral Technique and thus being unable to officially become 5th-grade Invincible Ones, could still possess 5th-grade combat power or even surpass ordinary 5th-grade Invincible Ones if their cultivation was profound enough.
The Ancestor of Dragon Calamity and the Ancestor of Ten Thousand Origin Swords both possessed combat power at the threshold of the 5th-grade, far beyond what an ordinary newly ascended Invincible One could compare to.
However, a 37-Calamity Beast also possessed combat power infinitely close to a 5th-grade Invincible One. A 6th-grade Invincible One would find it impossible to kill such a beast. After all, if the disparity in strength wasn't massive, it was very difficult for a battle between Invincible Ones to result in death.
For instance, while the Ancestor of Dragon Calamity was stronger than the 37-Calamity Beast, he still wouldn't be able to kill it on his own.
This was only possible now because the Cloud Mist World was currently undergoing a Great Calamity. Once the Great Calamity passed, they would have no way to hunt such a beast.
Furthermore, a 37-Calamity Beast was very likely to grasp a certain level of World Authority, allowing it to temporarily disperse the power of the Great Calamity. If that happened, the Invincible Ones would have to endure the suppression of the world's rules, and their strength would be greatly diminished.
At that point, under the suppression of the Cloud Mist World's rules, even the Ancestor of Dragon Calamity would be no match for the Calamity Beast.
Therefore, they needed to unite to surround and kill the 37-Calamity Beast; otherwise, they would never succeed.
"It's right here!"
Ye Tian pointed to a space-time node not far away.
The Invincible Ones from the Calamity Black Mountain and the Firmament Sword Tomb did not approach. Instead, they had Ye Tian strike the space-time node first. Only after confirming that this beast was indeed a 37-Calamity Beast would they take action.
Thus, Ye Tian struck without hesitation.
Boom!!!
The space-time node shattered, and a Calamity Beast carrying heaven-shaking rage appeared. Its massive body occupied the entire area, and its terrifying aura made even ordinary Invincible Ones tremble.
Thirty-seven calamity markings were visible on the beast's body, proving its strength.
"It truly is a 37-Calamity Beast!"
The Invincible Ones from the Calamity Black Mountain and the Firmament Sword Tomb exclaimed in pleasant surprise.
"Attack together!"
The Ancestor of Dragon Calamity shouted.
Rumble!!!!!
Ten Invincible Ones attacked simultaneously, easily overwhelming the Calamity Beast.
In a short time, the beast's body was covered in craters and wounds, with countless streams of blood flowing out. Its injuries were extremely severe.
Suddenly.
The Calamity Beast invoked the Authority of the Cloud Mist World, dispersing the power of the Great Calamity.
In an instant, several Invincible Ones were struck by the rules of the Cloud Mist World, and their strength was immediately and severely compromised.
However, they were Invincible Ones after all; their strength was merely suppressed.
Abruptly.
Ye Tian's duplicated body was suppressed by the rules, and at the same time, half of its body was blown apart by the beast's desperate strike, resulting in significant injuries.
As the duplicated body was injured, it retreated slightly, letting the clone take its place to give the duplicated body time to recover.
In this manner, one Invincible One after another was injured and retreated. Only the Ancestor of Dragon Calamity and the Ancestor of Ten Thousand Origin Swords remained completely uninjured. After all, their strength was superior to the beast's; even with the sudden suppression of the rules and the resulting drop in power, they were strong enough to ensure they weren't hurt.
Wielding World Authority was not without cost, and soon the Calamity Beast could no longer control it. Combined with its worsening injuries, its strength continued to plummet.
Finally.
The Calamity Beast was blasted to death, its massive corpse lying motionless in the void.
Now that the Calamity Beast was dead, the Invincible Ones breathed a sigh of relief, their faces lighting up with excitement.
The value of a 37-Calamity Beast's corpse was immense.
Swish, swish, swish!!!!
The beast's physical body began to disintegrate, and a dense cluster of Origin Rule Calamity Crystals flew out from its remains.
. . . . . . . . .
The number of these Origin Rule Calamity Crystals far exceeded those of a 1-Calamity Beast. Back then, a 1-Calamity Beast yielded over ten thousand crystals, but this 37-Calamity Beast yielded over a hundred thousand.
In addition to the hundred thousand plus Origin Rule Calamity Crystals, thirteen portions of Calamity Blood flew out, along with several bones emitting powerful auras.
"Let's divide the Origin Rule Calamity Crystals first!"
The Ancestor of Dragon Calamity suggested.
"Agreed!" Ye Tian concurred.
After some discussion, since Ye Tian contributed the combat power of two Invincible Ones and was the planner and discoverer of this hunt, he naturally received a larger share of the crystals, obtaining twenty thousand Origin Rule Calamity Crystals.
. . . . . . .
This was a massive harvest for Ye Tian. He had previously exhausted his supply of Origin Rule Calamity Crystals in order to break through to the Invincible level.
Originally, he had obtained over five thousand crystals, nearly six thousand in total. Combined with the crystals he had acquired from various factions, his travels to different foreign worlds, his conflicts with other powers, and the slaying of various supreme experts, he had amassed over six thousand.
However, between his main body and his clone both breaking through to the Invincible realm, those six thousand-plus crystals were just barely enough and had been completely consumed.
But now, suddenly acquiring over twenty thousand crystals, his wealth was once again substantial.
For an Invincible One, Origin Rule Calamity Crystals were of significant value, serving as a form of currency. If he went to the Eternal World in the future, he wouldn't be able to buy anything without them.
After dividing the crystals, the group began to distribute the thirteen portions of Calamity Blood.
"I want two portions of Calamity Blood! That's not asking too much, is it?"
Ye Tian spoke up.
With ten Invincible Ones dividing thirteen portions of Calamity Blood, and him counting as two Invincible Ones, asking for only two portions was definitely a modest request.
But he was well aware that the Calamity Blood of a 37-Calamity Beast was far superior to that of a 1-Calamity Beast. Its benefit to an Invincible One was immense, far exceeding that of the Origin Rule Calamity Crystals.
His current strength was still relatively low, so there was no need to fight these powerful Invincible Ones for more blood.
"That's acceptable!"
Seeing that Ye Tian only wanted two portions, the other Invincible Ones readily agreed.


Chapter 1534: Refining Tribulation Blood, Strength Greatly Increases!

Chapter 1534: Refining Tribulation Blood, Strength Greatly Increases!

Ye Tian took two portions of Tribulation Blood. Ancestor Dragon Calamity and Ancestor Wanyuan Sword, who contributed the most, each took two and a half portions. The remaining six Invincibles each received one portion. Thus, the thirteen portions of Tribulation Blood were distributed, and no one objected.
After all, for them, this opportunity was practically a windfall!
"Next is the distribution of these Tribulation Bones!"
Ancestor Dragon Calamity spoke.
"What are Tribulation Bones?" Ye Tian asked.
Ancestor Wanyuan Sword explained, "Tribulation Bones come from Tribulation Beasts. Generally, Tribulation Beasts of ten tribulations or more will produce Tribulation Bones, but the quantity is uncertain. We're lucky this time; a total of nine Tribulation Bones were produced from this Tribulation Beast. Tribulation Bones have only one use: artifact refining. Weapons suitable for us Invincibles are rare; for instance, Tribulation Artifacts refined from Tribulation Bones are of significant help to us. Tribulation Bones are extremely precious. A single bone from a thirty-seven tribulation beast is worth about thirty thousand Source Rule Tribulation Crystals."
"One bone is worth thirty thousand Source Rule Tribulation Crystals!!!"
Ye Tian was surprised.
He only now realized that the Source Rule Tribulation Crystals he had obtained before weren't actually worth much. Not only were they inferior to Tribulation Blood, they weren't even as valuable as these Tribulation Bones!
No wonder the Invincibles had little interest in one-tribulation beasts. A one-tribulation beast really didn't have much value. Any small item from a thirty-seven tribulation beast far exceeded the value of a one-tribulation beast. Hunting powerful Tribulation Beasts was the real money-making business.
Unfortunately, Tribulation Beasts were too dangerous. Without confirming a beast's strength, Invincibles didn't dare to seek them out, as they could perish with the slightest mistake.
After some discussion regarding the nine Tribulation Bones, Ye Tian received only one, and the others each received one as well.
However, the other Invincibles each gave Ye Tian over 1,000 Source Rule Tribulation Crystals as compensation. Since Ye Tian had discovered the beast, he naturally deserved more benefits.
Next, the flesh and blood of the beast were also distributed. They held some value, worth about several dozen Source Rule Tribulation Crystals.
In this way, the Tribulation Beast was completely divided up.
After the distribution, Ye Tian left the Cloud Mist World and returned to the Dark Forbidden Zone.
The Invincibles of the Calamity Black Mountain and the Firmament Sword Tomb also returned to their respective worlds, bringing the cooperation to an end.
Calamity Black Mountain.
An Invincible asked Ancestor Dragon Calamity, "Lord Ancestor Dragon Calamity, why didn't we just take down that Ancestor of Myriad Laws? With your strength plus ours, there was definitely hope of capturing him."
"Too risky!" Ancestor Dragon Calamity said. "For him to become an Invincible in just one or two Great Tribulation Eras, his talent is too terrifying. Moreover, can you guarantee that these two Invincible bodies are his main body? What if they are both clones? Once we act, it would be equivalent to offending an Invincible who can create clones. Once he grows up, it would be a disaster for our Calamity Black Mountain. Besides, for two portions of Tribulation Blood, one Tribulation Bone, and some Source Rule Tribulation Crystals, it's not worth it. Even if he really came in person, are you sure the people from the Firmament Sword Tomb wouldn't help him, perhaps creating a future enemy for us? Furthermore, this Ancestor of Myriad Laws might be using clones to find Tribulation Beasts, so he isn't afraid of falling. Perhaps in the future, we will have more opportunities to cooperate with him and obtain more Tribulation Blood, so there's no need to offend him."
"Lord Ancestor Dragon Calamity is right!"
The other Invincibles nodded one after another.
Similarly, a similar conversation took place at the Firmament Sword Tomb.
---------------
"They didn't make a move?"
Ye Tian thought to himself.
He had thought the Invincibles of the Firmament Sword Tomb and Calamity Black Mountain would attack him, but nothing happened. This was naturally a good thing.
After returning to the Dark Forbidden Zone, Ye Tian began secluded cultivation to absorb and refine those two portions of Tribulation Blood.
Meanwhile, the Firmament Sword Tomb and Calamity Black Mountain destroyed those two Second-Tier Gates and no longer established bases in the Dark Forbidden Zone.
From then on, except for the gates controlled by Ye Tian, there were no more gates of foreign forces in the Dark Forbidden Zone.
It could be said that the human race had completely taken control of the Dark Forbidden Zone, with no more external enemies.
Ye Tian absorbed and refined the Tribulation Blood of the thirty-seven tribulation beast. Endless, gentle tribulation power surged into Ye Tian's body, continuously tempering his Invincible Tribulation Body.
Other Invincibles' utilization rate of Tribulation Blood was likely only around ten percent, with most of it being wasted. But Ye Tian, who possessed the Tribulation Transformation Secret Technique and the Eternal Talent 'Tribulation', could definitely utilize the Tribulation Blood one hundred percent.
Therefore, two portions of Tribulation Blood in his hands were equivalent to at least twenty portions refined by other Invincibles.
It was conceivable that once he completely refined these two portions of Tribulation Blood, his cultivation would likely increase significantly, and his combat power would naturally surge by a great tribulation.
Time passed slowly. Ye Tian's Tribulation Blood was continuously refined, his Invincible Tribulation Body grew stronger, and his cultivation level rose higher.
Using the Tribulation Transformation Secret Technique, Ye Tian's refining speed was very fast. In just a few domain years, Ye Tian had completely refined one portion of Tribulation Blood. After spending some time stabilizing his realm, he began refining the second portion.
Perhaps due to his increased strength, the refining speed was even faster this time.
About two domain years passed, and the second portion of Tribulation Blood was also refined by Ye Tian.
Afterward, Ye Tian entered the Source Sea to test his strength and found that his combat power had increased by about three times.
Originally, his strength was already very powerful among Sixth-Tier Invincibles. Now that his strength had tripled, although he was still not as strong as Invincibles like Ancestor Dragon Calamity, he wasn't much weaker, roughly equivalent to the strength of a thirty-seven tribulation beast.
In other words, he was not far from the threshold of a Fifth-Tier Invincible.
However, if he didn't create an Invincible Ancestral Technique, the increase in strength from just using treasures and resources to raise his cultivation would be limited, and in the later stages, it wouldn't improve even a tiny bit.
However, to create an Invincible Ancestral Technique, one must go to the Eternal World to comprehend its rules.
The Eternal World had no Great Tribulations, so Source Rule Tribulation Crystals would not be born there; thus, one had to go to the Eternal World in person.
"I'll look for some more Tribulation Beasts. Once my strength reaches a point where it's hard to progress further, I'll go to the Eternal World!" Ye Tian planned.
In the following days, he continued to search for Tribulation Beasts.
This time, with his increased strength, even if he encountered a powerful Tribulation Beast, he wouldn't be easily killed instantly. However, if he encountered a beast with thousands of tribulations, he would still be unable to escape.
Finally, one day, Ye Tian encountered another Tribulation Beast that he had a hope of hunting. Moreover, he didn't need to rely on others; just by relying on his duplicated body and his clone—two Invincible-level combat forces—he had hope of hunting it down, as this Tribulation Beast only had twenty-eight tribulations.


Chapter 1535: Purchasing Intelligence!

Chapter 1535: Purchasing Intelligence!

Ye Tian could kill a 28th Tribulation beast on his own, so naturally, he wouldn't seek cooperation with other Invincible Ones; otherwise, he would have to share the profits with them.
Thus, on this day, he dispatched his duplicate body along with his Invincible Ancestor clone to enter this foreign world named Jiuhe.
Jiuhe World.
As soon as Ye Tian arrived, he immediately attacked the Tribulation Beast.
Rumble!!!
The battle erupted. Ye Tian used two Invincible-level combat forces to besiege this 28th Tribulation beast. The duplicate body was the strongest, while the Invincible Ancestor clone was the weakest.
Although the clone was decent and didn't occupy a duplicate body slot, it functioned as an individual entity that needed to cultivate on its own; it couldn't be as powerful as the main body like the duplicate body was.
Of course, having an extra clone was still beneficial.
Although Ye Tian's strength was greater than this Tribulation Beast's, the difference was limited. Therefore, it took a long time to besiege the beast. The duplicate body even went to any lengths, repeatedly inflicting heavy damage on the beast at the cost of sustaining severe injuries itself.
Eventually, the duplicate body collapsed and perished, but the Tribulation Beast was also on the brink of death and was subsequently slain by Ye Tian's clone.
This was a one-for-one trade. For an ordinary person, it would naturally be unprofitable, but Ye Tian didn't care about the death of this duplicate body; after all, it only cost some resources to replace.
In reality, if Ye Tian had been more careful, the duplicate body wouldn't have perished, as its strength was indeed greater than the Tribulation Beast's.
However, Ye Tian didn't want to waste time. If the time for the Great Tribulation in Jiuhe World passed, he wouldn't be able to kill the beast and would have to wait for another Great Tribulation Era.
That was why he chose this "life-for-a-life" method to quickly end the battle.
Crack!!!
The body of the 28th Tribulation beast disintegrated, turning into a large amount of Origin Rule Tribulation Crystals, Tribulation Blood, and Tribulation Bone.
Eighty thousand Origin Rule Tribulation Crystals, ten portions of Tribulation Blood, and six portions of Tribulation Bone.
Although the value of the Tribulation Blood and Bone wasn't as high as those from a 37th Tribulation beast, the value of these resources was still immense, far exceeding the harvest Ye Tian had gained from killing the 37th Tribulation beast previously.
After all, this time the harvest belonged entirely to him alone.
Ye Tian collected these items, even taking the entire carcass of the Tribulation Beast, and returned to the Dark Forbidden Zone.
...
"Hahaha, the harvest is massive! Hunting Tribulation Beasts alone is much more satisfying!"
Ye Tian said excitedly.
However, his current strength was limited; he could only kill weaker Tribulation Beasts. Once he encountered a truly powerful one, he wouldn't be able to kill it no matter what.
But this harvest was so significant that it was enough to push his strength a bit further. Perhaps it would be enough to rival the Ancestor of Dragon Calamity and the Wanyuan Sword Ancestor, those two Invincible Ones.
Subsequently, Ye Tian began to absorb and refine those ten portions of Tribulation Blood. Although each portion was less effective than the blood of a 37th Tribulation beast, there was a large quantity!
As portion after portion of Tribulation Blood was consumed and refined, Ye Tian's cultivation rose rapidly, and his strength grew steadily.
Finally, after a long time, all ten portions of Tribulation Blood were refined.
At this moment, Ye Tian felt a vague bottleneck. If he couldn't comprehend an Invincible Ancestral Technique to cause a qualitative change in his physical body, he wouldn't be able to increase his cultivation quickly.
In other words, at his current level, he could only go to the Eternal World to meditate on the world rules there and attempt to comprehend an Invincible Ancestral Technique.
"It's time to head to the Eternal World. My current strength is not inferior to the Ancestor of Dragon Calamity, which is equivalent to stepping over the threshold of a Fifth-Grade Invincible combat power, though I am not yet a true Fifth-Grade Invincible One."
Ye Tian murmured.
However, before heading to the Eternal World, he wanted to learn more about the situation there from the Firmament Sword Tomb power.
Although the Firmament Sword Tomb had destroyed the Tier 2 Gate connecting to the Dark Forbidden Zone, Ye Tian knew which foreign world the Firmament Sword Tomb was located in.
After all, he knew the locations of countless nearby foreign worlds and naturally understood the locations of those six super-tier powers.
In fact, there were more than six super-tier powers among the nearby foreign worlds; there were many, such as the Blood Mist Alliance, which was also a super-tier power.
However, Ye Tian had not made contact with the other super-tier powers, temporarily only dealing with these six.
On this day.
Through another foreign world, Ye Tian contacted a base of the Firmament Sword Tomb rather than entering their home world directly, which would have been equivalent to declaring war.
"I am looking for your Firmament Sword Tomb's Wanyuan Sword Ancestor!"
Ye Tian spoke.
The powerhouses of the Firmament Sword Tomb immediately went to notify their headquarters, and soon an Invincible One descended upon the base.
This Invincible One was not the Wanyuan Sword Ancestor, but another Invincible One of the Firmament Sword Tomb—the Shifang Sword Ancestor.
The Shifang Sword Ancestor was also one of the Invincible Ones who had cooperated with Ye Tian to hunt the Tribulation Beast last time. His strength wasn't particularly great, but his current aura was slightly stronger than before, though not by much.
After all, other Invincible Ones couldn't absorb and refine Tribulation Power as quickly as Ye Tian. Therefore, even if the Shifang Sword Ancestor had obtained Tribulation Blood, his refining speed was slow and his utilization rate wasn't high, so it was impossible for his strength to skyrocket all at once.
"Ancestor of Myriad Laws!"
The Shifang Sword Ancestor said politely.
"Shifang Sword Ancestor, is Wanyuan Sword Ancestor not here?" Ye Tian asked casually.
"He is not!" Shifang Sword Ancestor replied. "Wanyuan Sword Ancestor has left the Firmament Sword Tomb for the Eternal World. At his level, it is very difficult to increase his strength; he must comprehend an Invincible Sword Technique to undergo a transformation. Last time, he obtained Tribulation Blood and Bone, so he went to the Eternal World to sell them in exchange for treasures that could help him, thereby attempting to comprehend an Invincible Sword Technique."
"So that's how it is!"
Ye Tian understood.
It was difficult for Wanyuan Sword Ancestor's cultivation to improve further, and refining Tribulation Blood would be a waste, so selling it directly was the best choice.
"Shifang Sword Ancestor, I wish to learn about the situation in the Eternal World, such as the route and some details within the Eternal World. I wonder if the Firmament Sword Tomb can inform me?" Ye Tian asked.
Shifang Sword Ancestor smiled and said, "Ancestor of Myriad Laws, whether in the Eternal World or in the various foreign worlds, we follow the principle of equivalent exchange. If you want information, you must pay a certain amount in treasures; otherwise, our Firmament Sword Tomb will not provide any intelligence!"
Ye Tian didn't feel like haggling with the Shifang Sword Ancestor. Moreover, he was now an Invincible One and wouldn't do something as beneath him as capturing the Firmament Sword Tomb's powerhouses to threaten the Shifang Sword Ancestor; that would be too degrading.
Thus, Ye Tian chose to pay some Origin Rule Tribulation Crystals to purchase the information.
In the end, Ye Tian paid 3,000 Origin Rule Tribulation Crystals and obtained a route map to the Eternal World from the Shifang Sword Ancestor, as well as some specific intelligence regarding the Eternal World, including some of the powers within and things to watch out for.
For Ye Tian, using Origin Rule Tribulation Crystals to buy this information was naturally worth it.


Chapter 1536: Tianqi Realm, Eternal Realm!

Chapter 1536: Tianqi Realm, Eternal Realm!

The route map obtained from the trade with the Ten Directions Sword Ancestor recorded the coordinates of various exotic realms. He only needed to follow these coordinates, directly tear through the barriers of each exotic realm, and descend upon them to reach an Eternal Realm.
According to the instructions on the route map, he needed to traverse 298 exotic realms to reach the one closest to the Eternal Realm. At that time, he would enter the Source Sea and from there enter the Eternal Realm. After all, ordinary Invincible Ones could not tear through the barrier of an Eternal Realm and could only enter through the Source Sea.
Ye Tian memorized this route map and sent his duplicate body to the Eternal Realm. This way, even if it perished, his own life would not be at risk.
Ye Tian's speed was very fast. He crossed one exotic realm after another and arrived at the exotic realm closest to the Eternal Realm in just a few days.
This exotic realm was named Bogu. Ye Tian entered the Source Sea directly from the Bogu Realm and immediately saw an incomparably massive phantom. This phantom was an Eternal Realm.
Ye Tian could only vaguely sense the existence of the Eternal Realm, so the distance between them was still very far.
Thus, it took Ye Tian several years to fly to the vicinity of this Eternal Realm.
At this time, he discovered several gateways around the phantom.
"Those are Tier 3 Gates!"
Ye Tian guessed.
Because he could build Tier 2 Gates himself, and Tier 2 Gates were far inferior to these gates, it was clear they were Tier 3 Gates.
Tier 3 Gates could accommodate Invincible Ones, so all Invincible Ones could enter the Eternal Realm through them.
As for Supreme Ones, why would they need Tier 3 Gates? They could likely enter the Eternal Realm with ease.
Therefore, it was enough for the Eternal Realm to build these Tier 3 Gates.
According to the intelligence from the Ten Directions Sword Ancestor, entering the Eternal Realm was not without a price; a certain amount of Source Rule Tribulation Crystals had to be paid.
Although the Eternal Realm was good, it had no Great Tribulations, so it could not produce Source Rule Tribulation Crystals. Thus, the Eternal Realm used the collection of Source Rule Tribulation Crystals as a toll.
In this way, the Eternal Realm could obtain countless Source Rule Tribulation Crystals without paying any price.
Whoosh!
Ye Tian flew to a Tier 3 Gate and was immediately stopped by an Invincible One.
This Invincible One's aura was terrifying, far exceeding Ye Tian's imagination. He was clearly an incredibly powerful Invincible One.
"Stranger, are you paying one Source Rule Tribulation Crystal as a toll, or are you applying for a permanent Eternal Token?" the Invincible One asked.
"Applying for a permanent Eternal Token!" Ye Tian said.
If one did not apply for an Eternal Token, they would have to pay one Source Rule Tribulation Crystal every time they entered or exited the Eternal Realm.
Once or twice might not be much, but if one entered and exited dozens, hundreds, or even thousands of times, the cost in Source Rule Tribulation Crystals would be significant.
Applying for an Eternal Token only cost 1,000 Source Rule Tribulation Crystals. Therefore, most Invincible Ones would apply for one. Only some newly ascended Invincible Ones who did not have many crystals would choose to pay the single crystal toll.
Soon, Ye Tian completed the procedures, paid 1,000 Source Rule Tribulation Crystals, and received an Eternal Token.
Afterward, Ye Tian entered this Eternal Realm.
-------------------
This Eternal Realm was known as the Tianqi Realm. The Tianqi Realm was incredibly vast, divided into hundreds of thousands of regions. Each region had countless giant trading cities. No one knew how many Invincible Ones lived here; many were outsiders who resided here permanently.
However, living in the Tianqi Realm was not without a price. One Source Rule Tribulation Crystal had to be paid every Great Tribulation Era. This applied to everyone, and no one could avoid it.
If one tried to hide to avoid paying, the consequences would be miserable. No one could hide from it.
Although Ye Tian had obtained an Eternal Token, it only waived the entry and exit fees. If he stayed in the Tianqi Realm for a Great Tribulation Era, he would still have to pay one Source Rule Tribulation Crystal.
After entering the Tianqi Realm, Ye Tian kept a very low profile. He did not use his divine sense to probe the surroundings. If he provoked a powerful and ill-tempered Invincible One, they might attack him.
The ones that should never be provoked in the Tianqi Realm were the eight Great Eternal-rank powers. Each Eternal-rank power possessed at least one Supreme One.
Below the eight Eternal-rank powers were over a hundred Saint-rank powers. The requirements to become a Saint-rank power were also very high; they had to possess a First-class Invincible One.
As for Transcend-rank powers, they were too numerous to count.
Basically, as long as one did not provoke the Eternal-rank or Saint-rank powers, newly ascended Invincible Ones were relatively safe. Fighting did occur in the Tianqi Realm, but it was rare, especially inside the giant trading cities where fighting was prohibited.
Ye Tian came to the Tianqi Realm this time not only to comprehend an Invincible Ancestral Technique but also to join a power.
Although he possessed the Copying Talent, it would be difficult to obtain certain heritage knowledge and grow without a power to rely on.
