Knowledge was extremely important. If he had not threatened or infiltrated various exotic powers to obtain pieces of knowledge, he would not have been able to enter the Invincible Realm, or even become a Paramount Being.
Furthermore, joining a power meant having a backer. Before fully growing up, he would not have to worry about safety issues.
Just like when he was weak and joined the War Sect. The War Sect helped him a lot and protected him. Without the War Sect's protection, he would have died countless times already; the Copying Talent could not save his life every time!
But he also knew very well that the Eternal-rank and Saint-rank powers of the Tianqi Realm would not easily recruit Invincible Ones. Only those weak Transcend-rank powers would be eager to recruit Invincible Ones to expand their influence.
Ye Tian had no interest in Transcend-rank powers. His minimum requirement was a Saint-rank power, and ideally, he could join an Eternal-rank power.
Tianqi Realm, Juewu District, Juewu City.
This was a fairly famous giant trading city in the Tianqi Realm, where many powers had branches.
Ye Tian came here, first, to trade away the Tribulation Bones he had, and second, to purchase some knowledge and inquire about how to join those Saint-rank or Eternal-rank powers.
After arriving at Juewu City, he found that the cultivation level here was very high. Naturally, there were not many Invincible Ones, but there were many cultivators comparable to Ancestors, and the weakest were comparable to Domain Ancestors.
Soon, Ye Tian arrived at a shop in Juewu City.


Chapter 1537: Saint-Name Level Power—Tianfeng Sea!

Chapter 1537: Saint-Name Level Power—Tianfeng Sea!

Blood Wolf Pavilion.
Ye Tian walked into this shop. As soon as he entered, he encountered a Supreme Powerhouse clerk, and one in the Physical Body Tribulation Realm at that, with a cultivation of approximately the Third Physical Body Tribulation Realm.
In the Tianlin Realm, only Invincibles held a certain level of status. Supreme Powerhouses, even those in the Physical Body Tribulation Realm, had little status and it was quite normal for them to serve as clerks.
Blood Wolf Pavilion not only sold various treasures but also purchased them.
In the center of the Blood Wolf Pavilion was a massive screen displaying various treasures and their prices.
Nine-Leaf Blood Qi Grass: 1,000 Origin Rule Tribulation Crystals.
Yang Cloud Stone: 8,000 Origin Rule Tribulation Crystals.
Tribulation Stone: 100 Origin Rule Tribulation Crystals.
First Tribulation Blood: 80,000 Origin Rule Tribulation Crystals.
Tenth Tribulation Blood: 200,000 Origin Rule Tribulation Crystals.
Hundredth Tribulation Blood: 3,000,000 Origin Rule Tribulation Crystals.
Thousandth Tribulation Blood: 50,000,000 Origin Rule Tribulation Crystals.
...
"The value of Tribulation Blood is actually this high!"
Ye Tian was incredibly surprised.
If his strength grew in the future and he could easily slaughter Thousandth Tribulation Beasts, wouldn't he be able to effortlessly obtain countless Origin Rule Tribulation Crystals?
However, he then thought that once his strength increased, perhaps a hundred million Origin Rule Tribulation Crystals wouldn't mean much to him anymore.
367
The screen also listed Tribulation Bones for sale. Based on their value, a Thirty-Seventh Tribulation Bone was worth about 300,000 each, which was cheaper than Tribulation Blood, as Thirty-Seventh Tribulation Blood was worth roughly 800,000 Origin Rule Tribulation Crystals.
Of course, if Ye Tian were to sell Tribulation Bones, he certainly wouldn't get such a high price, as the Blood Wolf Pavilion also needed to make a profit.
Ye Tian did not sell the Thirty-Seventh Tribulation Bone; instead, he sold those Twenty-Eighth Tribulation Bones.
He didn't sell all of them, only three. Each bone sold for 180,000, totaling 540,000 Origin Rule Tribulation Crystals.
This caused the number of Origin Rule Tribulation Crystals on Ye Tian's person to skyrocket instantly.
"It seems that when hunting Tribulation Beasts, the real money is in the Tribulation Blood and Tribulation Bones. The Origin Rule Tribulation Crystals found on the beasts themselves are actually of the lowest value!" Ye Tian thought to himself.
The Blood Wolf Pavilion had many treasures, including many that were helpful to Ancestors and Supreme Ancestors. There was also a treasure called the Emperor Blood Soul. This type of treasure was a supreme rarity for Ancestors who had not ascended by creating their own Ancestral Laws. It could make the foundation of the physical body even stronger and remove the barrier between the body and the Ancestral Law, increasing their compatibility.
This way, those Ancestors could rival those who had created their own Ancestral Laws, giving them hope of ascending to higher realms in the future.
Ye Tian's wife and children had all become Ancestors by merging with his Ancestral Law and were thus affected by this limitation. However, if they refined the Emperor Blood Soul, this influence would cease to exist.
Of course, the Emperor Blood Soul was also incredibly precious, valued at 2 million Origin Rule Tribulation Crystals.
Ye Tian needed four pieces of Emperor Blood Soul, which would cost a total of 8 million Origin Rule Tribulation Crystals.
Ye Tian couldn't afford it right now; even if he sold all the Tribulation Bones he had, he still wouldn't be able to afford it.
Therefore, Ye Tian planned to purchase the Emperor Blood Souls the next time he came to the Tianlin Realm.
...
Over the following period, Ye Tian remained in Juewu City to understand the situation. Not only did he learn about the uses of many treasures and greatly expand his knowledge, but he also learned a secret: once the Supreme Ones of the Eternal Heaven and Earth leave the Eternal Heaven and Earth and enter a Foreign World, their strength is severely suppressed.
Because of this, it is incredibly difficult for Supreme Ones from the Eternal Heaven and Earth to enter Foreign Worlds to hunt Tribulation Beasts. Even an incredibly powerful First-Class Supreme One, under conditions where their strength is infinitely suppressed, could very likely perish if they went to hunt Tribulation Beasts.
For this reason, very few Supreme Ones from the Eternal Heaven and Earth go to hunt Tribulation Beasts. Only powerful Supreme Ones who rose from the Foreign Worlds dare to hunt them, and even then, they need to investigate thoroughly, sometimes even using weaker individuals as bait to understand the beast's strength before daring to strike.
Since more than ninety-nine percent of Supreme Ones come from the Eternal Heaven and Earth, Supreme Ones who go to hunt Tribulation Beasts are extremely rare.
This is also why the value of Tribulation Blood and Tribulation Bones is so high.
Furthermore.
If one kills too many Tribulation Beasts, they will carry the aura of the beasts' resentment. Once this aura accumulates to a certain level, it will attract the attention of some terrifying Tribulation Beasts.
Tribulation Beasts with over a hundred thousand Tribulations can leave their Foreign World and enter others. Once noticed by such a beast, even a First-Class Invincible has the possibility of falling.
Therefore.
Many Invincibles, despite their great strength, do not dare to hunt Tribulation Beasts in large numbers. Only some Invincibles who are proficient in clone abilities rely on clones to hunt them, as the resentment on the clone will not transfer to the main body. However, this requires sacrificing clones repeatedly, and the cost is too high. Those proficient in clone abilities do not hunt Tribulation Beasts frequently either; if they use too many clones, it becomes a losing venture.
However, Ye Tian did not need to worry about this problem.
Currently, what Ye Tian wanted most was to join a powerful organization. After some investigation, he learned that the eight Eternal-Name level powers almost never recruit outside Invincibles.
This is because six of the eight Eternal-Name level powers are race-based organizations, similar to the Human Race. Would the Human Race recruit experts from outside the race?
Although the other two Eternal-Name level powers do recruit outside Invincibles, their requirements are incredibly high, and they place immense importance on loyalty. One must swear an incredibly harsh Eternal Oath never to leave the Eternal-Name level power. Furthermore, they do not value ordinary Invincibles and only recruit those at the Fifth-Class Invincible level or higher.
Therefore, none of these eight Eternal-Name level powers were suitable for Ye Tian.
Consequently, Ye Tian lowered his sights and chose a Saint-Name level power.
Some Saint-Name level powers were also incredibly strong. Aside from lacking a Supreme One, they were not necessarily weaker than Eternal-Name level powers at the Invincible level.
After repeated investigations and screening, Ye Tian felt there was one Saint-Name level power he had a hope of joining.
This Saint-Name level power was the Tianfeng Sea. This organization was very powerful and incredibly ancient. Although it had no Supreme One, it possessed several First-Class Invincibles, and its reputation was very prominent in the Tianlin Realm.
Crucially, this power recruited outsiders and had few restrictions, so many Invincibles wanted to join the Tianfeng Sea.
However, joining the Tianfeng Sea was not easy. The entry threshold was being a Sixth-Class Invincible, and one must have passed six Physical Body Tribulations during the Physical Body Tribulation Realm; otherwise, they were ineligible to join.
Most Invincibles had originally broken through with five Physical Body Tribulations, and thus were ineligible to join the Tianfeng Sea.
Additionally, one needed to complete an entry mission for the Tianfeng Sea. Only after completing it could one become a member.
"I'll choose the Tianfeng Sea!"
Ye Tian decided.


Chapter 1538: Invincible Calamity Body Method, Ye Tian's Luck!

Chapter 1538: Invincible Calamity Body Method, Ye Tian's Luck!

The headquarters of Heavenly Wind Sea was not located in Absolute Martial City. As for its actual location, Ye Tian naturally couldn't find out, but Heavenly Wind Sea did have a branch in Absolute Martial City, along with quite a few businesses.
Therefore, Ye Tian headed directly to the Heavenly Wind Sea branch in Absolute Martial City.
Upon arriving at the Heavenly Wind Sea branch, Ye Tian directly stated his intention to join.
At this time, a sixth-grade Invincible from Heavenly Wind Sea received Ye Tian.
"You want to join our Heavenly Wind Sea?"
The sixth-grade Invincible, Mo Ji, looked at Ye Tian and asked.
"Yes!" Ye Tian nodded slightly.
Mo Ji said, "Follow me. We need to test what level of Flesh Calamity Realm you reached when you promoted to the Invincible level!"
Ye Tian followed Mo Ji to a testing area within the Heavenly Wind Sea branch.
Soon, they arrived before a massive stone mirror.
Mo Ji pointed at the stone mirror and said, "This is a high-grade Calamity Tool—the Cave Calamity Mirror. It can peer into how many Flesh Calamities an Invincible has passed. Of course, before the test, you need to pay 100 Source Rule Calamity Crystals. This is to prevent certain Invincibles who don't meet the requirements from intentionally coming to test and wasting our time. Once the test is complete, if you meet the requirements, the 100 Source Rule Calamity Crystals will be refunded to you!"
Ye Tian didn't find anything wrong with this, so he directly took out a hundred Source Rule Calamity Crystals and handed them to Mo Ji.
Subsequently, the test began.
Hum!!!
The Cave Calamity Mirror released a beam of light that enveloped Ye Tian, and soon, streaks of black light began to emerge.
One streak of black light represented one calamity!
Five streaks!
Six streaks!
Seven streaks!
When he saw the seven streaks of black light, Mo Ji was somewhat surprised: "This Invincible has quite good talent, a breakthrough from the Seven-Calamity Flesh Realm."
As for the Eight-Calamity Realm, he didn't dare to think about it, because those in the Eight-Calamity Flesh Realm were considered geniuses even in the Tianlin Realm. They would have been recruited by Saint-Name level powers back when they were still in the Supreme Flesh Calamity Realm; it was impossible for them to wait until they were Invincibles to join Heavenly Wind Sea.
But immediately after, the eighth streak of black light emerged.
Eight-Calamity Flesh Realm!
This time, Mo Ji's expression changed, filled with immense shock.
However, it hadn't ended yet.
The ninth streak of black light also appeared, and only then did the test conclude.
"Nine... Nine-Calamity Flesh Realm!"
Mo Ji's pupils shrank violently, utterly stunned.
It wasn't that he had never seen Nine-Calamity Flesh Realm monsters before, but every single one of them was an existence he looked up to. Even within Heavenly Wind Sea, Nine-Calamity Flesh Realm geniuses were not numerous!
Then, he realized that Heavenly Wind Sea had picked up a treasure.
Immediately, he notified the higher-ups of the Heavenly Wind Sea branch, lest this genius be snatched away by other powers.
The very second Mo Ji sent the notification, a figure appeared.
"Greetings, Lord Long He!"
Mo Ji bowed respectfully upon seeing the man in front of him.
Long He, the person in charge of the Heavenly Wind Sea branch in Absolute Martial City, was at the third-grade Invincible level, and his strength was incredibly formidable.
"Mo Ji, is it this person?"
Long He asked with some excitement.
"Yes, Lord Long He!" Mo Ji replied.
Long He stared at Ye Tian and said seriously, "Can you test one more time?"
Ye Tian guessed that his talent was too high and had caught the attention of the Heavenly Wind Sea higher-ups, which was a good thing.
Thus, Ye Tian replied, "I can!"
Subsequently, Ye Tian tested once more, and nine streaks of black light emerged in succession.
"It really is an Invincible promoted from the Nine-Calamity Flesh Realm!"
Long He said excitedly.
Immediately, he declared, "Congratulations, you can directly become a member of Heavenly Wind Sea!"
"Don't I need to complete an entry mission?" Ye Tian asked in confusion.
"No need!" Long He answered. "Those missions are prepared for ordinary Invincibles. For a genius like you, there's no need to complete those missions at all. Moreover, many missions are very time-consuming and even somewhat dangerous. It's just that there are too many Invincibles who want to join Heavenly Wind Sea. If we didn't have such restrictions, countless Invincibles without potential would join, and Heavenly Wind Sea would have to spend resources to nurture them, which simply isn't worth it."
Ye Tian nodded, finding this very logical.
A Saint-Name level power like Heavenly Wind Sea didn't need those ordinary sixth-grade Invincibles to increase its strength. Therefore, having a few more or a few less Invincibles was irrelevant to them.
What Heavenly Wind Sea needed were geniuses who could truly enhance their strength and prestige, or even bring benefits to the organization, rather than those who only took resources from it.
"Follow me!"
Long He said.
Afterward, he led Ye Tian to the internal area of the Heavenly Wind Sea branch.
There, he handled the procedures for Ye Tian to join Heavenly Wind Sea and prepared a Heavenly Wind Sea member badge.
The members of Heavenly Wind Sea were divided into five levels: Ordinary Member, Senior Member, Elite Member, Glory Member, and Supreme Member.
Most members were Ordinary Members, a few were Senior Members, and only those at the Elite level and above were considered part of the high-level management.
For example, Long He was one of the Elite Members.
And as soon as Ye Tian joined Heavenly Wind Sea, he was a Senior Member, which was preferential treatment for top-tier geniuses.
Of course, Ye Tian's status as a Senior Member still needed verification; he had to wait for the headquarters to send someone to investigate before it could be finalized.
Soon, several people arrived from the headquarters to conduct an assessment of Ye Tian.
The content of the assessment was simple, similar to the previous test.
· ········· Seeking Flowers··· ·····
Not long after, Ye Tian's status as a Senior Member was confirmed.
……
"Ye Tian, now that you are officially a Senior Member of Heavenly Wind Sea, you probably don't know much about us yet. Let me tell you about the situation of Heavenly Wind Sea."
Long He gave a general overview of Heavenly Wind Sea.
From its strength, occupied territories, to benefits and so on, he provided a detailed description of everything.
"Ye Tian, although you became a Senior Member as soon as you joined, if you want to be promoted in the future, you must complete various missions. Through these missions, you earn contribution points to advance step by step. Only by advancing can you gain access to more secret knowledge and exchange for rarer treasures—treasures that cannot be bought in the outside world," Long He said.
Ye Tian listened intently throughout, naturally gaining a deeper understanding of Heavenly Wind Sea.
... ...... .......
A few days later, a reward belonging to Ye Tian arrived. It was a reward that all top-tier geniuses received. Perhaps for those powerhouses, this reward wasn't worth much, but it was something Ye Tian desperately needed.
A mid-grade defensive Calamity Tool, a mid-grade saber-type Calamity Tool, a portion of Thirty-Calamity Blood, and a Calamity Body Token.
The Calamity Body Token was a token that could be used to exchange for an Invincible Calamity Body Method from Heavenly Wind Sea.
"Isn't the Invincible Calamity Body something one possesses after breaking through to the Invincible level? Why is there an Invincible Calamity Body Method?" Ye Tian was somewhat confused, so he asked Long He on the spot.
Long He replied, "Ye Tian, the Invincible Calamity Body after an Invincible's breakthrough is just an ordinary Invincible Calamity Body. No matter how powerful your previous body was or how terrifying the Ancestral Body you condensed, the essence of the Calamity Power you absorb is not much different from that of other Invincibles. Because your Invincible Calamity Body is essentially the same as others', just slightly stronger. However, there are higher-level Invincible Calamity Bodies that are distinct from the ordinary ones. For example, the Blood River Calamity Body that I cultivate has a physical limit three times that of an ordinary person of the same rank. Perhaps at the sixth-grade Invincible level, three times doesn't seem like much, but what if you reach the fifth-grade, fourth-grade, or even third-grade Invincible level?"
Long He didn't continue, but Ye Tian could already imagine it. An Invincible who cultivated a higher-level Invincible Calamity Body would easily crush ordinary Invincibles as their cultivation level increased.
Even if they were both third-grade Invincibles, Long He could definitely insta-kill those who only possessed an ordinary Invincible Calamity Body.
Therefore, for an Invincible, the quality of the Invincible Calamity Body was incredibly important.
At this moment, Ye Tian felt extremely lucky that he had joined Heavenly Wind Sea. Otherwise, if he had blindly cultivated and promoted to the fifth-grade Invincible realm with an ordinary Invincible Calamity Body, he would likely have been thrashed by the fifth-grade Invincibles of those Saint-Name level powers.


Chapter 1539: Ten Thousand Sources Returning to the Void, Top-grade Tribulation Stones!

Chapter 1539: Ten Thousand Sources Returning to the Void, Top-grade Tribulation Stones!

Ye Tian took his Tribulation Body Token to the resource exchange of the Tianfenghai branch. Here, as long as one had contribution points, any treasure could be exchanged.
Of course, senior members could only exchange for treasures available to their rank; certain items reserved for elite-level members and above were inaccessible to senior members.
The Tribulation Body Token, however, did not require any contribution points and could be used to exchange for any single Tribulation Body cultivation technique.
Ye Tian browsed through the various Tribulation Body cultivation techniques—
Rising Sun Tribulation Body!
Gold Spirit Tribulation Body!
Eternal Sun Tribulation Body!
Windfall Tribulation Body!
The catalog of techniques scrolled past as Ye Tian browsed. Most of the Tribulation Body techniques were quite average, but they had low cultivation difficulty, low risk, and required few resources, making them easy to master.
Conversely, those more formidable Tribulation Bodies were extremely difficult to start and even harder to improve. Even for monstrous geniuses, it was highly likely they wouldn't be able to perfectly cultivate the Tribulation Body to the completion stage, forcing them to promote prematurely, resulting in an incomplete Tribulation Body.
Therefore, the best Tribulation Body was the one that suited oneself; it wasn't necessarily the case that the more powerful it was, the better.
Ye Tian naturally understood this principle, but he would not choose an average Tribulation Body. Instead, he intended to select a powerful technique that was also suitable for him.
After a long time, Ye Tian finished browsing all the Tribulation Body techniques in Tianfenghai.
"I'll choose this one!"
Ye Tian's gaze fixed on the technique called the Ten Thousand Sources Returning to the Void Tribulation Body, and he immediately used his token to exchange for it.
When Ye Tian emerged after exchanging for the technique, Long He came over to inquire, "Ye Tian, which Tribulation Body technique did you choose?"
"Ten Thousand Sources Returning to the Void!"
Ye Tian replied truthfully.
"What? You actually chose that technique?" Long He was greatly shocked.
The Ten Thousand Sources Returning to the Void was known as one of the three great Tribulation Bodies of Tianfenghai. It seemed powerful, but the difficulty of cultivation was immense; even the descendants of first-class Invincibles might not dare to practice it.
The entry requirements for the Ten Thousand Sources Returning to the Void required proficiency in multiple paths of rules, the comprehension of rules from various foreign realms, and a vast amount of Tribulation Blood—and it couldn't be just one type, but blood from different foreign realms, as Tribulation Blood also contained the rules of its respective realm.
Most terrifyingly, the cultivation speed of the Ten Thousand Sources Returning to the Void was too slow, at most one-tenth the progress of other Tribulation Bodies, or even lower.
Furthermore, this technique would frequently hit bottlenecks and was prone to causing cultivation deviation, leading to the collapse of the physical body.
This was because the technique was somewhat incomplete, mainly because even its creator had never successfully cultivated it.
In reality, those top-tier Tribulation Body techniques all had some flaws to varying degrees because so few Invincibles practiced them, making it hard to perfect them. Moreover, every Invincible's body was different, so the flaws were naturally different as well.
Therefore, when practicing a top-tier Tribulation Body technique, one had to grope their way through and perfect it themselves.
But how many Invincibles could ultimately cultivate a top-tier technique to the completion stage?
"Yes, I've decided to practice the Ten Thousand Sources Returning to the Void!" Ye Tian said firmly.
Long He tried to persuade him, "Ye Tian, don't just look at how powerful this technique is. Do you understand the difficulty and the flaws? It's better to practice an average technique. It might not be as strong as a top-tier one, but it's safe, and there's plenty of experience to draw from so you won't go astray!"
Ye Tian shook his head and said, "Lord Long He, I've already made up my mind. Besides, I have confidence!"
Seeing this, Long He stopped trying to dissuade him.
As for Ye Tian saying he had confidence, he didn't believe it for a second.
Having joined Tianfenghai, Ye Tian not only became a senior member instantly but also received a manor as a residence. In Juewu City, the cost of obtaining a manor was not low; one couldn't buy one without a hundred thousand Source Rule Tribulation Crystals.
Subsequently, Ye Tian renamed the manor "Ye Residence" and began his cultivation there.
His purpose in coming here was to comprehend the rules of the Tianlin Realm to create an Invincible Ancestral Technique. Thus, there was no difference between his duplicate body and his main body; once the duplicate created an Invincible Ancestral Technique, it was as good as the main body creating it.
Then...
Ye Tian began to receive the inheritance of the Ten Thousand Sources Returning to the Void technique. It took a long time before the inheritance was finally complete.
Afterward...
Ye Tian's main body began practicing the Ten Thousand Sources Returning to the Void, but he immediately felt the difficulty of this technique.
He cultivated bitterly for an entire domain year, yet there was almost no progress.
"It seems I must use a large amount of Tribulation Blood to make rapid progress with the Ten Thousand Sources Returning to the Void!"
Ye Tian thought to himself.
Moreover, since the Ten Thousand Sources Returning to the Void was somewhat incomplete, for safety's sake, he had to let his duplicate body practice it first to perfect it step by step. Thus, the amount of Tribulation Blood needed would likely be even greater.
For an ordinary person, obtaining so much Tribulation Blood would be impossible.
But Ye Tian still had hope of acquiring a large amount.
However, using Tribulation Blood for cultivation wasn't actually the best way. Tribulation Blood was mild and expensive, but the tribulation power within wasn't particularly high. Many treasures contained more tribulation power than blood, but the power within them was incredibly chaotic and unsuitable for Invincibles to refine.
However, Ye Tian possessed the Eternal Talent: Tribulation and the Tribulation Transformation Secret Art, allowing him to refine even violent tribulation power.
Therefore, he planned to hunt Tribulation Beasts and exchange their blood for resources containing violent tribulation power. This was the most logical way to cultivate.
And Tianfenghai had such a resource: Top-grade Tribulation Stones.
The Tribulation Stones Ye Tian had traded for before were just ordinary low-grade stones. Above them were middle-grade, high-grade, and top-grade stones.
Among them, the tribulation power in a top-grade stone was even higher than that of thousand-tribulation blood, but the power inside was too chaotic for Invincibles to use. Thus, a top-grade stone was only worth about twenty-tribulation blood.
Consequently.
Ye Tian went to the Tianfenghai branch and exchanged the thirty-tribulation blood rewarded by Tianfenghai directly for top-grade stones, obtaining three of them.
To Ye Tian, these three top-grade stones were equivalent to three portions of thousand-year Tribulation Blood; their value was unimaginable.
Afterward.
Ye Tian's duplicate body used one top-grade stone to practice the Ten Thousand Sources Returning to the Void. If there were any flaws or problems, he could perfect them in time without affecting his main body.
In this way, Ye Tian began his formal cultivation of the Ten Thousand Sources Returning to the Void.


Chapter 1540: First Stage Middle Phase, Strength Skyrockets!

Chapter 1540: First Stage Middle Phase, Strength Skyrockets!

"The effect of the top-grade tribulation stone is simply too good!"
Ye Tian was quite excited.
He activated the Tribulation Transformation Secret Technique, and with the assistance of his Eternal Talent: Tribulation, an endless supply of tribulation force surged out from within the top-grade tribulation stone. It was many times more powerful than the thirty-seven tribulation blood.
Of course, Ye Tian was not using the top-grade tribulation stone to increase his cultivation level right now, but rather to cultivate the "Myriad Origins Returning to the Void," an invincible tribulation body technique.
At this moment, Ye Tian's invincible tribulation body seemed to be constantly compressing and condensing under the effect of the Myriad Origins Returning to the Void, making his physical body even stronger.
As time passed, Ye Tian gradually reached the entry level of the Myriad Origins Returning to the Void, and his progress became faster and faster, but he soon ran into trouble.
*Crack!*
Ye Tian's physical body split open during one cultivation session, and his entire physical form began to become unstable.
However, Ye Tian quickly recovered, though this cultivation session had caused a bit of damage to his invincible tribulation body.
"As expected, danger has appeared, and it has even brought some difficult-to-remove hidden consequences to the physical body. But compared to the gains, these consequences are nothing," Ye Tian thought to himself.
Of course, he was using a duplicate body to cultivate the Myriad Origins Returning to the Void, so it had no impact on his main body.
Subsequently, Ye Tian began to refine the Myriad Origins Returning to the Void to make it more compatible with his own invincible tribulation body.
After many attempts, Ye Tian finally managed to slightly improve the Myriad Origins Returning to the Void, ensuring that it would not cause hidden flaws or damage to his invincible tribulation body at the start.
Afterward, the duplicate body continued to cultivate the Myriad Origins Returning to the Void. Whenever he discovered a problem, he would begin to research it. He didn't care about the foundation of the duplicate body, treating it entirely as an experimental subject.
Regardless, the Myriad Origins Returning to the Void was still a terrifyingly powerful invincible tribulation body technique. It wouldn't affect Ye Tian's future breakthroughs; it was just that the hidden consequences it caused would require a long time to repair, and it might have some impact on his attempt to become a Supreme One.
However, not a single Invincible One in the Heavenly Wind Sea had been able to promote to a Supreme One, and the same was true for the entire Tianlin Realm, so no one worried about that point.
If Ye Tian didn't have his duplicate bodies, he wouldn't have dared to cultivate such a top-tier tribulation body technique.
After one domain year had passed, Ye Tian finally finished refining one top-grade tribulation stone. The duplicate body's invincible tribulation body was much stronger than before, having already reached the First Stage Middle Phase.
Whether it was the Myriad Origins Returning to the Void or other invincible tribulation bodies, they were all divided into six stages, which corresponded exactly to the six ranks of Invincible Ones.
If a sixth-rank Invincible One could cultivate their invincible tribulation body to the First Stage Circle, they could promote in a perfected state.
However, very few Invincible Ones could cultivate their invincible tribulation body to the Circle level because it consumed too many resources, and the difficulty increased the further one went.
The top-tier Myriad Origins Returning to the Void was the same; it was almost impossible to cultivate to the Circle stage, but the impact wasn't great. Even if one only cultivated it to the later stages, it could easily crush an ordinary invincible tribulation body at the Circle stage.
...
"It's about time to head back once. I have two top-grade tribulation stones left, and during this time the duplicate body cultivated the Myriad Origins Returning to the Void, it went through thirty-three points of incompatibility, three major dangers, and the rest were minor dangers, but they have all been refined one by one. Before the main body cultivates the Myriad Origins Returning to the Void to the First Stage Middle Phase, there's almost no need to worry about flaws in the invincible tribulation body," Ye Tian thought.
Subsequently.
He left the Tianlin Realm.
The Heavenly Wind Sea also knew that Ye Tian was a person from the exotic worlds outside the Tianlin Realm, so they weren't surprised by his departure at all.
Moreover, the Heavenly Wind Sea was very powerful and had branches outside the Tianlin Realm. These branches were established in exotic worlds. Ye Tian could enter those branches to exchange for resources, though those branches could only exchange for very ordinary resources; many rare resources were unavailable for exchange.
This was because the exotic worlds were very dangerous. If too many resources were placed in a branch and it was raided by other forces, the loss would be too great.
Furthermore, it was quite troublesome for the Heavenly Wind Sea to send reinforcements to the exotic worlds.
Not long after.
Ye Tian's duplicate body returned to the Dark Forbidden Zone and handed the tribulation artifacts and top-grade tribulation stones to his main body.
Then, Ye Tian's main body officially began to cultivate the initially refined Myriad Origins Returning to the Void.
In the blink of an eye, another domain year passed.
By this time, Ye Tian had consumed one top-grade tribulation stone and cultivated the Myriad Origins Returning to the Void to the First Stage Middle Phase. His invincible tribulation body had become incredibly powerful.
With his current combat strength, he was already comparable to an ordinary fifth-rank Invincible One.
This was the power of a top-tier invincible tribulation body; it allowed one to fight above their level, even though he still technically belonged to the sixth-rank Invincible Ones because he had not yet comprehended an Invincible Ancestral Technique.
Ye Tian was in no hurry to comprehend an Invincible Ancestral Technique and would not even attempt to perceive one. His invincible tribulation body had not yet reached the First Stage Circle stage; if he accidentally comprehended an Invincible Ancestral Technique now, that would be a bad thing!
Now, Ye Tian only had one top-grade tribulation stone left. If he wanted to exchange for more top-grade tribulation stones from the Heavenly Wind Sea, he had to prepare a large amount of tribulation blood to convert into contribution points.
Thus, Ye Tian had his duplicate body begin searching for tribulation beasts.
After many attempts, including some failures that led to the death of the duplicate body, Ye Tian eventually found a sixty-tribulation beast.
A sixty-tribulation beast was equivalent to a weaker fifth-rank Invincible One. With Ye Tian's current strength, he would have to pay a heavy price to kill it.
But Ye Tian didn't care.
He sent his duplicate body to attack this sixty-tribulation beast. After fighting for hundreds of millions of years, he finally killed the beast at the cost of the duplicate body being heavily injured and on the verge of death, but the harvest was immense.
Sixteen portions of tribulation blood, two hundred thousand Origin Rule tribulation crystals, and fifteen tribulation bones.
Sixteen portions of sixty-tribulation blood plus fifteen sixty-tribulation bones—how many contribution points would these treasures be worth if exchanged at the Heavenly Wind Sea!
On this day.
Ye Tian condensed a new duplicate body and brought these treasures to a branch of the Heavenly Wind Sea in an exotic world—the Yueyang Branch.
The Yueyang Branch was located in the Yueyang World. The master of this world was a fourth-rank Invincible One and an elite member of the Heavenly Wind Sea.
At the same time, thirty-three Invincible Ones were permanently stationed in this exotic world, and no other forces were allowed to open branches here. Only Invincible Ones from the Heavenly Wind Sea were allowed to enter and exit this exotic world freely.
*Boom!!!!*
Ye Tian tore through the barrier of the Yueyang World and arrived. After showing his badge, he faced no obstruction.
In the central void of the Yueyang World, a massive building stood tall.
This was the Yueyang Branch of the Heavenly Wind Sea.
Ye Tian walked in and met one of the people in charge of the Yueyang Branch—Qi Yang. He was also a fifth-rank Invincible One and a high-level member.
The Heavenly Wind Sea had long-term missions to collect tribulation blood and tribulation bones, and there were also options to exchange for them.
However, the price for selling to the Heavenly Wind Sea was definitely lower than the price for buying; otherwise, wouldn't the Heavenly Wind Sea lose money?
For example, if one wanted to exchange for a portion of tribulation blood, it would cost 1,000 contribution points, but if one wanted to sell it, they would only receive 960 contribution points.
Ye Tian didn't care about this; otherwise, if he really wanted to trade tribulation blood for top-grade tribulation stones, he would have nowhere else to go.
"I want to accept the tribulation blood and tribulation bone missions!"
Ye Tian said.
Qi Yang nodded and processed the mission for Ye Tian. Ye Tian immediately submitted the mission, handing over the tribulation blood and bones he had obtained.
"This is sixty-tribulation blood and bones!!!"
Qi Yang exclaimed in shock.


Chapter 1541: The First Stage of the Invincible Calamity Body Reaches Perfection!

Chapter 1541: The First Stage of the Invincible Calamity Body Reaches Perfection!

A 60-Calamity beast was nothing special; Qi Yang could easily slay one.
However, finding a 60-Calamity beast was no easy task.
Even with the strength of a top-tier fifth-rank Invincible, he wouldn't dare go looking for Calamity Beasts recklessly, or he would have been dead long ago.
Yet, Ye Tian had handed over so much 60-Calamity blood and bone, clearly indicating he had slain a 60-Calamity beast.
Although Qi Yang was shocked by Ye Tian's harvest, he didn't ask any questions. After all, how Ye Tian managed to kill a 60-Calamity beast was his own business. Since he wasn't close to Ye Tian, he naturally wouldn't pry.
Afterward, he processed the task submission for Ye Tian.
Sixteen portions of 60-Calamity blood plus fifteen 60-Calamity bones earned Ye Tian a total of 30,000 contribution points. This was a significant amount, considering a single top-grade Calamity Stone only cost fifty contribution points.
One could imagine how exaggerated a value 30,000 contribution points was.
Originally, Ye Tian only had a bit over a hundred contribution points, which he had earned by turning in a single portion of Calamity blood. Now, with 30,000 points added all at once, it was enough to exchange for a vast amount of good items.
In reality, if other members of the Tianfeng Sea obtained Calamity blood or bones, they would rarely turn them in for contribution points. They would use the blood and bones that were useful to them and give those that weren't to their descendants.
A sixth-rank Invincible like Ye Tian, who turned in all of his 60-Calamity blood and bones, was absolutely rare.
"I want to exchange for top-grade Calamity Stones. Are there any here?"
Ye Tian asked.
Qi Yang checked and said, "There are top-grade Calamity Stones, but only six!"
"I'll take them all!" Ye Tian said.
One top-grade Calamity Stone cost 50 contribution points, so six only cost 300 points.
In truth, these six top-grade Calamity Stones were far more helpful to Ye Tian than the 60-Calamity blood, but because others couldn't utilize top-grade Calamity Stones, they were almost entirely ignored.
After obtaining the six top-grade Calamity Stones, Ye Tian left and returned to the Dark Forbidden Domain.
In the days that followed, Ye Tian's duplicate body used the top-grade Calamity Stones to cultivate the Myriad Origins Returning to the Void, gradually perfecting the technique and making this Invincible Calamity Body method perfectly compatible with himself.
On the other hand, he would occasionally send his duplicate body to hunt suitable Calamity Beasts.
Time flew by, and one Dark Era passed.
During this Dark Era, Ye Tian hunted a total of six Calamity Beasts, yielding a great harvest. He also traveled to the Tianlin Realm again and exchanged for several hundred top-grade Calamity Stones from the Tianfeng Sea.
At Ye Tian's request, these Calamity Stones came from different foreign realms, thus containing the rules of various foreign worlds, which met the requirements for cultivating the Myriad Origins Returning to the Void.
After all, the Myriad Origins Returning to the Void required the rules of different foreign realms to temper the Invincible Calamity Body for it to progress.
Different Calamity Stones possessed different properties, allowing them to serve as substitutes for Calamity blood.
Through these hundreds of top-grade Calamity Stones, combined with his duplicate body, Ye Tian perfected the first stage of the Myriad Origins Returning to the Void Invincible Calamity Body technique.
If it were anyone else, they would have had no way to perfect this Invincible Calamity Body method.
It was also fortunate that Ye Tian possessed the Calamity Transformation Secret Technique and the Eternal Talent: Calamity. Otherwise, if he had to rely solely on absorbing and refining Calamity blood, he would likely have needed a massive amount of it to reach this step.
It had to be said that cultivating a top-tier Invincible Calamity Body required far too many resources. Moreover, since he had to repair the flaws of the Myriad Origins Returning to the Void, his resource consumption was several times, if not ten times, higher.
One by one, the top-grade Calamity Stones were consumed and refined by Ye Tian. Finally, on this day, Ye Tian's main body successfully cultivated the Myriad Origins Returning to the Void to the perfection of the first stage. Furthermore, it was a perfect first-stage completion without any flaws.
While ordinary Invincible Calamity Body methods only made a sixth-rank Invincible three times stronger than one who hadn't cultivated such a body, the top-tier Myriad Origins Returning to the Void made him nine times stronger.
More importantly, Ye Tian had laid a supreme foundation.
Once Ye Tian stepped into the fifth-rank Invincible realm and cultivated the Myriad Origins Returning to the Void to the perfection of the second stage, which would also be a nine-fold increase, the stacking effect might not reach eighty-one times, but it would at least reach forty to fifty times.
An Invincible Calamity Body forty to fifty times stronger—what kind of concept was that? He could easily insta-kill ordinary Invincibles of the same rank.
However, top-tier Invincible Calamity Bodies had flaws. If others couldn't resolve them, it was difficult to reach the perfection of the first stage. By the later stages, they might reach the minor success of the third stage and then be unable to progress further.
At that point, if each stage was only at minor success or entry-level, it would only be slightly stronger than an ordinary Invincible Calamity Body method, which wasn't very useful.
But Ye Tian could perfect the top-tier Invincible Calamity Body, reaching perfection at every stage. Once stacked to the first-rank Invincible realm, his strength would likely allow him to insta-kill those first-rank Invincibles, truly becoming invincible among Invincibles, and perhaps even fighting against Supremes.
...
"The Invincible Calamity Body has reached the perfection of the first stage. My current combat power has actually surpassed many fifth-rank Invincibles. It's time to try and create an Invincible Ancestral Skill!"
Ye Tian thought to himself.
Subsequently.
Ye Tian spent a few contribution points to exchange for a secret manual on comprehending Invincible Skills from the Tianfeng Sea. This information was very comprehensive and would save Ye Tian from taking many detours.
Whether it was a sixth-rank Invincible from a foreign realm or the Eternal Realm of Tianlin, if they wanted to advance to the fifth-rank Invincible realm, they had to comprehend an Invincible Skill, such as an Invincible Ancestral Skill or an Invincible Battle Skill. The names varied, but the essence was the same.
An Invincible Skill was an application of the Eternal Realm's rules—a higher level of rule that stood above ordinary foreign realm rules.
Under normal circumstances, it was nearly impossible for a sixth-rank Invincible to comprehend an Invincible Skill.
Because of this, countless sixth-rank Invincibles were stuck at this level, unable to advance to the fifth-rank Invincible realm.
There were three common ways for a sixth-rank Invincible to advance to the fifth rank. The first was through long periods of meditation while staying in the Eternal Realm. As long as one had potential, they would eventually comprehend the rules of the Eternal Realm and create an Invincible Skill.
The second way was through Rule Heavenly Objects born from the Eternal Realm. By using these to comprehend the rules of the Eternal Realm and create an Invincible Skill, the speed of comprehension was very fast. As long as one's talent wasn't poor, they could almost certainly create an Invincible Skill.
However, Rule Heavenly Objects were too precious. Ordinary Invincibles simply couldn't obtain them. Only powerful Saint-Name level organizations possessed Rule Heavenly Objects, and often more than one.
The third way was to refine an Eternal Rule Pill. These were created by Supremes or a few first-rank Invincibles through alchemy, using countless rare and precious materials to melt the rules of the Eternal Realm and forcibly integrate a wisp of those rules into a pill. After refining an Eternal Rule Pill, one could master that specific Eternal Realm rule and gradually create an Invincible Skill.
This third method was the most common in the Tianlin Realm. Countless sixth-rank Invincibles sought an Eternal Rule Pill, accumulating resources for ages just to buy one.
Measuring the value of an Eternal Rule Pill in Origin Rule Calamity Crystals, it was worth a full 10 million crystals, which was not something an ordinary Invincible could produce.
However, Ye Tian would not choose the third method. While it could lead to the fifth-rank Invincible realm, future progress would be difficult, making it far inferior to the second method.
In the past, Ye Tian naturally had no way to use the second method to advance, but now that he had joined the Tianfeng Sea, and the Tianfeng Sea possessed Rule Heavenly Objects, he only needed to pay a certain amount of contribution points to meditate on them.
This was also one of the reasons why countless Invincibles wanted to join Saint-Name level organizations.


Chapter 1542: Nine Yang Fish, Three Eternal Rules!

Chapter 1542: Nine Yang Fish, Three Eternal Rules!

"Since I've joined the Tianfeng Sea, I naturally intend to use their Rule Heavenly Objects to comprehend the rules of the Eternal Heaven and Earth. It would be foolish not to take advantage of such conditions, wouldn't it?"
Ye Tian said with a smile.
Therefore, he would not choose to rely on endless years to slowly comprehend them; that was merely a desperate measure taken by ordinary Invincibles.
Of course, even as a high-level member of the Tianfeng Sea with the qualifications to comprehend their Rule Heavenly Objects, the required contribution points were not small.
Even for the most ordinary Rule Heavenly Object, comprehending it for one Realm Year required one contribution point. One Realm Epoch was equivalent to 120,000 contribution points, and comprehending for one Dark Era would require over 10 million points.
Thus, wanting to comprehend a Rule Heavenly Object for a long period was a luxury; many Invincibles simply did not have that many contribution points.
Ye Tian's accumulated contribution points had reached several hundred thousand, and he had hardly spent any of his current points. After all, purchasing several hundred Extreme Grade Tribulation Stones didn't cost much—only a few tens of thousands of points.
Additionally, he had purchased some other treasures for his family, such as exchanging for Emperor Blood Souls and other items, which cost a bit more.
But now, he still had 260,000 contribution points remaining.
This amount was enough for him to comprehend for a long time, perhaps even enough to grasp an Eternal Heaven and Earth Rule in one go, thereby creating an Invincible Ancestral Technique and stepping into the rank of a Fifth-tier Invincible.
-------------380-
Tianlin Realm.
Ye Tian's duplicated body arrived here once again and proceeded to the headquarters of the Tianfeng Sea—Wufeng Mountain.
Of course, given Ye Tian's status, he could only enter the outer perimeter of Wufeng Mountain. To enter the inner perimeter, one needed at least the status of an Elite member.
At this time, Ye Tian arrived at Nine Yang Mountain within Wufeng Mountain, where there was a Rule Heavenly Object known as the Nine Yang Fish.
The Nine Yang Fish contained three Eternal Heaven and Earth Rules: Power, Defense, and Speed. These were the most fundamental yet most important rules. Consequently, many Invincibles came to comprehend this specific Rule Heavenly Object, and it was also the most suitable for Ye Tian.
The cost to comprehend the Nine Yang Fish was higher than that of ordinary Rule Heavenly Objects; one Realm Year cost three contribution points.
On Nine Yang Mountain.
Ye Tian stood before a Third-order Gate. After showing his badge to the Invincible guarding the area, he was allowed to enter.
Strictly speaking, the Nine Yang Fish was not on Nine Yang Mountain itself, but in a special space-time opposite it. One had to pass through the Third-order Gate to travel to that space-time to comprehend the Nine Yang Fish; otherwise, it was impossible to enter.
The Tianfeng Sea placed great importance on every Rule Heavenly Object. For instance, near the Third-order Gate, Ye Tian sensed many Invincibles, several of whom possessed auras far beyond his imagination—they could definitely kill him in an instant.
*Whoosh!*
Ye Tian passed through the Third-order Gate and arrived in a special space-time.
Here, numerous lotus platforms floated in the void. Some platforms were already occupied by Invincibles sitting cross-legged, comprehending the Eternal Rules.
In the center of this space-time, a massive black fish spanning hundreds of millions of miles was writhing, but its body was bound by chains, preventing it from leaving.
"This is the Nine Yang Fish?"
Ye Tian was surprised.
From its appearance, this Rule Heavenly Object did not seem like a dead object, but rather a true living being.
However, Ye Tian used his Copy Talent to investigate and found no talents at all, proving that this giant black fish was not a living creature.
In reality, when most Rule Heavenly Objects have existed for a long time, their rules manifest into forms, often taking the shape of living creatures. However, they remain Rule Heavenly Objects—treasures, not lifeforms.
The Nine Yang Fish was sealed. It was impossible to comprehend the Eternal Rules it carried from elsewhere; one had to sit on a lotus platform and establish a connection with the Nine Yang Fish through the platform to comprehend the rules on its body.
Ye Tian chose an empty lotus platform, sat down, and immediately extended his consciousness through the platform to the Nine Yang Fish.
*Boom!!!*
Ye Tian's consciousness observed the entire Nine Yang Fish. In his perception, the fish was like the incarnation of rules—Eternal Rules that far surpassed the rules of the Alien Realms. The so-called "Great Daos" of the Alien Realms were like child's play here, not even comparing to a single shred of these rules.
Power, Speed, Defense.
As Ye Tian perceived these three Eternal Rules, he truly felt the vastness of the Eternal Rules.
Between the three, Ye Tian unhesitatingly chose the Power Rule first. Speed and Defense could increase combat power to an extent, but they were more for survival. Ye Tian didn't need to worry about survival as much; he usually fought with his duplicated bodies. Even if a duplicated body perished, it wouldn't have much impact. Therefore, Power was more beneficial to him.
If he could comprehend the Eternal Power Rule, he could attempt to create a Power-type Invincible Ancestral Technique, which would significantly boost his combat strength.
In the days that followed, Ye Tian began to comprehend the Eternal Power Rule.
Compared to other Invincibles, Ye Tian's advantage wasn't particularly large. Although he possessed the Ultimate Power Ancestral Talent, it didn't help much with comprehending the Eternal Power Rule unless he could obtain an Eternal Power Talent, which would allow him to grasp it quickly.
"Perhaps I really do have a chance to obtain the Eternal Power Talent!"
Ye Tian thought to himself.
There might not be anyone with an Eternal Power Talent in the Tianlin Realm, but there were certainly Invincibles with the Ultimate Power Ancestral Talent. Although they were extremely rare, if he spent enough time searching, he could definitely find many of them.
If he copied and merged a large number of Ultimate Power Ancestral Talents, he might be able to fuse them into an Eternal Power Talent.
"I'll try comprehending here first and see the results!"
Ye Tian thought.
Years passed, and Ye Tian, like the other Invincibles, continued to comprehend the Eternal Rules, but his progress was not fast.
However, this was quite normal. Even with Rule Heavenly Objects, the Invincibles of the Tianfeng Sea still needed a long time to promote to Fifth-tier Invincibles. Many even spent vast amounts of time completing missions just to accumulate contribution points.
For an Invincible, let alone one or two Dark Eras, even the span of a Great Calamity Epoch was considered a very short time. To an Invincible, only a Kalpa Era was considered a relatively long period.
Later, he conversed with other Invincibles of the Tianfeng Sea and gained a general understanding of how long it took them to comprehend Eternal Rules.
Generally, even if an Invincible comprehended Rule Heavenly Objects continuously, it would take at least three Dark Eras. Those with exceptionally high comprehension still needed one Dark Era. After all, since they had all reached the rank of Invincible, the gap in their natural comprehension wasn't that massive.
But to comprehend continuously for three Dark Eras, how many contribution points would that require? Very few Invincibles possessed that many points.
Consequently, these Invincibles relied on accumulating points over long periods. Once they gathered some, they would come to comprehend for a while.
Thus, many Invincibles in the Tianfeng Sea practiced for thousands or even tens of thousands of Kalpa Eras before breaking through to the Fifth-tier Invincible realm.
"If I were to comprehend for an entire Dark Era, based on the cost of the Nine Yang Fish, I would need at least 30 million contribution points. I only have 260,000. It seems I was overthinking; a mere 260,000 points won't help me comprehend the Eternal Rules in one go," Ye Tian thought.
Of course.
He could go out and hunt Tribulation Beasts repeatedly to earn massive amounts of contribution points before returning to the Nine Yang Fish, but finding Tribulation Beasts also took time.
Alternatively, he could take on missions that offered large amounts of points at once, but those weren't missions he could complete alone. Unless he had someone in the Tianfeng Sea to carry him, he couldn't earn enough points that way, and it wouldn't necessarily be faster than hunting Tribulation Beasts himself.
"It's more reliable to try merging a large number of Ultimate Power Ancestral Talents into an Eternal Power Talent!"
Ye Tian thought.


Chapter 1543: Multiple Eternal-level Talents!

Chapter 1543: Multiple Eternal-level Talents!

In the Tianfeng Sea, there were some Invincibles who possessed Ultimate Power Ancestral Talents. Once Ye Tian detected them with his copying talent, he immediately copied the Ultimate Power Ancestral Talents of these Invincibles.
Of course, if there were other Ultimate Ancestral Talents, he would copy them all together as well.
Afterward, Ye Tian left the Tianfeng Sea headquarters at Wufeng Mountain and wandered through various regions of the Tianlin Realm. Any region where cultivation flourished was visited by him.
Countless giant cities similar to Juwu City, various trading markets, and gathering points—Ye Tian constantly traveled to places where Invincibles gathered. Although the harvest each time was small and it was nearly impossible to find practitioners with the Ultimate Power Ancestral Talent,
encountering one occasionally was already very good.
As time slowly passed, the Ultimate Power Ancestral Talents Ye Tian copied grew in number, and other types of Ultimate Ancestral Talents became quite numerous as well.
Finally, after the span of one Domain Era, Ye Tian had copied enough Ultimate Power Ancestral Talents and other Ultimate Ancestral Talents to begin fusing them.
Fusing Ultimate Ancestral Talents was extremely painful and the speed was very slow, somewhat like when he had first obtained the copying talent.
But Ye Tian was very excited, because with every additional Eternal talent, his potential and foundation received a massive boost.
For example, when he previously obtained the Eternal Talent "Calamity" from the Calamity Beast, he had instantly surpassed other geniuses by a wide margin. Even among Invincibles, he was considered an extraordinary monster.
If he didn't have an Eternal talent, he wouldn't have much of an advantage after breaking through to the Invincible level.
One could imagine what an Eternal talent meant to an Invincible; it was a symbol of invincibility.
In the vast Tianlin Realm, he had yet to see a single practitioner who possessed an Eternal talent. Perhaps there were none, or they were so rare that there were only a handful, and they weren't people he could easily meet.
Regardless, Ye Tian was about to possess multiple Eternal talents.
After a long period of time, Ye Tian fused a large number of Ultimate Power Ancestral Talents, finally ushering in the ultimate qualitative change.
BOOM!!!!
The Eternal Power Talent, or rather, the Eternal Ancestral Talent: Power, was born!
[Eternal Ancestral Talent: Power]
Seeing this talent, Ye Tian was incredibly excited.
An Eternal Ancestral-level talent was very close to the limit of the copying talent. At the Invincible level, a talent of this caliber was of immense help to him. It was an Eternal-level talent, and since the Eternal level was even linked to the Eternal Heaven and Earth, it might very well be the highest grade of talent.
Subsequently, Ye Tian activated this Eternal Power Talent, and his overall strength surged violently, comparable to the effect of performing a supreme ancestral technique. And this was just the effect of activating the talent itself.
"With the Eternal Ancestral Talent: Power, I should be able to create an Invincible Ancestral Technique very soon!" Ye Tian thought to himself.
He did not immediately head to the Tianfeng Sea to meditate on the Nine Yang Fish. Instead, he continued to fuse other Ultimate Ancestral Talents. After all, he had copied so many this time, including Ultimate Defense Ancestral Talents, Ultimate Speed Ancestral Talents, and Ultimate Five Elements Ancestral Talents.
Therefore, he could still obtain several more Eternal-level talents.
Fuse!
Fuse!
Fuse!
Ye Tian continued to fuse. Although he had no time to cultivate and spent it all on fusion, he was extremely happy with every successful fusion.
After a long time had passed, one Eternal-level talent after another was born.
[Eternal Ancestral Talent: Speed]
[Eternal Ancestral Talent: Defense]
[Eternal Ancestral Talent: Gold]
[Eternal Ancestral Talent: Fire]
...
With the birth of each Eternal-level talent, Ye Tian truly transformed into a supreme genius who stood above any other genius in the Tianlin Realm.
Of course, if he wanted to fully grow into his potential, he still needed a very long time.
After all, talent was just talent; it didn't represent his current realm or strength, only his potential.
One day.
Ye Tian once again arrived at the Nine Yang Fish cultivation and meditation space on Nine Yang Mountain in Wufeng Mountain, Tianfeng Sea.
Here, Ye Tian sat cross-legged on a lotus platform, once again meditating on the Eternal Power Rules on the body of the Nine Yang Fish.
In the past, meditating on the Eternal Power Rules felt as if there were an endless barrier and a rejection from the rules themselves. It wasn't just him; everyone else felt the same.
But now, Ye Tian possessed the Eternal Ancestral Talent: Power. The Eternal Power Rules no longer rejected him; instead, they were perfectly compatible with each other, allowing him to meditate on them freely.
Furthermore, the Eternal Ancestral Talent: Power gave Ye Tian an incredible boost in his comprehension of the Eternal Power Rules. In a short amount of time, Ye Tian's gains surpassed what he had achieved over a long period in the past.
"Such a fast comprehension speed! At this rate, I'm afraid it won't be long before I can grasp the Eternal Power Rules and attempt to create an Invincible Ancestral Technique!"
·········Seeking Flowers·········
Ye Tian thought to himself.
Of course, attempting to create an Invincible Ancestral Technique immediately after grasping the Eternal Rules was not necessarily a good thing. If the created technique was too weak, the boost in strength wouldn't be very significant.
Therefore, many geniuses would choose to spend more time meditating to grasp more of the Eternal Power Rules. That way, the Invincible technique they created would be incredibly powerful.
Invincible techniques created by ordinary Invincibles were classified as Common Invincible Techniques. Naturally, those above Common Invincible Techniques were Top-tier Invincible Techniques. There were only these two classifications.
What Ye Tian wanted to create was a Top-tier Invincible Technique; that was his pursuit.
... ........ 0
Time slowly passed, and in the blink of an eye, one Domain Year had gone by.
Such a short amount of time for other Invincibles was probably just the length of a nap. If it were before, Ye Tian definitely wouldn't have made much progress.
However, now, he actually—
"I've grasped it!!!!"
Ye Tian was also somewhat surprised, even shocked.
One Domain Year! How much time had passed? He had only spent a tiny bit of contribution points, and he had actually grasped the Eternal Power Rules!
Other Invincibles who meditated on the Nine Yang Fish would probably need tens of millions of contribution points to have a hope of grasping the Eternal Rules!
This comprehension speed had simply increased by countless times!
Having grasped a trace of the Eternal Power Rules, Ye Tian did not leave, nor did he attempt to create an Invincible Ancestral Technique. Instead, he continued his meditation.
He still had over 200,000 contribution points, so he was in no hurry. He planned to squander all 200,000 points here. This way, his mastery of the Eternal Power Rules would be very high, and when he went to create an Invincible Ancestral Technique, it would surely be the most top-tier one.
Time flew by, and in the blink of an eye, one Domain Era passed.
By this time, Ye Tian had consumed 120,000 contribution points, and his control over the Eternal Power Rules was many times greater than before—the difference was like a drop of water compared to a river.
"This should be enough. My realm is too low; continuing to meditate on the Eternal Power Rules will become quite difficult. It's time to create an Invincible Ancestral Technique and promote myself to the Fifth-tier Invincible Ancestral Realm!"
Ye Tian thought to himself.


Chapter 1544: Breakthrough, Becoming a Fifth-Tier Invincible Ancestor!

Chapter 1544: Breakthrough, Becoming a Fifth-Tier Invincible Ancestor!

Juewu City.
Ye Tian began his secluded cultivation in his manor, starting to create an Invincible Ancestral Technique.
Of course, an Invincible Ancestral Technique was not created out of thin air; there had to be a direction.
Ye Tian planned to create a top-tier Invincible Ancestral Technique based on his Supreme Ancestral Techniques combined with the Power Eternal Rule. For instance, he looked to techniques like the Overpowering Strength Supreme Ancestral Technique and the Extreme Arm Supreme Ancestral Technique, which involved the aspect of power.
By drawing on the strengths of these Supreme Ancestral Techniques and incorporating his insights into the application of the Power Eternal Rule, he would eventually forge them into an Invincible Ancestral Technique.
Comprehending an Eternal Rule was a difficult task, but the process from comprehending the rule to creating an Invincible Ancestral Technique also required a significant amount of time, though success was ultimately guaranteed.
With Ye Tian's comprehension, his level of insight into the Power Eternal Rule, and his possession of the Power Eternal Ancestral Talent, creating an Invincible Ancestral Technique naturally wouldn't take too long.
In the blink of an eye, ten domain eras passed.
On this day.
Ye Tian finally succeeded in creating an Invincible Ancestral Technique, and it was one that far surpassed those of ordinary fifth-tier Invincible Ones. After all, he had seen the Invincible Ancestral Techniques of the Invincible Ones from the Heavenly Wind Sea, and they were far inferior to the one he had created.
Ye Tian named this Invincible Ancestral Technique the Heavenly Limit Combat Technique. It was an extreme development of power that utilized the Power Eternal Rule; without a sufficiently high level of insight into the Power Eternal Rule, one simply could not perform this technique.
Once the Heavenly Limit Combat Technique was unleashed, physical strength would surge many times over, and the entire body would become like a weapon of slaughter, crushing everything in its path.
The moment he mastered the Heavenly Limit Combat Technique, Ye Tian had a moment of clarity. He could break through at any time with the help of this technique, but he could only allow either his main body or his duplicated body to break through; he could not have both break through simultaneously. This was a restriction of the rules.
Consequently.
Ye Tian allowed his main body to undergo the breakthrough.
Boom!!!!
Under the influence of the Heavenly Limit Combat Technique, his main body began to transform. This was equivalent to merging with the Invincible Ancestral Technique, causing his physical body to undergo a qualitative change.
Suddenly, under the influence of a mysterious power, countless strands of source power descended from the Source Sea into the Dark Forbidden Domain, surging into Ye Tian's body to help him complete his transformation.
The source power of the Source Sea was almost impossible to refine, but at this moment, under that mysterious influence, it turned into source power that was very easy to refine. This was the benefit brought by a breakthrough in realm.
Breaking through from a sixth-tier Invincible One to a fifth-tier Invincible One brought a massive increase due to the qualitative change. Furthermore, Ye Tian practiced the top-tier Invincible Calamity Body technique, Ten Thousand Origins Returning to the Void, and had reached the first layer of the Perfect Calamity Body at the Great Circle stage. Combined with the fact that the Invincible Ancestral Technique he created was a top-tier one.
Thus, with this breakthrough, Ye Tian's strength underwent an earth-shaking change.
After a long time, Ye Tian finally completed his breakthrough and officially stepped into the realm of a Fifth-Tier Invincible Ancestor.
"My current strength far exceeds that of an ordinary Fifth-Tier Invincible Ancestor. It is said that the mysterious leaders of the Calamity Black Mountain and the Firmament Sword Tomb are fifth-tier Invincible Ones, but if I wanted to kill them, I could probably crush them with a casual wave of my hand!" Ye Tian murmured.
This wasn't arrogance, but a fact.
When he was a sixth-tier Invincible One, his strength was already comparable to a powerful fifth-tier Invincible One. Now that he had broken through to the fifth tier and created a top-tier Invincible Ancestral Technique, his strength had increased by an unknown number of times. He was likely not much weaker than a weaker fourth-tier Invincible One.
The requirement to become a fourth-tier Invincible One was to raise one's cultivation to a very high level and create at least three Invincible Techniques. Only then could one be called a fourth-tier Invincible One.
Cultivation was the easiest to increase; it just required slow accumulation over long years. The difficult part was the three Invincible Techniques.
Moreover, these three techniques could not be of the same type. If they were of the same type—for example, if they were all power-based—then such an Invincible One could not become a fourth-tier Invincible One. Even if they created ten techniques of the same type, they could only be called a pseudo-fourth-tier Invincible One.
This was because creating a second technique of the same type provided little help in increasing strength and made it difficult for the physical body to undergo another qualitative change. Only by comprehending other Eternal Rules—comprehending three or more—and creating three different types of Invincible Techniques could one trigger three qualitative changes in the physical body and finally step into the realm of a fourth-tier Invincible One.
Moving from a fifth-tier to a fourth-tier Invincible One required even more time, and some might never reach it in their entire lives.
This was because some Invincible Ones only had an affinity for one type of Eternal Rule and none for others. Furthermore, having spent endless years and countless resources just to comprehend one Eternal Rule, the idea of comprehending two more was almost an extravagant hope.
Thus, many fifth-tier Invincible Ones in the Heavenly Wind Sea practiced for countless ages without being able to advance to the fourth tier.
But for Ye Tian, advancing to the fourth tier was truly not difficult.
He possessed multiple Eternal-level talents, allowing him to easily comprehend various Eternal Rules. This was his advantage.
Currently, Ye Tian's difficulty lay instead in accumulating cultivation and practicing the Ten Thousand Origins Returning to the Void; these two aspects would take a long time.
"I'll take it slow. First, I'll condense a new duplicated body and have it start practicing the second layer of Ten Thousand Origins Returning to the Void, perfecting it step by step, while my main body focuses on increasing cultivation. Then, I'll occasionally go to Nine Yang Mountain to study the Nine Yang Fish," Ye Tian planned.
However, before doing all that, Ye Tian prepared to take action against some Calamity Beasts...
Previously, he had been constantly searching for Calamity Beasts and had encountered some that weren't too powerful, but he couldn't kill them back then. Now that his cultivation had reached the fifth tier, he naturally had the confidence to slay them.
Basically, as long as it was a beast of one or two hundred Calamities, he was confident he could kill it. As for beasts around five hundred Calamities, he could only manage a stalemate, and he was no match for those over a thousand Calamities.
Consequently.
Ye Tian had his duplicated body begin to target these Calamity Beasts.
Bao'an World.
Ye Tian descended here. The Calamity Beast here was only at 118 Calamities. Although Bao'an World was not currently undergoing a Great Calamity, even though Ye Tian's strength was suppressed significantly by the world, he still had the confidence to slay this beast.
He didn't want to wait until the Bao'an World's Great Calamity to deal with this beast; that would require waiting a long time, and he didn't have that much patience.
Boom!!!!
After Ye Tian descended, the rules and source of Bao'an World suppressed him, and his strength was suddenly weakened by at least seventy percent, leaving him with only thirty percent of his power.
But even with only thirty percent, he still far surpassed an ordinary fifth-tier Invincible One.
Soon, Ye Tian found the Calamity Beast and shattered the space-time node where it resided with a single strike.
Crack!!!
The massive Calamity Beast appeared, staring angrily at Ye Tian. It recognized him; last time he had come to disturb it and had been heavily injured. It hadn't expected him to return.
Seeing the Calamity Beast, Ye Tian said nothing and directly activated his Invincible Ancestral Technique, the Heavenly Limit Combat Technique.
Instantly, Ye Tian's physical strength surged, and his entire body underwent a massive change, transforming into an incredibly terrifying existence.
Next, Ye Tian held a mid-grade Calamity Tool long saber and slashed at the beast.
With a squelch!
The Calamity Beast's body was slashed by Ye Tian, leaving a massive wound from which countless amounts of blood flowed.
Kill!
The two sides began to fight fiercely.
Before long, relying on his invincible Calamity Body and the Calamity Tool saber in his hand, Ye Tian forcibly bludgeoned the Calamity Beast to death.
This was merely the beginning.
In the following days, Ye Tian continued to hunt Calamity Beasts, slaying a total of thirteen in a short period.
As for other Calamity Beasts, he wasn't confident, unless he went further into the Source Sea domains to find other worlds.
But for Ye Tian, these current gains were enough to allow him to cultivate for a long time without worrying about a lack of resources.
Thus, Ye Tian paused his hunting of Calamity Beasts.


Chapter 1545: Occupying the Holy Region World!

Chapter 1545: Occupying the Holy Region World!

The weakest of the Calamity Beasts Ye Tian hunted were over a hundred-calamity level, making their value much higher than the sixty-calamity beasts he had hunted before.
A sixty-calamity beast was worth at least thirty thousand contribution points, while a beast of over a hundred calamities was worth at least a hundred thousand points.
The thirteen Calamity Beasts Ye Tian hunted were ultimately exchanged for 2.01 million contribution points. Since he hadn't spent much time doing so, his speed of accumulating contribution points was incredibly fast. If the other Invincibles of the Heavenly Wind Sea knew of this, they would likely be driven mad with envy.
With so many contribution points, Ye Tian not only lacked no resources, but he could also spend a long time at Nine Yang Mountain to comprehend the Nine Yang Fish.
As time passed, Ye Tian comprehended various Eternal Rules, slowly refining them as his mastery over the different Eternal Rules continued to improve.
Additionally, Ye Tian used his contribution points to purchase various treasures that could enhance his cultivation, among which top-grade Calamity Stones could also be used for that purpose.
As for the top-tier Invincible Calamity Body technique, "Ten Thousand Origins Returning to Ruins," Ye Tian's progress was not fast. This was because he frequently encountered flaws or dangers, requiring him to perfect it time and again to ensure it was perfectly compatible with himself before allowing his main body to practice it.
Consequently, his cultivation speed in this regard was much slower.
However, compared to others, Ye Tian's cultivation speed was already countless times faster.
One domain epoch after another passed. Unknowingly, Ye Tian's current seclusion had exceeded the duration of one Dark Era.
Ye Tian's contribution points had not decreased; instead, they grew more numerous. From the initial two million-plus points, they had reached over ten million points, and most of them remained unused, as he had only spent a small fraction.
In terms of strength, Ye Tian's progress was immense.
"The Ten Thousand Origins Returning to Ruins has finally reached minor success! My cultivation has also increased significantly compared to the past, equivalent to the late stage of a Fifth-tier Invincible!" Ye Tian said happily.
As for Invincible Ancestral Techniques, he could have easily created several, but he was in no hurry.
If he raised his cultivation to the point where it was difficult to improve further and brought his Invincible Calamity Body to the second stage of perfection, he could then create several Invincible Ancestral Techniques to step into the Fourth-tier Invincible realm, maximizing the benefits he would receive.
Although he hadn't continued creating Invincible Ancestral Techniques, his insights into them were not low. Many techniques were only one step away from being created, but he held back. Once his cultivation and Calamity Body reached their peak, he could immediately bring those unformed Invincible Ancestral Techniques to life.
This was his plan.
……
Dark Forbidden Zone.
The human race had already become the sole race of the Dark Forbidden Zone. Other races could no longer survive and had all perished. Furthermore, the humans occupied the vast majority of the Dark Forbidden Zone, abandoning only a few areas that were truly devoid of resources.
As time passed, the human population became too large, leading to the Dark Forbidden Zone becoming somewhat insufficient. If they forced themselves to stay within its confines, internal conflict would become inevitable.
Therefore, occupying other foreign worlds and transforming them to be suitable for human life was currently an urgent task for the human race.
In fact, any Super-Famous power would take this step; for instance, the Blood Mist Alliance had done the same in the past.
Additionally, powers like Calamity Black Mountain and the Firmament Sword Tomb also possessed more than one foreign world; they had several, all under their control.
As a member of the Heavenly Wind Sea, Ye Tian naturally knew how to transform foreign worlds, so he prepared to take action against one.
"I'll choose the Holy Region World!"
Ye Tian decided.
On this day.
The Great Calamity of the Holy Region World arrived. Ye Tian led a group of human Ancestors and a few Supreme Ancestors as they descended upon the Holy Region World.
The human race now had quite a few Supreme Ancestors. After all, Ye Tian could exchange for many treasures from the Heavenly Wind Sea, some of which helped Ancestors break through to the Supreme Ancestor level. Thus, the number of human Supreme Ancestors was constantly increasing and had already reached several dozen.
After Ye Tian descended upon the Holy Region World, he immediately set about wiping out its local powers.
In a short time, the forces of the Holy Region World were completely eradicated. Even those foreign powers could not withstand the human race; their gates were destroyed one by one, and they abandoned the Holy Region World, leaving only the Super-Famous power, the Blood Mist Alliance.
------------------------
Blood Mist World.
The high-level members of the Blood Mist Alliance were holding a meeting.
The several vice-leaders of the Blood Mist Alliance were not qualified to attend this meeting. Those eligible were the Alliance Leader and the three Grand Elders. The three Grand Elders almost never interfered with the alliance's internal affairs, spending most of their time cultivating in the Tianlin Realm.
But this time, all three Grand Elders had returned.
The Blood Mist Alliance Leader, Blood Shadow Mist Ancestor, spoke: "Three Grand Elders, the Holy Region World was originally one of the worlds we planned to occupy, but unexpectedly, our previous plan failed. Now, a human power is opposing us, and this time they have gone too far, actually wanting to seize the Holy Region World as well, even killing some of our Supreme experts."
"What is the opponent's strength?" asked Mingli Mist Ancestor, one of the three Grand Elders.
